### [1] [CanvasAgent: Enabling Complex Image Creation and Editing via Visual Tool Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05465)
*Hairui Zhu,Yiying Yang,Tengjin Weng,Ziyu Lu,Xiao Yao,Xiaoyang Ye,Lin Ma,Wenhao Jiang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CanvasCraft是一个包含140K可执行轨迹的大规模多工具图像创建与编辑数据集，CanvasAgent是一种通过SFT和GRPO训练的工具增强型多模态智能体，能编排异构视觉工具完成复杂图像创作任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态工具使用智能体主要优化感知、搜索或特定领域编辑任务，缺乏大规模可执行图像创建轨迹的监督信号，无法有效处理需要多工具协作的复杂视觉创作任务。

Method: 构建CanvasCraft数据集（140K可执行轨迹+10K RL任务规格）；提出CanvasAgent，先通过SFT学习可执行的推理-行动轨迹，再使用GRPO结合结果级与过程级混合奖励进行优化，在生成过程中检查中间结果、跟踪视觉资产并自适应调整工具决策。

Result: 实验评估了最终图像质量和轨迹行为，证明了CanvasAgent在多工具图像创建工作流中的有效性。

Conclusion: CanvasAgent通过大规模数据集和监督学习策略，实现了从感知增强推理向操作性视觉创作的转变，能有效编排多工具完成复杂图像创建与编辑任务。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域常需多工具协同（如目标检测→分割→变化检测→标注输出），CanvasAgent的框架可直接适配：1) 用CanvasCraft范式构建遥感多工具数据集（如SAR与光学影像融合、地物分割→矢量化→专题图生成）；2) 将GRPO混合奖励机制引入遥感流程评估（如分割精度+过程合规性）；3) 支持中间结果检查可缓解遥感数据量大、步骤冗长导致的错误累积问题。

Abstract (英文): Complex image creation and editing often require more than a single generation or editing model. A user request may involve synthesizing images, localizing objects, segmenting regions, editing selected content, compositing intermediate assets, reading text, and enhancing the final result. Such tasks shift multimodal agents from perception-augmented reasoning to manipulation-centered visual creation, where tools must actively transform visual states rather than merely inspect them. However, existing multimodal tool-use agents are mostly optimized for perception, search, or domain-specific editing, and lack large-scale supervision for executable image-creation trajectories. In this paper, we introduce CanvasCraft, a large-scale multimodal tool-use dataset for complex image creation and editing, and \textbf{CanvasAgent}, a tool-augmented multimodal agent that learns to orchestrate heterogeneous visual tools through multi-turn interaction. CanvasCraft contains 140K fully annotated executable trajectories and 10K
  RL task specifications. CanvasAgent is first trained with SFT to learn executable reasoning-action trajectories, and is then optimized with GRPO using a hybrid reward that combines outcome- and process-level signals. During rollout, CanvasAgent inspects intermediate results, tracks visual assets, and adapts tool decisions to the evolving visual state. Experiments evaluate both final image quality and trajectory behavior, demonstrating the effectiveness of CanvasAgent and the proposed dataset for complex multi-tool image creation workflows.

</details>


### [2] [A Task-Driven Evaluation of UAV Detection and Tracking under Synthetic Fog](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05467)
*Amir Pouladi,Vesal Ahsani,Haijun Li,Homayoun Najjaran,Afzal Suleman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向小型无人机在雾天场景下的任务驱动评估框架，将深度感知合成雾气生成、图像复原、目标检测与跟踪统一到同一流水线中。研究发现雾气主要增加漏检率，雾气包含训练最有效，且图像复原质量并不直接等价于下游感知性能的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型无人机在天空主导的长距离成像中，雾气严重降低可见度，影响下游检测和跟踪任务的可靠性。由于难以大规模采集和标注真实雾天无人机场景，现有研究缺乏将合成雾气、图像复原与下游感知任务联合评估的系统性框架。

Method: 采用单目深度估计和大气散射模型从真实晴天图像生成合成雾气；比较经典、CNN和Transformer三类复原方法；选择最优复原模型集成到检测-跟踪流水线；在仅晴空训练和含雾训练两种模式下评估多个检测器；在晴空、雾天和复原视频序列上评估基于检测的跟踪性能。

Result: 雾气大幅降低检测和跟踪性能，主要表现为漏检增加；含雾训练对鲁棒性提升最一致；测试时复原仅在检测器仅用晴空数据训练时最有帮助；图像级复原质量与下游感知性能改进不成比例。

Conclusion: 图像复原质量不能直接转化为下游检测和跟踪的性能增益，因此应在任务驱动框架下联合评估复原、检测和跟踪性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该框架可直接迁移到遥感中的雾天遥感影像目标检测与跟踪任务：(1) 利用卫星或无人机遥感影像的深度估计生成合成雾气，替代真实雾天数据采集；(2) 将任务驱动评估从无人机扩展到遥感场景，评估不同复原方法对遥感目标（车辆、船舶、建筑物等）检测与跟踪的影响；(3) 可进一步引入多光谱/高光谱数据辅助去雾，提升遥感影像的复原质量。

Abstract (英文): Fog severely degrades the visibility of small unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) in skydominant, long-range imagery, reducing the reliability of downstream detection and tracking. This paper presents a task-driven evaluation framework that links depth-aware synthetic fog generation, image restoration, object detection, and tracking within a unified pipeline. Given the practical difficulty of collecting and annotating foggy UAV scenes, synthetic fog is generated from real clear-weather outdoor images containing UAV targets using monocular depth estimation and the atmospheric scattering model. Representative restoration methods from classical, convolutional neural network (CNN)-based, and transformer-based families are first compared, after which the selected restoration model is integrated into the downstream perception pipeline. Detection is evaluated under both clean-only and fog-inclusive training regimes using multiple detector variants, while tracking-by-detection is assessed on clean, foggy, and restored video sequences. Beyond image-level restoration metrics, the study evaluates how fog and restoration affect detection robustness and tracking performance. The results show that fog substantially degrades both detection and tracking, primarily through increased missed detections. Fog-inclusive training provides the most consistent improvement in robustness, whereas test-time restoration is most beneficial when the detector has been trained only on clean imagery. These findings show that restoration quality does not necessarily translate into proportional gains in downstream perception and therefore should be evaluated jointly with detection and tracking performance.

</details>


### [3] [Binocular Gaze Estimation with Single Camera and Single Light Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05473)
*Tongbing Huang,Yang Fu,Yunfei Wang,Zhaocan Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种仅用单摄像头和单光源的视线估计方法，通过引入"虚拟光源"（与真实光源关于相机对称放置）生成"虚拟光斑"，利用瞳孔间距与光斑间距的关系估计虚拟光斑位置，结合多项式回归实现头部自由移动下的视线估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在移动设备等场景中，传统双光源视线追踪系统硬件成本较高且组件占用空间大，有必要探索使用更少光源（尤其是单光源）实现自由头部运动下的视线估计，以降低硬件复杂度和系统成本。

Method: 1) 引入"虚拟光源"概念，其与真实光源关于相机光轴对称放置，生成对应的"虚拟光斑"；2) 利用捕获图像中双眼瞳孔间距与双光斑（真实光斑+虚拟光斑）间距的几何关系，估计虚拟光斑在图像中的位置；3) 假设双光源可用，采用多项式回归模型进行视线估计；4) 提出一种适用于单光斑系统的归一化因子，改善回归方法的性能。

Result: 单光源系统的视线估计性能可达到可接受水平，但与双光源系统相比存在性能退化。

Conclusion: 单摄像头+单光源方案在降低硬件需求的同时能够实现可用的视线估计，为移动设备等资源受限场景提供了可行的低成本解决方案，但精度与双光源系统仍有差距。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。1) 将虚拟光源概念引入遥感图像中的目标定位：利用单光源（如太阳）和虚拟光斑的几何关系，辅助遥感图像中地物阴影分析，实现无主动照明条件下的三维姿态或高度估计；2) 多项式回归+归一化因子方法可迁移至遥感影像中地物特征点的配准与几何校正，在少量控制点下提升拟合精度；3) 单传感器+虚拟参考点的思路可用于轻量化遥感平台（如无人机）以降低载荷，实现无需多传感器融合的场景理解。

Abstract (英文): According to commonly consented theories, the minimum hardware requirement for gaze tracker is one camera and two light sources to realize gaze estimation with free head movements. However, in some scenarios such as eye tracking on mobile devices, it is preferable to use less components, especially light sources. We propose a gaze estimation method with one camera and one light source. A "virtual light source" is introduced, which is geometrically placed symmetrically to the real light source with respect to the camera, and generates a "virtual glint" in the acquired image. We estimate the "virtual glint" by exploiting the relationship between the distance between two pupils and two glints in the captured image, and estimate the gaze with polynomial regression assuming two light sources are available. A new normalization factor for regression method is verified, which turns out to be practical for one-glint system. The performance is proved to be acceptable, while degradation is noticed compared to system with two actual light sources.

</details>


### [4] [Ground3D-LMM: Fine-Grained 3D Point Grounding and Spatial Reasoning with LMM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05493)
*Amol Harsh,Zongyan Han,Jean Lahoud,Ye Liu,Rao Muhammad Anwer,Hisham Cholakkal,Salman Khan,Fahad Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Ground3D-LMM，一个统一模型，以点云和可选RGB图像为输入，支持3D空间对话，具备点级空间定位和公制度量数值输出能力（如尺寸、厚度、间隙、距离）。构建了基于ScanNet/ScanNet++的大规模数据集（约250万QA对），定义了3D Grounded Measurement任务，为可验证、可度量的3D对话理解建立了强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D大多模态模型要么只能对话但缺乏显式3D空间定位，要么只能做3D定位但不支持交互式、度量感知的对话。缺乏同时具备3D定位能力和公制度量输出的统一模型。

Method: 提出Ground3D-LMM统一模型，输入点云和可选RGB图像，输出点级定位结果和公制度量数值；定义了3D Grounded Measurement任务；基于ScanNet和ScanNet++构建大规模数据集，含密集物体/部件标注和约250万QA对，覆盖8个子任务。

Result: 在多数据集和多任务上进行了大量实验，证明Ground3D-LMM为有定位、有度量感知的3D对话理解提供了强基线。

Conclusion: Ground3D-LMM实现了3D空间中可验证（显式点级定位）且可度量（公制单位数值输出）的对话能力，填补了现有3D LMM在定位与度量交叉领域的空白。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1) 将点云+RGB输入框架直接迁移至遥感3D点云场景理解，如建筑物、植被的尺寸/高度/间距测量结合语义定位；(2) 借鉴其"点级定位+公制度量输出"的对话范式，构建遥感领域的交互式查询系统（如"该建筑物的高度是多少？→定位建筑并输出米制高度"）；(3) 引入八类任务设计，可扩展至遥感地物属性问答（如树冠直径、楼间距、道路宽度等）；(4) 需适配遥感点云的数据稀疏性、大尺度范围和标注体系差异。

Abstract (英文): Natural-language queries about 3D environments become actionable when responses are verifiable and metric. Verifiability requires explicit grounding to the referred 3D region, while metric answers report physical measurements in real-world units (e.g., size, thickness, clearance, and distance). Existing 3D large multimodal models (LMMs) approaches remain limited: conversational systems typically respond without explicit 3D grounding, while 3D grounding models are not designed for interactive, metric-aware dialogue. In this paper, we present Ground3D-LMM, a unified model that takes a point cloud and an optional RGB image as input and supports 3D spatial conversation with (i) point-grounded responses and (ii) metric numeric outputs at both object and part granularity, including multi-object queries. To evaluate this intersection of grounding and measurement, we define the 3D Grounded Measurement task, which requires predicting the referred 3D region and the corresponding metric quantities in real-world units. We introduce a large-scale dataset built on ScanNet and ScanNet++ datasets with dense object and part annotations and roughly 2.5M question-answer pairs spanning eight tasks, along with a manually verified test set. Extensive experiments on multiple datasets and tasks show that our proposed Ground3D-LMM model provides a strong baseline for grounded, metric-aware 3D conversational understanding. Our dataset and model are publicly available.

</details>


### [5] [Light-Omni: Reflex over Reasoning in Agentic Video Understanding with Long-Term Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05511)
*Chang Nie,Jiaju Wei,Junlan Feng,Chaoyou Fu,Caifeng Shan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Light-Omni 是一种轻量级多模态视频智能体框架，通过双重上下文状态（全局状态和参数化潜状态）实现无需迭代推理的快速视频理解，在多个基准上取得精度提升2.4%、速度提升12.1倍、GPU内存效率提升2.6倍的显著效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频智能体依赖“侦探式”迭代推理（如搜索、证据聚合）来补偿全局上下文缺失和语义对齐不足，导致高昂的计算成本和延迟。本文旨在设计一种轻量级、反射式的视频理解框架，避免繁重的迭代推理。

Method: 提出Light-Omni框架，核心是双重上下文状态设计：(1) 全局状态——通过层次化合并持续整合情景记忆的有限大小多模态脚本，保留近期细节并总结过去事件；(2) 参数化潜状态——基于全局上下文生成，直接驱动自主行动并产生检索嵌入，实现语义对齐的检索和反射式响应。

Result: 在多个视频基准上验证有效性，相比M3-Agent：平均准确率提升2.4%，速度提升12.1倍，GPU内存效率提升2.6倍；同时可作为记忆系统提升现有MLLM的性能和效率。

Conclusion: Light-Omni通过耦合的双重上下文设计成功实现了无需迭代推理的轻量级视频理解，兼顾了性能、速度和效率，并可作为通用记忆系统增强其他多模态大模型。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感视频分析（如卫星视频监控、无人机长时航拍）同样面临长时序、多模态数据处理的效率和延迟问题。可将Light-Omni的双重上下文状态机制引入遥感视频理解：(1) 全局状态用于维护遥感场景的时空上下文（如地物变化、目标轨迹）；(2) 参数化潜状态直接驱动目标检测/跟踪的检索嵌入生成，避免逐帧迭代推理。尤其适用于边缘设备上的实时遥感视频分析场景，显著降低计算开销。

Abstract (英文): Agentic video understanding equips models with long-term memory to autonomously process and respond to continuous, long-horizon multimodal streams. However, advanced video agents often rely on ``detective-style'' iterative reasoning for action control (e.g., $\mathtt{search}$) and evidence aggregation, incurring prohibitive costs and latency. We argue that such heavy reasoning primarily compensates for the lack of global context and semantic misalignment in retrieval. This paper introduces Light-Omni, a multimodal agent framework for reflexive and lightweight video understanding. It achieves this through dual contextual states that instantly build the required context in a single forward pass. First, we maintain a global state, a finite-sized multimodal script continuously consolidated from episodic memory, serving as the global context for Light-Omni. Through hierarchical merging, it preserves recent details while summarizing past events. Second, conditioned on this global context, we generate a parametric latent state that directly drives autonomous actions and produces retrieval embeddings, with minimal latency. Benefiting from this coupled design, Light-Omni achieves semantically aligned retrieval and reflexive responses while avoiding iterative reasoning. Extensive experiments validate the effectiveness of Light-Omni across multiple video benchmarks. Notably, it outperforms M3-Agent with an average 2.4% accuracy gain, a 12.1$\times$ speedup, and a 2.6$\times$ improvement in GPU memory efficiency. Furthermore, it serves as a memory system to enhance both the performance and efficiency of existing MLLMs. Project page: https://clare-nie.github.io/Light-Omni.

</details>


### [6] [Statistical Adversaries: Natural Backdoor-like Features in Vision Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05516)
*Paul K. Mandal,Pavan Reddy,Tristan Malatynski*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文发现视觉数据中天然存在的统计信号可以像后门触发器一样影响模型预测，无需恶意插入，并将这些信号称为"统计对手"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注模型特定的人为对抗攻击，但忽视了数据集中天然存在的、非人为注入的统计信号也能像后门触发器一样操纵模型预测，这一潜在安全漏洞尚未被充分认知。

Method: 在ImageNet中分析与特定标签强相关的统计模式，通过统计控制去除候选信号中的随机相关性，然后验证这些信号是否直接且可预测地改变模型预测。

Result: 这些统计信号比通用数据损坏更具针对性，且能在不同模型架构之间迁移，表明某些脆弱性源于数据集结构和分布特征，而非单个模型的特异性。

Conclusion: 普通数据集即使在没有恶意投毒的情况下也存在可被利用的对抗表面，建议数据集审计不仅应将虚假结构视为偏差或可解释性失败，还应将其视为视觉模型的潜在攻击面。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感数据中存在大量天然统计信号（如特定地物在不同季节/光照下的光谱模式、云覆盖与特定地理区域的关联），这些信号可能充当统计对手。具体方案：(1) 在遥感分类任务中检测与特定标签（如"森林"与"阴影"）存在虚假关联的统计模式；(2) 验证这些模式能否跨传感器/分辨率迁移；(3) 在遥感数据集构建时增加统计对抗审计流程，识别并消除可能被利用的虚假相关性。

Abstract (英文): Model-specific adversarial attacks have been extensively studied. We study a different failure mode: naturally occurring statistical signals in vision data that can behave like backdoor-like triggers without being maliciously inserted. We call these signals statistical adversaries. We analyse Imagenet to find patterns that are strongly linked to certain labels. We then use statistical controls to remove random correlations from our candidate signals. Finally, we demonstrate that these signals directly and predictably alter model predictions. These statistical adversaries are more targeted than generic corruptions and transfer across different model architectures. This suggests that some vulnerabilities are driven by dataset structure and distribution rather than a single model's idiosyncrasies. We conclude that ordinary datasets can contain exploitable adversarial surfaces even in the absence of poisoning, and suggest that dataset audits should treat spurious structure not only as a source of bias or interpretability failure, but also as a latent attack surface for vision models.

</details>


### [7] [Rendering-Aware Bayesian 3D Gaussian Splatting with Native Uncertainty and Adaptive Complexity Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05522)
*Gaoxiang Jia,Vikram Appia,Junzhou Huang,Xinlei Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种渲染感知的贝叶斯3D高斯泼溅（3DGS）框架，利用Normal-Inverse-Wishart后验对高斯的均值和协方差进行建模，并引入Dirichlet过程扩展以提供概率化的分量使用信号。在主动视图选择任务中，该方法在PSNR和LPIPS上优于标准集成基线，且95%覆盖率误差较深度集成降低约10倍，训练成本仅为约三分之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准3DGS训练依赖于点估计和手工启发式规则，缺乏不确定性量化和原理性的复杂度控制，特别是在稀疏视图或固定采集预算下，模型难以识别弱支持的几何结构并选择信息量高的视图。

Method: 1) 采用Normal-Inverse-Wishart（NIW）后验对高斯原语的均值和协方差进行建模，利用渲染器导出的代理摘要实现闭式推断；2) 引入可选的Dirichlet过程扩展，提供概率化的分量使用信号；3) 显式区分训练调度中闭式推断与近似推断的边界；4) 通过重新渲染后验几何样本，获得原生的预测不确定性，用于区间校准和主动视图选择。

Result: 主动视图选择（16→32视图）下，NIW采集比标准集成基线PSNR提升+0.453 dB、LPIPS降低-0.0146，在39个场景-种子对中胜出29个；NIW原生区间将95%覆盖率误差从0.796降至0.046（约17倍提升），相比3成员深度集成的0.454降低约10倍，训练成本约为后者的三分之一；重建兼容性检查中，NIW相比标准3DGS仅增加1.6%训练时间，PSNR提升+0.030 dB。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯3DGS作为一种实用的概率化场景表示，能够有效服务于决策型任务（如主动视图选择），在提供可靠不确定性估计的同时保持较低的计算开销。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1) 遥感领域常面临有限视角（如卫星遥感的多时相、多角度成像受限），可将贝叶斯3DGS用于稀疏视图下的三维重建与不确定性引导的主动视角规划；2) 将NIW后验的不确定性估计用于遥感变化检测，识别几何重建置信度低的区域作为潜在变化候选；3) 结合遥感多光谱/高光谱数据，将不同波段视为多视图输入，利用主动视图选择策略优化波段组合采集；4) 将Dirichlet过程扩展用于遥感场景中的地物类别数量自适应推断，实现无监督的地物分割。

Abstract (英文): 3D Gaussian splatting (3DGS) is a strong representation for real-time novel-view synthesis, but its standard training pipeline relies on point estimates and hand-tuned heuristics, providing no native uncertainty or principled complexity control. This is most limiting under sparse views or fixed acquisition budgets, where a model must identify weakly supported geometry and select informative views. We introduce a rendering-aware Bayesian 3DGS framework that tracks Gaussian geometry with a Normal-Inverse-Wishart posterior over means and covariances using renderer-derived surrogate summaries. An optional Dirichlet-process extension adds a probabilistic component-usage signal, and the training schedule makes the closed-form versus approximate inference boundary explicit. Re-rendering posterior geometry samples yields native predictive uncertainty for interval calibration and active view selection. In a fixed-budget 16-to-32 active-view task, native NIW acquisition improves PSNR by +0.453 dB and LPIPS by -0.0146 over a scoring-only 3-member standard-ensemble baseline, winning 29/39 scene-seed pairs and 10/13 scene means; it also improves over PPU-style (+0.355 dB) and NIW-proxy (+0.401 dB) acquisition. NIW native intervals reduce 95% coverage error by about 17x relative to a shared proxy (0.046 vs. 0.796) and are about 10x closer to nominal coverage than a 3-member deep ensemble (0.047 vs. 0.454) at roughly one-third the training cost. As a reconstruction compatibility check, paired NIW-vs-standard analysis over 39 scene-seed runs yields +0.030 dB PSNR with 1.6% additional training time. These results position Bayesian 3DGS as a practical probabilistic scene representation for decision-facing tasks such as active view selection.

</details>


### [8] [Multi-Teacher Contrastive Distillation for Edge-Efficient Pathology Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05533)
*Tim Lenz,Maurice Heide,Marco Gustav,Nic G. Reitsam,Jakob Nikolas Kather*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MuCoDi是一个将计算病理学基础模型(PFMs)蒸馏为轻量级边缘编码器的预训练框架。通过对比蒸馏目标(改进自MoCo v3)，使用MobileOne和RepViT学生网络学习多个PFMs的冻结瓦片嵌入。在14.3M TCGA瓦片上预训练后，RepViT学生模型在23个分类任务上达到接近教师性能(71.0%外部AUROC vs 教师71.8%)，而参数量减少数个数量级(R1.0仅6.4M参数)。在树莓派5上，百万参数以下的MobileOne模型相比Virchow2实现605倍加速，同时保持66.5%-66.9%外部AUROC。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算病理学基础模型体积庞大、推理成本高，难以在病理科进行本地部署。现有蒸馏方法通常针对单一教师回归训练，未能充分利用多个互补教师模型的优势，且学生模型仍不够轻量。

Method: 提出MuCoDi框架：(1)从Virchow2、UNI2和H-Optimus-1三个PFMs中提取冻结的瓦片嵌入作为教师；(2)采用MoCo v3的对比蒸馏目标，用教师嵌入替代动量编码器键；(3)训练轻量级MobileOne和RepViT学生编码器；(4)在14.3M TCGA瓦片(仅11.8K全切片图像)上预训练，并在23个下游分类任务上评估冻结编码器。

Result: RepViT学生(MuCoEdge-R2.3和R1.5)达到71.0%外部AUROC，距最佳教师Virchow2(71.8%)仅差0.8个百分点；MuCoEdge-R2.3获得最佳外部F1(51.8%)和第二佳AUPRC(53.3%)；MuCoEdge-R1.0仅6.4M参数、1.12 GFLOPs即达70.9% AUROC；MobileOne学生在树莓派5上实现最高605倍单瓦片加速，保持66.5%-66.9%外部AUROC。

Conclusion: 通过多教师对比蒸馏，可以在保持接近PFM性能的同时大幅压缩模型体积，实现计算病理学模型的实际边缘部署。证明了PFM质量的特征表示可以迁移到极轻量级的编码器中，在资源受限硬件上仍保持有效性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1)遥感领域同样存在大规模基础模型(如SatMAE、SpectralGPT等)推理成本高的问题，可将MuCoDi的多教师对比蒸馏框架迁移至遥感，从多个遥感基础模型中蒸馏轻量级边缘编码器；(2)针对遥感多光谱/高光谱特性，可引入通道级对比蒸馏策略，替代原方法的瓦片级特征蒸馏；(3)MoCo v3对比蒸馏中的教师嵌入缓存策略可直接应用于遥感大尺寸影像的patch级特征学习；(4)在无人机或星载边缘计算场景中(类似树莓派部署实验)，可评估MobileOne等轻量架构在嵌入式设备上的推理加速比与精度权衡。

Abstract (英文): Computational pathology foundation models (PFMs) have advanced whole-slide image analysis. However, their size and inference cost hinder local deployment in pathology departments. We propose MuCoDi, a pretraining framework that distills frozen tile embeddings from multiple PFMs into compact edge-oriented encoders. Instead of regressing individual teacher features, MuCoDi trains lightweight MobileOne and RepViT students with a contrastive distillation objective adapted from MoCo v3, where cached Virchow2, UNI2, and H-Optimus-1 embeddings replace momentum-encoder keys. We pretrain students on 14.3M TCGA tiles from only 11.8K WSIs and evaluate frozen encoders on 23 clinically curated downstream classification tasks. RepViT-based MuCoEdge students retain near-teacher performance while reducing model size by orders of magnitude: MuCoEdge-R2.3 and MuCoEdge-R1.5 reach 71.0% external AUROC, within 0.8 percentage points of the best teacher (Virchow2, 71.8%), while MuCoEdge-R2.3 obtains the best external F1 and the second-best AUPRC (51.8% and 53.3%). MuCoEdge-R1.0 reaches 70.9% AUROC with only 6.4M parameters and 1.12 GFLOPs. On a Raspberry Pi 5, sub-million-parameter MobileOne students achieve up to 605-fold single-tile speedup over Virchow2 while retaining 66.5% to 66.9% external AUROC, demonstrating that PFM-quality pathology representations can be moved toward practical edge deployment. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/mucodi-6243.

### [9] [Harnessing Generative Image Models for Training-Free Primitive Shape Abstraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05568)
*Gregor Kobsik,Tim Elsner,Leif Kobbelt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种无需训练的无参数管线，利用多视图渲染、视觉-语言模型和生成式图像模型，将3D物体分解为语义部件并拟合超二次曲面基元，在HumanPrim和Toys4K数据集上以最少基元数达到了最优的Chamfer距离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D形状基元表示方法依赖特定任务训练，缺乏类别通用性和方向不变性；而大规模预训练的生成式图像模型虽具备通用视觉理解能力，但通常需要微调才能用于下游任务。本文探索能否直接利用预训练能力（无需任何训练）实现3D形状的基元分解。

Method: 1) 对3D物体渲染多视角图像；2) 用视觉-语言模型分析语义部件；3) 用生成式图像模型生成颜色编码的部件分割掩码；4) 将分割掩码反投影到3D几何上；5) 通过参数优化为每个部件拟合超二次曲面基元。整个管线无任何可学习参数。

Result: 在HumanPrim和Toys4K数据集上，该方法以平均每物体5-9个基元实现了所有评估方法中最低的Chamfer距离。地面真值分割实验表明部件分割（而非基元拟合）是当前精度瓶颈，说明该方法精度上限随生成式模型改进而提升。

Conclusion: 验证了无需训练即可利用大规模预训练生成模型实现3D部件分解与基元表示的可行性，方法具有类别无关性和方向不变性，且精度有望随生成式模型进步而持续提升。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感3D场景（如LiDAR点云、卫星城市场景）中存在大量规则几何结构（建筑物、屋顶、车辆等）。具体方案：1) 对遥感3D点云进行多视角渲染（如正视/俯视图），利用视觉-语言模型识别语义部件（屋顶、墙面、窗户）；2) 生成式模型分割后反投影至3D点云，拟合超二次曲面或长方体基元，实现无需标注的建筑物结构分解；3) 针对遥感数据特点，可引入正交投影渲染和位姿归一化以增强方向不变性；4) 可扩展为城市级别的3D基元重建，服务于数字孪生和规划应用。

Abstract (英文): Representing 3D shapes as compact sets of geometric primitives is fundamental to robotics, simulation, and scene understanding. Generative image models trained at scale have recently emerged as generalist visual learners that can identify and segment object parts directly in the image domain, across arbitrary categories and without task-specific training. Adapting such models to downstream tasks typically requires fine-tuning; we ask whether their pretrained capability can instead be harnessed directly, without any training, and answer affirmatively with a training-free harness. Our pipeline renders multi-view images of a 3D object, uses a vision-language model to analyze its semantic parts, prompts a generative image model to paint a color-coded part segmentation mask, reprojects it onto the geometry, and fits a superquadric primitive to each part via parameter optimization. The approach contains no learned parameters: it is category-agnostic and orientation-invariant, properties that previous learning-based models struggled with. Its accuracy ceiling rises with future generative-model improvements, which we confirm with a ground-truth segmentation study showing that part segmentation, not primitive fitting, is the current accuracy bottleneck. On HumanPrim and Toys4K, our method achieves the lowest Chamfer distance among all evaluated methods, using 5--9 primitives per object on average.

### [10] [Hierarchical Classification via Cascading Feature Elimination: Application to Human Phenotype Ontology-Aligned Facial Phenotyping (FaceMesh2HPO)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05585)
*Fabio Hellmann,Alexander Hustinx,Benjamin D. Solomon,GestaltMatcher Database Consortium,Tzung-Chien Hsieh,Peter Krawitz,Elisabeth André*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FaceMesh2HPO是一个基于3D面部网格和层次化PointNet的分类框架，用于将面部表型描述符映射到人类表型本体（HPO），在10种疾病、107个HPO术语上训练，AUROC在0.55-0.89之间，在父节点表现优于叶节点，外部泛化性因疾病而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有面部表型分析缺乏与标准临床本体（HPO）的系统对齐，且2D图像对复杂面部的表征能力有限，亟需一种可解释、基于3D几何且与本体链接的分类方法以支持临床诊断。

Method: 收集124名临床医生对10种疾病的107个HPO术语标注，结合非综合征对照组，从2D图像生成478个关键点的3D面部网格；构建层次化PointNet流水线，采用级联分类和特征消除策略，并融合3D网格、面部轮廓和人口统计元数据。

Conclusion: 层次化3D面部几何建模可实现可解释、本体链接的表型分类，但稀有叶节点性能不足，需提升数据多样性和特征选择策略以增强鲁棒性和临床实用性。

Abstract (英文): FaceMesh2HPO is a framework for classifying facial phenotypic descriptors aligned with the Human Phenotype Ontology (HPO) to support clinical diagnosis. Using annotations from 124 clinicians across 10 disorders (107 HPO terms) combined with non-syndromic controls, we generated 3D facial meshes (478 landmarks) from 2D images and trained a hierarchical PointNet-based pipeline with cascading classification and feature elimination. The best models, incorporating 3D meshes, facial outline, and demographic metadata, achieved AUROCs between ~0.55 and ~0.89, with higher performance at parent nodes than leaf terms. External validation showed variable generalizability across disorders. Results demonstrate that hierarchical modeling of 3D facial geometry enables interpretable, ontology-linked phenotype classification, though performance on rare leaf terms remains limited. Improved data diversity and feature selection strategies are needed to enhance robustness and clinical utility.

### [11] [Patch Knowledge Transfer for Efficient AI-Generated Image Quality Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05605)
*Jiquan Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Patch Knowledge Transfer (PKT)框架，通过知识蒸馏实现AI生成图像质量评估中视觉表征能力与推理效率的协同优化，在4个AIGIQA数据库上学生模型保持与教师模型相当的性能同时降低67.7%的计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决AI生成图像质量评估中现有方法的两大局限：复杂特征提取方法计算成本高无法实时推理，简单图像缩放方法评估精度显著不足。目标是在高效推理与高精度评估之间取得更好的平衡。

Method: 提出PKT知识蒸馏优化框架，设计双模型架构：教师模型采用局部-全局混合处理提供高质量监督信号，学生模型仅依赖全局处理通过多层级监督继承教师表征能力，实现视觉表征能力与推理效率的协同优化。

Result: 在4个AIGIQA数据库上，PKT框架使学生模型在保持与教师模型相当性能的同时，计算成本降低67.7%，且相比现有方法在模型效率与评估精度之间实现了更优平衡。

Conclusion: PKT框架通过多层级知识转移机制有效解决了生成图像质量评估中效率与精度的权衡问题，为大规模AI生成图像的高效质量评估提供了可行方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1) 遥感图像质量受传感器噪声、大气影响等复杂因素干扰，可将PKT的教师模型扩展为多尺度遥感特征提取器（局部纹理+全局地物结构），学生模型用于星载或边缘设备上的实时质量评估；2) 遥感图像通常存在标注稀缺问题，可利用PKT框架在学生模型上实现轻量化推理，适用于大规模遥感图像数据的快速筛选与质量分拣；3) 可引入遥感领域特定的退化模型（如云雾遮挡、条带噪声）到教师模型的局部处理分支中，提升对学生模型在真实遥感场景下的泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): With the rapid advancement of image generation technologies, perceptual quality assessment of AI-generated images has emerged as a crucial research direction in computer vision. The core challenge of this task lies in achieving efficient quality assessment for massive generated images. Current mainstream approaches exhibit two key limitations: 1) Methods employing complex feature extraction strategies, while improving performance, incur prohibitive computational costs that hinder real-time inference; 2) Simple image scaling-based solutions, despite their computational efficiency, demonstrate significantly inferior assessment accuracy. To address this critical issue, we propose Patch Knowledge Transfer (PKT), a knowledge distillation-based optimization framework that achieves synergistic optimization of visual representation capability and inference efficiency through an innovative multi-level knowledge transfer mechanism. Specifically, we design a dual-model architecture: a teacher model with local-global hybrid processing provides high-quality supervision signals, while a student model relying solely on global processing efficiently inherits the teacher's representation capacity through multi-level supervision. Extensive experiments conducted on 4 AIGIQA databases demonstrate that the PKT framework enables the student model to maintain performance comparable to the teacher while reducing computational costs by 67.7\%. Furthermore, compared to existing methods, our approach achieves a superior balance between model efficiency and assessment accuracy.

### [12] [Cross-Contextual Vision-Language Adaptation with LoRA for Personalized Severe Adverse Event Detection in Clinical Wound Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05625)
*Aditi Naiknaware,Jian Sun,Aminreza Khandan,Shengyang Huang,Sean Dow,Bijan Najafi,Salimeh Sekeh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多模态框架，用于自动化伤口监测和严重不良事件（SAE）检测。该框架基于冻结的BiomedCLIP骨干网络，通过双流LoRA融合机制结合临床笔记和伤口描述，并引入伤口专用的OOD检测框架（结合语义匹配、视觉典型性、字幕-文本对齐和字幕-视觉对齐），同时利用协变量一致性和时间漂移惩罚捕捉愈合动态。在纵向伤口数据集上的实验表明，该方法在伤口愈合评估和SAE检测方面均表现良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伤口监测是一个重要但未被充分解决的临床问题，及时识别感染、组织恶化、延迟愈合等严重不良事件对患者预后至关重要。现有视觉-语言模型虽具备多模态推理能力，但缺乏领域特定的临床知识融合机制，且难以检测偏离训练分布的异常情况。

Method: 1）基于冻结的BiomedCLIP骨干网络，采用双流LoRA框架编码临床笔记和伤口描述；2）提出跨上下文LoRA融合机制，实现临床语义与视觉伤口描述之间的信息交换；3）构建伤口专用的OOD检测框架，融合语义匹配、视觉典型性、字幕-文本对齐和字幕-视觉对齐，形成统一的SAE评分；4）引入协变量一致性和时间漂移惩罚，利用随访间伤口特征变化捕捉愈合动态。

Result: 在临床随访收集的纵向伤口数据集上，该方法在伤口愈合评估和SAE检测任务上均取得了有竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了语义增强、时间感知的视觉-语言系统在临床伤口监测和早期风险识别方面的潜力，为多模态融合和异常检测提供了新思路。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1）遥感时序变化检测可借鉴本文的时间漂移惩罚和协方差一致性机制，用于监测地表覆盖变化或灾害损伤演变；2）遥感领域的多模态数据（如光学影像+雷达+地理文本描述）可采用双流LoRA融合架构，实现异源数据的高效对齐；3）遥感异常检测（如森林火灾、非法建筑）可引入本文的OOD评分框架，结合语义匹配和视觉典型性进行分布外检测；4）BiomedCLIP可替换为遥感专用的CLIP变体（如RemoteCLIP），LoRA微调策略同样适用于遥感大模型。

Abstract (英文): Wound monitoring is a critical yet underserved clinical challenge, where timely identification of severe adverse events (SAEs) such as infection, tissue deterioration, and delayed healing can significantly impact patient outcomes. While vision-language models (VLMs) show strong multimodal reasoning, they often lack domain-specific grounding to integrate wound imagery with heterogeneous clinical information, and provide limited mechanisms for detecting cases that diverge from the training distribution. We present a multimodal framework for automated wound monitoring and SAE detection. Our approach leverages paired clinical notes and wound descriptions capturing visual characteristics such as appearance, surrounding skin condition, color changes, and signs of inflammation or healing progression, encoded through a dual-stream Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) framework built on a frozen BiomedCLIP backbone. We introduce a cross-contextual LoRA fusion mechanism enabling information exchange between clinical semantics and visual wound descriptors, producing context-aware multimodal representations without full model fine-tuning. To identify personalized SAEs, we propose a wound-specific out-of-distribution (OOD) detection framework combining semantic matching, visual typicality, caption-text alignment, and caption-visual alignment into a unified SAE (OOD) score. To capture healing dynamics, we incorporate covariate consistency and temporal drift penalties that leverage changes in wound characteristics across visits. Experiments on a longitudinal wound dataset collected through clinical visits show promising performance on both wound healing assessment and SAE detection, highlighting the potential of semantically enriched, temporally aware vision-language systems for clinical wound monitoring and early risk identification.

</details>


### [13] [Taxlifier: Leveraging Disease Taxonomy for Enhanced Multi-Label Classification in Chest Radiography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05628)
*Mohammad S. Majdi,Jeffrey J. Rodriguez*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了两种层次化多标签分类方法（基于损失和基于logit），通过利用胸部病理之间的层级关系，在三个大规模CXR数据集上显著提升了疾病分类的准确性（提升12%）、AUC（提升13%）和F1分数（提升24%），优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出两种层次化多标签分类技术：1）基于损失的方法（loss-based），将层次信息直接整合到优化过程中；2）基于logit的方法（logit-based），根据疾病分类学中父类信息调整每个类别的预测概率。

Abstract (英文): Accurate and efficient classification of thoracic diseases in chest X-ray (CXR) images is crucial for timely diagnosis and treatment. However, the presence of multiple pathologies with overlapping visual characteristics poses significant challenges for automated classification systems. In this study, we propose two novel hierarchical multi-label classification techniques, namely the loss-based and logit-based methods, to address these challenges by leveraging the hierarchical relationships among different thoracic pathologies. The loss-based technique integrates hierarchical information directly into the optimization process, while the logit-based method adjusts the predicted probabilities of each class based on its parent class in the disease taxonomy. We evaluate the performance of both techniques using three large-scale CXR datasets: CheXpert (224,316 CXRs), PADCHEST (160,000 CXRs), and NIH (112,120 CXRs). The experimental results demonstrate significant improvements in accuracy, AUC, and F1 scores compared to the baseline method across various pathologies. The logit-based and loss-based methods improve accuracy by 12\% and 11\%, AUC by 13\% and 10\%, and F1 scores by 24\% and 12\%, respectively compared to the baseline. These results represent a substantial improvement over the baseline method. Furthermore, we conduct a comprehensive statistical analysis to validate the robustness and reliability of the proposed techniques. The integration of domain-specific hierarchical knowledge not only enhances the classification performance but also provides a more interpretable output for clinical decision support. Our findings highlight the potential of hierarchical multi-label classification in advancing computer-aided diagnosis systems for chest radiography.

### [14] [Recovering Cloud Microstructures with Cascaded Diffusion Inversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05637)
*Hanan Gani,Guy Pulik,Daniel Rosenfeld,Duncan Watson-Parris,Salman Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种两阶段扩散超分辨率框架，用于将多光谱云微结构图像提升4倍分辨率。第一阶段利用真实配对数据学习退化处理和传感器对齐，第二阶段通过自监督内部降级细化结构学习和纹理合成。该方法在重建精度和视觉质量上优于现有Transformer和扩散基线模型，能更好捕捉对云播种决策至关重要的精细云微结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率卫星影像对于观测精细云结构至关重要，但当前对地静止和极轨卫星的空间分辨率不足以捕捉小尺度云特征。现有的超分辨率方法主要针对自然图像设计，无法泛化到卫星捕获的多光谱云覆盖图像。

Method: 提出两阶段扩散超分辨率框架：Stage 1使用真实世界配对数据进行鲁棒退化处理和跨传感器对齐；Stage 2采用自监督方式对高分辨率数据进行内部降级，以细化结构学习和纹理合成。整体通过逆扩散过程从低分辨率恢复高分辨率属性，实现4倍超分辨率重建。

Result: 在重建精度和视觉质量上均优于当前最先进的Transformer和扩散基线模型。能更好捕捉对有效云播种决策至关重要的精细云微结构（如对流塔和云隙）。消融研究证实了两阶段的互补优势：Stage 1擅长粗结构保真度，Stage 2贡献了增强的细节和真实感。

Conclusion: 该两阶段方法为改进云微物理分析提供了实用路径，是利用AI促进气候与可持续发展的重要一步。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身即为遥感领域的超分辨率研究，可直接应用于以下改进方向：1) 将两阶段扩散框架扩展到其他遥感任务，如植被指数、水体/城市分类等多光谱图像的超分辨率重建；2) 引入更丰富的物理约束（如辐射传输模型）到扩散过程中，使重建结果更符合遥感物理特性；3) 扩展到视频遥感领域，实现时间序列云图的超分辨率重建，提升对云动态演变的观测能力；4) 结合多传感器数据（如SAR与光学融合），利用两阶段框架中的跨传感器对齐能力实现异源遥感图像的超分辨率重建。

Abstract (英文): High-resolution satellite imagery is critical for observing fine-scale cloud structures that inform weather modification strategies like cloud seeding for rain-enhancement. However, the spatial resolution of current geostationary and polar-orbiting satellites is often insufficient for capturing small cloud features. Current super-resolution methodologies are suited for natural images and, therefore, struggle to generalize to satellite-captured spectral images of cloud cover. To address this, we propose a two-stage diffusion-based super-resolution framework to enhance the resolution of multi-spectral cloud microstructures by a factor of $4\times$. Specifically, we use inverse diffusion to recover the high resolution properties from low resolution. Stage 1 utilizes real-world paired data to learn robust degradation handling and inter-sensor alignment, while Stage 2 employs a self-supervised internal downgrading of high resolution data to refine structural learning and texture synthesis. Our approach outperforms the state-of-the-art transformer and diffusion-based baselines in both reconstruction accuracy and visual quality. We demonstrate that the two-stage method better captures fine cloud microstructures (e.g. convective turrets and cloud gaps) that are crucial for effective cloud seeding decisions. Ablation studies confirm the complementary benefits of the two stages: Stage 1 excels in coarse structural fidelity, while Stage 2 contributes enhanced detail and realism. These results highlight a practical path toward improving cloud microphysics analysis and as a step towards utilizing AI for climate and sustainability. Our code and models are publicly available at: https://github.com/hananshafi/superresolution-cloud-microphysics.

### [15] [VEIL: How Visual Encoding Hijacking Induces Bias In Vision Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05641)
*Suranjana Sooraj,Xuyang Chen,Madhumitha Venkatesan,Dongyu Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VEIL系统研究了图表编码方式如何影响CNN基于图表的时间序列分类学习到的表征，发现模型可能依赖编码特定的视觉线索而非真实的时间模式，注意力引导训练仅在编码敏感性一致时有效。论文将图表基TSC定位为表征与测量问题而非简单建模决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管将时间序列渲染为图表图像并用CNN进行分类的做法日益普遍，但模型究竟是在学习时间模式还是依赖图表设计引入的特定视觉线索尚不清楚。VEIL旨在系统探究图表编码如何影响所学表征。

Method: 通过相似性分析、迁移性分析和归因分析三种互补的诊断方式，系统研究图表编码对学习表征的影响，并评估注意力引导训练在缓解编码敏感性方面的效果。

Result: 当编码敏感性在各种诊断中一致时，注意力引导训练可以缓解该效应；但当此类信号缺失时，其效果有限甚至产生负面影响。

Conclusion: 图表可视化设计选择会深刻影响模型学到的表征，因此图表基TSC应被视为表征与测量问题而非简单的建模决策。研究将图形感知从人类读者拓展到视觉模型。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域大量使用时间序列数据（如植被指数NDVI时序、SAR时序、物候监测等），且遥感时间序列分类同样面临可视化编码偏差问题。改进方案：1) 将VEIL的分析框架直接应用于遥感时序图表分类，识别遥感特定图表编码（如假彩色合成、多波段渲染）引入的视觉偏差；2) 在遥感时序分类模型中引入注意力引导训练，针对遥感场景中地表变化的时间模式进行解耦；3) 设计遥感专用编码标准，减少由颜色映射或坐标设计引入的伪相关。

Abstract (英文): Rendering time series as chart images for CNN-based classification has become increasingly common in time-series classification (TSC). However, it remains unclear whether models learn underlying temporal patterns or rely on encoding-specific visual cues introduced by chart design. We present VEIL: a systematic study examining how chart encodings influence learned representations through complementary analyses of similarity, transferability, and attribution. Attention-guided training appears to mitigate this effect when encoding sensitivity is consistently identified across diagnostics, but provides limited or negative benefit when such signals are absent. These findings position VEIL within the broader question of how machines perceive visualizations -- extending graphical perception from human readers to vision models -- and show that visualization design choices shape learned representations in ways that warrant treating chart-based TSC as a representation and measurement problem rather than a simple modeling decision.

### [16] [REVIVE: A Multi-Modal Framework for Vandalism Detection and Recovery in Autonomous Vehicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05649)
*Abdullah Tariq Choudhry,Tapadhir Das*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出REVIVE框架，针对自动驾驶车辆摄像头因故意破坏导致的遮挡攻击（VOA）问题，集成了VOA检测、模式分类、EfficientNet-based U-Net分割和类型感知恢复（包括BLIP-guided Stable Diffusion修复、直接像素替换和自适应中值滤波）。实验表明，在参考对齐条件下，直接像素替换可将YOLOv8l目标检测召回率从0.588恢复至0.967，F1-score达0.970。引入质量门控机制确保恢复后图像质量不低于原始受损帧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注如何检测被故意破坏的图像，但对物理遮挡发生后如何恢复摄像头数据流以提高下游感知效用的研究不足，亟需一套结构化的VOA恢复框架。

Method: (1) 二元VOA检测；(2) 多类VOA模式识别；(3) EfficientNet-based U-Net分割；(4) 类型感知恢复：使用BLIP-guided Stable Diffusion修复、直接像素替换、自适应中值滤波三种策略，并引入质量门控机制过滤恢复候选。

Result: YOLOv8l检测：未恢复VOA召回率0.588；直接像素替换召回率0.967，F1-score 0.970；无质量门控时召回率降至0.304，有质量门控时恢复至0.608。Stable Diffusion重建SSIM 0.667-0.867，PSNR 15.4-26.7dB。

Conclusion: REVIVE提供了一种从VAO中有效恢复的结构化框架，质量门控机制确保输出帧质量不低于原始受损帧，为自动驾驶摄像头安全提供了实用解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域常面临传感器遮挡（云层遮盖、卫星镜头污损、无人机物理干扰等），该框架可直接迁移至遥感图像恢复任务中：(1) VOA检测可扩展为遮挡检测；(2) U-Net分割适用于遥感地物分割任务中的遮挡区域定位；(3) BLIP-guided Stable Diffusion可用于遥感图像的缺失区域重建；(4) 质量门控机制确保恢复后的遥感图像不会降低后续分类/检测性能。但需注意遥感图像的多光谱/高光谱特性，需扩展修复模型以处理多通道数据。

Abstract (英文): Autonomous vehicles (AVs) face increasing threats from vandalism-induced occlusion attacks (VOAs) that compromise camera-based perception. While detection frameworks can identify vandalized images, restoring camera-stream utility after physical occlusion remains underexplored. This paper presents present the Recovery and Enhancement of Vandalized Images for Vision Excellence (REVIVE) framework, a vandalism recovery pipeline integrating: (1) binary VOA detection, (2) multi-class VOA pattern identification, (3) EfficientNet-based U-Net segmentation, and (4) type-aware recovery using Bootstrapping Language-Image Pre-training (BLIP)-guided Stable Diffusion inpainting, direct pixel replacement, or adaptive median filtering. Stable Diffusion shows variable reconstruction performance (per-pattern SSIM 0.667-0.867, PSNR 15.4-26.7dB) across VOA patterns, while aligned direct pixel replacement achieves near-identical reconstruction under the aligned-reference condition. On 500 tracked clean/vandalized image pairs, unrecovered VOAs reduce YOLOv8l object-detection recall to 0.588, while direct pixel replacement restores recall to 0.967 and F1-score to 0.970 under that aligned-reference condition. LaMa, Telea, and Navier-Stokes baselines improve image similarity but provide more limited downstream detection recovery, and Stable Diffusion is treated as an asynchronous recovery branch subject to a quality gate rather than a blocking real-time perception step. We evaluate a reference-available quality gate that filters recovered candidates before downstream use: without it, type-aware routing degrades per-image recall to 0.304, whereas with it, recall returns to 0.608, at or above the unrecovered baseline, ensuring the forwarded stream is never worse than the unrecovered frame. REVIVE therefore, provides a structured recovery framework from VOAs in AVs.

TL;DR: FASR++是一个基于扩散模型的超分辨率算法，利用多张低质量辅助图像和一张参考低分辨率图像生成高质量人脸图像，在不依赖显式软属性或梯度引导的情况下恢复面部特征，在两个人脸识别数据集上达到了验证、识别和图像质量指标的最先进水平。

Method: 提出FASR++算法，基于扩散模型实现超分辨率。算法输入一张参考低分辨率图像和多张辅助低质量图像（如视频连续帧）提取的特征，通过扩散过程生成超分辨率输出，无需显式提供软属性或计算函数梯度来引导重建，从而最小化身份信息的失真。

Abstract (英文): Images acquired in surveillance environments often suffer from conditions such as low resolution, variations in pose, irregular illumination, and occlusions. Due to the low quality of these images, face recognition algorithms often struggle. This major limitation can be addressed by employing super-resolution techniques that enhance the details of the image. However, due to the high degree of difficulty of the problem, most super-resolution algorithms tend to cause distortions in the image and in the individual's identity. Thus, additional information must be incorporated into the processing to improve recognition robustness. In this regard, surveillance cameras can capture multiple images, even at low quality, and the data extracted from these images, such as consecutive video frames, can significantly enhance both super-resolution and facial recognition. In this work, we introduce FASR++, a diffusion-model-based super-resolution algorithm. It leverages a reference low-resolution image and features extracted from multiple auxiliary low-quality images to generate a super-resolved output, minimizing distortions in the individual's identity. Our approach recovers facial features without explicitly providing soft attributes or computing a function gradient to guide the reconstruction process. FASR++ generates high-quality images that can considerably improve performance in face recognition tasks when used as a pre-processing step. We validate our approach on two standard face recognition datasets and attain state-of-the-art results for verification, face recognition, and image quality metrics such as PSNR, SSIM, and LPIPS.

Method: 1) 自动化数据引擎将平铺图文数据转化为结构化场景图，层次化实体为节点、视觉关系为边；2) 构建12万高质量训练数据；3) 两阶段图对齐后训练：监督微调内化结构化推理能力，强化微调以节点为代理的图奖励来巩固高效图探索。

Result: 在八个多模态基准上取得显著改进，在细粒度感知和推理任务上表现优异。

Conclusion: SaGe通过结构化场景图表示有效提升了MLLMs的细粒度视觉推理能力，验证了图对齐训练范式的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感图像中地物目标（建筑、道路、植被等）及其空间关系（邻接、包含、距离、方位等）天然适合场景图建模。具体方案：1) 将遥感图像中的地物实体作为节点，空间/拓扑关系作为边构建遥感场景图；2) 利用SaGe的自动化数据引擎处理遥感标注数据（如建筑轮廓、道路网络）生成结构化场景图；3) 针对遥感特有的多层次尺度关系（如城市-街区-建筑）设计层次化节点；4) 在强化微调阶段引入遥感任务特定的图奖励（如空间关系正确性、目标检测精度），提升遥感图像理解与目标导航能力。

Abstract (英文): Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated strong perception and reasoning capabilities. However, most existing models focus on isolated objects and neglect structured relationships for efficient target navigation, limiting their performance on visually intensive tasks. To address this challenge, we introduce Scene Graph Thinking (SaGe), a novel paradigm that enables fine-grained and structured visual reasoning through explicit scene-graph representations. Specifically, we first introduce an automated data engine that converts flat image-text corpora into structured scene graphs, where hierarchical entities constitute the nodes and diverse visual relations define the edges. Building upon this, we construct 120K high-quality training data by sampling reasoning traces from scene graphs. Then, two-stage graph-aligned post-training paradigms are introduced, where supervised fine-tuning internalizes MLLMs with structured reasoning, and subsequent reinforcement fine-tuning proposes node-as-proxy graph rewards to consolidate efficient graph exploration. With curated data and graph-aligned training, our approach achieves significant improvements across eight multimodal benchmarks, demonstrating strong effectiveness on fine-grained perception and reasoning tasks. Code is available at https://github.com/zwyang6/SaGe.

</details>


### [20] [Association Restoration Test: Revealing Restorable Shortcuts after Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05726)
*Amy Lu,Changxiu Ji*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出关联恢复测试(ART)，用于评估关联遗忘方法是否真正消除了模型中的标签-属性捷径关联，而非仅改变输出或隐藏特征中的可读性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法仅测量输出级鲁棒性或探测冻结特征中捷径属性的可读性，但无法判断保留的关联是否仍能被原始分类器功能性地使用，缺乏对功能性捷径可恢复性的诊断工具。

Method: 提出关联恢复测试(ART)，一种事后诊断方法。ART首先估计类条件关联方向，然后放大残差成分，最后用原始分类器头评估修改后的特征，以此检验捷径关联是否仍可功能性恢复。

Result: 在Waterbirds、CelebA、SpuCoDogs以及ISIC时间戳伪影扩展数据集上验证，表明输出度量、表示探测和ART三者刻画了捷径缓解的不同方面，具有互补性。

Conclusion: 需要基于恢复感知(restoration-aware)的评估来指导关联遗忘和捷径缓解方法，这些方法应针对学习到的关联而非单个类别或概念。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感数据常存在环境伪影（如季节、光照、传感器差异）作为捷径关联。ART可诊断遥感分类模型是否依赖这些伪影捷径，并在去偏后验证捷径是否被真正消除而非隐藏。具体方案：在遥感场景分类或地物分类任务中，将已知环境伪影作为关联属性，用ART测试去偏后模型是否仍可通过原始分类器恢复该捷径关联。

Abstract (英文): Association unlearning aims to disable learned label-attribute shortcuts while preserving task performance. Existing evaluations mainly measure output-level robustness or probe whether shortcut attributes remain readable in frozen features, but neither test determines whether a retained association remains functionally usable by the original classifier. We propose the Association Restoration Test (ART), a post-hoc diagnostic for functional shortcut restorability. ART estimates class-conditional association directions, amplifies residual components, and evaluates the modified features with the original classifier head. Across Waterbirds, CelebA, SpuCoDogs, and an ISIC timestamp-artifact extension, we show that output metrics, representation probes, and ART characterize distinct aspects of shortcut mitigation. These findings motivate restoration-aware evaluation for unlearning and shortcut-mitigation methods that target learned associations rather than individual classes or concepts.

### [21] [SAMPLe: SAM-based Optimizer for Prompt Learning in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05727)
*Hossein Rajoli,Fatemeh Lotfi,Niloufar Alipour Talemi,Hossein Kashiani,Xiaolong Ma,Fatemeh Afghah*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SAMPLe（锐度感知最小化提示学习），一种即插即用的锐度感知优化器，通过考虑损失 landscape 的锐度来增强预训练视觉语言模型（如CLIP）中提示的泛化能力，在保持泛化性的同时提升任务特定性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的提示学习方法在预训练VLM中存在性能-泛化困境：提示调优虽能在seen分布上取得高准确率，但往往损害对unseen数据的泛化能力。有限的可学习提示容易过拟合训练数据，导致任务特定性能与保持泛化性之间存在权衡。

Method: SAMPLe是一种锐度感知最小化优化器，通过考虑损失landscape的锐度来增强提示泛化性。它在每一步通过满足目标函数约束来平衡探索与利用，基于局部曲率和梯度属性动态适应当前优化状态，从而减少对seen分布的过拟合，提高对unseen数据的适应性。

Result: 将SAMPLe集成到多种提示学习框架（CoOp、CoCoOp、MaPLe、TCP、Co-Prompt）中，实验表明SAMPLe能提升这些框架的性能，并在多种设置下持续优于现有优化器，是一种鲁棒、模型无关的提示学习解决方案。

Conclusion: SAMPLe有效解决了VLM提示学习中的性能-泛化困境，作为一种即插即用的优化器，能够在不改变模型架构的前提下提升提示的泛化能力，并适用于多种提示学习方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该优化器可应用于遥感领域基于VLM的少样本分类、场景识别等任务中。具体方案：(1) 将SAMPLe替代传统优化器应用于遥感CLIP提示学习框架，缓解遥感数据分布差异大导致的过拟合问题；(2) 针对遥感多尺度、多传感器特性，可结合遥感专用的提示学习方法（如RS-CLIP、RemoteCLIP等）引入SAMPLe优化，提升模型在不同遥感场景、不同分辨率下的跨数据集泛化能力；(3) 在遥感目标检测或分割任务中，也可将SAMPLe用于视觉提示调优阶段，提高模型在未见过的遥感分布上的适应能力。

Abstract (英文): Pre-trained Vision-Language Models (VLMs) like CLIP have proven highly effective as foundation models for various downstream applications. However, prompt learning in VLMs encounters a performance-generalization dilemma: while prompts can be tuned to achieve high accuracy on seen distributions, this tuning process often undermines their generalizability to unseen data. The limited set of learnable prompts, which contextualize and condition the input to steer it toward the task within the pretrained VLM, tends to overfit the training data, leading to a trade-off between task-specific performance and preserving generalization. To address this dilemma, we introduce SAMPLe (Sharpness-Aware Minimization Prompt Learning), a plug-in sharpness-aware optimizer that enhances prompt generalizability by accounting for loss landscape sharpness. Unlike conventional methods, SAMPLe balances exploration and exploitation by satisfying objective function constraints at each step, dynamically adapting to the current optimization state based on the local curvature and gradient properties. This approach reduces overfitting on seen distributions and improves adaptability to unseen data, preserving the generalization potential of pre-trained VLM models. We integrate SAMPLe into multiple prompt learning frameworks, including CoOp, CoCoOp, MaPLe, TCP, and Co-Prompt, demonstrating its effectiveness across diverse methods. Experiments show that SAMPLe elevates prompt learning frameworks and consistently outperforms existing optimizers across diverse settings, establishing itself as a robust, model-agnostic solution for prompt learning.

### [22] [ARMS: Anchor-Relational Motion Streaming for Seamless Solo-Social Motion Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05733)
*Huakun Liu,Qing Yu,Kent Fujiwara,Hideaki Uchiyama,Kiyoshi Kiyokawa*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ARMS提出了一种锚点关系运动流框架，通过动力学非对称表示和因果关系扩散模型，在单一因果生成过程中统一了单人运动与人-人交互的生成，实现了无缝的社交耦合切换和长时间稳定的运动流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在静态智能体配置下生成固定长度运动片段，难以处理单人-社交过渡场景，且不适用于长时间增量生成，缺乏统一建模单人运动与人际交互的框架。

Method: 提出ARMS框架：1) 动力学非对称表示，通过伙伴引用的相对平移项解耦个体时间演化与人际对齐；2) 因果潜在空间上的因果关系扩散模型，逐段渐进细化运动；3) 模态感知关系门控，激活或屏蔽跨智能体连接以支持单人及交互生成。

Result: 实验表明ARMS在过渡平滑性和社交连贯性上优于交互中心基线，并在人-人交互基准上达到竞争性结果。

Conclusion: ARMS证明了通过单一因果生成过程统一建模单人运动和人际交互的可行性，为长时间、可流式生成的社会行为建模提供了新思路。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：55%。遥感领域存在类似的多目标时空动态建模需求（如多车辆轨迹预测、人群疏散行为建模）。ARMS的动力学非对称表示（解耦个体演化与相对对齐）可直接迁移至遥感多目标跟踪场景，因果扩散模型可用于连续帧间目标的渐进式预测。但遥感数据缺乏文本条件输入，需将文本条件替换为遥感图像特征或历史轨迹编码。

Abstract (英文): Generating temporally continuous and socially coherent human motion from text remains a fundamental challenge, particularly in realistic streams where people act alone, enter interactions, and later disengage. Most existing methods generate fixed-length motion clips under static agent configurations, which makes them brittle to solo-social transitions and unsuitable for incremental generation over long horizons. We propose ARMS, an Anchor-Relational Motion Streaming framework that unifies solo motion and human-human interaction within a single causal generative process. ARMS introduces a dynamics-asymmetric representation that decouples per-person temporal evolution from inter-person alignment via a partner-referenced relative-translation term, enabling seamless switching of social coupling without sacrificing long-horizon stability or spatial consistency between agents. On top of a causal latent space, a causal relational diffusion model progressively refines motion segment by segment using only past context, capturing both intra-person temporal dependencies and inter-person relations. Mode-aware relational gating activates or masks cross-agent connections, allowing the same model to support both solo and interaction generation. Experiments show that ARMS improves transition smoothness and social coherence compared to interaction-centric baselines, while also achieving competitive results on human-human interaction benchmarks.

### [23] [Optimized Adaptive Loop Filter in Versatile Video Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05737)
*Meng Xuewei,Zhang Jiaqi,Jia Chuanmin,Zhang Xinfeng,Wang Shanshe,Ma Siwei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 针对VVC标准中自适应环路滤波器(ALF)计算复杂度高、图片缓存访问次数多的问题，提出了一种优化ALF框架，包括GALF和CCALF的并行设计、GALF自适应参数决策以及基于失真估计的单次CCALF方案。相比VTM-8.0，图片缓存访问从152次降至1次，ALF模块时间节省约25%，编码性能几乎不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VVC标准中ALF虽能有效减少压缩伪影，但其编码复杂度高且需要大量图片缓存访问，导致外部内存访问增加，对软硬件设计不友好。

Method: 1) GALF与CCALF的并行设计；2) GALF自适应参数决策；3) 通过有效估计CCALF滤波失真而无需实际执行滤波操作的单次CCALF方案。

Result: 相比VTM-8.0，图片缓存访问从152次降至1次，ALF模块时间节省约25%，编码性能几乎无损失（RA配置下）。部分方法已被VVC参考软件采纳。

Conclusion: 提出的优化ALF框架显著降低了编码复杂度和内存访问开销，同时保持了编码效率，具有良好的软硬件友好性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像通常数据量大、分辨率高，编码复杂度问题突出。可将该优化ALF框架应用于遥感图像编码标准中，尤其是GALF与CCALF并行设计可加速高分辨率遥感影像的环路滤波处理；自适应参数决策可针对不同类型遥感场景（如城区、植被、水体）动态调整滤波强度；单次CCALF失真估计方案适合资源受限的星载或无人机遥感平台。此外，遥感图像中的多光谱/高光谱波段间相关性可借鉴CCALF跨分量滤波思想进行进一步优化。

Abstract (英文): In the Versatile Video Coding~(VVC) standard, adaptive loop filter~(ALF), including Geometry transformation-based Adaptive Loop Filter~(GALF) and Cross Component Adaptive Loop Filter~(CCALF), plays an essential role in reducing compression artifacts. However, it also has high coding complexity and requires many picture buffer accesses in the encoder that will increase external memory access and is unfriendly to the software and hardware design. Therefore, we propose an optimized ALF framework, including the parallel design of GALF and CCALF, the adaptive parameter decision of GALF, and one-pass CCALF scheme by effectively estimating the CCALF filtering distortion without conducting filter operation. Compared to VTM-8.0, the proposed method can reduce the picture buffer access from 152 to 1 and achieve roughly 25\% time-savings of the ALF module with negligible coding performance change under RA configuration. Some of the proposed methods have been adopted in the VVC reference software.

### [24] [Image2Sim: Scaling Embodied Navigation via Generative Neural Simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05765)
*Zihan Wang,Seungjun Lee,Yinghao Xu,Gim Hee Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Image2Sim，一个从RGB-D图像序列实时构建高质量交互式神经仿真环境的框架，通过解耦3D空间锚定与逼真观测合成，实现了大规模导航训练数据的自动生成，并在真实世界零样本场景中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身导航研究受限于缺乏可扩展、高保真且物理交互真实的仿真环境：真实扫描数据集视觉真实但规模有限，合成仿真器易扩展但存在较大的仿真到真实差距。

Method: Image2Sim采用双模块设计：(1) 前馈特征高斯模型，将带位姿的RGB-D观测单次前向传播提升为3D特征-高斯基元表示；(2) 几何感知单步像素流模型，将稀疏噪声高斯投影转换为高质量全景RGB-D观测。

Result: 将大量视频和图像转换为近2万个交互场景，合成超1000万导航训练样本；在此神经环境中训练的导航模型在主要基准测试上取得显著提升，并能有效迁移到真实世界零样本场景。

Conclusion: 可扩展的神经仿真可作为大规模具身导航训练的实用基质，有效缩小仿真与真实之间的差距。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域可借鉴Image2Sim的核心思想——解耦3D空间锚定与观测合成：利用卫星或无人机获取的带位姿多视角RGB-D影像，构建大规模遥感场景的神经仿真环境，用于生成多样化的遥感导航/路径规划训练数据；其前馈特征高斯模型可推广至遥感三维重建，实现从稀疏航片到连续三维特征表示的快速构建；几何感知像素流模型可用于遥感影像的超分辨率重建或缺失视角合成。

Abstract (英文): Embodied navigation aims to build agents that interpret multimodal goals, reason in 3D space, and reach target destinations reliably in the real world. However, progress remains constrained by the lack of scalable, high-fidelity, and physically grounded interactive environments. Although real-world scanned datasets offer visual realism, they are limited by scale. In contrast, synthetic simulators scale more easily but often exhibit large sim-to-real gaps. We introduce Image2Sim, a real-time neural simulation framework that constructs high-quality interactive environments from posed RGB-D image sequences. The central idea is to decouple 3D spatial anchoring from photorealistic observation synthesis. For scene construction, Image2Sim uses a feed-forward feature Gaussian model that lifts posed RGB-D observations into a 3D feature-Gaussian representation in a single pass. For rendering, we propose a Geometry-Aware One-Step Pixel Flow model that transforms sparse and noisy Gaussian projections into high-quality panoramic RGB-D observations. Image2Sim also serves as a fully automated embodied data engine that generates high-fidelity observations, executable actions, and diverse navigation instructions at scale. It converts large collections of videos and images into nearly 20K interactive scenes and synthesizes more than 10 million navigation training samples. Navigation models trained entirely in these neural environments achieve strong improvements on major benchmarks and transfer effectively to real-world zero-shot settings. These results suggest that scalable neural simulation can serve as a practical training substrate for embodied navigation at scale.

### [25] [LEGATO 2: Toward Multimodal Sheet Music Recognition and Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05769)
*Guang Yang,Brian Siyuan Zheng,Victoria Ebert,Noah A. Smith*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Legato 2是一个新型管线，用于从乐谱图像中提取符号标注和语义知识。它首次采用逐系统（system-by-system）的序列化方式处理光学音乐识别（OMR），能够处理任意长输入，并首次在符号转录中嵌入文本内容（如标题和注释），在多个数据集上超越先前最先进水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有OMR方法通常将整页乐谱视为无差别的图像进行识别，无法有效扩展至长输入，且无法在符号转录中嵌入文本内容（如标题和注释）。作者旨在解决这些问题，提出一种能够按乐谱系统水平方向序列化识别并同时处理文本内容的OMR方法。

Method: Legato 2包含两个核心组件：（1）系统级分割（system-level segmentation），将乐谱图像按系统（行）切分；（2）自回归视觉语言模型（autoregressive vision-LM），沿水平方向逐系统序列化处理音符，捕获局部音符细节和乐谱整体结构。该管线按照人类阅读乐谱的方式——沿水平符号行顺序处理，而非整页无差别识别。

Result: 在多个数据集上，Legato 2一致性地超越先前最先进方法。符号转录还能作为视觉输入的补充，提升前沿语言模型（如GPT-4等）对密集音乐文档的理解能力。Legato 2在OMR和下游乐谱理解任务中均建立了新的最先进性能。

Conclusion: Legato 2通过按系统序列化处理乐谱图像，有效解决了OMR中长输入扩展和文本内容嵌入的问题，为光学音乐识别和乐谱理解设立了新的性能标杆。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：70%。遥感图像中的文本（如地图注记、卫星影像中的标签文字）和空间结构（如按行/列排列的地理要素）与乐谱的系统级结构有相似之处。可将Legato 2中“逐系统序列化”的思路迁移至遥感文档图像理解：遥感图像中带有文字注释的区域（如地图图例、标注框）可先进行区域级分割，再使用自回归视觉语言模型沿空间顺序（如从左到右、从上到下）序列化提取符号和文本信息，实现遥感图像中结构化文本与空间符号的联合解析。

Abstract (英文): We propose a novel pipeline, Legato 2, for extracting symbolic notation and semantic knowledge from images of sheet music. Legato 2 features the first large-scale neural model for optical music recognition (OMR) to operate sequentially on a system-by-system basis, following the horizontal lines of notation as they are read on the page, rather than treating the page as an undifferentiated image, enabling better scaling to arbitrarily long inputs. It is also the first OMR model capable of generating symbolic transcriptions that include embedded textual content, such as titles and annotations. The pipeline combines system-level segmentation with an autoregressive vision-LM to capture both local notation details and score structure. Across multiple datasets, Legato 2 consistently outperforms prior state of the art. We also show that symbolic transcriptions complement visual inputs for frontier language models, improving their interpretation of dense musical documents. Legato 2 establishes new state-of-the-art performance in both OMR and downstream sheet music understanding.

### [26] [Benchmarking the Robustness of Autonomous Driving to Environmental Illusions: A Lane Perception Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05783)
*Tianyuan Zhang,Xianglong Liu,Aishan Liu,Lu Wang,Yitong Zhang,Peng Yue,Mingchuan Zhang,Siyuan Liang,Dacheng Tao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出首个面向环境幻觉（阴影、反射、轮胎痕迹等）的自动驾驶车道感知鲁棒性基准LanEvil++，涵盖14种幻觉类型、9万+标注图像及4万+VQA对。实验表明幻觉显著降低车道检测和视觉语言模型性能（Accuracy下降5.27%，F1下降10.49%），阴影干扰最严重。提出多模态幻觉防御方法MIDA，提升鲁棒性4.23%（LD）和3.82%（ADVLM）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实驾驶环境中广泛存在但被忽视的环境幻觉（阴影、反射、轮胎痕迹等）会干扰视觉感知，导致场景误判并威胁自动驾驶安全。现有研究缺乏对此类现象的 systematic 评估与防御手段。

Method: 1) 构建LanEvil++基准，包含14种幻觉类型，利用CARLA生成94个高保真3D场景；2) 评估传统车道检测模型和视觉语言模型（ADVLM）在幻觉下的性能；3) 提出多模态幻觉防御方法MIDA，通过多模态融合增强鲁棒性。

Result: LD模型Accuracy下降5.27%，F1下降10.49%；ADVLM的GPT-score下降2.03%，Language-score下降0.75%；阴影影响最大（Accuracy下降7.20%）。MIDA分别提升LD鲁棒性4.23%和ADVLM鲁棒性3.82%。

Conclusion: 环境幻觉是自动驾驶安全的重要隐患，现有模型对此鲁棒性不足。所提基准和防御方法为后续研究奠定基础。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中同样存在大量环境幻觉现象（如云影、建筑物阴影、水面反射、车辆轮胎痕迹等），影响目标检测和语义分割。具体交叉方案：1) 将LanEvil++的14类幻觉分类体系迁移至遥感场景，构建遥感幻觉基准数据集；2) MIDA的多模态融合策略可适配遥感中的多光谱/高光谱数据，用于消除阴影和反射干扰；3) 车道检测中的幻觉鲁棒性评估方法可直接用于遥感道路提取任务，提升复杂光照条件下的分割精度。

Abstract (英文): Environmental illusions (eg., shadows, reflections, and tire marks) are naturally existing yet overlooked phenomena in real-world driving environments. They can disturb visual perception, leading to misinterpretation of the scene and posing serious safety risks to autonomous driving (AD) systems. However, existing researches largely overlook these phenomena, leaving a critical gap. To address this issue, we study AD robustness through the lane perception perspective, a fundamental task supporting core functions like cruise control and lane centering. We focus on two representative models: conventional lane detection (LD) and vision-language model-based systems (ADVLMs). In this work, we introduce the first benchmark, LanEvil++, for evaluating the robustness of lane perception under environmental illusions. LanEvil++ encompasses 14 types of illusions and leverages the CARLA simulator to generate 94 high-fidelity, fully controllable 3D scenes, yielding a dataset of 90,292 annotated images, 1,596 video clips, and 41,855 visual question answering pairs. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that environmental illusions substantially degrade the performance of state-of-the-art LD methods. On average, LD models experience a 5.27% drop in Accuracy and a 10.49% decline in F1-score, while ADVLMs show a 2.03% reduction in GPT-score and a 0.75% drop in Language-score. Among all illusions, shadows emerge as the most disruptive factor, reducing accuracy by up to 7.20%. Furthermore, closed-loop simulations reveal that these illusions can lead to incorrect driving decisions. Complementary real-world case studies highlight safety-critical failures in actual traffic scenes. To enhance robustness, we propose the Multimodal Illusion Defense Approach (MIDA). MIDA achieves substantial gains under challenging conditions, boosting robustness by 4.23% on LD models and 3.82% on ADVLMs.

</details>


### [27] [DeSeG: Decoupling Semantic Intent and Geometric Constraints for Physically Plausible Human-Scene Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05787)
*Jiakun Li,Zhe Li,Wenqiang Wu,Zheng Chang,Mingqi Gao,Jinyu Yang,Feng Zheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DeSeG框架，通过解耦语义意图与几何约束，结合残差语义规划器和物理正则化扩散执行器，在人-场景交互合成中减少47%的穿透率并提升29%的语义对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型存在语义-几何纠缠问题：空间约束与特定动作在训练数据中强相关，导致单体型模型学习捷径偏差，在严格几何线索下会覆盖语义意图；同时这种纠缠加剧了身体-场景穿透等物理幻觉。

Method: 提出层次化框架DeSeG：(1) 残差语义规划器，将文本指令和规范化目标体素编码到紧凑潜空间，实现独立于空间轨迹的细粒度语义控制；(2) 物理正则化扩散执行器，将可微排斥势场直接融入扩散目标函数，强制生成碰撞感知的运动。

Result: 在Lingo数据集上，DeSeG实现SOTA性能：平均场景穿透减少47%，语义对齐提升29%。

Conclusion: 明确解耦语义与几何是解决HSI合成中捷径学习和物理幻觉的有效途径，层次化设计优于单体型模型。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。具体方案：(1) 将DeSeG的语义-几何解耦框架迁移至遥感中的地物-行为关系建模，例如用残差语义规划器解耦遥感图像中的地物语义（如“道路”“建筑区”）与几何形态特征，减少语义混淆；(2) 物理正则化扩散执行器可适配用于遥感时序数据生成（如植被变化轨迹），将地物间物理约束（如地形坡度限制）融入扩散过程，抑制不合理的空间变化；(3) 可进一步引入遥感特有的多模态输入（如光谱、地形DEM）替代文本指令，拓展语义规划器的输入维度。

Abstract (英文): Synthesizing physically plausible human-scene interactions (HSI) remains a critical challenge in computer vision and the development of human avatars. Although recent generative models enable diverse motion synthesis, they suffer from an inductive bias referred to as semantic-geometric entanglement. Because spatial constraints often strongly correlate with specific actions in training data, monolithic models will learn the shortcut bias, aggressively overriding the semantic intent when faced with strict geometric cues. Furthermore, this entanglement exacerbates physical hallucinations, such as body-scene penetrations. To address these limitations, we propose DeSeG, a hierarchical framework that explicitly decouples semantic intent from geometric constraints. First, we introduce a Residual Semantic Planner that encodes textual instructions and canonicalized goal voxels into a compact latent space, enabling fine-grained semantic control independent of spatial trajectories. Second, we propose a physics regularized diffusion executor that incorporates differentiable repulsive potential fields directly into the diffusion objective, enforcing collision-aware motion generation. Extensive experiments on the Lingo dataset demonstrate that DeSeG achieves state-of-the-art performance, reducing mean scene penetration by 47% and improving semantic alignment by 29% over the SOTA baselines.

### [28] [Segmentation before Answering: Pixel Grounding for MLLM Visual Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05798)
*Yake Wei,Yuan Wang,Fengyun Rao,Jing Lyu,Di Hu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SegAnswer提出将MLLM中的“放大查看”操作从边界框（bounding box）切换到像素级分割掩码（segmentation mask），通过精细掩码隔离目标区域、滤除背景和干扰，实现更精确的视觉-语言推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM在“用图像思考”时，通常依赖边界框来定位感兴趣区域，但边界框会包含大量无关背景和干扰物体，导致细粒度视觉信息不够精确。

Method: 提出SegAnswer框架，用像素级分割掩码替代边界框作为“放大查看”的单位，先分割目标区域再回答问题，使得视觉输入更精确地聚焦目标，且分割后的离散块与MLLM的位置编码机制更契合。

Result: 在高分辨率感知、通用感知和幻觉检测等多个基准上取得一致性改进，同时在分割任务上也表现出色。

Conclusion: 基于像素级掩码的“先分割后回答”策略优于基于边界框的放大方式，能实现更可靠的像素级定位与推理。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感图像中目标密集、背景复杂（如多类地物、不同尺度的建筑物/车辆/舰船），SegAnswer的分割-回答范式天然适合遥感场景：1）用分割掩码代替遥感检测框（如旋转框/水平框），可精准提取任意形状地物（如道路、河流、不规则建筑）；2）MLLM在遥感问答（RSVQA、GeoChat等任务）中可直接受益于精确的目标隔离，减少相邻地物干扰；3）可结合SAM等基础分割模型处理遥感大尺度图像，实现从“框选地物”到“像素级地物问答”的升级。

Abstract (英文): Recent advancements in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have evolved from static perception to interleaved visual-language reasoning, often referred to as ``thinking with images''. A basic operation in this reasoning process is to zoom in on regions of interest (often represented with bounding boxes) to acquire finer visual details. In this paper, we propose \textbf{Seg}mentation before \textbf{Answer}ing (SegAnswer), which shifts the unit of zoom-in from the popular bounding box to pixel-level segmentation mask. By employing fine-grained masks to isolate the target area from cluttered environments, segmented visual input yields a more precise region of interest, effectively filtering out redundant background and interfering objects. Furthermore, the discrete patches of segmented visual input align more seamlessly with how MLLMs structure visual tokens via positional embeddings. In experiments, we evaluate SegAnswer across diverse benchmarks, including high-resolution perception, general perception, and hallucination. It achieves consistent improvements and also exhibits considerable performance on segmentation tasks, validating its capability for reliable pixel grounding.

### [29] [TRIG: Trajectory-Rig Decoupled Metric Geometry Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05801)
*Lizhou Liao,Wentao Xu,Handong Wang,Lirong Yang,Shuai Yang,Weiwei Liu,Chang Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出TRIG框架，将自动驾驶中的相机位姿解耦为轨迹（ego-motion）和刚体结构（camera-rig），分别建模时序运动和静态多相机拓扑，实现度量一致的几何感知，在五个自动驾驶基准上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉几何模型将相机位姿编码为纠缠表示，时变自运动和静态相机刚体几何被联合建模，限制了车辆侧几何先验的利用，缺乏针对刚性多相机驾驶系统的专门设计。

Method: 1) 将相机位姿分解为ego-trajectory（自车轨迹）和camera-rig（相机刚体）两组分量；2) 引入解耦的位姿编码与监督，分别约束轨迹演化和刚体几何；3) 设计稀疏时空注意力，将跨相机交互与时序聚合分离，降低全局注意力成本。

Result: 在五个自动驾驶基准（pose estimation, metric depth prediction, 3D reconstruction）上达到SOTA性能。

Conclusion: TRIG通过解耦位姿表示和注意力机制，有效提升了多相机驾驶场景下的几何感知精度，验证了分离建模时序运动与静态拓扑的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域同样存在多传感器（卫星/无人机）的刚体配置与时序轨道运动问题。可借鉴TRIG思路：1) 将卫星平台轨迹（轨道运动）与多载荷（相机/雷达）的刚性几何解耦，分别建模运动与安装拓扑；2) 利用稀疏时空注意力处理多载荷时序遥感数据，降低计算量同时保留几何推理能力；3) 适用于卫星编队飞行、无人机多视角测图等需要分离平台运动与传感器结构的遥感任务。

Abstract (英文): Vision-centric autonomous driving requires accurate metric geometry and ego-motion estimation from synchronized multi-camera observations. Recent visual geometry models show strong performance in pose estimation, depth prediction, and 3D reconstruction, but are not tailored to rigid multi-camera driving systems. They often encode camera poses as entangled representations, in which time-varying ego-motion and static camera-rig geometry are jointly modeled, limiting the utilization of vehicle-side geometric priors. We propose Trajectory-Rig Decoupled Metric Geometry Learning (TRIG), a geometry perception framework for autonomous driving. TRIG factorizes camera poses into ego-trajectory and camera-rig components, enabling separate modeling of ego-motion and static multi-camera topology. We introduce decoupled pose encoding and supervision, which separately constrain trajectory evolution and rig geometry for metric-consistent learning. Moreover, sparse Temporal--Spatial attention separates cross-camera interaction from temporal aggregation, reducing global attention cost while preserving geometric reasoning. Experiments on five autonomous driving benchmarks show that TRIG achieves state-of-the-art performance in pose estimation, metric depth prediction, and 3D reconstruction.

### [30] [Complementary Roles of Image Classification and Vessel Segmentation in AI-Based Screening for Retinopathy of Prematurity Plus Disease in a Kenyan Preterm Cohort](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05825)
*Fred Mutisya,Oscar Onyango,Sarah Sitati,Syokau Ilovi,Aeesha NJ Malik,Brenda W'mosi,Brian Makini,Jalemba Aluuvala,Josiah Onyango,Rachael Kanguha Mmene,Steven Wanyee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文分析了121名肯尼亚早产儿的1635张眼底图像，评估了11种AI配置用于ROP Plus病变检测。研究发现，RGB分类器灵敏度高但易过度转诊，血管分割模型特异性更强，两者结合（概率集成）达到最佳平衡性能（灵敏度0.692，特异性0.914，平衡准确率0.803），优于单一视觉分类器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ROP是可预防的儿童致盲原因，但在中低收入国家缺乏经过ROP培训的眼科医生。Plus病变（视网膜血管扩张和迂曲）是治疗触发指标，但其判别主观且变异大。非洲地区关于自动化筛查的证据仍然有限，因此需要开发适用于该地区的人工智能辅助筛查系统。

Method: 研究包含121名肯尼亚早产儿（237只眼，1635张眼底图像），由两名标注者对血管进行分割标注。评估了11种配置用于眼级Plus检测，包括图像分类器、多实例学习、多任务分割-分类以及先分割后分类流水线，采用患者分组嵌套交叉验证。

Result: 血管分割在留出图像上达到Dice 0.533、IoU 0.368、灵敏度0.623、特异性0.979。RGB分类器灵敏度高但过度转诊，分割耦合模型特异性更强。组合方法中，OR筛选获得最高灵敏度，AND确认获得最高特异性，概率集成获得最佳平衡性能（灵敏度0.692，特异性0.914，平衡准确率0.803）。

Conclusion: 分类和血管分割在肯尼亚ROP Plus检测中具有互补性：分类器支持灵敏的病例发现，分割提高特异性并减少过度转诊。非洲ROP AI系统应采用组合工作流程，并需进行前瞻性多中心验证。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：（1）遥感血管分割可直接借鉴本文的眼底血管分割方法（Dice 0.533虽不高但可作为基线），用于遥感图像中的道路、河流线性特征提取；（2）本文的"分类+分割"互补策略可迁移到遥感目标检测中，分类器做粗筛（高召回），分割做精确认（高精度），减少遥感解译中的误报；（3）多任务分割-分类框架可用于遥感场景分类与建筑物/道路分割的联合学习；（4）AND/OR组合逻辑可应用于遥感变化检测中多时相结果的融合决策。

Abstract (英文): Background. Retinopathy of prematurity (ROP) is a preventable cause of childhood blindness, with rising burden in low- and middle-income countries where ROP-trained ophthalmologists are scarce. Plus disease, marked by retinal vessel dilation and tortuosity, triggers treatment but is subjective and variable. Automated screening could extend specialist reach, but African evidence remains limited.
  Methods. We analysed 121 Kenyan preterm infants, covering 237 eyes and 1,635 fundus images graded as No Plus, Pre-Plus or Plus. Vessel annotations from two graders supported segmentation training. Eleven configurations were evaluated for eye-level Plus detection using patient-grouped nested cross-validation, including image classifiers, multiple-instance learning, multi-task segmentation-classification, and segment-then-classify pipelines.
  Results. Vessel segmentation was feasible, achieving pooled Dice 0.533, IoU 0.368, sensitivity 0.623 and specificity 0.979 on held-out images. RGB classifiers were highly sensitive but over-referred, while segmentation-coupled models were more specific. Combining approaches improved performance: an OR-based screen achieved the highest sensitivity, an AND-based confirmation achieved the highest specificity, and a probability ensemble gave the best balanced performance, with sensitivity 0.692, specificity 0.914 and balanced accuracy 0.803, outperforming the vision classifier alone.
  Conclusions. Classification and vessel segmentation are complementary for ROP Plus detection in Kenyan data. Classifiers support sensitive case-finding, while segmentation improves specificity and reduces over-referral. African ROP AI systems should use combined workflows and undergo prospective multi-site validation.

### [31] [Realistic Compound-Lens Defocus Blur Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05837)
*Yunkyu Lee,Woohyeok Kim,Sunghyun Cho*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过波光学PSF计算、深度感知散焦渲染和相机ISP模拟的管道，用于合成具有多样化镜头特性的真实散焦去模糊数据集（CLDefocus）。实验表明，在该数据集上训练的模型相比现有真实和合成数据集，在跨设备泛化方面表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习去模糊方法依赖于训练数据，但现有数据集缺乏光学多样性和真实性，导致模型在不同相机和镜头间的泛化能力受限。

Method: 提出一个统一的合成管道，包括：(1) 基于Debye CZT传播的高效波光学PSF计算；(2) 深度感知的散焦渲染与遮挡处理；(3) 在辐射线性空间中进行模糊合成并模拟相机ISP。

Result: 生成了大规模合成数据集CLDefocus，包含多样化镜头的散焦图像对；在该数据集上训练的模型相比使用现有真实和合成数据集的模型，实现了更好的跨设备泛化性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的合成管道能够高效生成具有高光学真实性和镜头多样性的散焦去模糊数据集，有效提升模型的跨设备泛化能力。此外，真实捕获数据集的缺陷可能会对全参考评估产生偏差。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像（如卫星、无人机影像）常因大气扰动、光学系统散焦等因素导致图像模糊，该管道的波光学PSF计算和深度感知渲染可直接迁移至遥感成像仿真。具体方案：(1) 利用Debye CZT传播模拟大气湍流和光学系统联合PSF；(2) 结合遥感场景的深度图（如DSM/DEM）进行深度感知散焦渲染；(3) 生成多样化传感器（不同焦距、光圈）的遥感散焦数据集，用于训练鲁棒的去模糊模型，提升遥感图像在不同平台间的泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Defocus blur degrades fine image structures and limits visual perception, which can adversely affect downstream vision tasks. Although recent deep learning deblurring methods have achieved strong performance, their effectiveness depends on training data and often degrades across cameras and lenses due to limited optical diversity and realism in existing datasets. In this paper, we propose a pipeline for synthesizing realistic defocus deblurring datasets for diverse compound lenses. It integrates efficient wave-optics PSF computation via Debye CZT propagation, depth-aware defocus rendering with occlusion handling, and blur synthesis in the radiometrically linear space with camera ISP simulation. This unified pipeline enables the scalable generation of photorealistic defocus datasets with diverse lens characteristics. Using our pipeline, we generate CLDefocus, a large-scale synthetic dataset containing lens-diverse defocus image pairs. We further analyze the limitations of real-captured defocus datasets and show that such imperfections can bias full-reference evaluation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that models trained on CLDefocus achieve improved cross-device generalization compared to models trained on existing real and synthetic datasets.

### [32] [Breaking Spurious Correlations via Generative Randomization and Cross-Variant Self-Supervised Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05850)
*Suraj Yadav,Anjaneya Sharma,Siddharth Yadav*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个两阶段框架，通过生成式干预（生成式反事实图像+跨变体自监督学习）来学习背景不变的视觉表征，从而解决深度神经网络在分布偏移下因依赖背景与标签的虚假关联而失败的问题。在Waterbirds、MetaShift和NICO++等基准上取得了最优的最差组性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络在经验风险最小化（ERM）训练下，容易利用目标标签与背景上下文之间的虚假关联，导致分布偏移时泛化失败。现有的生成式方法虽能创建反事实图像（改变背景），但仅将其作为标准数据增强，模型仍可保留对背景敏感的表示。

Method: 1) 零样本分割提取前景目标，利用结构保持扩散模型生成上下文改变（背景变换）的变体图像，保留目标身份同时改变环境；2) 提出跨变体自监督学习（CV-SSL），将同一目标在不同背景下的变体作为正样本对进行对比学习，对齐目标中心表示并抑制背景特异性线索；3) 对预训练编码器进行微调，采用ERM warm-up后接GroupDRO与逐层学习率策略。

Result: 在分布偏移基准上实现了最优的最差组性能：Waterbirds 92.5%，MetaShift 81.7%，NICO++ 87.4%。

Conclusion: 通过生成式干预和跨变体自监督对比学习，能够有效学习背景不变的视觉表征，显著提升模型在分布偏移场景下的泛化鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：92%。遥感图像中目标（如船只、飞机、建筑物）与背景（海洋、机场、城区）之间的虚假关联同样严重。具体方案：1) 利用遥感领域的零样本分割模型（如SAM-Remote）提取目标，用扩散模型生成不同地理环境（如将海面船只置于港口或内陆河流）的变体图像；2) 跨变体自监督对比学习可帮助遥感模型学习地物类别本身的不变特征，缓解"城区建筑vs郊区建筑"等背景偏移导致的误分类；3) 结合遥感中常见的多时相、多视角数据，将同一目标在不同时间、不同角度的图像也纳入正样本对，进一步增强不变性。

Abstract (英文): Deep neural networks trained with Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM) often fail under distribution shifts because they exploit spurious correlations between object labels and background context. Recent generative approaches address this issue by creating counterfactual images with altered contexts, but typically use these samples as standard data augmentation, leaving the model free to retain background-sensitive representations. We propose a two-stage framework that uses generative intervention to explicitly learn background-invariant visual representations. First, we isolate the foreground object using zero-shot segmentation and generate context-shifted variants with a structure-preserving diffusion model, preserving object identity while varying the surrounding environment. We then introduce Cross-Variant Self-Supervised Learning, where variants of the same object under different backgrounds form positive pairs in a contrastive objective. This encourages the encoder to align object-centric representations while suppressing background-specific cues. Then, we fine-tune the pretrained encoder using an ERM warm-up followed by GroupDRO with layer-wise learning rates. Experiments on distribution-shift benchmarks demonstrate best worst-group performance, achieving 92.5% on Waterbirds, 81.7% on MetaShift, and 87.4% on NICO++. Code: https://github.com/surajyadav-research/GRSSL

</details>


### [33] [AVA-VLM: Adaptive Visual Attention-Vision Language Model for In-the-Wild Construction Site Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05859)
*Younggun Kim,Taeheon Kim,Youngseo Kim,Seunghee Park*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AVA-VLM提出一种自适应视觉注意力机制，模拟人类由粗到细的推理策略：先分析低分辨率全局图像，仅在需要详细检查时才选择性请求高分辨率局部裁剪，从而提升远程/低分辨率条件下的可靠性并减少视觉token使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有面向建筑工地的VLM主要采用基于全局图像的直接QA微调范式，在野外部署时存在操作范围有限、低分辨率输入下可靠性不足、推理效率低等问题。

Method: 提出AVA-VLM，核心思想是模拟人类检查员的"由粗到细"推理：1) 先处理低分辨率全局图像；2) 仅当需要详细检查时，才选择性请求高分辨率局部裁剪区域；3) 引入区域感知的Chain-of-Thought数据集，教会模型何时检查、裁剪何处以及如何利用局部证据。

Result: AVA-VLM在远程/低分辨率条件下提升了可靠性，同时大幅减少了视觉token的使用量。

Conclusion: 模拟人类由粗到细的视觉推理策略可以有效提升VLM在建筑工地监测等野外场景中的实用性和效率。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该方法的"由粗到细"策略可迁移至遥感场景：1) 先对低分辨率卫星/航拍全局图进行快速筛查，发现疑似目标区域后再请求高分辨率局部裁剪做精细判别，大幅降低遥感大图推理的计算开销；2) 区域感知CoT数据集设计可直接适配遥感目标检测与变化检测任务，教会模型在何处"放大"检查；3) 对于多尺度遥感影像（如不同分辨率卫星数据），该自适应注意力机制天然适合处理跨分辨率推理问题。

Abstract (英文): Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are promising for construction-site monitoring, and recent construction-tailored VLMs have primarily adapted pretrained VLMs through direct QA-style fine-tuning from a single global image. We argue that this direct paradigm remains limited for in-the-wild deployment in terms of operational range, reliability under reduced-resolution inputs, and inference efficiency. To address these challenges, we propose AVA-VLM, an Adaptive Visual Attention-Vision Language Model that follows a human-inspired coarse-to-fine reasoning strategy. AVA-VLM first reasons over a low-resolution global image and selectively requests a high-resolution local crop only when detailed inspection is needed, similar to how a human inspector zooms in on hard-to-see yet important areas. We further introduce a region-aware Chain-of-Thought dataset that teaches the model when to inspect, where to crop, and how to use local evidence. Experiments show that AVA-VLM improves reliability under long-distance and reduced-resolution conditions while substantially reducing visual-token usage.

### [34] [Harrison.Rad 1.5 Technical Report: A radiology foundation model that can draft reports from images, priors and clinical context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05880)

Method: 三阶段训练流程：1) 基础语言模型在放射学报告上进行领域适应；2) 基于约600万图像-报告实例的对比视觉编码器训练，使用课程式难负样本；3) 多轮对话的视觉问答微调。评估采用Findings-Diagnosis评分框架，扩展RadGraph-XL实体提取，结合基于本体的同义词匹配和极性矛盾检测。
