  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉-嗅觉对齐面临挑战，因为许多嗅觉线索来自像素中不可见的上下文环境因素，现有数据集虽已配对视觉场景与电子鼻测量值，但仍缺乏有效的跨模态对齐方法。作者希望通过语言作为语义桥梁来解决这一对齐问题。

Method: 1）使用VLM生成包含物体、环境和合理气味线索的场景描述；2）训练气味编码器将电子鼻信号映射到与视觉和文本表征对齐的共享嵌入空间；3）引入语言引导的潜在分解，将物体特定气味与环境上下文气味分离。

Result: 在New York Smells数据集上，SCENT在气味到图像和气味到文本的检索任务上均显著优于仅基于视觉的基线方法，达到SOTA性能，并能实现复杂气味混合的解耦。

Conclusion: 上下文语义信息对多模态学习中嗅觉感知的接地至关重要，该框架为未来嗅觉与视觉的跨模态研究奠定了基础。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像同样存在"像素不可见"的环境语义信息（如土壤湿度、污染程度、植被健康状况等），可借鉴SCENT的语言引导跨模态对齐思路：1）用遥感VLM生成场景语义描述（如"干旱区、植被稀疏、扬尘"），作为遥感图像与地面传感器（如空气质量监测站、土壤传感器）数据的语义桥梁，实现遥感影像到环境指标的反演；2）引入语言引导的潜在分解，分离"地物类型相关信号"与"环境上下文信号"；3）应用于遥感气味/气体排放监测（如甲烷泄漏）的多模态融合。

Abstract (英文): Images tell us what a scene looks like, but rarely what it would feel like to be there. While recent datasets pair visual scenes with electronic-nose measurements, aligning smell signals with images remains challenging because many olfactory cues arise from contextual environmental factors that are not directly visible in pixels. We introduce SCENT, a multimodal framework that uses language guidance as a semantic bridge between vision and olfaction. Our approach leverages Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to generate scene descriptors capturing objects, environmental context, and plausible ambient smell cues suggested by the visual scene. These descriptors provide semantic guidance for learning olfactory representations. We train a smell encoder that maps electronic-nose signals into a shared embedding space aligned with both visual and textual representations, and introduce a languageguided latent decomposition that separates object-specific odors from contextual environmental contributions. Experiments on the New York Smells dataset demonstrate that SCENT significantly improves crossmodal retrieval compared to vision-only baselines, achieving state-of-theart performance on smell-to-image and smell-to-text retrieval tasks. In addition, our framework produces interpretable olfactory representations that enable the disentanglement of complex smell mixtures. Our results reveal the importance of contextual semantic information for grounding olfactory perception in multimodal learning and pave the way for future research in this area.

</details>


### [69] [MAC-XA: Multi-view Anatomy-Correspondence Fusion for Coronary Stenosis Reporting from X-ray Angiography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06268)
*Chen Jia,Baochang Zhang,Fatia Kusuma Dewi,Amir Yousefi,Heribert Schunkert,Reza Ghotbi,Nassir Navab*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种对齐约束的多视图融合方法用于冠脉X射线造影中的狭窄报告生成。通过可控合成数据生成策略提供几何驱动的块级对应监督，并设计解剖对应模块学习跨视图对应矩阵，在融合前显式对齐辅助视图特征，从而在解剖一致区域约束证据聚合。实验表明该方法在对应一致性和结构化狭窄报告方面优于单视图建模和传统多视图融合方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 冠脉X射线造影中的多视图推理本质上是跨投影几何问题，但自动化报告生成在此领域尚未被充分探索。单视图建模因3D血管拓扑导致的投影依赖性分支重叠和缩短而不完整且不稳定。现有多视图融合方法由于真实血管造影中无法观察和显式监督跨视图对齐，只能依赖隐式相关性而非验证的解剖对应，导致融合效果受限。

Method: 1) 可控合成血管造影生成策略，提供几何驱动的块级对应监督；2) 解剖对应模块，学习跨视图对应矩阵，在主视图坐标空间中显式对齐辅助视图特征；3) 对齐约束的证据聚合，将融合限制在解剖一致区域。

Result: 在合成数据和真实血管造影的零样本迁移实验中，对齐约束设计在对应一致性和结构化狭窄报告方面均优于单视图建模和传统多视图融合方法。

Conclusion: 将多视图狭窄报告重新定义为对齐约束的聚合问题，通过合成数据提供的可监督对应关系和解剖对应模块的显式对齐，有效克服了真实数据中跨视图对齐不可观测的瓶颈，提升了多视图融合的解剖一致性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该方法的对齐约束多视图融合框架可迁移至遥感领域中的多角度/多视角影像分析任务，例如：1) 遥感立体影像中的目标检测与变化检测，通过可控合成数据生成（如3D建筑模型渲染不同视角影像）提供像素级对应监督；2) 多视角遥感图像融合中的几何一致性约束，学习跨视角对应矩阵对齐特征后再融合；3) 遥感图像中的遮挡和透视缩短问题的处理，类似冠脉造影中的分支重叠问题。

Abstract (英文): Multi-view reasoning in coronary X-ray angiography is inherently a cross-projection geometric problem, yet automated report generation in this setting remains largely unexplored. The 3D vascular topology leads to projection-dependent branch overlap and foreshortening, rendering single-view modeling fundamentally incomplete and unstable for lesion localization and stenosis grading. Although multi-view fusion appears promising, learning anatomically consistent fusion from real angiograms is impeded by a critical limitation: cross-view alignment is unobservable and cannot be explicitly supervised. Consequently, conventional fusion relies on implicit correlations rather than verified anatomical correspondence. We address this by reformulating multi-view stenosis reporting as an alignment-constrained aggregation problem. A controllable synthetic angiography generation strategy is introduced to expose geometry-derived patch-level correspondence supervision unavailable in real data. An anatomy-correspondence module learns cross-view correspondence matrices that explicitly align auxiliary features within the main-view coordinate space prior to fusion, thereby constraining evidence aggregation to anatomically consistent regions. Experiments on synthetic data and zero-shot transfer to real angiograms show that this alignment-constrained design improves correspondence consistency and structured stenosis reporting compared to single-view modeling and conventional multi-view fusion methods. The code will be publicly available upon publication.

### [70] [Analysis-by-Proxy: Localization Signals in VLMs Operating as Condition Encoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06445)
*Yoav Baron,Sara Dorfman,Roni Paiss,Daniel Cohen-Or,Or Patashnik*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出“代理分析”（Analysis-by-Proxy）框架，通过训练轻量级代理模型分析VLM在扩散图像编辑中的中间表征，发现当前编辑管线因将VLM视为单次前传的条件编码器，导致其定位信号无法可靠传播到预设层，而是隐藏在不同位置的中间表征中，揭示了现有条件提取策略的根本性失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于VLM的扩散图像编辑管线在复杂多实体场景中无法保持VLM本身具备的定位精度，作者假设这种性能差距源于将VLM作为条件编码器的单一前向传播限制，无法发挥其自回归生成优势，因此需要系统性地探究VLM作为条件编码器时其空间理解能力是否、以及如何被保留。

Method: 提出Analysis-by-Proxy（代理分析）框架，在VLM的中间表征上训练轻量级、可解释的代理模型，执行辅助定位任务，通过代理模型的分析来揭示VLM内部编码定位信息的具体表征层及其行为特征。

Result: 发现当前编辑管线存在根本性的表征-提取不匹配：VLM条件编码器中的定位信号在单次前传约束下无法可靠传播到预设的条件层，而是隐藏在输入提示词变化而变化的中间表征中，现有固定层配置的提取策略无法捕获该信号。

Conclusion: 现有条件提取策略存在根本性失败，该框架为更合理设计条件化架构打开了新方向。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。方案：(1) 遥感图像编辑（如多时相变化编辑、目标替换）可借鉴该框架分析现有VLM+扩散模型结合方案中定位信息丢失的具体环节，设计自适应层选择策略以提升编辑精度；(2) 遥感目标检测/定位任务中，可将VLM作为辅助编码器，利用代理分析框架自动识别最佳特征层提取定位信息，避免手调层配置的盲目性；(3) 注意遥感图像通常具有多尺度、大场景特性，VLM中间表征的位置依赖性可能更强，该框架可帮助设计多尺度条件提取策略。

Abstract (英文): Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are increasingly utilized as the conditioning backbone for diffusion-based image editing due to their remarkable multimodal reasoning capabilities. While standalone VLMs demonstrate strong localization capabilities, editing pipelines frequently struggle to maintain this accuracy, particularly in complex, multi-entity scenes. In this work, we investigate this performance gap, hypothesizing that it stems from treating the VLM as a condition encoder. In this role, the model is restricted to a single forward pass, preventing the autoregressive generation process for which it was optimized, thereby failing to fully expose its capabilities. To investigate whether this spatial understanding persists when the VLM is used as a condition encoder, we introduce Analysis-by-Proxy. In this framework, we train a lightweight, interpretable proxy model on the VLM's intermediate representations using an auxiliary localization task. By analyzing the VLM through this proxy, we uncover the specific VLM representations that encode localization information. Our findings expose a fundamental mismatch between how spatial knowledge is represented within a VLM condition encoder and how it is extracted by current editing pipelines. We reveal that under single-pass constraints, the localization signal does not reliably propagate to the predefined layer configurations commonly used for conditioning. Instead, this crucial signal remains hidden within intermediate representations, at locations that vary depending on the input prompt. Using our introduced Analysis-by-Proxy framework, we reveal the fundamental failures of existing condition extraction strategies in editing pipelines, opening the door to more principled design of conditioning architectures.

### [71] [Straight-Path Flow Matching for Incomplete Multi-View Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06281)
*Yiteng Yuan,Junyan Wang,Zheyuan Liu,Hong Jia,Lei Fan,Zhulin Tao,Lianbo Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于流匹配（flow-matching）的端到端生成式不完整多视图聚类框架，利用确定性ODE流替代扩散模型的随机轨迹，在缺失视图补全与聚类一致性之间建立更好的对齐，并在多个基准数据集上取得了SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的端到端生成式不完整多视图聚类方法依赖扩散模型，但扩散模型从聚类无关的噪声初始化，且随机去噪动力学并非为聚类任务显式设计，导致聚类目标与生成过程之间存在错配。

Method: 1）提出流匹配框架，使用观测视图与缺失视图对表示之间的线性插值路径，以确定性ODE流替代扩散的随机轨迹；2）从理论上证明确定性ODE流在类条件数据分布传输和聚类一致性保持方面优于扩散模型；3）构建端到端架构，集成直路流匹配视图补全与聚类级及熵对齐损失，强制跨视图聚类一致性。

Result: 在标准不完整多视图聚类基准数据集上的大量实验表明，所提出的框架取得了新的最先进性能。

Conclusion: 确定性ODE流比扩散模型的随机轨迹更有利于聚类目标，通过合理设计概率路径和聚类对齐损失，可以在不完整多视图聚类中同时实现高质量补全和聚类一致性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。1）遥感中常存在多模态数据（如光学-SAR）缺失问题，可将该流匹配框架直接应用于遥感多模态聚类任务，尤其适用于云遮挡导致的光学影像缺失场景；2）可结合遥感影像的空间-光谱特征，在流匹配路径中引入地理空间先验（如地形约束）以提升补全质量；3）遥感中的多时相数据可视为多视图，该框架可扩展至时序遥感影像的不完整聚类分析；4）可尝试将直路流匹配与遥感场景的语义分割任务联合训练，实现缺失区域的补全与分类一体化。

Abstract (英文): Incomplete Multi-View Clustering addresses the problem of clustering multi-modal data when certain views are missing. Recent end-to-end generative approaches leverage diffusion models to recover missing views via stochastic noise-to-data trajectories. While expressive, such mechanisms are not explicitly designed for clustering, as they initialize from cluster-agnostic noise and rely on stochastic denoising dynamics. In this work, we revisit probability path design in end-to-end generative IMVC. We introduce a flow-matching framework with a linear interpolation path between paired view representations, that replaces diffusion with probability flows between observed and missing views. We provide a formal analysis showing that deterministic ODE flows are inherently better aligned with clustering objectives than diffusion-based stochastic trajectories, especially in terms of transport mechanisms that respect class-conditional data distributions and maintain cluster consistency in finite-step regimes. Building upon this insight, we develop an end-to-end IMVC architecture that integrates straight-path flow-matching view completion with cluster-level and entropy-based alignment to enforce cross-view clustering consistency. Extensive experiments on standard IMVC benchmarks demonstrate that the proposed framework establishes new state-of-the-art performance.

### [72] [Prompt-Adapter Context Routing for Parameter-Efficient Multi-Shot Long Video Extrapolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06481)
*Anna Córdoba,Adam Puente Tercero,Nerea Angulo Hijo,Mar Linares Tercero,Julia Barrientos,Ainhoa Miranda,Jesús Olivera*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PACR-Video，一种参数高效的帧扩展框架，通过冻结文本到视频扩散变换器并添加低秩时间适配器、递归提示库和门控路由机制，实现多镜头长视频外推，在多个基准上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长视频外推面临保持跨镜头实体一致性、场景结构、视觉风格和因果连贯性的挑战，现有方法要么需要全模型微调（计算成本高），要么在长程连贯性上表现不佳。

Method: 1) 冻结文本到视频扩散变换器，添加低秩时间适配器；2) 引入可学习的镜头角色提示token；3) 构建递归提示库，存储实体、位置、动作和风格提示，并通过适配器门控根据预测的叙事依赖关系路由；4) 设计镜头局部/故事全局优化目标（下一镜头重建、跨镜头身份对比、提示稀疏正则化）；5) 适配器组合调度平衡早期视觉一致性与后期事件进展和视角变化。

Result: 在六个多镜头和长视频基准上，在分布质量、语义对齐、身份一致性、时间平滑性、运动稳定性、过渡连贯性和人类偏好方面均优于文本到视频、微调、记忆增强、流式和递归上下文基线。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：70%。遥感视频外推（如连续卫星图像预测）可借鉴该框架：1) 将遥感时序中的地理实体（建筑物、水体、植被）作为实体提示，地理坐标和区域作为位置提示；2) 递归提示库可存储多时相遥感影像中的变化模式；3) 低秩适配器适配遥感扩散模型可减少计算开销；4) 需改进：遥感数据缺乏自然语言描述，需设计视觉特征嵌入替代文本token，且因果进展约束需替换为物理规律（如植被生长周期）约束。

Abstract (英文): We present PACR-Video, a parameter-efficient framework for multi-shot long video extrapolation that preserves recurring entities, scene structure, visual style, and causal progression without full generator fine-tuning. PACR-Video keeps a text-to-video diffusion transformer frozen and augments it with low-rank temporal adapters conditioned by learned shot-role prompt tokens. To maintain long-horizon coherence, it builds a recursive prompt bank that stores compact entity, location, action, and style prompts from previous shots, then routes them through adapter gates according to predicted narrative dependencies. A Shot-Local/Story-Global tuning objective combines next-shot reconstruction, cross-shot identity contrast, and prompt sparsity regularization, while an adapter composition schedule balances early-shot visual consistency with later-shot event progression and viewpoint change. Across six multi-shot and long-video benchmarks, PACR-Video outperforms text-to-video, tuning-based, memory-augmented, streaming, and recursive-context baselines on distributional quality, semantic alignment, identity consistency, temporal smoothness, motion stability, transition coherence, and human preference. These results show that compact prompt routing and lightweight temporal adaptation provide sufficient controllable capacity for stable long video extrapolation.

Rather than explicitly authoring every component of a virtual environment, these models autoregressively synthesize future observations conditioned on the current world state and user interactions, enabling playable worlds to be generated online. Trained on both gameplay recordings and real-world videos, they can capture diverse visual appearances and physical dynamics, opening new opportunities for interactive applications beyond gaming, including embodied intelligence. In this paper, we present \textbf{AlayaWorld}, a full-stack open-source framework for building interactive generative worlds. ### [74] [AirflowAttack: Thermal-Airflow Adversarial Perturbations against Infrared Remote-Sensing Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06485)
*Cong Su,Jiaju Han,Xuemeng Sun,Chengyin Hu,Qike Zhang,Jiujiang Guo,Yiwei Wei,Jiahuan Long*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 首次针对红外遥感视觉语言模型（VLM）提出对抗攻击方法 AirflowAttack，利用热空气流动湍流作为先验生成物理可行的通用扰动，在多个模型和任务上实现了高攻击成功率，并揭示了模型将扰动误判为真实热证据的悖论现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红外遥感图像在安全关键场景中日益重要，但现有视觉语言模型在该领域的对抗鲁棒性尚未被研究，且缺乏针对红外模态物理特性的对抗攻击方法。

Method: 提出 AirflowAttack 方法：设计轻量级生成器，合成与输入无关的通用扰动，并通过正则化使其逼近物理上合理的空气流动模式；在单一代理 CLIP 模型上优化后，迁移攻击其他模型。

Result: 在5种CLIP骨干上平均零样本场景分类攻击成功率达48.5%，远超基线方法（27.7%-37.0%）；对6种先进VLM可使场景分类准确率相对下降最高38.2%；消融实验表明空气流动先验在不牺牲攻击成功率的前提下提升了物理可行性。

Conclusion: 红外遥感VLM生态系统存在严重安全漏洞：模型不仅易受攻击，还可能在置信度上反常提升，将扰动误判为真实的温度梯度和对流等热证据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。本文直接针对红外遥感VLM，是遥感安全领域的开创性工作。改进方向：（1）可进一步探索多模态（可见光+红外）联合攻击；（2）可结合真实红外大气传输模型生成更逼真的扰动；（3）可设计针对遥感场景下不同地形/气候条件的自适应扰动；（4）可扩展至目标检测、语义分割等更多遥感下游任务。

Abstract (英文): Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly deployed on infrared (IR) remote sensing imagery in security-critical settings, yet their adversarial robustness remains unexamined. We present AirflowAttack, to our knowledge the first adversarial attack for IR remote-sensing VLMs and the first to weaponize thermal-airflow turbulence as the perturbation prior. A lightweight generator synthesizes a single input-agnostic perturbation regularized toward physically plausible airflow patterns. Optimized on one surrogate CLIP model, it attains a mean zero-shot scene-classification attack success rate (ASR, the fraction of samples whose top-1 class changes) of 48.5% across five diverse CLIP backbones, far exceeding four IR-specific physical baselines (27.7--37.0%). Applied to six state-of-the-art VLMs, it cuts scene-classification accuracy by up to 38.2% relative, yet paradoxically makes some models more confident in their IR analysis, confabulating the perturbation as genuine thermal evidence such as temperature gradients and convection. Ablations show the airflow prior raises physical plausibility at no measurable cost to attack success. Together with a benchmark spanning eleven models and four tasks, these findings expose critical vulnerabilities in the rapidly expanding IR VLM ecosystem.

</details>

*Alessandra Ibba*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了固定三层GCN架构下不同图构建技术对视觉任务性能的影响，揭示了网络结构对计算流程的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习模型在视觉任务中表现优异，但无法充分编码图像中的空间、拓扑和语义信息；图神经网络虽有潜力，但其在视觉任务中的有效应用尚未被系统探索。

Result: 网络结构显著影响模型性能；图构建阶段（图构建前的计算流程）受结构本身的强烈影响，是重要的方法学贡献。

Abstract (英文): Deep learning models have emerged in machine learning and related fields, demonstrating astonishing performance in various visual tasks. Graph neural networks offer a good framework to face this aspect, but their effective use for visual tasks has been only partly explored and mainly starting from a limited perspective. This work aims to address this gap by conducting a systematic comparison of current graph construction techniques within the context of a fixed three-layer GCN architecture. Through an empirical study, it demonstrates in particular how the network structure affects performance and provides an important methodological contribution regarding the computational stages preceding graph utilization, which will be strongly influenced by the structure itself.

### [76] [ELSA3D: Elastic Semantic Anchoring for Unified 3D Understanding and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06565)
*Tianjiao Yu,Xinzhuo Li,Yifan Shen,Onkar Susladkar,Yuanzhe Liu,Xiaona Zhou,Ismini Lourentzou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ELSA3D 是一个统一的三维基础模型，通过弹性语义锚定机制，在共享骨干网络中实现文本与三维几何的精细化交互。它采用尺度感知的八叉树分词器（octree tokenizer）和锚点令牌（Anchor Tokens），在多个抽象尺度上联合结构语言与几何推理，实现了图像/文本到三维生成以及三维描述任务的最优性能，同时将FLOPs和推理延迟降低约一半。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一三维基础模型将文本和三维令牌简单拼接为扁平序列并依赖自注意力机制，导致粗粒度结构线索和细粒度几何细节被混合成一个无差异的表示，文本-三维交互本质上是隐式的、低效的。ELSA3D旨在解决这一问题，实现显式、精准且可弹性分配的跨模态交互。

Method: 1) 尺度感知八叉树分词器（Scale-aware Octree Tokenizer）：以层次化八叉树结构表示几何，不同深度对应不同抽象尺度；2) 锚点令牌（Anchor Tokens）：稀疏的跨模态单元，负责选择语义线索、路由至最相关的三维尺度、检索该尺度的几何证据并将融合信号写回统一表示；3) 轻量级逐块路由器（Per-block Router）：决定哪些文本令牌在哪个几何尺度上实例化锚点，使计算和推理都具备弹性。

Result: 在图像到三维生成、文本到三维生成和三维描述任务上均达到最先进水平，显著超越最强的统一基线模型，同时相较于非弹性版本的同一模型，FLOPs和推理延迟减少约一半。

Conclusion: ELSA3D通过弹性语义锚定机制，在统一三维基础模型中实现了稀疏、精准、尺度感知的跨模态交互，同时大幅提升计算效率，为统一三维理解与生成提供了一种高效的范式。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感三维重建与理解任务（如基于卫星/无人机影像的三维城市建模、地形生成、建筑物描述）可从ELSA3D中受益：1) 遥感影像具有多尺度特征（全局场景布局 vs. 局部建筑细节），ELSA3D的尺度感知八叉树分词器可直接适配遥感三维点云/网格的多层级表示；2) 锚点令牌可用于将遥感文本描述（如“东侧有高层建筑，屋顶为蓝色”）与对应尺度的几何特征对齐；3) 轻量级路由器可降低大规模遥感三维场景的计算开销。改进方向：需将八叉树结构适配为遥感常见的多视角影像+深度图输入，并增加对地理坐标系和绝对空间位置的编码支持。

Abstract (英文): Unified 3D foundation models aspire to generate 3D assets and reason about them in language within a single backbone, but their text-3D interaction remains largely implicit. Existing methods concatenate text and 3D tokens into a flat sequence and rely on self-attention, collapsing coarse structural cues and fine geometric details into one undifferentiated representation. We introduce ELSA3D, a unified 3D model that addresses this with elastic semantic anchoring, structuring language and geometric reasoning jointly along matched abstraction scales. ELSA3D represents geometry with a scale-aware octree tokenizer and introduces Anchor Tokens, sparse cross-modal units that select semantic cues, route them to the most relevant 3D scale, retrieve scale-specific geometric evidence, and write the fused signal back into the unified representation, keeping interaction sparse yet precise. A lightweight per-block router makes both computation and reasoning elastic, choosing which text tokens instantiate anchors at which geometric scale so that cross-modal capacity concentrates where alignment is most needed. ELSA3D achieves state-of-the-art performance across image-to-3D generation, text-to-3D generation, and 3D captioning, outperforming the strongest unified baseline while roughly halving FLOPs and inference latency relative to the non-elastic version of the same model.

### [77] [Synthetic-to-Real Translation for Class-Agnostic Motion Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06319)
*Yizheng Wu,Hongwei Fan,Kewei Wang,Ruibo Li,Xingyi Li,Xiao Song,Zhe Wang,Chenjing Ding,Dongliang Wang,Zhiguo Cao,Guosheng Lin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对自动驾驶中运动预测的合成数据到真实数据迁移问题，提出了一种融合物体感知运动预测和物体辅助运动增强的运动知识迁移框架，并构建了首个面向运动预测的合成4D LiDAR数据集Motion4D，实验表明该方法有效弥合了域间差异并在真实场景中取得优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界运动标签获取成本高昂，若能实现从合成数据到真实数据的运动知识迁移将极具价值。然而，当前朴素的运动回归方法对合成-真实域偏移高度敏感，导致知识迁移不可靠，因此需要探索更有效的合成到真实运动预测方法。

Method: 提出运动知识迁移框架，包含两个关键组件：(1) 物体感知运动预测——显式建模运动模式与物体先验的联合分布以增强域不变特征学习；(2) 物体辅助运动增强——利用学习到的物体先验过滤运动噪声的标签精炼机制。同时构建了首个面向运动预测的合成4D LiDAR数据集Motion4D。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提方法有效弥合了合成域与真实域之间的域差距，在真实场景中取得了优于现有方法的性能。

Conclusion: 物体感知的联合分布建模与物体先验引导的运动标签精炼是弥合合成-真实域差距的有效策略，Motion4D数据集为后续运动预测研究提供了有价值的资源。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样面临真实运动/变化标注稀缺的问题。(1) 可将该框架迁移至遥感视频中的运动目标检测与跟踪任务，利用合成遥感数据（如模拟卫星视频）预训练物体感知运动预测模型，再微调到真实遥感场景；(2) 物体感知运动预测可应用于遥感时序影像的变化检测，通过建模变化模式与地物先验的联合分布提升跨时相域泛化能力；(3) 物体辅助运动增强机制可迁移至遥感中的伪变化噪声过滤，利用地物先验（如建筑物、植被的时序变化规律）过滤变化检测中的虚假变化。

Abstract (英文): Motion understanding is critical for ensuring safety and robustness in autonomous driving systems, driving increasing interest in motion prediction. A key challenge in this domain is the high cost associated with acquiring real-world motion labels. It is therefore ideal if we could transfer motion knowledge from synthetic data to real data. In this context, we explore the potential of synthetic-to-real translation for motion prediction (SRMP). However, the most used naive motion regression methods are notably sensitive to the synthetic-to-real domain shift, resulting in unreliable knowledge translation. To address this, we propose a novel approach integrating a motion knowledge translation framework with two key components: (1) objectness-aware motion prediction, which explicitly models the joint distribution of motion patterns and objectness priors to improve domain-invariant feature learning, and (2) objectness-aided motion enhancement, a motion label refinement mechanism that leverages learned objectness priors to filter motion noise. Furthermore, we present a physically-based pipeline for generating Motion4D, the first synthetic 4D LiDAR dataset tailored for SRMP research, addressing the lack of synthetic motion datasets. Experimental results demonstrate that our approach effectively bridges the domain gaps and yields superior performance on real scenes.

### [78] [Bridging Diffusion Pruning and Step Distillation with Teacher-Aligned Repair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06335)
*Jincheng Ying,Li Wenlin,Minghui Xu,Yinhao Xiao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SiDA方法，通过在剪枝和一步蒸馏之间引入短期的教师对齐修复阶段，解决了直接替换后训练为蒸馏失败的问题。在ImageNet-512上，20%剪枝的一步生成器（98.826M参数，1次网络评估）达到FID 3.12，优于EDM2-XS基线（124.713M参数，63次评估，FID 3.53）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型推理成本高昂，源于大模型和多次去噪步骤。现有压缩方法分别处理剪枝（需长后训练恢复多步采样器）和步骤蒸馏（需学生已能很好跟随教师），本文探索能否用步骤蒸馏替代剪枝后的重训练，从而压缩两个成本。

Method: 提出SiDA（Step Distillation after Pruning）框架：1）对EDM2-XS教师模型进行剪枝；2）引入短期的教师对齐修复阶段（bridge），在带噪声的真实图像潜特征上匹配剪枝生成器与教师；3）将修复后的检查点交给一步蒸馏。通过合适的蒸馏目标实现剪枝与一步蒸馏的联合压缩。

Result: ImageNet-512上：EDM2-XS基线（124.713M参数，63次评估，FID 3.53）；20%剪枝一步生成器（98.826M参数，1次评估，FID 3.12）；30%剪枝一步生成器（88.029M参数，1次评估，FID 4.26）。剪枝后直接蒸馏失败，加入对齐修复阶段后成功。

Conclusion: 剪枝后的重训练可以被步骤蒸馏替代，但需要短期的教师对齐修复作为桥梁。该方法能同时压缩网络规模和去噪步数，实现参数和推理效率的双重提升。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像生成任务（如高分辨率遥感图像超分辨率、云去除、域适应）同样面临扩散模型推理成本问题。可将SiDA框架迁移到遥感扩散模型上，先对遥感数据训练的扩散模型（如用于遥感图像翻译或超分辨的模型）进行剪枝，再用带遥感噪声潜特征的教师对齐修复阶段桥接，最后蒸馏为一步生成器，极大降低遥感应用的推理延迟。需注意遥感图像多光谱/高光谱通道数与自然图像不同，对齐修复阶段的潜特征需适配通道结构。

Abstract (英文): Diffusion models generate high-quality images, but their inference cost comes from two sources: large denoising networks and repeated denoising steps. Existing compression pipelines usually attack these costs separately. Pruning reduces the network, but most pruning methods still rely on a long post-pruning retraining stage to recover a many-step sampler. Step distillation reduces the number of denoising steps, but it usually assumes a student that can already follow the teacher well enough to receive useful distillation gradients. This paper asks whether post-pruning retraining can be replaced by step distillation. We find that the direct replacement fails: after pruning an EDM2-XS teacher, starting SiDA from the pruned checkpoint produces unusable samples. We introduce a short teacher-alignment repair stage as a bridge between pruning and step distillation. The bridge matches the pruned generator to the teacher on noisy real-image latents, then hands the repaired checkpoint to one-step distillation. On ImageNet-512, the original EDM2-XS baseline uses 124.713M parameters and 63 network evaluations, reaching an FID of 3.53. With a suitable distillation objective, our 20% pruned one-step generator uses 98.826M parameters and one network evaluation, reaching an FID of 3.12. With 30% pruning, the model uses 88.029M parameters and one network evaluation, with an FID of 4.26.

</details>


### [79] [Generalized Synthetic Image Detection with Enhanced RGB-Noise Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06354)
*Zhen Li,Gang Cao,Tian Zhang,Lifang Yu,Shaowei Weng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了RNSIDNet，一种通过增强RGB-噪声表示学习实现鲁棒生成式图像检测的框架。采用双分支架构，利用注意力优化的CLIP骨干提取全局RGB语义，通过特征线性调制模块动态调制Bayar卷积捕获的高频噪声伪影，并设计了难样本感知对比学习策略来最大化真实与合成图像间的判别边界。在八个基准数据集上取得了最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模生成模型使得AI生成图像的欺骗性增强，现有检测方法因依赖单域表示和传统二分类优化，在跨模型泛化和真实场景退化方面表现不佳。

Method: 1) 双分支架构：RGB分支使用注意力优化的CLIP骨干提取全局语义特征，噪声分支使用Bayar卷积捕获高频噪声伪影；2) 特征线性调制模块：用RGB语义动态调制噪声特征；3) 难样本感知对比学习策略：通过惩罚困难训练样本来重塑潜在特征空间，最大化真实域与合成域之间的判别边界。

Result: 在八个公开基准数据集上实现最先进性能，在泛化能力、鲁棒性和计算效率方面均优于现有方法。

Conclusion: RGB-噪声联合表示学习结合难样本对比学习策略能有效提升生成式图像检测的跨模型泛化能力和真实场景鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1) 将RNSIDNet的双分支架构直接迁移至遥感图像真伪鉴别任务，用于检测GAN/Diffusion生成的虚假遥感图像；2) 针对遥感图像多尺度、多光谱特点，在RGB分支中引入多尺度CLIP特征提取，噪声分支可扩展至多光谱噪声域分析；3) FiLM模块可进一步用于遥感图像融合任务中的质量评估。

Abstract (英文): The rapid advancement of large-scale generative models has accelerated the spread of highly deceptive AI-generated images, making generalized synthetic image detection a critical imperative. Existing forensic networks often struggle with cross-model generalization and realworld degradations due to their reliance on single-domain representations and conventional binary classification optimization. To overcome these limitations, we propose RNSIDNet, a novel forensic framework that achieves robust detection through enhanced RGB-Noise representation learning. Specifically, our method employs a dual-branch architecture where global RGB semantics, extracted by an attention-refined CLIP backbone, dynamically modulate highfrequency noise artifacts captured by Bayar convolutions via a Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM) module. To further enhance the learned representations, we design a Hard Sample-aware Contrastive Learning (HSCL) strategy. By explicitly penalizing challenging training samples, HSCL reshapes the latent feature space to maximize the discriminative margin between pristine and synthetic domains. Extensive experiments across eight public benchmark datasets verify that our model achieves state-of-the-art performance, delivering superior generalization ability, robustness, and computational efficiency. Code and dataset will be publicly available on https://github.com/multimediaFor/RNSIDNet.

### [80] [VaseMuseum: Digital Intelligent Museum for Ancient Greek Pottery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06374)
*Jiazi Wang,Nonghai Zhang,Qiushi Xie,Zeyu Zhang,Yufeng Chen,Yang Zhao,Ling Shao,Hao Tang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VaseMuseum，一个轻量级模块化多模态智能体框架，用于古希腊陶器数字博物馆，通过源级控制和响应级控制减少幻觉并提高引用有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在文化遗产领域（如古希腊陶器），VLM在开放解释时面临两个挑战：1）细粒度2D/3D视觉证据需结合策展知识，但检索可能引入弱来源和不可验证的引用；2）证据不完整或有歧义时，VLM常产生自信但无依据的回答，而非校准的不确定性。

Method: 提出VaseMuseum框架，包含交互式虚拟博物馆和VaseAgent。VaseAgent支持2D/3D感知、3D感知推理、外部知识检索和推理时可靠性控制。具体包括：1）源级控制：从权威网站和博物馆知识源检索证据，生成前选择多样且可验证的证据；2）响应级控制：生成后检查claims与证据池的匹配，在证据不足或冲突时鼓励中立、有依据的回答；3）无需训练的GRPO风格选择机制，在不更新VLM主干的条件下选择具有有效引用和校准置信度的响应。

Result: 在逼真的数字博物馆模拟中，与支持检索的VLM基线相比，VaseMuseum提高了引用有效性，减少了知识密集型查询上的幻觉，并在歧义下产生更中立的回答。

Conclusion: VaseMuseum通过源级和响应级双重控制机制，有效提升了VLM在文化遗产数字博物馆场景中的可靠性和可信度，特别是在处理不完整或歧义证据时表现更好。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样面临多源数据（卫星影像、DEM、GIS）检索质量不一、证据冲突等问题。具体方案：1）将VaseMuseum的源级控制机制应用于遥感多源数据融合，在生成地物分类或变化检测结果前筛选权威数据源；2）响应级控制可用于遥感解译中的不确定性表达，当影像模糊或数据冲突时给出带置信区间的中性结论；3）GRPO风格选择机制可用于遥感大模型在多个解译结果中选择引用有效且置信度校准的输出。

Abstract (英文): Vision-language models (VLMs) have made interactive digital museums increasingly feasible by connecting 3D digitization with natural-language artifact exploration. However, in cultural heritage domains such as ancient Greek pottery, reliable VLM assistance is limited by two challenges. First, open-ended interpretation requires grounding fine-grained 2D/3D visual evidence in specialized curatorial knowledge, yet the retrieval process may introduce weak sources and unverifiable references. Second, when the available evidence is incomplete, noisy, or ambiguous, VLMs often produce confident but unsupported answers instead of calibrated uncertainty. To address these challenges, we propose VaseMuseum, a lightweight and modular multimodal agent framework for intelligent digital museums of ancient Greek pottery. VaseMuseum combines an interactive virtual museum with VaseAgent, which supports both 2D images and 3D artifacts through multimodal perception, 3D-aware reasoning, external knowledge retrieval, and inference-time reliability control. Specifically, VaseAgent retrieves evidence from authoritative web and museum knowledge sources, and source-level control selects diverse and verifiable evidence before generation. Meanwhile, response-level control checks generated claims against the evidence pool and encourages neutral, evidence-bounded answers when support is insufficient or conflicting. Moreover, a training-free GRPO-style selection mechanism favors responses with valid references and calibrated confidence without updating the VLM backbone. Experiments in a realistic digital museum simulation show that VaseMuseum improves citation validity, reduces hallucinations on knowledge-intensive queries, and produces more neutral answers under ambiguity compared with search-enabled VLM baselines.

</details>


### [81] [FADRA: Frequency-Aware Diffusion with Residual Adaptation for Video Face Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06389)
*Jin Jiang,Jia Wang,Panwen Hu,Weiran Zhao,Shengcai Liao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出FADRA，一种基于频率感知扩散框架的视频人脸修复方法，通过轻量级LoRA适配器、LQ像素对齐特征融合模块、重复残差适应头（RRAH）以及频率感知损失，在保持时间一致性的同时恢复高质量人脸细节，在定量指标和视觉感知上均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频人脸修复方法在复杂退化条件下难以平衡空间保真度与时间一致性，亟需一种能同时兼顾高质量细节恢复与时序稳定性的鲁棒框架。

Method: 1）利用预训练文本到视频扩散模型的强时间一致性，引入轻量级LoRA适配器和LQ像素对齐特征融合模块高效适配冻结的生成先验；2）提出重复残差适应头（RRAH），在扩散骨干后逐步进行残差精炼，RRAH同时输入LQ潜变量和当前速度预测，使模型在每个流匹配步骤中反复参考LQ线索并预测残差更新；3）引入频率感知损失，对多个频谱波段提供显式监督，重点关注对感知质量关键且易产生时间抖动的频率成分。

Result: 大量实验表明，FADRA在恢复更好人脸结构的同时产生比最先进方法更时间一致的视频，在定量指标和视觉感知上均有明显提升。

Conclusion: FADRA通过频率感知的迭代残差适应策略，有效结合了预训练扩散模型的时序先验与LQ引导的细节恢复，为视频人脸修复提供了更鲁棒的解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感视频（如卫星视频）常面临运动模糊、云雾遮挡等复杂退化，且对时空一致性要求高。可将FADRA框架迁移至遥感视频恢复：1）LoRA适配器可针对遥感场景的退化模式（如条纹噪声、运动模糊）进行轻量级微调；2）RRAH中的LQ引导残差适应机制适用于遥感中多帧融合去模糊；3）频率感知损失可增强对高频地物纹理（如道路边缘、建筑物轮廓）的保持，同时抑制帧间闪烁。需调整之处：预训练扩散模型需替换为遥感视频领域的基础模型，特征对齐模块需适配遥感多光谱/高光谱通道。

Abstract (英文): Video face restoration (VFR) aims to recover high-quality and temporally consistent facial details from severely degraded video sequences; however, existing methods still struggle to balance spatial fidelity and temporal coherence under complex degradations. To address this, we propose FADRA, a frequency-aware diffusion framework with iterative residual adaptation specifically tailored for robust VFR. We first leverage the strong temporal consistency of a pre-trained text-to-video diffusion model and introduce lightweight LoRA adapters together with a Low-Quality (LQ) Pixel-Alignment Feature Fusion module to efficiently adapt the frozen generative prior to the VFR task. To further adapt the frozen diffusion backbone to the downstream VFR task beyond LoRA-based adaptation, we introduce a Repeated Residual Adaptation Head (RRAH) for step-wise residual refinement after the diffusion backbone. To make this refinement explicitly guided by the degraded observation, RRAH further takes the LQ latent together with the current velocity prediction as input, allowing the model to repeatedly revisit LQ cues and predict residual updates at each flow-matching step. This LQ-guided repeated residual adaptation helps recover fine facial details while preserving the inherent temporal priors of the pre-trained model. Furthermore, to ensure the structural integrity of perceptually important details, we introduce a Frequency-Aware Loss that provides explicit supervision across multiple spectral bands, emphasizing visually sensitive frequency components that are crucial for perceptual quality and prone to temporal jittering. Extensive experiments demonstrate that FADRA recovers better facial structures and produces more temporally consistent videos than state-of-the-art methods, leading to clear gains in both quantitative metrics and visual perception.

### [82] [Temporal Modeling of Optically Variable Devices in Identity Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06408)
*Glen Pouliquen,Joseph Chazalon,Guillaume Chiron,Oriol Ramos Terrades,Thierry Géraud,Ahmad Montaser Awal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出两种自监督方法，通过建模OVD（光变器件，即全息图）的动态行为来验证身份文档的真实性，无需攻击样本即可训练，在开放集场景下超越现有方法，并验证了时序建模对于防御复杂攻击的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有身份文档远程验证系统存在三个关键局限：1）将视频帧孤立处理，忽视OVD的动态特性，易受交换攻击；2）仅检测全息图存在性，无法验证特定OVD类型；3）逐帧视频标注成本过高，使监督训练不切实际。因此需要无需攻击样本、可建模时序动态、且能在开放集场景下工作的自监督方法。

Method: 提出两种新颖的自监督方法，专注于验证保护持证人肖像的透明OVD的动态行为。方法设计为开放集场景（训练时未知攻击类型），无需任何攻击样本，通过序列建模（Sequence Modeling）和异常检测（Anomaly Detection）来捕捉OVD在视频中的真实时序动态特征。

Result: 在公开数据集上超越了此前最先进的方法，同时严格遵守工业部署约束。结果表明建模时序动态对于在真实条件下击败复杂攻击至关重要。

Conclusion: 序列建模和异常检测是OVD验证的有效范式，证明了利用时序信息而非孤立帧分析是提升远程身份文档验证鲁棒性的关键路径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样存在大量时序影像（如多时相卫星图像、视频遥感），可借鉴本文的自监督序列建模思路：1）将OVD动态验证中的异常检测框架迁移至遥感变化检测任务，训练时无需大量标注的变化样本；2）利用时序建模区分真实地物变化与传感器伪影或人为篡改；3）开放集思想可应用于遥感中未知类型的地表覆盖变化检测，增强模型泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Robust remote verification of identity documents relies on analyzing faint, transparent security features like Optically Variable Devices (OVDs), or "holograms", within user-captured videos under uncontrolled conditions. Current systems, however, face critical limitations: existing methods often treat video frames in isolation, neglecting the intrinsic dynamic nature of OVDs and leaving systems vulnerable to swapping attacks, or focus on general holographic presence and lack the ability to verify specific OVD types. Moreover, the economic infeasibility of frame-by-frame video annotation makes supervised training impractical. In this work, we introduce two novel approaches for verifying the dynamic behavior of transparent OVDs protecting the holder's portrait, specifically designed for open-set scenarios where attack types are unknown during training. We demonstrate that these approaches can be trained without any attack samples in a self-supervised setting, surpassing previous state-of-the-art methods on public datasets while adhering strictly to industrial constraints. Our results confirm that modeling temporal dynamics is essential for defeating sophisticated attacks under realistic conditions, and underscores the promise of sequence modeling and anomaly detection for OVD verification. Code is available at https://github.com/EPITAResearchLab/pouliquen.26.icdar.

### [83] [HoloCount: A Holistic Visual Counting Benchmark for MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06420)
*Jinhong Deng,Limeng Qiao,Guanglu Wan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 HoloCount，一个基于三层层次分类法的全面视觉计数基准，用于诊断多模态大模型在语义计数、分析计数和鲁棒性测试中的计数能力。对20余个MLLM的评估显示，模型在从感知到复杂推理和对抗场景时性能显著下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计数基准主要关注简化语境下的基本感知，无法捕捉逻辑约束或对抗条件下出现的复杂失效模式，而MLLM的定量精度仍是瓶颈，存在数值幻觉问题。

Method: 构建HoloCount基准，采用三层层次分类法：(1) 语义计数（原子和属性枚举）；(2) 分析计数（空间和集合推理的逻辑组合）；(3) 鲁棒性测试（高密度场景、语言偏差等对抗性先验下的模型完整性）。

Result: 对20余个SOTA MLLM的评估揭示了关键性能差距：即使是顶级模型，在任务从感知转向复杂分析推理和对抗场景时也显著退化。

Conclusion: HoloCount系统性地揭示了当前MLLM计数能力图谱，为开发更扎实、更可靠的多模态系统提供了路线图。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感场景中地物计数（如建筑物、车辆、船只）对精细定位和空间推理要求极高。具体方案：(1) 将HoloCount的三层层次分类法迁移至遥感计数基准，构建遥感专用版本Remote-HoloCount；(2) 语义计数层可评估不同地物类别的原子计数（如"有多少辆汽车"）和属性计数（如"红色的屋顶有几个"）；(3) 分析计数层可评估空间关系计数（如"十字路口东北角的车辆数"）和集合运算计数（如"被阴影覆盖的建筑数量"）；(4) 鲁棒性测试层可引入遥感特有对抗场景，如云雾遮挡、光照变化、多尺度密集排列等，测试MLLM在高密度遥感场景下的计数可靠性。

Abstract (英文): Visual counting is a fundamental pillar of multimodal intelligence, requiring a seamless integration of fine-grained grounding and spatial reasoning. While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have achieved remarkable success in qualitative scene understanding, their quantitative precision remains a significant bottleneck, often characterized by persistent numerical hallucinations. Existing counting benchmarks primarily focus on basic perception in simplified contexts, failing to capture the complex failure modes that emerge under logical constraints or adversarial conditions. To address these limitations, we introduce HoloCount, a holistic and diagnostically rich benchmark structured around a three-level hierarchical taxonomy. HoloCount evaluates MLLMs across: (1) Semantic Counting, focusing on atomic and property-based enumeration; (2) Analytical Counting, assessing logical composition through spatial and set-based reasoning; and (3) Robustness Testing, probing model integrity against adverse scenarios and grounded counter-priors, such as high-density scenes and linguistic biases. Through an exhaustive evaluation of over 20 state-of-the-art MLLMs, we reveal a critical performance gap: even top-tier models degrade significantly as tasks transition from perception to complex analytical reasoning and adverse scenarios. Our findings provide a systematic landscape of current MLLM counting capabilities and offer a roadmap for developing more grounded and reliable multimodal systems. The dataset is available at https://mm-mvr.github.io/HoloCount/.

### [84] [XRFormer: Multiscale Tokenization for XRF Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06424)
*Sofiane Daimellah,Sylvie Le Hégarat-Mascle,Clotilde Boust*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出XRFormer，一种专为XRF光谱设计的Transformer架构，通过多尺度卷积分词器注入局部性和多分辨率归纳偏置，并结合掩码光谱建模(MSM)和物理启发的峰值存在预测(PPP)自监督预训练方法。在颜料鉴定和分离任务上，XRFormer以更少的参数(1.5M vs 3.37M)和更低的token分辨率(128 vs 512)超越ViT、SpectralFormer和1D-CNN基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: XRF光谱作为文化遗产材料分析的关键手段，现有学习模型未能充分考虑其作为一维信号的复杂性——由尖锐元素峰、宽结构和背景变化组成，自动学习面临挑战。

Method: 提出XRFormer架构：1) 多尺度卷积分词器，逐步降低光谱分辨率同时增加嵌入维度，注入局部性和多分辨率偏置；2) 标准Transformer编码器处理token序列；3) 自监督预训练结合掩码光谱建模(MSM)和物理启发的峰值存在预测(PPP)目标。

Result: 在Pigments Checker STANDARD v.5数据集上，XRFormer在颜料鉴定和分离任务上全面优于ViT、SpectralFormer（带/不带CAF）和1D-CNN基线。仅用1.5M参数（SpectralFormer的3.37M的一半）和128 token分辨率（SpectralFormer的512 token）实现更优性能。MSM和PPP预训练均带来一致性提升。

Conclusion: 多尺度、模态感知的分词策略是基于Transformer的XRF建模在数据有限条件下的有效且参数高效的解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1) XRF与遥感高光谱成像(HSI)同属光谱分析领域，可将XRFormer的多尺度卷积分词器直接迁移至遥感高光谱地物分类与丰度反演任务；2) 遥感场景下光谱分辨率更高、波段更多，可扩展XRFormer的多尺度层级以适应更长序列；3) PPP预训练目标可适配遥感中已知地物光谱特征峰（如矿物、植被红边等）的先验知识；4) 将MSM改进为空间-光谱联合掩码，利用相邻像素的空间相关性增强自监督学习效果。

Abstract (英文): X-ray fluorescence (XRF) spectroscopy is a key modality for material analysis in cultural heritage. However, automated learning from XRF spectra remains challenging: XRF spectra are complex one-dimensional signals composed of sharp elemental peaks, broader structures, and background variations that are not taken into account by existing learning-based models. This paper introduces XRFormer, a transformer architecture tailored to XRF spectra through a multiscale convolutional tokenizer that injects locality and multi-resolution inductive biases before global self-attention. The tokenizer progressively reduces spectral resolution while increasing embedding dimensionality, and the resulting token sequence is processed by a standard transformer encoder. We further investigate self-supervised pretraining for XRF representation learning using Masked Spectral modeling (MSM) and a physics-informed Peak Presence Prediction (PPP) objective. Experiments on the Pigments Checker STANDARD v.5 dataset for pigment identification and unmixing show that XRFormer consistently outperforms ViT, SpectralFormer (with and without CAF), and a 1D-CNN baseline for pigment identification. For pigment unmixing, XRFormer achieves robust abundance estimation while maintaining significantly higher parameter efficiency than SpectralFormer, operating at a lower token resolution (128 vs. 512 tokens) and with less than half the number of parameters (1.5M vs. 3.37M). MSM yields consistent gains across both tasks, while PPP further enhances performance for both identification and unmixing when tuned with an appropriate peak prominence. These results highlight multiscale, modality-aware tokenization as an effective and parameter efficient foundation for transformer-based XRF modeling under data-limited conditions. A GitHub repository is provided at https://github.com/sofiane1010/XRFormer.

To this end, we introduce PIPBench, the first profile-inclusive benchmark for evaluating personalized image generation. We further propose a novel data construction pipeline that leverages psychological and demographic profiling dimensions for both real-user data collection and scalable agent-based data generation. Using PIPBench, we conduct a thorough evaluation of representative line of methods. Our experiments reveal key limitations in existing methods, suggesting new challenges and opportunities for personalized text-to-image synthesis. Project page: https://wuyuhang05.github.io/PIPBench/

### [86] [Andha-Dhun: A First Look at Audio Descriptions in Hindi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06457)
*Ritabrata Chakraborty,Divy Kala,Nisheeth Bhooshan Gupta,Ganji Sreeram,Pailla Balakrishna Reddy,Makarand Tapaswi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究印地语音频描述（AD），建立了首个印地语人工AD数据集Andha-Dhun（8部电影），探索了两种生成方法（直接生成和翻译），并发现直接机器翻译存在文化参考不适应和多样性降低的问题，强调AD应以受众可及性为目标而非严格忠实于源语言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 印度中央电影认证委员会要求扩展AD至英语以外的语言，但目前尚无任何为印度语言生成AD的研究工作，存在明显空白。

Method: 构建了首个印地语人工AD数据集Andha-Dhun（来自8部完整电影），探索两种AD生成方法：（i）从英语密集视频描述直接生成印地语AD；（ii）将英语AD翻译为印地语。使用困惑度和LLM-as-a-judge指标分别评估流畅度和质量，并对比分析英印双语人工AD。

Result: 直接机器翻译引入伪影并缩小了多样性；机器翻译无法适应文化参考，人工翻译效果更好但仍不足；印地语AD应以面向印度BLV受众的可及性为目的，而非严格忠实于源语言。

Conclusion: 印地语AD生成的关键在于面向受众的内容适配而非翻译忠实性，现有翻译方法在文化适应方面存在显著不足。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：35%。遥感领域多为地理空间影像描述，与电影AD任务场景差异较大。若交叉，可将遥感影像的密集描述生成与AD迁移学习思路结合：先利用已有的遥感英文描述数据集预训练描述生成模型，再通过小样本翻译/适配策略迁移至非英语语种（如中文）的遥感影像描述，同时需设计文化/地理适应性评估指标，避免直接翻译导致的地物命名偏差。

Abstract (英文): Audio Descriptions (ADs) narrate visual content for Blind and Low Vision (BLV) audiences during gaps in audiovisual media. There is growing momentum around ADs in movies and TV shows, and with mandates from India's Central Board of Film Certification (CBFC), there is a need to expand ADs beyond English. Yet, there is no work that generates ADs for any Indian language. To address this gap, we present the first systematic study of ADs in Hindi, contributing to aspects such as data, generation, and evaluation. We introduce Andha-Dhun, the first dataset of human-authored Hindi ADs collected from 8 full-length movies. We explore two approaches for generating ADs in Hindi: (i) directly from English dense video descriptions, and (ii) translating English ADs into Hindi. We evaluate these approaches using perplexity and LLM-as-a-judge metrics to assess fluency and quality respectively. We also analyze movies that have both English and Hindi human-authored ADs and find that naive translation introduces artifacts and narrows diversity compared to original Hindi ADs. Direct machine translation fails to adapt cultural references, while human-translated ADs do better but still fall short. Our findings emphasize that the purpose of Hindi ADs is accessibility for Indian BLV audiences, and that this requires adapting content for the audience more than strict fidelity to the source.

### [87] [Verification of Dynamic Holographic Behavior in Identity Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06466)
*Glen Pouliquen,Joseph Chazalon,Guillaume Chiron,Thierry Géraud,Ahmad Montaser Awal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对身份证件上全息图（光学可变器件）的远程真伪验证问题，提出了三个贡献：1) 新发布的MIDV-DynAttack数据集，包含静态和动态攻击样本；2) 一种无需动态攻击样本即可训练的新验证方法，通过分析动态行为和外观实现全息图真伪判别，达到SOTA性能；3) 对现有方法进行基准测试，揭示了它们在应对动态攻击时的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 新方法在动态攻击检测上达到了新的SOTA性能，同时基准测试表明现有方法无法有效应对动态攻击及新的具有挑战性的攻击类型。

Conclusion: 本文通过发布高质量数据集和提出泛化能力更强的新方法，填补了全息图动态攻击验证的研究空白，为后续研究提供了标准化的评估基准和公开资源。

Abstract (英文): This paper addresses the remote verification of the authenticity of Optically Variable Devices (commonly known as holograms) on identity documents. Typically placed over the cardholder's photo, these devices provide strong and easily verifiable security for human inspection but pose challenges for automated verification. Existing approaches easily cover static frauds (e.g. paper photocopy) and can be evaluated for such, but their capacity to detect real, dynamic fraud cases (e.g. handcrafted hologram) has not been evaluated to date because of the lack of public datasets. Furthermore, they are usually trained to detect known attack types, and few of them can generalize to new, unseen attacks. This work features three contributions to address these limitations: 1) a new public dataset, MIDV-DynAttack, which extends the existing MIDV-Holo dataset with realistic, static and dynamic attacks against identity document specimens, tripling the number of attack samples compared to the original dataset, 2) a novel verification method which can assess the authenticity of a specific hologram thanks to the analysis of its dynamic behavior and appearance, can be trained without dynamic attack samples, and exhibits new state-of-the-art performance, 3) a benchmark of existing approaches which follows a clear evaluation protocol and emphasizes the inability of other approaches to deal with dynamic attacks, as well as new challenging attacks to deal with. Code and dataset are publicly available at https://github.com/EPITAResearchLab/pouliquen.25.icdar.

### [88] [EgoPolice: A Benchmark for Egocentric Video Understanding in High-Stakes Police Body-Worn Camera Footage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06468)

TL;DR: 本文提出了EgoPolice数据集，包含真实的警察-平民交互的第一人称视角视频（来自执法记录仪），以秒级粒度标注关键行为，并提供了分类和多项选择问答两个任务。实验表明，即使像Gemini 2.5 Pro这样的顶尖视频模型在高风险行为识别（如"Weapon Out"）上仍然表现不佳。该数据集为运动鲁棒和上下文感知的第一人称感知提供了具有挑战性的基准。

Abstract (英文): We introduce EgoPolice, a carefully curated dataset of real, egocentric police-civilian interactions, sourced from publicly available body-worn camera videos. We select police-civilian action labels that are critical for police behavioral research and annotate them at a second-by-second granularity. The videos feature rapid and irregular camera motion, dense human interactions, and rare high-stakes events, making the dataset a challenging benchmark for motion-robust and context-aware egocentric perception. We provide two different tasks, classification and multiple-choice question-answering, and benchmark both open-source and closed-source models. We find that even the best video models like Gemini 2.5 Pro still struggle to accurately predict high-risk actions such as "Weapon Out". Beyond serving as a benchmark, EgoPolice provides a foundation for developing models capable of identifying events of interest in large-scale body-worn camera video repositories, enabling more efficient downstream human review.

### [89] [A VLM-Enhanced Framework for Comprehensive Traffic Sign Condition Assessment Integrating Daytime Visual Performance and Nighttime Retroreflectivity Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06478)
*Linlin Zhang,Neema Jakisa Owor,Xiang Yu,Abby Watts,Yaw Adu-Gyamfi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种集成日间与夜间评估的交通标志综合检测框架，利用微调的视觉语言模型（VLM）评估日间视觉性能（可读性、颜色、表面完整性、周围环境），结合LiDAR-derived retroreflectivity评估夜间性能，构建综合标志状况指数（SCI），在462个标志中识别出68个需立即更换，为传统人工检测提供了经济有效的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交通标志检测依赖人工巡检，主观性强、劳动密集且存在安全隐患，而专业反光测量设备价格昂贵，小规模机构难以负担。现有研究多单独关注日间或夜间性能，缺乏两者综合评估的框架，因此亟需一种经济、全面、自动化的评估方法。

Method: 1) 使用三种微调的视觉语言模型（LLaVA、Qwen、InternVL）评估日间视觉性能，涵盖可读性、颜色、表面与形状完整性、周边环境四个维度；2) 通过情感分析和CLIP评分将VLM预测转化为数值分数；3) 夜间性能依托LiDAR反照率（retroreflectivity）经校准流程评估；4) 将日间与夜间评分整合为综合标志状况指数（SCI）。

Result: LLaVA和Qwen表现优于InternVL，在所有评估维度上双向余弦相似度达0.67-0.76。在462个经验证的交通标志中，68个因反照率性能不足被框架标记为需立即更换。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的日间-夜间综合评估框架有效实现了交通标志状况的自动化、低成本评估，可作为传统人工检测的可靠替代方案，尤其适用于资源有限的小型机构。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该框架可直接迁移至遥感领域的道路基础设施评估，具体方案：1) 将VLM+CLIP的日间评估方法用于遥感影像中道路标线、交通设施状况的自动解译；2) LiDAR反照率评估方法可扩展至遥感LiDAR数据（如机载LiDAR）对道路标志、路面标志的夜间性能进行大范围监测；3) 综合指标SCI可类比构建遥感尺度下的道路设施健康指数，实现从单点检测到区域级评估的升级。

Abstract (英文): Traffic signs are crucial components of road safety, serving as visual tools under all lighting conditions. The Manual on Uniform Traffic Control Devices (MUTCD) specifies daytime visual factors such as legibility and color contrast, and nighttime retroreflectivity requirements. Traditional assessment methods rely on manual inspections, which the Federal Highway Administration (FHWA) notes are subjective, labor-intensive and pose safety concerns, while retroreflectometers are expensive and unaffordable for smaller agencies. Most existing studies focus on either daytime factors or nighttime retroreflectivity but rarely integrate both aspects comprehensively. This study develops a novel framework that systematically evaluates traffic signs through integrated daytime-nighttime assessment. The methodology employs three fine-tuned Vision Language Models (VLMs) for daytime visual performance assessment across four key factors: legibility, color, surface and shape integrity, and surrounding environment conditions. VLM predictions are converted to numerical scores through sentiment analysis and Contrastive Language-Image Pre-Training (CLIP) scoring, while nighttime performance is assessed using LiDAR-derived retroreflectivity following established calibration procedures. The framework integrates these components into a comprehensive Sign Condition Index (SCI) for maintenance guidance. Evaluation results demonstrated that LLaVA and Qwen outperformed InternVL, achieving bidirectional cosine similarity scores of 0.67-0.76 across all factors. Among 462 validated traffic signs, 68 were flagged by the proposed framework as requiring immediate replacement due to inadequate retroreflectivity performance. This research provides a cost-effective alternative to traditional manual inspections for comprehensive traffic sign condition assessment.

### [90] [Mitigating Domain Shift in Conditioned Floor Plan Generation: Synthetic Pre-training for Data-Efficient Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06483)
*Matthieu Ospici,Arnaud Gueze,Luc Bourrat,Adrien Bernhardt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了条件化楼层平面生成模型在域迁移下的鲁棒性问题，发现现有模型在跨域时性能下降可达一个数量级。为此，提出一种大规模合成训练数据生成方法，通过强制物理约束（房间不重叠、门有效放置、图一致性）但牺牲建筑逼真度（不规则布局、几何扰动），在合成数据上预训练显著提升了零样本跨域性能，并在低数据微调场景下优于真实数据初始化基线高达40%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 楼层平面图在不同地区因建筑文化、空间约束和施工实践差异而呈现广泛分布偏移，而获取新标注数据集成本高昂且高度领域特定。然而，尚无先前工作研究过条件化楼层平面生成模型在这种域偏移下的鲁棒性，亟需评估并解决这一问题。

Method: 1) 评估两类生成范式（三类数据集：RPLAN、MagicPlan、Swiss Dwellings）的SOTA模型跨域性能；2) 提出一种程序化合成数据生成方法，强制执行物理约束（房间不重叠、门有效放置、图一致性），同时故意牺牲建筑逼真度（高度不规则空间排布、房间形状的激进几何扰动）；3) 在合成数据上预训练后微调或零样本迁移。

Result: 1) 现有模型对域高度敏感，跨域迁移时性能下降达一个数量级；2) 合成数据预训练显著提升零样本跨域性能，甚至超过MagicPlan域内训练效果；3) 合成数据作为微调初始化在低数据场景下比真实数据初始化基线提升高达40%。

Conclusion: 通过牺牲建筑逼真度但强制物理约束的合成数据预训练，能有效提升楼层平面生成模型的跨域鲁棒性和低数据适应能力，为减少对昂贵领域标注数据的依赖提供了可行方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样面临严重的域偏移问题（不同卫星传感器、地理区域、季节、分辨率），本文提出的合成数据预训练策略可直接迁移：1) 设计合成遥感数据集，强制执行物理约束（如地物空间一致性、拓扑关系），牺牲视觉逼真度但保留关键结构特征；2) 在合成数据上预训练，再少量真实遥感数据微调，可显著降低标注成本；3) 类似思路可应用于遥感语义分割、变化检测、建筑物提取等任务中的域泛化难题。

Abstract (英文): Robustness to domain shift is a key requirement for floor plan generative models to be applicable beyond the single dataset they were trained on, as floor plans vary widely across regions due to distinct architectural cultures, spatial constraints, and construction practices, while acquiring new annotated datasets remains costly and domain-specific. Yet, no prior work has studied this robustness in the context of conditioned floor plan generation. In this paper, we evaluate state-of-the-art models from two fundamentally different generative paradigms across three public datasets (RPLAN, MagicPlan and Swiss Dwellings) and show that they are highly sensitive to domain shift, with up to an order of magnitude performance degradation when transferred across domains. To mitigate this with minimal target-domain supervision, we introduce a procedural method to generate a large-scale synthetic training dataset that enforces strict physical constraints (non-overlapping rooms, valid door placement, graph consistency) while intentionally sacrificing architectural realism through highly irregular spatial arrangements and aggressive geometric perturbation of room shapes. We show that pre-training on this synthetic data considerably improves zero-shot cross-domain performance, outperforming in-domain training on MagicPlan. Furthermore, it provides a highly effective initialization for fine-tuning, accelerating target domain adaptation and outperforming real-world initialization baselines by up to 40% in a low-data regime.

### [91] [Point as Skeleton: Accumulated Point Cloud Enhanced Autoregressive Generation for Closed-Loop Autonomous Driving Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06516)
*Songbur Wong,Xiaosong Jia,Junqi You,Bo Zhang,Pei Xu,Renqiu Xia,Yuping Qiu,Shaofeng Zhang,Zelin Zhao,Xuechao Yan,Yuchen Zhou,Yurui Chen,Wen Guo,Hang Xu,Junchi Yan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Point as Skeleton 是一种生成式传感器模拟框架，通过自回归视频生成和点云骨架条件，实现闭环自动驾驶仿真，在保持视觉保真度的同时支持状态更新的闭环交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端自动驾驶仿真方法在闭环交互性（如CARLA）和真实世界视觉保真度（如nuScenes）之间存在权衡，缺乏既能实现闭环滚动又能保持高视觉真实感的仿真方案。

Method: 提出点云骨架（Point-cloud Skeleton）作为条件，解耦前景与背景资产并映射为相机视角的涂色点与模板深度条件；引入Reset-and-Roll策略，适配滚动扩散推理至仿真场景，防止未来条件潜状态跨仿真步骤提交；构建基于nuPlan的渲染级闭环生成评估接口。

Result: 在nuScenes和nuPlan数据集上的实验表明，Point as Skeleton在闭环滚动过程中提升了自回归生成质量，验证了其在视觉保真的闭环驾驶仿真中的潜力。

Conclusion: 点云骨架能够有效稳定自回归滚动过程中的误差累积，结合Reset-and-Roll策略可实现视觉保真且具备闭环交互能力的驾驶仿真。

Abstract (英文): Evaluating end-to-end autonomous driving (E2E-AD) remains challenging, as existing driving simulation methods often trade off closed-loop interactivity (e.g., CARLA) and real-world visual fidelity (e.g., nuScenes). We present \textbf{\emph{Point as Skeleton}}, a generative sensor simulation framework for state-updated autoregressive driving video generation, in which an autoregressive generator synthesizes visual observations from step-wise updated ego states, actor states, scene maps, and point-cloud skeleton conditions. To support closed-loop rollout, we introduce Reset-and-Roll, which adapts rolling diffusion inference to simulation by preventing future-conditioned latent states from being committed across simulation steps. To stabilize error accumulation during step-wise autoregressive rollout, we introduce point-cloud skeletons that decouple foreground and background assets and project them into camera-view painted-point and template-depth conditions, providing appearance and geometric cues. We further implement a nuPlan-based renderer-level closed-loop generative interface for evaluating generation under ego deviations from the original log. Experiments on nuScenes and nuPlan show that \textit{Point as Skeleton} improves autoregressive generation quality during closed-loop rollout, demonstrating its potential for visually faithful closed-loop driving simulation. The code is available at https://github.com/krauwu/point-as-skeleton.

### [92] [CAIRN: Cross-Room 3D Scene Understanding with Topology-Aware Large Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06534)
*He Liang,Chenyang Ma,Yiming Zhang,Sangyun Shin,Andrew Markham,Niki Trigoni,Yuhang He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CAIRN提出了一种拓扑感知的3D-LLM，能够理解多房间3D场景，通过层级注意力机制和图神经网络显式建模物体级关系和房间级连通性，在CAIRN-MR基准上大幅超越此前方法，同时在单房间任务上保持竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D-LLM仅能处理简化的单房间3D场景，无法推理真实家庭环境中包含多互通房间和多样物体类别的复杂场景，缺乏对场景拓扑结构的显式建模能力。

Method: 1) 利用图神经网络丰富物体token的房间局部关系上下文；2) 引入可学习的房间token实现房间级抽象；3) 设计层级注意力掩码结合几何偏置，根据场景拓扑结构路由信息，使transformer注意力与场景层级对齐。

Result: CAIRN在CAIRN-MR基准的所有任务（定位、描述、4个QA任务）上大幅超越此前3D-LLM，同时在5个单房间基准上保持竞争力。

Conclusion: 显式建模场景拓扑结构（物体关系与房间连通性）是提升3D-LLM多房间场景理解能力的关键，所提层级注意力机制可有效将先验几何结构融入Transformer。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。1) 将房间token替换为地块/建筑区域token，GNN建模相邻地块间的空间拓扑关系（如道路连通性、缓冲区重叠）；2) 层级注意力掩码可应用于遥感图像的瓦片级-场景级-地物级多粒度理解，例如对遥感大图中的建筑群进行跨瓦片关系推理；3) 几何偏置可引入地理空间坐标约束，如地理邻居关系、方位角等先验知识；4) 多房间QA任务可类比为多景遥感图像的跨场景问答（如"A区域与B区域之间的植被变化是什么"）。

Abstract (英文): Existing 3D scene-grounded Large Language Models (3D-LLMs) focus on answering questions grounded in simplified single-room 3D scenes, lacking the ability to reason over real-world household environments containing multiple interconnected rooms and diverse object categories. We introduce CAIRN, a topology-aware 3D-LLM for multi-room 3D scene understanding. CAIRN aligns transformer attention with scene hierarchy, giving the model explicit awareness of object-level relations and room-level connectivity. It enriches object tokens with room-local relational context via a graph neural network, introduces learned room tokens for room-level abstraction, and applies a hierarchical attention mask with geometric bias to route information according to scene topology. CAIRN is developed on CAIRN-MR, a benchmark we introduce on HM3D for multi-room 3D scene understanding, covering grounding, captioning, and four question-answering tasks that progressively evaluate from intra-room perception to cross-room reasoning. Experiments show that CAIRN outperforms prior 3D-LLMs by a large margin across all CAIRN-MR tasks while remaining competitive on five single-room benchmarks.

</details>

Abstract (英文): Deep learning-based computer-aided diagnosis (CAD) systems have shown strong performance in breast cancer diagnosis, particularly for classification tasks in mammography. In this work, we proposed a calcification classification framework to improve malignant versus benign breast disease classification across multi-site mammography datasets. ### [94] [MonoIR-RS: Infrared Remote Sensing Vision-Language Learning with CLIP and VLM Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06552)
*Jiaju Han,Ma Yaqi,Yahui Chai,Xuemeng Sun,Xin Li,Qike Zhang,Yingying Zhao,Xiang Chen,Luwei Yang,Chengyin Hu,Jiahuan Long*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MonoIR-RS是一个大规模红外遥感视觉-语言数据集和基准，通过红外感知数据构建、CLIP对比适应和VLM指令微调，将红外遥感证据与语言对齐。实验表明，红外感知适应使CLIP平均召回率提升12.8点，VLM字幕红外线索覆盖率达100%，RGB颜色泄漏降至接近零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遥感视觉-语言资源和模型主要聚焦可见光波段，红外遥感视觉-语言理解领域尚未被充分探索。红外图像能捕捉RGB图像中不可见的强度结构、目标-背景对比度和光照不变线索，但缺乏相应的数据集和模型。

Method: 基于FusionRS同源数据池和划分，保留红外图像作为模型可见模态，构建60万张合成红外图像和59,032条红外感知字幕记录。采用CLIP风格对比适应和VLM指令微调，字幕围绕灰度结构和红外风格对比重写而非RGB外观。微调5个CLIP骨干和6个VLM骨干，并与零样本行为进行校准。

Result: 合成红外图像在AVIID基准上比灰度转换更接近真实热成像。红外感知适应使CLIP平均召回率提升12.8点，VLM字幕红外线索覆盖率达100%，残差RGB颜色泄漏降至接近零。

Conclusion: 通过将红外模态从RGB-IR双模态学习中分离出来，MonoIR-RS为将红外遥感证据与语言对齐提供了一个可控、可复现的测试平台。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。作为纯红外遥感视觉-语言论文，改进方向包括：1) 引入多光谱/高光谱波段以丰富红外特征表示；2) 探索时空融合策略，结合时序红外影像增强动态目标理解；3) 扩展至多任务学习框架，如同时进行红外目标检测和语义描述；4) 引入物理红外辐射特性建模，提升合成图像物理真实性；5) 探索更高效的跨模态对齐策略，如对比学习与生成式方法的混合。

Abstract (英文): Infrared remote-sensing imagery captures intensity structure, object-background contrast, and illumination-invariant cues often invisible in RGB imagery. Yet, most remote-sensing vision-language resources and models focus on visible-band semantics, leaving infrared vision-language understanding underexplored. We introduce MonoIR-RS, a large-scale infrared remote-sensing vision-language dataset and benchmark that couples IR-aware data construction with CLIP-style contrastive adaptation and VLM instruction tuning. Built from the same source pool and split as FusionRS, MonoIR-RS retains the infrared image as the model-facing modality, yielding 600,000 synthesized infrared images and 59,032 retained IR-aware caption records. The model experiments use this retained language-supervision subset, whose captions rewrite supervision around grayscale structure and infrared-style contrast instead of RGB appearance. We show that the synthesized infrared imagery is markedly closer to real thermal imagery than a grayscale conversion on the AVIID benchmark. We fine-tune five CLIP backbones and six VLM backbones, and calibrate them against zero-shot behavior: IR-aware adaptation lifts CLIP mean recall by up to 12.8 points and drives VLM captioning IR-cue coverage to 100% while reducing residual RGB-color leakage to near zero. By isolating the infrared modality from RGB-IR dual-modal learning, MonoIR-RS offers a controlled, reproducible testbed for aligning infrared remote-sensing evidence with language.

### [95] [From RGB Generation to Dense Field Readout: Pixel-Space Dense Prediction with Text-to-Image Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06553)
*Zanyi Wang,Xin Lin,Haodong Li,Dengyang Jiang,Yijiang Li,Pengtao Xie*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出ReChannel，通过直接利用预训练DiT的patch-to-token-to-patch网格结构，用共享线性头将每个token映射为任务原生量（如深度、法线等）的像素级patch，避免了传统方法将密集预测任务重构为RGB生成任务所带来的额外开销。在6个密集预测任务上取得SOTA或竞争性结果，且比同类方法快2.48倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将密集预测任务（如深度估计、抠图等）转化为目标生成问题，即把标注编码到RGB训练的VAE潜空间再解码回图像。这种做法继承了生成模型的输出接口，但密集预测实际只需要像素正确的任务原生场，而非新的RGB内容。作者认为预训练DiT已经通过patch-to-token-to-patch网格组织输入，每个token天然对应一个固定输出patch，可以直接在其中承载任务原生量，无需经过RGB解码。

Method: ReChannel方法：1) 保留VAE编码器用于DiT输入分布；2) 丢弃目标侧解码器；3) 冻结DiT主干，引入任务LoRA进行适配；4) 每个token通过一个共享的token局部线性头（约33K参数，无空间混合）映射到其对应的p×p×K_t像素空间patch。基于FLUX-Klein模型，在6个密集预测任务上评估。

Result: 在trimap-free抠图、KITTI深度估计和指代分割上取得SOTA；在法线估计、显著性检测和姿态估计上保持竞争力。在匹配的4B参数设置下，比编辑+潜解码方案更准确且快2.48倍。

Conclusion: 密集感知任务可以从生成式预训练中受益，但无需继承其输出接口。ReChannel表明，通过直接利用DiT的token-patch对应关系，可以用极简的线性头实现高效且精准的密集预测。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域常见密集预测任务（如DSM深度估计、语义分割、建筑物提取、道路提取等）可直接套用ReChannel框架。具体方案：1) 使用遥感预训练DiT（如SatMAE风格的变体）替换FLUX-Klein；2) 对遥感多光谱/高光谱数据，调整VAE编码器输入通道数，并相应修改token-local线性头的输出通道K_t；3) 遥感任务中的大尺度变化问题可通过多尺度patch尺寸或金字塔token策略增强；4) 对于遥感特有的边界精细任务（如建筑物轮廓提取），可在共享线性头后加轻量级边界细化模块。

Abstract (英文): Large-scale text-to-image models are attractive backbones for dense prediction because RGB generation pretraining learns rich semantic, structural, and geometric priors. Existing generative and editing approaches reuse these priors by casting dense prediction as target generation: annotations such as depth, normals, alpha mattes, masks, and heatmaps are encoded into an RGB-trained VAE latent space and decoded back as image-like targets. We argue this inherits more of the generative output interface than dense prediction requires: unlike RGB synthesis, dense prediction asks for pixel-correct, task-native fields on the same image plane, not new RGB content to be rendered. Our key observation is that a pretrained DiT already organizes RGB inputs through a patch-to-token-to-patch lattice on the image plane, so each token indexes a fixed output patch whose channels can carry task-native quantities instead of RGB appearance. We instantiate this as ReChannel: we keep the VAE encoder for the DiT's input distribution but drop the target-side decoder, adapt the frozen DiT with task LoRA, and map each token to its p x p x K_t pixel-space patch through a shared token-local linear head--about 33K parameters, no spatial mixing. Using FLUX-Klein, we evaluate on six dense prediction tasks and over a dozen benchmarks. This minimal interface sets new state-of-the-art on trimap-free matting, KITTI depth, and referring segmentation, and stays competitive on normals, saliency, and pose. In a matched 4B setting it is more accurate and 2.48x faster than an edit-plus-latent-decode counterpart--dense perception can benefit from generative pretraining without inheriting its output interface.

</details>


### [96] [ProxyPose: 6-DoF Pose Tracking via Video-to-Video Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06555)
*Ruihang Zhang,Felix Taubner,Pooja Ravi,Kiriakos N. Kutulakos,David B. Lindell*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ProxyPose将6-DoF位姿跟踪重新建模为视频到视频的翻译问题，仅需单目视频和首帧一个标记像素，通过微调的视频扩散模型生成已知几何和外观的代理视频（彩色多面体），再通过经典位姿估计方法恢复完整6-DoF轨迹，在无需3D模型、深度图等额外输入的情况下达到SOTA精度，并拓展到面部跟踪、相机位姿估计等场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有6-DoF位姿跟踪方法需要3D模型、深度图、物体掩码等额外输入，且难以处理无纹理、透明、反光或可变形表面，作者希望消除这些限制，仅利用视频本身实现鲁棒的位姿跟踪。

Method: 将位姿跟踪转化为视频到视频的翻译：输入单目视频和首帧一个标记像素，微调视频扩散模型生成一个彩色多面体的代理视频，该代理与标记像素处的局部表面区域经历相同的刚体运动；由于代理的几何和外观已知，通过经典位姿估计方法即可恢复6-DoF轨迹。

Result: 在不需要竞争方法所需的额外输入条件下，ProxyPose实现了SOTA的6-DoF位姿跟踪精度；仅使用合成数据微调视频模型即达到此效果；方法可扩展到面部跟踪、相机位姿估计以及超出现有方法能力的复杂野外场景。

Conclusion: ProxyPose利用大规模视频预训练将位姿跟踪中最困难的部分（处理挑战性材质、遮挡和变形）吸收到翻译步骤中，在像素级别操作，无需任何关于物体身份、边界或全局刚性的假设，为6-DoF跟踪提供了新的范式。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中的平台（如无人机、卫星）位姿估计和地面目标跟踪常面临纹理匮乏、光照变化剧烈等问题。具体方案：（1）将ProxyPose应用于无人机视频中的地面目标6-DoF跟踪，利用其无需纹理的特性处理遥感图像中常见的弱纹理目标；（2）将代理视频概念引入遥感相机自标定，通过生成已知几何的代理帧序列估计相机运动轨迹；（3）针对遥感视频中云层遮挡、阴影变化等挑战，ProxyPose的像素级操作和预训练扩散模型的鲁棒性可提供更稳定的跟踪。主要挑战在于遥感场景的尺度变化大和全局运动与局部运动耦合问题，需要对代理多面体的尺度进行自适应调整。

Abstract (英文): Tracking the six-degree-of-freedom (6-DoF) pose of objects and surfaces from monocular video is a long-standing problem in computer vision. To tackle this problem, existing methods require inputs beyond the video itself-such as 3D models, depth maps, object masks, or task-specific learned features-and they struggle with textureless, transparent, reflective, or deformable surfaces. Here, we introduce ProxyPose, which recasts 6-DoF pose tracking as video-to-video translation. Given only a video and a single marked pixel in the first frame, a fine-tuned video diffusion model translates the input into a proxy video-a synthetic video depicting a colored polyhedron undergoing the same local rigid-body motion as the surface region at the marked pixel. Because the proxy's geometry and appearance are known by construction, recovering its full 6-DoF trajectory reduces to classical pose estimation with off-the-shelf solvers. This formulation leverages large-scale video pre-training to absorb the hardest aspects of pose tracking-handling challenging materials, occlusions, and deformations-into the translation step, while operating at the pixel level with no assumptions about object identity, boundaries, or global rigidity. ProxyPose achieves state-of-the-art 6-DoF pose tracking accuracy without the additional inputs required by competing methods and after fine-tuning the video model only on synthetic data. We further demonstrate that ProxyPose extends to face tracking, camera pose estimation, and challenging in-the-wild scenes that are beyond the reach of existing approaches. Project page: https://ruihangzhang97.github.io/proxypose/.

</details>


### [97] [Vision as Unified Multimodal Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06560)
*Xiaoyang Han,Jianhua Li,Kewang Deng,Zukai Chen,Xuanke Shi,Sihan Wang,Boxuan Li,Linyan Wang,Siyi Xie,Xin You,Jinsheng Quan,Zhongang Cai,Haiwen Diao,Ziwei Liu,Lei Yang,Dahua Lin,Quan Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出将计算机视觉统一表述为多模态生成任务，通过一个统一的文本和图像生成空间处理异构视觉任务，无需特定任务架构。基于此范式训练的SenseNova-Vision模型在检测、分割、深度估计等多种视觉任务上达到与专业系统相当的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前计算机视觉任务通常需要为不同任务设计专用架构和预测头，缺乏统一的通用解决方案。作者希望将视觉任务统一到多模态生成框架中，使一个通用模型能够处理所有视觉任务，无需任务特定的架构修改。

Method: 将多种视觉任务表述为统一的多模态生成问题：文本输出用于符号结果，图像输出用于密集空间预测，图文混合输出用于组合任务。构建大规模SenseNova-Vision语料库，将各类视觉标注转换为指令-响应示例。基于预训练的统一多模态模型进行训练，使用该语料库为主并结合辅助多模态数据，无需任务特定预测头或架构修改。

Result: 单个统一模型在结构化视觉理解、密集几何预测、分割和多视图视觉几何等多个任务上，达到了与领先任务专用系统相匹配的性能。

Conclusion: 统一多模态生成是一种可扩展的路线，能够将计算机视觉能力整合到通用基础模型中。模型和语料库已公开。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域包含大量异构视觉任务（目标检测、分割、深度估计、三维重建等），该统一生成范式可天然适配：1) 将遥感图像中地物检测、变化检测等任务统一为文本+图像生成，避免为每个任务设计独立模型；2) 利用视觉提示灵活指定遥感图像中的感兴趣区域或视角；3) 多模态输出可同时生成地物分类标签（文本）和语义分割图（图像），满足遥感综合解译需求；4) 该方法无需任务特定架构的特性，尤其适合遥感数据标注碎片化、任务类型多样的场景。建议改进：在训练语料中增加遥感专用标注数据（如多光谱、SAR图像标注），并加入地理空间坐标提示机制。

Abstract (英文): We formulate computer vision as unified multimodal generation, where heterogeneous visual tasks are expressed in the native text and image generation spaces of a unified multimodal model, without task-specific architectures. Under this formulation, SenseNova-Vision uses natural-language instructions and optional visual prompts to specify tasks, target regions or views, and decoding conventions, and generates responses as text for symbolic outputs, images for dense spatial predictions, or mixed text-and-image outputs for compositional tasks. To support large-scale training, we convert diverse computer vision annotations into instruction-response examples compatible with these generation spaces, resulting in the SenseNova-Vision Corpus, a computer-vision instruction-response corpus spanning text, image, and mixed targets. Starting from an off-the-shelf pretrained unified multimodal model, SenseNova-Vision is trained primarily on this corpus, with auxiliary multimodal data used as a capability-preserving mixture, and requires no task-specific prediction heads or architectural modifications. The resulting model covers a broad range of vision tasks, including detection, OCR, keypoint estimation, segmentation, depth estimation, surface normal prediction, point maps, and camera pose estimation, while supporting language-defined variants that combine category, color, region, and other visual cues. Experiments show that a single unified model can match leading task-specialized systems across structured visual understanding, dense geometric prediction, segmentation, and multi-view visual geometry. These results suggest unified multimodal generation as a scalable route for integrating computer vision capabilities into general-purpose foundation models. The model and corpus are publicly available.

</details>

### [98] [UAV-satellite synergies for crop monitoring: current landscape, challenges, and future directions](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.isprsjprs.2026.06.038)
*Jiale Jiang,Qianyi Zhang,Kasper Johansen,Tao Cheng,Xia Yao,Qi Su,Matthew F. McCabe,Yan Zhu,Wenping Yuan*

Main category: ISPRS J P&RS

TL;DR: 未提供摘要，无法生成TL;DR总结。


<details>

### [103] [PoseIDON: 6DoF pose estimation with foundation model features for marine sediment burial mapping](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.isprsjprs.2026.06.032)
*Jerry Yan,Chinmay Talegaonkar,Nicholas Antipa,Eric Terrill,Sophia Merrifield*

Main category: ISPRS J P&RS

TL;DR: PoseIDON是一种结合深度基础模型特征与多视图摄影测量的计算机视觉流程，可从ROV视频中估计海底人造物体的6自由度姿态及周围海床方向，通过CAD模型与观测图像的对齐来推断掩埋深度。在圣佩德罗盆地历史海洋倾倒场的54个物体（包括桶和弹药）上验证，平均掩埋深度误差约10厘米，能反映沉积物输运过程的空间掩埋模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海底人造物体的掩埋状态对评估生态风险、污染物迁移以及危险材料（如弹药）的回收或缓解策略至关重要，但现有遥感图像因部分遮挡、能见度差和物体退化而难以准确估计掩埋深度。

Method: 提出PoseIDON计算机视觉流程：1) 利用深度基础模型特征结合多视图摄影测量，从ROV视频中估计物体的6自由度位姿及周围海床方向；2) 通过将CAD模型与观测图像对齐，拟合海床局部平面近似，进而推断掩埋深度。

Result: 在圣佩德罗盆地历史海洋倾倒场的54个物体（桶和弹药）上验证，平均掩埋深度误差约10厘米，并能解析反映底层沉积物输运过程的空间掩埋模式。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了可扩展、非侵入式的海底掩埋测绘，为受污染场地的环境评估提供了有效支持。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该方法的遥感交叉方案：1) 将PoseIDON的深度基础模型特征迁移至卫星或航空遥感影像中的近岸/浅海人工目标（如沉船、管道）掩埋状态估计，结合多时相卫星影像代替ROV视频进行多视图重建；2) 将局部海床平面拟合推广为基于遥感水深数据（如多光谱反演或LiDAR测深）的海底地形约束，提升掩埋深度估计的绝对精度；3) 融合SAR影像对海底目标的散射特征，增强在低能见度或浑浊水体环境下的检测与位姿估计鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): The burial state of anthropogenic objects on the seafloor provides insight into localized sedimentation dynamics and is also critical for assessing ecological risks, potential pollutant transport, and the viability of recovery or mitigation strategies for hazardous materials such as munitions. Accurate burial depth estimation from remote imagery remains difficult due to partial occlusion, poor visibility, and object degradation. This work introduces a computer vision pipeline, called PoseIDON, which combines deep foundation model features with multiview photogrammetry to estimate six degrees of freedom object pose and the orientation of the surrounding seafloor from ROV video. Burial depth is inferred by aligning CAD models of the objects with observed imagery and fitting a local planar approximation of the seafloor. The method is validated using footage of 54 objects, including barrels and munitions, recorded at a historic ocean dumpsite in the San Pedro Basin. The model achieves a mean burial depth error of approximately 10 cm and resolves spatial burial patterns that reflect underlying sediment transport processes. This approach enables scalable, non-invasive mapping of seafloor burial and supports environmental assessment at contaminated sites.

</details>
