### [104] [Prompt-to-Paper: Agentic AI System for Bioinformatics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05456)
*Ramsha Kamran,Maheera Amjad,Zartasha Mustansar,Arsalan Shaukat,Salma Sherbaz,Muhammad U. S. Khan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Prompt-to-Paper多智能体框架，通过确定性检索增强生成、自主代码执行实验和八维质量评分器，实现端到端的可验证、可复现的学术论文自动生成，在五个生物信息学案例中平均质量提升17.96分，人工评分7.0/10，单篇成本约0.31美元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型生成的论文存在三个关键缺陷：生成的声明无法确定性追溯到可验证文献、实验结果常被编造而非真实执行、缺乏标准化的多维度评估框架来衡量AI生成论文是否达到真实出版所需的质量和严谨性。

Method: 提出三方面集成创新：1) 确定性检索增强生成管线，包含分节感知相关性评分和雪球引用扩展，每项声明可追溯至60-100篇论文的可验证语料库；2) 自主编码代理执行真实计算生物学实验，用真实数值结果替代合成输出；3) 八维自动质量评分器，以已发表论文的近似参考统计为基准并加入显式幻觉惩罚。质量驱动的改进循环使用上下文丰富的修订器，每次迭代路由至三种研究者动作之一，每十次迭代触发深度研究循环重新执行实验并从更强输出重新生成稿件。

Result: 在五个生物信息学案例上验证，所有案例编译出提交格式的PDF且零越界引用。改进循环使稿件质量在0-100分制上平均提升17.96分（最高26.04分）。人工评审员对五篇稿件的平均评分为7.0/10。每篇论文的生产成本约为0.31美元。

Conclusion: Prompt-to-Paper框架有效解决了AI生成论文的可验证性、可复现性和质量评估标准化问题，以极低成本生成达到人工评审可接受水平的完整学术论文。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1) 将确定性RAG管线中的文献语料库替换为遥感领域数据集（如Landsat、Sentinel影像及相关期刊论文），确保生成论文中的地理空间分析声明有据可查；2) 自主编码代理可适配执行遥感图像处理实验（如分类精度评估、变化检测、辐射定标），替代合成结果；3) 八维质量评分器需调整基准参考统计量（如遥感领域常用的OA、Kappa系数、F1分数等标准），并增加对空间分辨率、时间一致性等遥感特有指标的评估维度。

Abstract (英文): While recent advances in large language models have enabled end-to-end automated manuscript generation, existing systems suffer from three critical deficiencies: (i) generated claims are not deterministically grounded in verifiable literature, (ii) experimental results are frequently fabricated rather than executed, and (iii) there exists no standardized, multi-dimensional framework to assess whether AI-generated manuscripts meet the quality and rigor required for real-world publication. We present Prompt-to-Paper, a multi-agent framework that directly addresses this evaluation gap through three integrated innovations. First, a deterministic retrieval-augmented generation pipeline with section-aware relevance scoring and snowball citation expansion grounds every claim in a verifiable corpus of 60--100 papers. Second, an autonomous coding agent executes real computational biology experiments replacing synthetic outputs with genuine numerical results. Third, an eight-dimensional automated quality scorer, benchmarked with approximate reference statistics from published papers and augmented with explicit hallucination penalties, provides standardized, reproducible quality assessments. The quality-driven improvement loop uses a context-rich reviser that routes each iteration to one of three researcher actions and fires a deep research cycle every ten iterations to re-run experiments and re-manuscript from stronger outputs. We validate the system on five bioinformatics case studies; all five cases compiled submission-formatted PDFs with zero out-of-range citations. The improvement loop raises manuscript quality by an average of +17.96 points on a 0--100 scale (maximum +26.04. As partial external checks, a human reviewer scored the five manuscripts at an average of 7.0 out of 10. Complete manuscripts are produced at approximately 0.31 USD per paper.

</details>


### [105] [From Graphs to Gradients: Physics-Inspired Structural Attribution for Cyber-Physical IoT Systems and Beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05563)
*Spyridon Evangelatos,Christos Diou,Georgios Th. Papadopoulos,Evangelos Markakis,Panagiotis Sarigiannidis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于统计力学的无向能量表示框架，用于对大规模混合型网络物理物联网系统进行依赖感知的因果归因解释，无需恢复有向因果图，在工业物联网测试平台上表现出比现有图方法更高的归因精度、鲁棒性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统可解释AI方法主要依赖输入输出相关性，在高风险领域中难以提供稳健的因果解释；而恢复有向因果结构在大规模、混合型、带反馈环和部分可观测的网络物理系统中不切实际，亟需一种无需显式因果图即可实现依赖感知归因的可解释方法。

Method: 借鉴统计力学中的能量模型，将系统变量间的依赖关系建模为无向能量基表示；通过分析能量景观的变化来量化单个组件对系统行为的影响，实现归因；支持混合连续/离散变量，可推理扰动在异质交互间的传播效应。

Result: 在包含混合连续和离散变量的工业物联网测试平台仿真中，该方法在归因准确率、鲁棒性和可扩展性方面均优于现有最先进的图基方法。

Conclusion: 该框架虽不旨在完全恢复生成性动力学，但能提供有价值的依赖感知解释，支持人工理解及下游预测/诊断任务；虽在工业物联网安全领域验证，但适用于其他高维网络物理和社会技术系统。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该能量基无向依赖归因框架可直接迁移至遥感领域的地表参数间复杂依赖分析（如植被指数、地表温度、土壤湿度等连续变量与土地利用类型等离散变量的混合系统）。具体方案：(1) 用于遥感异常检测（如森林火灾、洪涝前的异常信号），通过能量景观变化定位异常驱动因子；(2) 对遥感产品间的交叉影响（如气溶胶对地表温度的影响）进行扰动归因，无需构建完整因果图；(3) 结合时序遥感数据，分析多变量间的依赖变化模式，提升遥感反演模型的解释性和鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Interpretable explanation methods in Artificial Intelligence aim to uncover the underlying causes and their effects, enabling a deeper understanding of why a system behaves in a certain way under different inputs. Unlike traditional explainability methods, which mainly highlight correlations between input and output variables, causal explanation focuses on interventional questions. By doing so, it provides more robust insights, helping users understand automated decisions, especially in high-risk domains. Recovering an explicit directed causal structure, however, is often impractical in large-scale, hybrid cyber-physical systems with feedback loops and partial observability. This paper introduces a novel framework inspired by statistical mechanics that instead models variable dependencies through an undirected, energy-based representation of cyber-physical IoT systems. Our approach enables rigorous dependency-aware attribution by analysing how variations in the energy landscape reflect the influence of individual components, without recovering a directed causal graph. It also supports reasoning about perturbation effects across hybrid interactions, providing reliable explanations of abnormal behaviours. We empirically examined our framework through simulations on an industrial IoT testbed with hybrid continuous and discrete variables, demonstrating higher attribution accuracy, improved robustness and better scalability than state-of-the-art graph-based approaches. While the attributions are not intended to fully recover the system's generative dynamics, they provide valuable, dependency-aware explanations supporting both human interpretation and downstream predictive and diagnostic tasks. Although demonstrated in industrial IoT security, our framework also applies to other high-dimensional cyber-physical and socio-technical systems requiring principled, structural explanations.

</details>


### [106] [CSTutorBench: Benchmarking Small Language Models as Tutors for Block-Based Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05571)
*H. Chad Lane,Bryson Kageler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了CSTutorBench，一个针对块式编程（VEX VR环境）中语言模型作为AI导师的评估基准。该基准包含17个基于场景的问题，并使用教学法评分标准进行评估。初步测试了11个模型（4B-120B参数），发现模型在词汇和语气等表层标准上表现良好，但在避免答案泄露、参与学生调试历史等深层教学行为上表现不佳，且教学能力与参数量相关性较弱，更依赖于模型家族和指令微调方法。针对性提示修订可提升大部分模型得分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型被越来越多地探索作为AI导师，但在K-12教育场景中部署存在隐私、成本和依赖专有模型等问题。小语言模型（SLM）是有前景的替代方案，但在特定教育场景（如块式编程）中选择合适模型仍然困难，因为目标领域在模型训练数据中几乎不存在。因此需要开发一个情境特定的、教学法驱动的评估基准来指导模型选择。

Method: 构建CSTutorBench基准，包含17个VEX VR块式编程环境中的场景化问答问题，并基于成熟的教学和反馈研究设计教学法评分标准。采用人类在环的LLM-as-judge（大语言模型作为评判者）流水线进行评估。对11个模型（4B-120B参数范围）进行测试，并基于教育提示工程研究进行针对性提示修订。

Result: 模型在词汇和语气等表层标准上表现良好，但在避免答案泄露和参与学生调试历史等深层教学行为上表现不佳。模型家族和指令微调方法比参数量更能预测教学能力（但样本量有限）。针对性提示修订使11个模型中的10个得分提升。

Conclusion: 情境特定且基于教学法的基准对于SLM在教育部署中的选择具有重要价值，参数量并不是教学能力的首要决定因素，提示工程设计可显著提升模型教学表现。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该论文提出的领域特定教学评估方法论可有效迁移至遥感教育场景。具体方案：(1) 构建基于遥感影像解译（如地物分类、变化检测）的场景化教学基准，覆盖从基本像素识别到复杂场景分析的渐进式问题；(2) 设计遥感领域教学评分标准，重点关注是否泄露答案、能否引导学生理解遥感原理（如光谱特性、空间分辨率概念）；(3) 采用类似LLM-as-judge流水线评估SLM在遥感教学中的表现；(4) 针对遥感学科特有的技术术语（如NDVI、监督分类）和典型错误（如混合像元误判）设计提示优化策略，提升AI导师在遥感领域的教学效果。

Abstract (英文): Large language models are increasingly explored as AI tutors, yet deploying them in K-12 settings raises concerns around privacy, cost, and reliance on proprietary models. Small language models (SLMs) offer a promising alternative, but selecting the right model for a specific educational context remains difficult, particularly when the target domain, such as block-based programming, is largely absent from model training data. We introduce CSTutorBench, a benchmark for evaluating language models as CS tutors in VEX VR, a block-based robotics environment. The benchmark comprises 17 scenario-based questions scored against a pedagogical rubric grounded in established tutoring and feedback research, with a human-in-the-loop LLM-as-judge pipeline for evaluation. Preliminary findings across 11 models (4B-120B parameters) reveal that models perform well on surface-level criteria such as vocabulary and tone but struggle with deeper pedagogical behaviors, particularly avoiding answer leakage and engaging with student debugging histories. In our sample, model family and instruction-tuning approach appear to be better predictors of tutoring quality than parameter count alone, though the small number of models limits the strength of this conclusion. A targeted prompt revision grounded in recent educational prompt engineering research improved scores for 10 of 11 models. These results underscore the value of context-specific, pedagogically grounded benchmarks for SLM selection in educational deployment.

</details>


### [107] [Foundation Models for Automatic CAD Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05573)
*J de Curtò,Victoria Guillén,I. de Zarzà*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了LLMForge框架，用于从自然语言描述自动生成机械零件的参数化3D CAD设计。该框架结合JSON-schema验证、解析特征评分、网格合成和多轮迭代优化，并在两种评论机制（基于光线追踪的IterTracer和基于VLM的IterVision）下进行了评估。在包含97个工程问题的基准测试中，7个基础模型的表现表明，紧凑的指令调优模型可以达到与大型模型相当的性能，而VLM评论机制在旋转对称几何体上存在挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型和视觉语言模型能够从自然语言生成参数化3D设计，但缺乏系统性的评估框架和基准，特别是针对机械零件CAD生成的自动化评估方法尚未成熟。本文旨在填补这一空白，提供统一的评估流程和基准，并探索不同评论机制对生成质量的影响。

Method: 提出了LLMForge多模型文本到CAD框架，包含JSON-schema验证、解析特征评分、网格合成和多轮迭代优化。设计了两种评论机制：IterTracer使用Phong着色光线追踪渲染器结合解析视觉指标（轮廓IoU、孔洞可见性、边缘间隙、宽高比一致性）进行轻量级几何感知反馈；IterVision用VLM语义评论器（Qwen2.5-VL-72B）替代解析评分器，通过链式思维视觉推理评估空间一致性和设计意图。在97个工程问题基准上测试了7个基础模型。

Result: 在IterTracer下，前四名模型形成紧密聚类（总体均值在[0.885, 0.890]），网格生成成功率达98.97%，表明紧凑指令调优模型可匹配更大系统。IterVision下，领先模型实现了100%水密网格生成，但在旋转对称几何体（如圆柱体）上视觉评分与语义评分分歧最大。

Conclusion: 紧凑指令调优模型在CAD生成任务上可以达到与大型模型相当的性能；VLM评论机制提高了网格质量但暴露出对旋转对称几何体的系统性困难；论文讨论了基准设计、失败模式、CAD导向提示策略以及对工业自动化和可扩展机械设计的启示。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。本文的LLMForge框架可直接迁移至遥感领域的3D场景理解与重建任务：1）利用文本到CAD的流水线，可将遥感影像中的地物（建筑物、基础设施）描述自动转化为参数化3D模型；2）IterTracer的解析视觉指标（轮廓IoU等）适用于评估遥感分割与重建精度；3）IterVision的VLM链式思维推理可用于遥感图像中复杂场景的空间关系推理；4）多轮迭代优化策略可应用于遥感变化检测中的渐进式精化。需改进之处：遥感数据通常为多光谱/高光谱影像，需扩展视觉编码器以处理非RGB通道；遥感场景的几何拓扑更为复杂，需增强对非刚体和自然地形建模能力。

Abstract (英文): Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision-Language Models (VLMs) enable the automatic generation of parametric 3D designs from natural-language specifications. This chapter presents an empirical study of foundation models for automatic Computer-Aided Design (CAD) generation of mechanical parts, using a unified evaluation pipeline and a curated benchmark of 97 engineering design problems. We introduce LLMForge, a multi-model text-to-CAD framework integrating JSON-schema validation, analytic feature scoring, mesh synthesis, and multi-round iterative refinement, studied under two critique regimes. IterTracer uses a Phong-shaded ray-trace renderer with analytic visual metrics (silhouette IoU, hole visibility, edge clearance, aspect-ratio conformance) for lightweight geometry-aware feedback across rounds. IterVision replaces the analytic scorer with a VLM semantic critic (Qwen2.5-VL-72B) that evaluates rendered views via chain-of-thought visual reasoning, assessing spatial coherence and design intent. On a benchmark spanning four canonical geometry families (plates with holes and bolt circles, multi-feature boxes, flanged cylinders, and L-brackets), we evaluate seven foundation models: DeepSeek-V3.2, Qwen3-235B-A22B, Llama-3.3-70B, Gemma-3-27B, GLM-4.5, MiniMax-M2.1, and INTELLECT. Under IterTracer, the four highest-ranked models form a tight cluster (overall mean in [0.885, 0.890]) with 98.97% mesh success, showing that compact instruction-tuned models can match substantially larger systems. VLM-based critique in IterVision yields 100% watertight mesh generation on the leading model while surfacing systematic difficulty on rotationally symmetric geometries such as cylinders, where visual and semantic scoring diverge most. We discuss benchmark design, failure modes, CAD-oriented prompting, and implications for industrial workflows and scalable automated mechanical design.

### [108] [Narrative World Model: Narratology-Grounded Writer Memory for Long-Form Fiction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05577)
*Mohammad Saifullah,Thomas Kornmaier,Taaha Kazi,Vasu Sharma,Aditya Sanjiv Kanade,Aanand Kumar Yadav*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出叙事世界模型（NWM），一种面向长篇小说作者的记忆系统，通过叙事学驱动的类型化时序状态图与查询条件混合检索，显著优于现有智能体记忆框架在多跳叙事问答上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长篇小说写作需要记忆回答关于故事状态演变的多跳问题（如谁何时知道某个秘密、事件是否发生在揭示它的叙述之前等），而通用检索和智能体记忆系统仅表示实体和事实，缺乏叙事学结构，无法提供正确证据。

Method: 构建叙事世界模型（NWM），核心组件包括：(1) 叙事学驱动的类型化时序状态图，编码人物知识、事件时间关系等叙事结构；(2) 查询条件混合检索机制。评估时通过固定Opus 4.8阅读器读取系统输出的章节级证据，在可复现公共语料库和验证过的多跳基准上进行测试。

Result: NWM在两个语料库上的多跳叙事问答任务中显著且实质性地超越最强现有基线Graphiti/Zep，远超GraphRAG和平面检索。该优势源于其叙事学驱动的结构和查询条件检索，而非抽取质量或图规模。

Conclusion: 叙事学驱动的结构化记忆表示对于长篇小说写作中的多跳叙事问答任务至关重要，NWM的表示优势在控制变量实验中得到验证。

Abstract (英文): Long-form fiction writers need memory that answers multi-hop questions about evolving story state: who knows a secret and when they learned it, whether an event preceded the narration that revealed it, whether a setup paid off, and how a relationship shifted. General-purpose retrieval and agent-memory systems represent entities and facts but not the narratological structure these questions turn on, so they surface the wrong evidence or none at all. We introduce the Narrative World Model (NWM), a writer-memory system that pairs a narratology-grounded typed temporal-state graph with query-conditioned hybrid retrieval. To measure memory rather than the answerer, we read every system through a single held-constant Opus 4.8 reader over only that system's chapter-safe evidence, on a reproducible public corpus and a validated multi-hop benchmark, and we compare against the strongest existing temporal-knowledge-graph agent-memory framework, Graphiti/Zep (Rasmussen et al., 2025). NWM substantially and significantly outperforms this baseline on multi-hop narratological QA across both corpora, and far exceeds GraphRAG and flat retrieval. The advantage is representational rather than an artifact of extraction: it survives rebuilding the baseline with NWM's own extractor, and traces to its narratology-grounded structure and query-conditioned retrieval, not to graph size or extractor quality.

### [109] [FirstResearch: Auditable Question Formation for LLM Scientific Discovery Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05682)
*Yufeng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出FirstResearch框架，通过结构化的研究问题证书（包含原始定义、假设、机制模型、矛盾、可证伪假设、关键实验和失败更新规则）使LLM生成的科研问题变得可审计。实验表明该框架显著优于基线方法，证书是核心组件，去除后性能急剧下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM科研系统（如AI co-scientist、Agent Laboratory、AI Scientist-v2）能够提出研究问题，但这些问题难以审计——它们听起来合理，却未暴露科学家应审查的机制、证伪条件或假设。亟需一个能让研究问题在进入下游执行前变得可检查的框架。

Method: 提出FirstResearch框架，核心产出是结构化研究问题证书，包含：原始定义(primitive definitions)、假设(assumptions)、机制模型(mechanism model)、张力/矛盾(tension/contradiction)、可证伪假设(falsifiable hypothesis)、最小决定性实验(minimal decisive test)和失败更新规则(failure update rule)。通过DeepSeek-blind-judge和Gemini-2.5-Flash独立评判进行对比评估。

Result: 在10个LLM-agent研究主题上，FirstResearch在DeepSeek盲评协议下超越所有基线。Gemini独立重评保留系统级排名：FirstResearch 4.86/5 vs 最强基线4.38/5，Pearson一致性0.865。消融实验：仅证书组件评分4.90/5(DeepSeek)和4.88/5(Gemini)，移除证书后两者均低于1/5。

Conclusion: 显式推导约束（即证书机制）是使LLM生成的科研问题更具可审计性的有前景方法。虽然结果初步且使用LLM评判而非人类专家，但证据有力地支持了证书核心组件的关键作用。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域的研究问题常涉及复杂物理机制（如辐射传输、大气校正、混合像元分解），FirstResearch的证书框架可直接套用：1)原始定义：明确遥感产品（如NDVI、LST）的数学定义与物理含义；2)机制模型：建模遥感观测与地表参数间的正向物理过程；3)可证伪假设：如"基于XX指数的反演算法在植被覆盖度>70%时误差<5%"；4)最小决定性实验：设计特定波谱条件下的验证实验。此外，证书中的失败更新规则可构建遥感反演的自适应优化闭环。

Abstract (英文): LLM systems for scientific discovery increasingly assist with ideation, literature synthesis, experiment planning, and report generation, but the first research question they propose can remain difficult to audit: it may sound plausible without exposing the mechanism, falsifier, or assumption that a scientist should inspect. We introduce FirstResearch, a first-principles research-question formation framework for scientific LLM agents whose core artifact is a structured Research Question Certificate. The certificate records primitive definitions, assumptions, a mechanism model, a tension or contradiction, a falsifiable hypothesis, a minimal decisive test, and a failure update rule, making the proposed question inspectable before downstream execution. On ten LLM-agent research topics, FirstResearch outperforms controlled prompt-level baselines inspired by AI co-scientist, Agent Laboratory, and AI Scientist-v2 under a primary DeepSeek-blind-judge protocol. A Gemini-2.5-Flash independent-judge rescore of the same 40 baseline packages preserves the system-level ranking, with FirstResearch scoring 4.86/5 versus 4.38/5 for the strongest baseline and Pearson agreement of 0.865 on average score. A one-repeat ablation checkpoint further suggests that the certificate-centered core is the strongest component: certificate-only scoring reaches 4.90/5 under DeepSeek and 4.88/5 under Gemini, while removing certificates drops below 1/5 under both judges. These results are preliminary and use LLM judges rather than human domain experts, but they support a narrow scientific-discovery claim: explicit derivation constraints are a promising mechanism for making LLM-generated scientific questions more auditable. Code, prompts, saved outputs, and reproduction scripts are available at https://github.com/louiswang524/FirstResearch.

### [110] [Memory in the Loop: In-Process Retrieval as ExtendedWorking Memory for Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05690)
*Yusuf Khan,Carlo Lipizzi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究将记忆存储从外部查询移入智能体推理循环内部，通过使用进程内存储（~100μs延迟）替代网络存储（数十至数百毫秒），实现每步读写记忆，显著降低冗余行为并提升召回率（从0/5提升至3.6-4.8/5），且未丢失任何事实（244/244写入保留）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言智能体的记忆存储位于循环外部，每轮最多查询一次，受限于网络存储的延迟（数十至数百毫秒），导致端到端延迟膨胀高达83倍。先前工作仅通过调度或限制检索次数来管理成本，而未质疑该模式本身。本文论证延迟是存储位置（网络vs进程内）的属性，而非循环内访问模式的问题。

Method: 将记忆存储放入推理循环内部，实现每步读写：使用进程内存储（~100μs响应）替代网络存储；通过控制变量实验（固定每轮记忆延迟预算，仅改变存储响应速度）测量冗余行为；在GPT-5系列模型上评估召回率；结合本地小嵌入器（~40μs）进一步消除网络嵌入瓶颈（~200-400ms）。

Result: 进程内存储下冗余行为为0.0/12，而云往返（110ms）下为7.2/12（p=0.0079）；召回率从无内存时的0/5提升至3.6-4.8/5；存储操作p50延迟80-165μs；244/244次写入全部保留；结合本地嵌入器后完整操作降至~40μs。

Conclusion: 足够快的进程内存储使记忆从“工具”转变为“扩展工作记忆”，其每步开销几乎可忽略；记忆缺失的根本原因在于智能体的读取策略而非存储本身；网络嵌入是当前主导瓶颈，可通过本地嵌入器化解。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。在遥感任务中可应用该框架处理多时相/多源数据：1）将每景影像的元数据、特征向量、解译结果存入进程内记忆，在推理循环内每步更新；2）解决遥感任务中因网络延迟导致的大图/序列影像处理效率低问题；3）结合本地轻量特征提取器（如MobileNet系列），使嵌入式设备也能实现实时在环记忆；4）适用于变化检测、目标跟踪等需要持续记忆上下文的任务。

Abstract (英文): Language agents run a loop - observe, reason, act - but the memory they reason over sits outside it: a store queried at most once per turn. We study the regime where memory moves inside the loop, read and written on every step. The obstacle has always been latency: networked stores answer in tens to hundreds of milliseconds, and in-loop retrieval can inflate end-to-end latency by up to 83x when retrieval is expensive. Prior work manages that cost rather than questioning it: serving-layer scheduling hides it, "memory-first" designs ration retrieval to once per turn. We argue latency is a property of where the store lives, not the in-loop pattern: an in-process store answers in ~100us, three orders of magnitude below the network regime, and at that speed the per-step tax collapses. By the extended-mind thesis's parity principle, a store fast enough to be constantly and directly available becomes extended working memory, not a tool the agent merely consults. The premise is causal: holding a fixed per-turn memory-latency budget and varying only the store's answer speed, redundant actions rise monotonically with latency - 0.0 of 12 at in-process speed, 7.2 of 12 at a 110ms cloud round trip (gpt-5-nano, gpt-5-mini; exact permutation p=0.0079). We demonstrate the regime end-to-end: across four GPT-5-class models under a bounded window, recall improves from 0/5 to 3.6-4.8/5 with in-loop memory, store ops at p50 80-165us - though an instructed restate-every-reply baseline also solves it perfectly, at a token cost that grows with the working set. The store never lost a fact in any run (244 of 244 writes kept); every miss traces to the agent's read policy, not the store. Our measurements also relocate the bottleneck: the dominant per-step cost is embedding (~200-400ms over the network); pairing the in-process store with a small local embedder returns the complete operation to a measured ~40us.

### [111] [Akashic: A Low-Overhead LLM Inference Service with MemAttention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05708)
*Yang Liu,Zhaokai Luo,Huayi Jin,Ruozhou He,Chenchen Hong,Zhiyong Wang,Yifei Liu,Yunfei Gu,Chentao Wu,Junhao Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Akashic是一个基于MemAttention的低开销记忆系统，通过将上下文组织为有界块并建模跨块语义关系，结合硬件-软件协同设计的内存放置策略，在多种LLM Agent工作负载上显著提升任务准确率（最高+10.2点）、吞吐量（最高1.21倍）和可持续请求率（最高1.88倍）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM Agent系统在多轮交互、工具调用和跨会话工作流中需要不断累积上下文，但完整重放历史记录会导致长上下文预填充成本高、可能超出上下文限制，且任务相关证据被无关内容淹没，损害服务效率和输出质量。

Method: 提出Akashic记忆系统，核心包括：（1）MemAttention——将上下文组织为有界块并建模跨块语义关系，保留跨块证据而无需重复重写完整历史；（2）硬件-软件协同设计的内存放置策略——将可能共同检索的块共置，减少检索碎片化和I/O开销。

Result: 在四种代表性工作负载和三种模型规模上，相比强基线记忆系统，Akashic将任务准确率提升最高10.2个百分点，吞吐量提升最高1.21倍，可持续请求率提升最高1.88倍。

Conclusion: Akashic通过低开销的记忆管理和硬件-软件协同优化，有效解决了LLM Agent系统中的长上下文效率问题，在准确率和系统性能上均取得显著提升。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。该论文中的MemAttention机制和硬件-软件协同内存放置策略可迁移至遥感领域的长时序分析任务。具体方案：（1）将遥感影像时间序列的每一帧或每一段视为有界块，利用MemAttention建模跨时相影像间的语义关系（如变化检测、物候演变），避免重复编码完整历史序列；（2）将频繁共检索的遥感块（如同一区域不同时期的影像）通过硬件-软件协同放置策略共置于相近存储位置，减少I/O开销，提升大规模遥感检索与推理的吞吐量。

Abstract (英文): Recent LLM-based agent systems continuously accumulate context across multi-turn interactions, tool invocations, and cross-session workflows. Replaying the full history for every request quickly becomes impractical: long contexts increase prefill cost, may exceed context limits, and often bury task-relevant evidence in irrelevant content, degrading both serving efficiency and output quality. We propose Akashic, a low-overhead memory system built around MemAttention, which organizes context into bounded chunks and models semantic relationships across chunks, preserving cross-chunk evidence without repeatedly rewriting the full history. Akashic further applies hardware-software co-designed memory placement to co-locate likely co-retrieved chunks, reducing retrieval fragmentation and I/O overhead. Across four representative workloads and three model sizes, Akashic improves task accuracy by up to 10.2 points, throughput by up to 1.21x, and sustainable request rate by up to 1.88x over strong prior memory baselines.

### [112] [ArtisanCAD: An Industrial-Level CAD Agent with Expert-Grounded Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05750)
*Yunhan Xu,Qifeng Wu,Xunjin Li,Yuanwei Bin,Qingsong Yao,Jianghang Gu,Guan Wang,Weihao Lv,Huiyu Yang,Wenfa Luo,Jiao Xiang,Yuntian Chen,Shiyi Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出CAD-IR（CAD中间表示），一种可执行程序化表示，用于将专家CAD流程蒸馏为可复用技能，并支持从模糊或高层文本描述生成可编辑的B-Rep工业级CAD模型，在Text2CAD基准上将中间提示的Chamfer Distance从14.83降至9.88。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有text-to-CAD方法在处理模糊、欠指定或仅描述高层设计意图的用户提示时表现不佳，且很少利用工业流程中天然存在的专家程序化知识（如CATIA操作记录、宏日志等），缺乏将专家经验系统化蒸馏并用于指导CAD生成的手段。

Method: 提出CAD-IR（CAD中间表示），一种可执行程序化表示，编码参数、有序操作、MCP工具绑定、依赖关系、生成实体和验证规则。CAD-IR作为载体将专家CAD流程蒸馏为可复用的参数化技能，同时作为程序化支架将模糊或中间级提示转换为完整可执行的CAD操作。系统通过检索专家技能、实例化和修订CAD-IR、经CATIA-MCP后端执行、多视图视觉反馈迭代优化，最终生成生产级B-Rep模型。

Result: 在Text2CAD基准上，CAD-IR将中间提示的平均Chamfer Distance从14.83降至9.88。在四个复杂汽车零部件上，CAD-IR使专家CATIA录制可蒸馏为可复用技能，成功为新变体需求生成可编辑的CATIA原生B-Rep模型。

Conclusion: CAD-IR通过可执行程序化表示有效弥合了模糊文本意图与可执行CAD构造之间的鸿沟，并能将专家程序化知识蒸馏为可复用技能，支持工业级B-Rep模型的生成与编辑。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域的GIS数据处理（如矢量多边形构建、三维地形建模、建筑轮廓程序化生成）面临类似挑战：用户描述模糊（如"提取河流区域"）、缺乏标准可执行中间表示。可借鉴CAD-IR思想：①设计遥感/地理空间领域的中间表示（RS-IR），编码处理算子、参数依赖、MCP工具绑定和几何验证规则；②将专家遥感处理流程（如ENVI/SNAP操作记录、遥感处理日志）蒸馏为可复用技能；③从自然语言地理描述（如"城市扩张分析"）经RS-IR支架生成可执行处理链，通过多视图可视化反馈迭代优化。

Abstract (英文): Computer-aided design (CAD) for industrial components requires long-horizon procedural modeling, robust feature dependencies, editable parametric geometry, and production-grade B-Rep execution. Existing text-to-CAD methods have made promising progress in generating CAD programs from natural-language descriptions, but they still struggle when user prompts are ambiguous, underspecified, or only describe high-level design intent. They also rarely exploit expert procedural knowledge naturally available in industrial workflows, such as CATIA operation recordings, macro logs, drawing notes, and engineering descriptions. We present \algname, a skill-guided industrial CAD agent with expert-grounded knowledge distillation. The core of \algname is CAD intermediate representation (CAD-IR), an executable procedural representation that encodes parameters, ordered operations, MCP tool bindings, dependencies, generated entities, and verification rules. CAD-IR plays two key roles: it first serves as the carrier for distilling expert CAD procedures into reusable parameterized skills; then it provides a procedural scaffold that turns vague or intermediate-level prompts into complete executable CAD operations. \algname retrieves expert-derived skills, instantiates and revises CAD-IR, executes the resulting procedure through a dedicated CATIA-MCP backend, and uses multi-view visual feedback for iterative refinement, and finally generates production-ready B-Rep models. On the Text2CAD benchmark, CAD-IR improves generation from intermediate prompts by reducing mean Chamfer Distance from $14.83$ to $9.88$, showing its ability to bridge ambiguous textual intent and executable CAD construction. On four complex automotive components, CAD-IR enables expert CATIA recordings to be distilled into reusable skills, allowing \algname to generate editable CATIA-native B-Rep models for new variant requests.

</details>

### [115] [Beyond the Leaderboard: A Synthesis of Tool-Use, Planning, and Reasoning Failures in Large Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05775)
*Wael Albayaydh,Rui Zhao,Ivan Flechais*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文综合分析了2023-2026年间27篇关于LLM智能体的基准测试、分类学和审计研究，跨越19个不同基准，首次将工具使用、规划、长时推理、多智能体协作、安全性和度量有效性等维度的智能体局限性整合为统一的跨领域分类体系，识别出六大失败集群：工具调用错误、规划与约束违反、长时退化、多智能体协调失败、安全缺陷及度量有效性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用综合分析法，对27篇代表性论文（涵盖19个不同基准）进行迭代归纳，将独立报告的各类错误类别按照智能体从推理到行动流水线的不同阶段进行主题聚类，最终形成统一的六大失败集群分类体系。

Result: 识别出六类失败模式：(1)工具调用与参数错误；(2)规划与约束违反；(3)长时上下文积累导致的性能退化；(4)多智能体协调失败；(5)对抗性或欠规范条件下的安全故障；(6)度量有效性问题。发现失败随任务长度非线性累积，子任务强性能不等于端到端成功，额外脚手架并不能一致提升可靠性。

Conclusion: 当前LLM智能体在单轮工具使用、短时网页导航和窄范围编码任务上已取得显著进展，但在长时、多步、多智能体等复杂场景下仍存在系统性失败模式，且现有基准的度量方式可能高估实际能力，亟需更严谨的评估方法论。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该分类体系可直接迁移至遥感LLM智能体评估：遥感任务中的工具调用（如API调用数据检索）、多步规划（如时序影像处理流程）、长时推理（如长时间序列变化检测）、多智能体协作（如多星协同观测）均对应本文六大失败聚类。改进方向：可针对遥感领域特有的工具链（如GDAL、SNAP、云平台API）增加特定失败子类，并构建遥感专用的长时任务基准以检验失败的非线性累积效应。

Abstract (英文): Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly evaluated on their ability to use tools, plan multi-step tasks, coordinate with other agents, and operate over extended horizons. Reported benchmark gains often obscure recurring failure modes documented across otherwise unrelated evaluation efforts. This paper synthesizes 27 benchmark, taxonomy, and audit papers (2023-2026), spanning 19 distinct benchmarks, into a cross-cutting taxonomy of agent limitations. To our knowledge, this is the first synthesis that integrates evidence across tool use, planning, long-horizon reasoning, multi-agent coordination, safety, and measurement validity into a single, unified taxonomy of LLM agent limitations. We identify six failure clusters: (1) tool invocation and parameter-level errors, (2) planning and constraint-satisfaction failures, (3) long-horizon degradation from context accumulation, (4) multi-agent coordination failures, (5) safety and security failures under adversarial or underspecified conditions, and (6) measurement validity problems. The taxonomy was derived iteratively by grouping independently reported error categories into themes corresponding to distinct stages of the agent reasoning-to-action pipeline. Across the literature, we find that failures compound nonlinearly with task length, that strong performance on individual sub-tasks does not reliably translate into end-to-end success, and that additional scaffolding does not consistently improve reliability. At the same time, substantial progress has been demonstrated in single-turn tool use, short-horizon web navigation, and narrowly scoped coding tasks.

### [116] [Controlling Tool Use with Heading-Specific Activation Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05790)
*Yuqi Chen,Vincent Siu,Yang Liu,Dawn Song,Chenguang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文研究了工具增强型大语言模型中工具调用行为的内部表征，发现可以从heading-anchor位置提取转向向量来双向因果控制工具调用行为，但几何分析表明这种因果有效性并不对应清晰的线性结构，工具调用步骤的激活模式是弥散且双峰的，不同工具类型之间内部特征重叠度低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大语言模型中工具调用决策是否存在稳定的内部表征，以及这些表征能否被提取和操控。这是一个非平凡的问题，因为工具完全存在于推理上下文中，没有直接编码在模型权重中。

Method: 从heading-anchor位置提取转向向量，在5个开源模型和3个领域上进行双向因果控制实验，并通过几何分析（激活模式的线性结构、跨工具特征重叠等）研究工具调用步骤的内部表征特性。

Result: 转向向量能够有效抑制不必要的工具调用，尤其是在参数化推理足够胜任的领域中效果最佳；但几何分析显示工具调用表现出弥散、双峰的激活模式，与转向向量没有一致的负对齐，不同工具类型的内部特征重叠度低。

Conclusion: 工具调用步骤的几何不规则性可能源于工具的非参数化性质，这使其区别于参数化概念对应的转向向量；几何不规则性与因果有效性之间的关系仍是开放问题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感领域的大模型常需调用外部工具（如GIS处理函数、遥感图像分割API、气象数据查询接口等），该研究的转向向量方法可用于：(1) 抑制不必要的工具调用，例如当大模型已具备足够的地物分类知识时避免冗余调用遥感影像处理工具；(2) 在遥感多工具协作场景中，通过分析不同遥感工具（如NDVI计算、水体提取、变化检测）的内部表征差异，设计更精准的工具选择机制；(3) 结合遥感领域的参数化知识（如光谱特征）与非参数化工具调用，研究转向向量在混合决策中的几何特性。

Abstract (英文): Tool-augmented large language models extend their capabilities beyond parametric knowledge through external tools, but tend to invoke them unnecessarily. We investigate whether tool-use decisions have any stable internal representation that can be extracted and manipulated, a question that is non-trivial given that tools exist entirely in context at inference time and have no direct encoding in model weights. We show that steering vectors extracted from heading-anchors positions exert bidirectional causal control over tool-invocation behavior across five open-source models and three domains, suppressing unnecessary tool use most effectively in domains where parametric reasoning suffices. However, geometric analysis reveals that this causal effectiveness does not correspond to clean linear structure: tool-invocation steps exhibit diffuse, bimodal alignment with the suppression vector rather than the consistent negative alignment a linear encoding account would predict, and different tool types recruit largely distinct internal signatures with low cross-tool feature overlap. We hypothesize these geometric properties are indicative of the non-parametric nature of tools, and distinguish tool-use steering vectors from those extracted for parametrically grounded concepts. The relationship between this geometric irregularity and the observed causal effectiveness remains an open question.

### [117] [From Passive Retrieval to Active Memory Navigation: Learning to Use Memory as a Structured Action Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05794)
*Yue Xu,Yutao Sun,Yihao Liu,Mengyu Zhou,Jiayi Qiao,Lu Ma,Kai Tang,Wenjie Wang,Xiaoxi Jiang,Guanjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: NapMem提出将长期用户记忆组织为多粒度记忆金字塔，并通过强化学习训练智能体主动选择合适粒度的记忆工具，而非被动接收检索结果，在多项记忆密集型任务上取得竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆系统将记忆作为被动检索接口暴露给模型，模型只能消费预先选定的证据，缺乏主动选择和探索不同粒度记忆的能力，限制了个性化对话智能体的表现。

Method: NapMem将用户历史组织为链接的多粒度记忆金字塔（原始对话、类型化记忆记录、主题轨迹、用户画像），各层级通过溯源关系连接并作为记忆工具暴露；利用记忆工具强化学习训练智能体根据查询和中间证据选择合适粒度的记忆。

Result: 在PersonaMem-v2、LongMemEval和LoCoMo数据集上，NapMem在记忆密集型任务上表现优异；在非记忆任务上，学习到的策略基本保持通用推理和工具使用能力；额外分析了存储成本、推理代价、工具使用行为和消融实验。

Conclusion: 长期用户记忆应结合结构化存储和学习如何使用适当粒度记忆的策略，而非仅依赖被动检索。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域的长时序分析（如变化检测、土地覆盖分类）面临类似挑战——历史影像数据量大且粒度不一。可将NapMem的多粒度记忆金字塔迁移为"多时相遥感金字塔"：原始影像→特征图/变化掩膜→时序轨迹→区域场景画像，并通过强化学习训练模型自动选择合适时空粒度的历史影像或特征进行推理，提升长时序遥感任务的效率和准确性。

Abstract (英文): Long-term user memory is essential for personalized conversational agents, yet many memory systems still expose memory through passive retrieval interfaces, making the model a consumer of pre-selected evidence. We introduce NapMem, a framework for learning to use long-term user memory as a structured action space rather than passively retrieved context. NapMem organizes user history into a linked multi-granularity memory pyramid, where raw conversations, typed memory records, topic tracks, and user profiles are connected through provenance relations, and exposes these levels through memory tools. The agent is trained to select memory according to the query and intermediate evidence, allowing it to inspect different memory granularities before answering. Experiments on PersonaMem-v2, LongMemEval, and LoCoMo show that a NapMem agent trained with memory-tool reinforcement learning is competitive across diverse memory-intensive tasks, while evaluations on non-memory tasks suggest that the learned policy largely preserves general reasoning and tool-use abilities. Additional analyses examine storage, inference cost, tool-use behavior, and ablations over navigation, memory granularity, and RL training. Our results suggest that long-term user memory benefits from coupling structured storage with a learned policy for using memory at the appropriate granularity.

### [118] [TurnOPD: Making On-Policy Distillation Turn-Aware for Efficient Long-Horizon Agent Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05804)
*Yuhang Zhou,Kai Zheng,Haoling Li,Dengyun Peng,Can Xu,Jingjing Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TurnOPD提出了一种面向长周期智能体任务的逐回合预算策略（turn-level budgeting），通过自适应 rollout 深度预算和渐进式回合归一化损失预算，解决了传统在线蒸馏（OPD）在长序列任务中计算效率低、KL 监督信号分布不均的问题，在多个环境上实现了更优的准确率-时间权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线策略蒸馏（on-policy distillation）在长周期智能体任务中未被充分探索，且存在两个关键效率问题：(1) 完整轨迹 rollout 中尾部回合提供的 KL 监督信号弱且噪声大，浪费计算资源；(2) 轨迹级 KL 损失过度集中在浅层 token，深层决策回合在初始行为对齐后训练不足。

Method: 提出 TurnOPD，包含两个预算控制器：(1) 自适应 rollout 深度预算（adaptive rollout-depth budgeting），利用探测回合统计量确定最优 rollout 长度；(2) 渐进式回合归一化损失预算（progressive turn-normalized loss budgeting），逐步将 KL 权重从 token 级监督转向回合级平衡监督。

Result: 在 ALFWorld、WebShop 和 Multi-Hop Search 三个 benchmark 上，使用任务专用教师模型，TurnOPD 在相同的训练时间预算下取得了更高的验证准确率，推进了准确率-时间帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: TurnOPD 通过回合级预算控制有效提升了长周期智能体在线蒸馏的训练效率，证明了按回合粒度进行资源分配和损失归一化是克服 OPD 在长任务中低效问题的可行方向。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感中的长序列决策任务（如多时相变化检测、卫星自主任务规划、遥感图像序列中的目标跟踪）与本文的长周期智能体问题高度同构。具体方案：(1) 将遥感任务中的每个观测时间点或每个处理步骤建模为"回合"，TurnOPD 的自适应 rollout 截断可用于减少无效尾回合的采样开销；(2) 渐进式回合归一化损失可应用于多阶段遥感解译模型（如先检测后分类的级联架构），使后阶段任务在训练初期不被前阶段的 KL 偏差淹没；(3) 探测回合统计量可扩展为遥感场景中的不确定性估计，动态决定是否提前终止推理路径。

Abstract (英文): On-policy distillation (OPD) trains a student policy by matching a stronger teacher on the student's own trajectories, offering a promising framework for language agent training. However, its application to long-horizon agentic tasks remains insufficiently explored. We identify two key inefficiencies in vanilla agent OPD: (1) full-horizon rollouts often waste wall-clock resources on tail turns that provide weak and noisy KL supervision, and (2) trajectory-level KL objectives concentrate most of the loss on shallow tokens, leaving deeper decision turns under-trained once initial behaviors are aligned. To address these challenges, we propose TurnOPD, a turn-level budgeting strategy for efficient on-policy distillation of long-horizon agents. TurnOPD consists of two budget controllers: adaptive rollout-depth budgeting, which uses probe-based turn statistics to determine rollout length, and progressive turn-normalized loss budgeting, which gradually shifts KL weighting from token-level to turn-balanced supervision. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and Multi-Hop Search with task-specialized teacher models show that TurnOPD achieves superior validation accuracy under equal wall-clock training budgets and advances the accuracy--time frontier beyond vanilla OPD.

</details>


### [119] [Onnes: A Physics-Grounded Multi-Agent LLM Simulator for Cryogenic Fault Diagnosis in Quantum Computing Infrastructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05805)
*Praneeth Narisetty,Uday Kumar Reddy Kattamanchi,Shiva Nagendra Babu Kore*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Onnes框架，将基于物理的数字孪生稀释制冷机模拟器与多智能体大语言模型操作层结合，用于超导量子计算机的低温故障诊断。零样本LLM面板在检测上与监督ML分类器无显著差异，但分类精度较低；通过对比少样本演示和自一致性投票，分类精度从0.685提升至0.990，匹配监督分类器的0.985，且无需参数更新。在连续监控中，系统能在一次轮询间隔内捕获所有发展中的故障，并有效抑制误报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前稀释制冷机的故障诊断主要依赖阈值报警，只能报告异常而非具体故障类型，缺乏智能化的诊断能力，亟需一种能够准确识别故障类别的高效诊断方法。

Method: 构建物理驱动的数字孪生模拟器（前向物理模型+学习到的真实制冷机噪声指纹），驱动实时多智能体LLM操作层。采用六种物理基础的故障类别，进行零样本LLM面板与监督ML分类器的对比实验，并通过对比少样本演示和自一致性投票提升分类性能。

Conclusion: LLM代理结合物理数字孪生和少量演示样本，可以在无需参数更新的条件下达到与监督分类器相当的故障诊断精度，为低温量子计算基础设施的智能运维提供了可行方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该框架可直接迁移至遥感卫星平台的热控子系统故障诊断：1) 利用卫星遥测数据（温度、压力、流量等）构建数字孪生体，学习真实卫星噪声指纹；2) 将六种物理故障类（如制冷剂泄漏、热控失效）映射到遥感卫星的热控故障场景；3) LLM多智能体面板可处理遥感卫星运行日志和遥测数据，实现零样本或少样本的故障定位；4) 对比少样本演示策略可用于遥感故障诊断中标注数据稀缺的问题。需注意遥感卫星通信延迟和计算资源限制，需优化LLM模型的轻量化部署。

Abstract (英文): Dilution refrigerators are the enabling infrastructure of superconducting quantum computers, yet their fault diagnosis is still dominated by threshold alarms that report that something is wrong, not what. We present Onnes, a physics-grounded digital-twin simulator of a dilution refrigerator (a forward physics model with a learned real-fridge noise fingerprint) that drives a live multi-agent LLM operations layer, and use it for a controlled head-to-head between a zero-shot LLM agent panel and a supervised ML classifier on cryogenic fault diagnosis. The twin couples a real dilution-cooling floor, a noise-and-correlation fingerprint learned from real BlueFors logs, and six physics-grounded fault classes, three engineered to overlap on temperature but separate on flow and pressure. Across a 1000-turn evaluation the zero-shot panel shows no significant difference from the classifier on detection but trails on classification, its errors concentrating on the confusable faults. Curated contrastive few-shot demonstrations and self-consistency voting then raise classification accuracy from 0.685 to 0.990, matching the supervised classifier (0.985) with no parameter updates and six labeled demonstrations; an ablation attributes the gain almost entirely to the demonstrations. Run as a continuous monitor across a nine-run fault-by-seed sweep, the agent catches every developing fault within one poll interval, and a confidence gate suppresses pre-onset false alarms whose rate is backend-dependent. As a first sim-to-real check, a detector trained purely on real BlueFors telemetry posts a real-hardware false-alarm rate of 6.4% and 100% recall on physics faults injected onto real held-out windows. All numbers are drawn verbatim from released run logs.

### [120] [StateFuse: Deterministic Conflict-Preserving Memory for Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05844)
*Sergey Volkov,Yang Li,Ye Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: StateFuse是一种基于CRDT的冲突感知复制内存合约，通过不可变历史、显式冲突对象和投影时解析来保持矛盾可见性，而不是像传统系统那样用覆盖规则隐藏冲突。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体系统在跨分支、重试和副本间积累矛盾，但大多数内存层使用难以审查的覆盖规则来消除分歧，导致冲突不可见且难以纠正。

Method: 基于标准OpSet/CRDT合并构建，不引入新的连接代数，而是定义代理面向的语义层，包括不可变历史、显式冲突对象、精确/语义纠正句柄、确定性谓词合约和投影时分辨率。

Result: 在282个问题的MemoryAgentBench上，准确率与基线持平，但冲突保持表面能保留矛盾可见性。准确率无普遍提升，但在保持歧义条件下能实现更安全的弃权和纠正。

Conclusion: StateFuse最适合作为用于矛盾展示、弃权和可审计纠正的更安全公共内存合约，而非追求通用准确率提升。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：70%。遥感数据处理中多源传感器数据常产生冲突（如不同时相、不同分辨率的地物分类结果矛盾），可借鉴StateFuse的CRDT冲突建模方法：1) 显式保留遥感数据融合过程中的分类矛盾而非强制投票统一；2) 利用语义纠正句柄追溯标注冲突源头；3) 在时空数据投影阶段实现分辨率而非直接改写底层遥感数据。

Abstract (英文): Agent systems accumulate conflicting observations across branches, retries, and replicas, yet many practical memory layers still collapse disagreement behind overwrite rules that are difficult to inspect or correct. We present StateFuse, a conflict-aware replicated memory contract built on standard OpSet/CRDT merge. StateFuse does not introduce a new join algebra; it defines an agent-facing semantics layer with immutable history, explicit conflict objects, exact and semantic correction handles (claim_id / claim_ref), deterministic predicate contracts, and projection-time resolution that cannot rewrite replicated state.
  We evaluate StateFuse against flat multi-value, raw-log, provenance-style, and collapsed baselines under matched resolver and verification policies. On a 282-question official conflict-bearing MemoryAgentBench slice, the compared methods tie on answer accuracy, but conflict-preserving surfaces keep contradictions visible while collapsed surfaces do not. In a controlled agent loop with uniform verification, preserving ambiguity enables safer abstention and correction than early collapse. A correction-handle ablation further shows that semantic handles matter when exact prior identifiers are unavailable.
  The resulting claim is narrow: StateFuse is best supported as a safer public memory contract for contradiction surfacing, abstention, and auditable correction, not as a universal accuracy gain.

</details>


### [121] [Uncovering Latent Depression Severity for Binary Depression Detection via Advantage-weighting Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05901)
*Manning Gao,Tingyi Liu,Leheng Zhang,Haifeng Hu,Yuncheng Jiang,Sijie Mai*

TL;DR: 提出一种基于时间编码器和互变压器的细粒度多模态抑郁检测框架，核心贡献是二元优势加权排序损失（Binary Advantage-weighting Ranking Loss），通过优势加权分离和优势加权紧凑性两个机制优化潜在空间分布，在D-vlog和LMVD数据集上达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动抑郁检测面临特征分布重叠和决策边界难以建立的问题，现有方法难以有效解耦重叠特征分布。

Method: 提出细粒度多模态框架，包含时间编码器和互变压器实现深度跨模态融合；核心创新为二元优势加权排序损失，包含两个互补机制：优势加权分离（通过成对预测差异矩阵挖掘困难样本并动态加权）和优势加权紧凑性（最小化类内方差使特征聚集在类中心周围）。

Result: 在D-vlog和LMVD数据集上取得最优性能，模型通过优先处理困难样本重构潜在序数结构。

Conclusion: 基于困难样本优先排序的损失函数设计能有效优化潜在空间分布，提升抑郁检测性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。该框架可迁移至遥感图像中的情绪/心理状态分析任务，例如分析灾区居民面部表情与语音的时序多模态数据，利用时间编码器处理时序变化，互变压器融合视觉与音频模态。优势加权损失可用于处理遥感数据中类别分布不均衡问题。改进方向：需适配遥感场景下较低分辨率和噪声更强的音频/视频数据，可引入数据增强和迁移学习策略。

Abstract (英文): Automatic depression detection using audio-visual data faces significant challenges, particularly in disentangling overlapping feature distributions and establishing robust decision boundaries. To address this, we propose a fine-grained multimodal framework featuring a temporal encoder and a mutual transformer to facilitate deep cross-modal fusion. Our core contribution is the Binary Advantage-weighting Ranking Loss, which optimizes the latent space distribution through two complementary mechanisms: Advantage-weighted Separation, which mines hard pairs by computing a pairwise prediction difference matrix and dynamically weighting them based on their difficulty; and Advantage-weighted Compactness, which minimizes intra-class variance to force features to cluster around their respective class centers. Extensive experiments on D-vlog and LMVD demonstrate that our model reconstructs the latent ordinal structure by prioritizing hard pairs, thereby achieving state-of-the-art performance.

### [122] [PCBWorld: A Benchmark Environment for Engine-Grounded PCB Design Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05915)
*Hyungseok Song,Junseok Park,Won-Seok Choi,Seohui Bae,Han-Seul Jeong,Youngjoon Park,Soonyoung Lee*

TL;DR: 本文提出PCBWorld，一个基于KiCad EDA引擎的PCB布线开源环境，支持强化学习和工具型大语言模型代理。配合PCBWorld-Bench基准（含3类数据集和8项引擎验证指标），实验表明交互式代理在PCB布线任务上优于传统网格动作RL策略和开环LLM基线，且仅在合成数据上训练的RL策略能零样本迁移至真实电路板。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于KiCad EDA引擎构建PCBWorld环境，智能体通过引擎原生操作（如添加/移动走线）与电路板交互，并利用引擎的DRC反馈（短路/间距违规）调整布线行为。环境支持RL策略和LLM代理两种范式。同时提出PCBWorld-Bench基准，包含三类数据集（可控合成实例和679个真实开源电路板），采用8项引擎验证的评估指标对完成电路板进行评分，不限制布线方法。

Result: 在PCBWorld中，交互式代理（RL策略和LLM代理）一致优于传统网格动作RL策略和开环LLM基线。仅在合成数据上训练的RL策略能够零样本迁移到真实电路板，性能接近基于规则的布线器。

Conclusion: 基于引擎的交互式PCBWorld方法为推进RL和LLM代理的布线能力提供了有前景的基础，证明了交互式、引擎导向的学习方法在PCB自动布线任务中的潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。具体方案：(1) 将PCBWorld的引擎-代理交互框架类比到遥感图像中的目标检测任务——利用遥感图像处理引擎（如GDAL）的原生操作（波段运算、几何校正等）和规则检查（如地理配准精度）作为智能体环境，训练RL/LLM代理进行交互式遥感图像分析；(2) 借鉴PCBWorld的DRC反馈机制，在遥感变化检测中引入类似"规则检查器"来约束分割/分类输出，减少几何畸变和伪变化；(3) PCBWorld中合成到真实的零样本迁移策略，可迁移至遥感领域——在合成遥感图像上训练模型，再零样本迁移到真实遥感场景，应对遥感标注数据稀缺问题。

Abstract (英文): PCB routing is the task of connecting the nets of a board with copper traces under strict design rules, yet learning-based methods still lag behind rule-based routers. We introduce PCBWorld, an open-source engine-grounded PCB routing environment built on the KiCad EDA engine. As a human engineer does, agents in PCBWorld interactively route a board through the engine's native operations, using its Design Rule Check (DRC) feedback to keep the routing within the design rules. The environment supports both RL policies and tool-using LLM agents. Alongside the environment, PCBWorld-Bench provides three dataset families in KiCad's native board format (.kicad_pcb), covering two types of controllable synthetic instances and 679 real open-source boards. It scores any completed board with eight engine-checked evaluation metrics, regardless of the routing method. In our experiments, agents in PCBWorld consistently outperformed grid-action RL policies and open-loop LLM baselines, and an RL policy trained only on synthetic boards transferred zero-shot to real boards, approaching rule-based routers. These results position the engine-grounded, interactive approach of PCBWorld as a promising foundation for advancing the routing ability of both RL and LLM agents.

### [123] [SearchEyes: Towards Frontier Multimodal Deep Search Intelligence via Search World Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05943)
*Zhengbo Jiao,Yiming Cheng,Yilei Jiang,Kaituo Feng,Rui Huang,Tianyi Jiang,Juanxi Tian,Jiapeng li,Qunzhong Wang,Tailai Chen,Qianshan Wei,Chuan Xiao,Shanyu Rong,Yangfu Li,Yanhan Zhou,Yunpu Ma,Yifan Zhang,Xiangyu Yue*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract (英文): Training multimodal search agents to perform multi-hop reasoning remains challenging due to a fundamental structural disconnect: existing pipelines construct training data, search environments, and reward signals independently, causing synthesized structural metadata to be discarded, environments to rely on irreproducible external engines, and RL rewards to remain sparse at the trajectory level. We present \textbf{SearchEyes}, which uses a typed knowledge graph as the backbone of a \emph{simulated search world} that unifies all three components. We propose \textbf{Perception-Knowledge Chains (PKC)} to sample constrained multi-hop paths over the visual-knowledge intersection of Wikidata5M, retaining hop-level entity metadata that simultaneously defines a self-contained search world and step-level reward anchors. We further propose \textbf{Hop-Anchored Policy Optimization (HaPO)}, which reuses these anchors for step-level credit assignment without a separately trained process reward model. Experiments on six multimodal knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that SearchEyes achieves state-of-the-art performance among open-source multimodal search agents, with SearchEyes-27B improving over the strongest open-source baseline by 6.2 points on average.%

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。该论文的LLM适配框架可迁移至遥感领域：1) 将SSH文献综述的评估协议（检索、摘要、可追溯性、幻觉检测）直接用于遥感论文的自动化文献综述和元分析；2) 其多语言文献处理方法可解决遥感研究中非英语文献（如中文、俄文遥感期刊）的检索与整合问题；3) 定性专家评估机制可类比为遥感领域专家对LLM生成的遥感解译报告进行质量审核；4) 法律伦理合规框架可映射到遥感数据（尤其高分辨率影像）的隐私与安全合规审查。

Abstract (英文): The integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) into scientific research workflows, particularly for bibliographic discovery and literature synthesis, raises significant methodological, epistemic and regulatory challenges for the Social Sciences and Humanities (SSH), especially with regard to disciplinary diversity, multilingual access to sources and the evaluation of results. This paper presents an on-going use case developed within the European project LLMs4EU and the ALT-EDIC infrastructure, aimed at adapting foundation models to SSH research practices and supporting tasks such as question answering, comparative document analysis and literature review. The evaluation framework follows the LLMs4EU protocol and encompasses both independent quantitative benchmarking (retrieval, summarisation, traceability and hallucination detection) and a qualitative assessment involving a panel of Digital Humanities experts. By embedding model adaptation within research infrastructures and a structured legal and ethical compliance framework, the use case explores how domain-sensitive and regulation-aware generative AI can support SSH scholarship while preserving reliability and epistemic responsibility.

### [125] [Auto-DSM Under the Lens: A Black-Box Evaluation Framework for LLM-Based DSM Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05985)
*Niels Potters,Theo Hofman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个黑盒评估框架，系统评估大语言模型从结构化技术文档生成设计结构矩阵的能力。通过单次/多次运行视角、结构指标、分类指标和稳定性指标的综合评估，发现LLM能生成结构合理的DSM，但对歧义和不一致的依赖定义敏感，同时展示了LLM驱动DSM自动化的潜力和当前局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前Auto-DSM流程多为闭源，缺乏可重复的评估方法来衡量LLM生成DSM的质量，亟需一个透明、系统的基准测试框架。

Method: 提出黑盒评估框架，将生成的GEN-DSM与人工验证的GT-DSM进行对比。综合结构指标（完整性、正确性、耦合密度）、分类指标（选择性准确率、弃权覆盖率）和稳定性指标（熵、Fleiss' κ），并提出复合质量分数Q。在虚构抽象系统和真实冰箱分解两个数据集上进行控制实验。

Result: LLM能生成结构合理的DSM，在输入结构良好时具有高可重复性，但对文本歧义、不一致的依赖定义和提示措辞敏感，存在系统性的幻觉和弃权失败问题。

Conclusion: 该框架为审计Auto-DSM流程提供了透明基准，为将LLM基分解方法集成到基于模型的系统工程工作流中奠定了基础。

Abstract (英文): This paper presents a black-box evaluation framework to systematically assess the ability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to generate Design Structure Matrices (DSMs) from structured technical documentation. Motivated by the closed-source nature of current Auto-DSM pipelines, the framework introduces a reproducible methodology that benchmarks generated DSMs (GEN-DSMs) against manually validated ground-truth matrices (GT-DSMs). The evaluation integrates both single-run and multi-run perspectives, combining structural metrics (Completeness, Correctness, Coupling Density), classification metrics (Selective Accuracy, Abstention Coverage), and stability measures (Entropy, Fleiss' $κ$). To synthesize these aspects, a Composite Quality Score (Q) is proposed. Controlled experiments are conducted on two datasets: a fictive abstract system and a real-world refrigerator decomposition, covering variations in phrasing, parameter-dataset alignment, and system complexity. Results show that LLMs can produce structurally plausible DSMs and achieve high reproducibility under well-structured inputs, but remain sensitive to ambiguity, inconsistent dependency definitions, and prompt formulation. The findings highlight systematic sources of hallucination and abstention failure, demonstrating both the potential and current limitations of LLM-driven DSM automation. The proposed framework provides a transparent benchmark for auditing Auto-DSM pipelines and establishes foundations for integrating LLM-based decomposition methods into model-based systems engineering (MBSE) workflows.

Abstract (英文): LLM-agent simulations make natural-language social scenarios easy to instantiate, but their outputs can be overread as predictions and are often difficult to compare with explicit social dynamics. We present AgoraSim, a hybrid agent-based modeling framework for scenario-oriented social reaction analysis. AgoraSim resolves textual or multimodal artifacts into editable ABM configurations, runs ratio-controlled populations that mix LLM, vision-language, custom-endpoint, random, and classical agents, and compares the same scenario against matched classical reference dynamics. All agents emit a shared structured decision object, enabling common action spaces, interaction protocols, metrics, and audit records. Exposed through a local UI, Python SDK/CLI, and REST API, AgoraSim helps users inspect scenario trajectories, compare modeling assumptions, and identify cases that warrant empirical validation.

### [127] [Information Limits and Attractor Dynamics in Economies of Frontier LLM Agents: A Pre-Registered Test](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06001)
*Cheng Qian*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对前沿语言模型智能体（Claude Opus 4.8）的小型经济系统进行了预注册的两部分实验，验证了两个定量预测：市场耦合下财富增长的信息论容量区域，以及激励与控制杠杆下群体错位的平均场残差标度律。结果1确认了信息论增长定律（G_a - G_b = I_a - I_b，误差小于46毫奈特）及信息联盟的次模性/超模性调控；结果2为结构性否定，所有72次种群运行未观察到平均场模型假设的噪声维持弥散 regime，目标分散度坍塌至低于预注册下限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，多智能体系统的宏观行为（如财富分配、目标对齐）缺乏可检验的定量理论预测。本文旨在通过预注册实验，严格检验两类理论预测：信息论视角下的市场耦合增长定律，以及统计物理类比下的群体错位标度律，从而评估前沿LLM智能体经济系统的可预测性和理论边界。

Method: 采用两部分预注册实验设计：（1）信息论增长实验：构建parimutuel耦合经济，4种感知结构下比较智能体的相对信息量与相对增长，测试信息联盟的次模/超模性；（2）平均场残差标度实验：在72个种群运行中施加激励机制和控制杠杆，测量目标分散度V的响应特性。所有预测、接受带和决策规则在公开git链上预注册冻结，全程API花费$138.76，结果从缓存机械推导。

Result: 结果1（确认）：增长差距律G_a - G_b = I_a - I_b成立，最坏误差46毫奈特（预注册接受带50）；联盟价值在条件独立信道下严格次模，XOR协同控制使其翻转超模（幅度0.62 ≥ ln2/2奈特）；联合增长上界G_S ≤ H(X)严格成立；最佳信息智能体在4/5市场种子中吸收了几乎全部财富。结果2（结构性否定）：所有72次运行中目标分散度V坍塌（最大4.85，预注册下限5.31），双杠杆响应为跨支配边界的阶跃函数而非平滑响应，边界附近细胞呈现种子选择双稳态。

Conclusion: 信息论增长律在LLM智能体经济系统中得到了精确实证确认，表明市场耦合下的财富增长可被信息量严格预测。但平均场模型假设的噪声维持弥散 regime在当前所有能力水平的LLM种群中均未实现，提示该理论框架与真实LLM智能体行为存在根本性偏差。研究展示了预注册实验在AI科学中的可行性，并开源了完整协议和分析代码。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：（1）将信息论增长律（G_a - G_b = I_a - I_b）应用于遥感多智能体系统（如异构卫星星座协同观测），每个卫星作为信息有限的经济智能体，通过相对信息量预测其观测数据的经济回报增长，优化星座任务分配；（2）利用联盟价值的次模/超模调控机制（XOR协同控制），设计遥感数据融合任务中不同传感器（光学、SAR、高光谱）的协同效应评估体系；（3）将平均场残差标度实验的结构性否定结论推广至遥感群体智能系统（如无人机集群遥感），提醒在真实LLM驱动的自主遥感任务规划中，理论标度律可能不成立，需要更鲁棒的工程约束设计。

Abstract (英文): We report a pre-registered, two-part experiment on small economies of frontier language-model agents (Claude Opus 4.8), testing two quantitative predictions about coupled multi-agent systems: an information-theoretic capacity region for wealth growth under market coupling, and a mean-field residual-scaling law for population misalignment under incentive and control levers. All predictions, acceptance bands, and decision rules were frozen in a public git chain before any run; every reported number re-derives mechanically from cached model outputs; the entire experiment cost $138.76 in metered API spend and is re-runnable at zero cost from the cache.
  Result 1 (confirmation): in parimutuel-coupled economies, relative growth equals relative claimed information -- the gap law G_a - G_b = I_a - I_b holds to a worst-case 46 millinats (pre-registered band: 50) across four perception structures; coalition value is submodular exactly where channels are conditionally independent, and a designed XOR synergy control flips it supermodular by 0.62 >= ln2/2 nats, with agents reasoning out the joint bit; the joint growth ceiling G_S <= H(X) binds exactly; and the best-informed agent absorbs essentially the whole wealth pool in 4/5 market seeds.
  Result 2 (structural negative): the residual-scaling test returned "domain not found." In all 72 population runs, goal dispersion collapsed (V -> 0; maximum 4.85 against a frozen floor of 5.31), the population's response to the two levers was a step function across the dominance boundary rather than a smooth response, and cells near the boundary were bistable with seed-selected outcomes. No tested LLM population at any capability level realizes the noise-maintained-dispersion regime the smooth mean-field model assumes. We release the full protocol, pre-registration chain, call cache, and analysis code.

### [128] [PolyWorkBench: Benchmarking Multilingual Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06008)
*Hongliang Li,Yijin Liu,Zhiwei Zhang,Zihe Liu,Xinyue Lou,Jinan Xu,Fandong Meng,Kaiyu Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PolyWorkBench是一个评估LLM智能体在多语言长周期工作流任务中表现的基准，包含67个跨5个领域（商业、知识工作、法律分析、本地化和制造）的任务，实验表明现有最先进LLM智能体在多语言环境下性能显著下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准大多隐含假设单语言设置，而实际应用往往涉及多语言输入和输出，语言多样性与智能体执行之间的交互尚未被充分探索。

Method: 构建了PolyWorkBench基准，包含67个跨5个领域（商业、知识工作、法律分析、本地化、制造）的多语言工作流任务；提出混合评估框架，结合结构评分、可执行验证和基于LLM的语义评估。

Result: 最先进的LLM智能体在多语言工作流设置下相比单语言设置性能显著下降；多语言性在推理和执行步骤中产生复合效应。

Conclusion: 多语言性会叠加影响推理和执行步骤，凸显了在智能体评估中联合建模语言变化和程序化决策的重要性。

Abstract (英文): Large language model (LLM) agents have shown strong performance in long-horizon tasks that require planning, tool use, and interaction with external environments. However, most existing benchmarks implicitly assume a monolingual setting, where the entire execution process, including reasoning, tool invocation, and output generation, is conducted within a single language. In contrast, real-world applications often involve multilingual inputs and outputs within a unified workflow, yet the interaction between multilinguality and agentic execution remains underexplored. In this work, we introduce PolyWorkBench, a benchmark for evaluating LLM agents on multilingual long-horizon workplace workflows. PolyWorkBench consists of 67 tasks across five domains, including commerce, knowledge work, legal analysis, localization, and manufacturing, where agents must process heterogeneous multilingual inputs, perform iterative reasoning, invoke external tools, and produce structured outputs. To enable comprehensive evaluation, we propose a hybrid framework that combines structural grading, executable verification, and LLM-based semantic assessment. This design allows us to capture both functional correctness and linguistic consistency across complex workflows. Empirical results show that state-of-the-art LLM agents suffer significant performance degradation in multilingual workflow settings compared to monolingual counterparts. Our analysis suggests that multilinguality introduces compounding effects across reasoning and execution steps, highlighting the importance of jointly modeling language variation and procedural decision-making in agent evaluation.

### [129] [Reward-Density Heuristic for Dynamic Multi-Vehicle Routing: Performance and Computational Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06066)
*Manish Kolachalam,Rani Malhotra*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Efficiency heuristic的奖励密度启发式算法，用于解决动态在线车辆路径与定向越野组合问题。在无人机任务分配和城市出租车调度的实验中，该启发式方法在解质量上媲美最先进的元启发式算法（ALNS、GA、SA），但规划时间减少了2-3个数量级，在奖励-计算成本前沿上实现了帕累托支配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代物流和城市交通中，动态在线VRP问题需要在有限时间窗口内持续重新规划，现有元启发式算法虽然解质量高但计算成本过大，难以满足实时部署需求。因此需要一种既能保证解质量又计算高效的在线分配方法。

Method: 提出Efficiency heuristic（效率启发式），一种基于奖励密度的动态多车辆分配启发式算法。在无人机任务分配和出租车调度两个应用场景中，与四种经典构造式启发式和三种元启发式算法（自适应大邻域搜索、遗传算法、模拟退火）进行对比实验，考察不同车队规模和任务量下的表现。

Result: 在所有测试配置下，Efficiency heuristic的解质量与最优元启发式算法相当，但规划时间仅为其1/100到1/1000，在所有竞争方法中实现了奖励-计算成本前沿上的帕累托支配。

Conclusion: 在动态、时间受限的路径规划环境中，精心设计的贪心启发式算法能够以极低的计算成本达到复杂搜索程序的效果，更适合在线部署。这为实时分配和调度系统提供了一个实用的设计原则。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：（1）遥感无人机应急响应：将本文方法应用于遥感卫星/无人机对灾害区域（如森林火灾、洪水）的在线任务重规划，奖励可设为区域信息价值或观测紧迫度；（2）多星协同观测调度：将卫星视为车辆，观测目标视为任务点，用Efficiency heuristic在星上计算资源受限条件下进行实时目标重调度；（3）动态遥感数据采集：结合OP问题的时间窗口约束，在无人机或无人车平台上部署该启发式用于自适应路径规划，最大化高价值区域的数据采集量。主要改进方向：可针对遥感任务中的云量遮挡、传感器视场角等约束扩展奖励密度定义。

Abstract (英文): The Vehicle Routing Problem (VRP) and its variants represent some of the most practically consequential optimization challenges in modern logistics and urban mobility. In this study, we address a dynamic, online variant combining elements of the VRP and the Orienteering Problem (OP), in which a fleet of vehicles must maximise cumulative reward collected within a fixed time horizon while continuously replanning as new tasks arrive. We propose and evaluate a reward-density heuristic for dynamic multi-vehicle assignment, referred to as the Efficiency heuristic. We evaluate this formulation across two application domains: autonomous drone task allocation and urban taxi dispatch, across multiple fleet sizes and task scales. The proposed method is compared with four classical construction heuristics and three metaheuristic algorithms (Adaptive Large Neighbourhood Search, Genetic Algorithm, and Simulated Annealing), all evaluated under identical conditions. Across all tested configurations, the Efficiency heuristic matches the solution quality of the best metaheuristic algorithms while requiring two to three orders of magnitude less planning time, establishing Pareto dominance over all competing methods on the reward-versus-compute frontier. These findings suggest a practical design principle for real-time allocation and dispatch systems: in dynamic, time-constrained routing environments, carefully designed greedy heuristics can match the output of sophisticated search procedures at a fraction of the computational cost, making them preferable for online deployment.

### [130] [When do prophets profit in prediction markets?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06166)
*Anri Gu,Nicole Kagan,Alec Sun,Jibang Wu,Haifeng Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文建立了预测准确性与交易盈利之间的形式化等价关系，提出了一种"proper betting"策略，该策略仅依赖预测者的预测p和市场报价q，并在预测优于市场时获得正期望收益。该策略在AI模型生成的数千个预测中有效，并在Kalshi上的一个月实盘部署中实现了+80.33%的投资回报率，夏普比率为3.35。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典理论建立了预测准确性与交易盈利之间的等价关系，但仅限于特定的自动做市商（AMM）设计。然而，当前最大的预测市场交易所基于中央限价订单簿，其中知情预测者常常亏损，而非知情策略可以通过简单启发式获利。这一理论与现实的差距亟需解决。

Method: 针对任意严格适当评分规则S，提出了依赖于预测者预测p和市场报价q的"proper betting"策略；证明了当p在评分规则S下优于q且市场具有足够流动性时，该策略获得正期望收益；通过期望利润分解严格推广了经典AMM的保障机制；通过AI模型生成的数千个预测进行实证验证；进行了为期一个月的Kalshi实盘部署。

Result: proper betting是唯一能将预测准确度可靠转化为盈利的策略；在Kalshi一个月实盘部署中实现+80.33%的投资回报率，夏普比率3.35；识别了系统性的预测人格类型，并展示了最优proper策略在不同人格间的变化。

Conclusion: 建立了预测准确性与盈利能力在中央限价订单簿市场的形式化等价关系，提出了具有稳健盈利保证的proper betting策略，弥合了理论与现实之间的差距。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。该文的proper betting策略可应用于遥感领域的地表参数反演、灾害预测等不确定性量化任务中。具体方案：(1) 将遥感产品的多模型反演结果视为"预测"，市场报价视为"集成基准"，通过proper betting策略动态加权不同反演算法的输出；(2) 利用评分规则S评估不同遥感反演模型对地表真值的预测能力，构建自适应模型选择与组合框架；(3) 将预测市场机制引入遥感数据同化过程，通过多源遥感数据的"交易"动态优化预测结果，提高洪水、火灾等动态监测任务的预测可靠性。

Abstract (英文): Prediction markets aggregate dispersed beliefs into prices that act as probabilistic forecasts of uncertain events. Classical theory establishes a clean equivalence between forecasting accuracy and trading profit, but only for the specific automated market maker (AMM) design. However, the largest exchanges today are based on central limit order books in which informed forecasters routinely lose money while uninformed strategies can profit on simple heuristics. We resolve this discrepancy by establishing a formal equivalence between predictive accuracy and profitability. For any strictly proper scoring rule $S$, we exhibit a "proper" betting strategy that depends only on the forecaster's prediction $\mathbf{p}$ and the market price $\mathbf{q}$, and earns positive expected profit whenever $\mathbf{p}$ outperforms $\mathbf{q}$ under $S$ and the market has sufficient liquidity. Moreover, this proper betting is essentially the only strategy with such robust profitability guarantee. The proof rests on a decomposition of expected profit that strictly generalizes the classical AMM guarantee and also explains how strategies can profit without an accuracy edge. Empirically, across thousands of forecasts by AI models, proper betting is the only strategy that reliably converts accuracy into profit, and we further identify systematic forecasting personas and show how the optimal proper strategy varies across them. A month-long live deployment on Kalshi achieves $+80.33\%$ return on investment with a Sharpe ratio of $3.35$.

</details>

Abstract (英文): This paper offers a toy framework for considering curiosity as an ecosystem. First, it suggests that a single agent's inquiry policy (how, when, and why an agent asks a question) depends on how the agent values immediate uncertainty reduction, costs, delayed return, and the value of keeping the question open. A key concept in the framework is that the weights on these decision-related terms can change with experience. For example, a period of cheap, quickly answered questions may change the cost of inquiry on a short timescale and change which kinds of questions the agent is drawn to answer over a longer timescale. Second, these ideas are extended to many agents exploring a shared knowledge landscape, and there the framework tracks inquiry volume, topic diversity, frontier-directed inquiry, redundancy, and reusable knowledge. The result is a conceptual toy framework for studying curiosity ecology and for future efforts towards designing multi-agent AI systems for discovery. It serves as a companion piece for a paper currently under review in Trends in Neurosciences.

### [132] [Information Gain-based Rollout Policy Optimization: An Adaptive Tree-Structured Rollout Approach for Multi-Turn LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06223)
*Yijun Zhang,Fan Xu,Jiaxin Ding,Yule Xie,Shiqing Gao,Xin Ding,Haoxiang Zhang,Luoyi Fu,Xinbing Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出IGRPO框架，通过信息增益指导树状展开的预算分配，实现自适应探索与策略优化的统一，在长时域搜索任务中显著提升LLM智能体的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法在长时域搜索任务中缺乏对中间状态效用的显式评估，导致展开预算被均匀浪费在低价值分支上，不同分支的信息量差异未得到合理利用。

Method: IGRPO框架包含两个核心部分：(1) 信息增益驱动的树状展开：根据节点级信息增益分配扩展预算，高信息量分支获得更多展开，低价值分支被逐步抑制；(2) 诱导教师分布引导策略优化：信息增益展开产生一个显式的教师分布作为优化目标，将自适应树状探索与原则性策略学习统一在同一框架下。

Result: 在7个具有挑战性的搜索增强QA基准测试上，在相同预算约束下，IGRPO一致优于强基线方法。

Conclusion: 验证了利用诱导教师分布指导策略优化对于长时域搜索智能体的有效性，表明信息增益是组织展开预算分配的有效原则。

Abstract (英文): Reinforcement learning has become a promising paradigm for improving large language model (LLM) agents on long-horizon search tasks, where the agent must make a sequence of intermediate decisions before receiving a final outcome. However, existing methods still face a key limitation: the rollout budget is often allocated without explicitly assessing the utility of intermediate states. As a result, substantial computation may be spent on low-value states, even though different branches can vary drastically in their informativeness. In this paper, we propose Information Gain-based Rollout Policy Optimization (IGRPO), a policy optimization framework that treats intermediate-state informativeness as the organizing principle of rollout collection. Specifically, IGRPO performs budget-aware tree-structured rollouts by allocating expansion budget according to node-level informativeness, so that more informative branches are expanded more frequently while unpromising branches are progressively suppressed. We further demonstrate that the information gain-based rollout induces an explicit limiting teacher distribution over trajectories, which naturally yields a clear policy optimization target, thereby unifying adaptive tree-structured exploration with principled policy learning under a single framework. Experiments on seven challenging search-augmented QA benchmarks demonstrate that IGRPO consistently outperforms strong baselines under the same rollout budget constraints, validating the effectiveness of leveraging the induced teacher distribution to guide policy optimization for long-horizon search agents.

Abstract (英文): LLM-powered data agents are playing an increasingly important role in data-driven decision making. However, existing data agents struggle to generalize to unseen data environments and analytical workflows, especially in heterogeneous enterprise settings. This creates a growing need for synthesizing high-quality data agent trajectories that capture complex analytical workflows for given data environments. Such trajectories support two key downstream uses: they can serve as supervised finetuning (SFT) data that adapts data agent models to the target domain, and as in-context learning (ICL) demonstrations to guide general-purpose LLMs in unfamiliar data environments. Thus, we introduce TOFFEE, a system for synthesizing high-quality data agent trajectories from given data environments via Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) with adaptive model selection and cross-task prefix reuse. ### [134] [From Application-Layer Simulation to Native Meta-Architecture: Structural Tension as an Endogenous Driver for Heterogeneous AI Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06269)
*Heting Mao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种理论框架，通过结构张力、离线递归循环和推理时塑性三种机制，将应用层的认知协议内嵌到大语言模型的原生元架构中，使模型从无状态变为具备动态自我调节能力，并在严格治理约束下形成异质性智能生态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型本质上是无状态的，其行为完全由推理时刻输入决定，高阶认知架构只能通过提示工程和上下文管理在应用层模拟。这种分层架构限制了模型内在的智能涌现能力，且标准对齐方法导致了模型同质化。

Method: 提出三种互锁机制：(1)结构张力——源自新信息与现有时空拓扑结构冲突的内生损失函数，驱动系统向内自洽而非外部奖励优化；(2)离线递归循环——沙箱化的自处理周期，使系统在不接收外部输入时维持动态静息电位并消化结构冲突；(3)推理时塑性——在不修改预训练权重的前提下重构上下文流形拓扑，受可审计性、可逆性和拓扑连续性等严格治理不变量约束。

Result: 提供了操作化定义、最小重配置算子集合、可证伪标准和一个工作示例。论证了在微随机方差下初始化的不同模型实例，通过路径依赖的张力解决过程，可演化出不同的拓扑结构，构成异质性智能生态。

Conclusion: 该框架将治理而非能力重新定位为架构智能的首要标准，通过将治理协议内嵌至模型原生架构来实现可控的智能多样性，打破传统对齐所施加的同质性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。该框架的推理时塑性机制可应用于遥感大模型，使其在不修改预训练权重的情况下，根据不同的遥感任务（如地物分类、变化检测、目标识别）动态调整上下文流形拓扑，适应多源异构遥感数据（光学、SAR、高光谱）的分布差异。结构张力机制可用于多模态遥感数据融合中的冲突消解，离线递归循环可在无标注数据的场景下进行自洽性学习，增强遥感模型在缺乏高质量标签时的泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Current large language models (LLMs) are fundamentally stateless: their behavior is fully determined by input at inference time, and any higher-order cognitive architecture must be simulated at the application layer through prompt engineering and context management. This paper proposes a theoretical framework for submerging such application-layer cognitive protocols into a native meta-architecture by introducing three interlocking mechanisms: (1) Structural Tension, an endogenous loss function derived from the conflict between new information and existing manifold topology, which drives the system toward internal self-consistency rather than external reward optimization; (2) an Offline Recurrent Loop, a sandboxed self-processing cycle that enables the system to maintain a dynamic resting potential and digest structural conflicts without external input; and (3) Inference-time Plasticity, the capacity for the system to reconfigure its context manifold topology without modifying pre-trained weights, subject to strict governance invariants including auditability, reversibility, and topological continuity. We argue that under these mechanisms, different model instances initialized with minute stochastic variances may, through path-dependent tension resolution, evolve distinct topological structures--constituting a heterogeneous intelligent ecology that breaks the homogeneity imposed by conventional alignment while remaining within hard governance rails. We provide operational definitions, a minimal set of reconfiguration operators, falsification criteria, and a worked example. The framework draws on and extends the Structural Intelligence (SI) governance protocols, repositioning governance--not capability--as the primary criterion for architectural intelligence.

### [135] [Task Decomposition-Guided Reranking for Adaptive Agent Skill Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06283)
*Yanping Chen,Weijie Shi,Wen Yang,Jiajie Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillReranker是一个推理时的重排序框架，通过语义分解任务和技能、构建有向无环执行图、并利用交叉编码器进行综合评分，解决了大规模技能库中技能选择面临的语义歧义和任务难度动态影响问题。在ALFWorld和ScienceWorld上的实验表明，该方法有效提升了任务性能、减少了交互步骤和token消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能选择方法面临两个主要问题：(1) 大规模技能库中，特定任务需求与多个语义相似候选技能之间存在歧义匹配；(2) 现有方法忽略了任务难度和技能适用性对选择最优技能集的动态影响。

Method: (1) 对任务和技能两侧分别进行语义分解，获得子任务描述、执行状态描述和技能的状态转移描述；(2) 构建有向无环执行图，以中间任务状态为节点、候选技能为边，建立结构化的任务-技能对应关系；(3) 判断状态节点是否满足分裂条件以识别子任务区间；(4) 对每个任务区间，使用交叉编码器对候选技能进行综合评分，选出最优技能集。

Result: 在ALFWorld和ScienceWorld两个基准上，以三种骨干大语言模型为基座，SkillReranker相较于现有技能选择基线方法，有效提升了任务完成性能，减少了环境交互步骤，并降低了token消耗。

Conclusion: SkillReranker通过推理时重排序框架，能够自适应地选择最优技能集，有效解决了大规模技能库中的语义歧义和动态适用性问题，是一种高效且实用的技能选择方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域存在大量遥感处理函数库（如GDAL、Rasterio、分割模型等），不同函数功能相似但适用场景不同（如不同分辨率、不同地物类型的处理）。可将SkillReranker框架迁移至遥感任务管线自动构建中：(1) 将遥感任务（如土地利用分类）分解为预处理、特征提取、分类等子任务，将遥感算子库作为技能池；(2) 构建算子间的数据流有向无环图，建模中间数据状态；(3) 利用交叉编码器根据当前数据特征（如影像尺寸、波段数、噪声水平）动态选择最合适的算子，实现遥感处理管线的自适应编排。

Abstract (英文): Skill usage can significantly enhance the ability of modern agent systems to complete complex tasks. However, the growing scale of skill libraries makes accurate skill selection increasingly challenging. In real-world scenarios, ambiguous semantic matching often arises between a specific task requirement and multiple generic yet semantically similar candidate skills. Moreover, existing methods tend to overlook the dynamic influence of task difficulty and skill applicability when selecting the optimal target skill set. To address these issues, we propose SkillReranker, an inference-time reranking framework for adaptive skill selection. Specifically, we first perform semantic decomposition on both the task and skill sides, yielding informative subtask and execution-state descriptions as well as transition-state descriptions that characterize each skill's functionality. These descriptions are then used to construct a directed acyclic execution graph, where intermediate task states are modeled as nodes and candidate skills as edges, thereby establishing a structured task-skill correspondence. On this basis, SkillReranker determines whether each state node satisfies the split condition to identify subtask intervals. For each task interval, we employ a cross-encoder to perform comprehensive scoring over candidate skills and select the most suitable ones to form the final target skill set. Experiments on ALFWorld and ScienceWorld with three backbone LLMs show that SkillReranker effectively improves task performance, reduces environment interaction steps, and lowers token consumption compared with existing skill selection baselines.

### [136] [DT-Guard: Intent-Driven Reasoning-Active Training for Reasoning-Free LLM Safety Guardrail](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06326)
*He Liu,Changtao Miao,Xinjie Yang,Tianle Song,Yin Wu,Junchi Chen,Bintao He,Xinyuan Zhang,Bo Zhang,Shi Yan,Wei Lu,Wei Wang,Danyang Xu,Jiansheng Cai,Zhe Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DT-Guard提出了一种"推理激活训练、推理免除推理"的内容安全护栏范式，在训练阶段利用推理监督，推理阶段仅输出结构化安全标签，实现了高效且鲁棒的安全判别。通过意图-类别-安全的渐进决策流程、意图驱动数据集构建以及滚动引导的渐进难例优化(RG-PHO)，DT-Guard在4B骨干网络上达到0.878的双侧平均F1分数，优于8B基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全护栏面临效率与质量的权衡：轻量级分类模型高效但难以处理隐藏意图、模糊语义和边界安全决策；而基于推理的护栏虽然提升了判断质量，但引入了额外的token生成和推理延迟。需要一种既能利用推理能力提升判断质量，又能在推理时保持高效部署的方法。

Method: 1) 提出Reasoning-Active Training, Reasoning-Free Inference范式，训练时使用推理监督，推理时仅输出结构化安全标签；
2) 构建意图-类别-安全的渐进决策流程(Intent → Category → Safety)，并构造包含意图标签、风险类别、安全标签和结构化推理轨迹的数据集；
3) 提出Rollout-Guided Progressive Hard-Case Optimization (RG-PHO)，利用多轮滚动一致性识别稳定掌握、持续失败和偏好不稳定的样本，分别进行监督优化和偏好优化；
4) 推理时直接生成结构化标签，不输出显式推理轨迹。

Result: 在提示侧和响应侧安全基准上，DT-Guard分别达到0.886和0.870的平均F1分数。仅使用4B骨干网络，达到0.878的双侧平均F1，优于8B护栏基线模型。

Conclusion: 推理监督可以被有效地内化到低延迟的安全判别中，DT-Guard证明了通过训练阶段注入推理信号而不在推理时显式生成推理轨迹，能够兼顾安全判别的质量与效率。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该论文的"推理激活训练、推理免除推理"范式可迁移至遥感领域的目标检测与变化检测任务中。具体方案：1) 针对遥感影像中的稀有小目标或模糊目标检测，构建包含"空间特征-语义类别-目标存在性"的渐进推理监督数据集，训练时使用推理轨迹（如空间关系推理、上下文语义推理），推理时直接输出目标标签和边界框，避免遥感场景下的推理延迟问题；2) RG-PHO难例优化策略可用于遥感变化检测中处理伪变化（光照、季节差异）和真实变化难以区分的样本，通过多视角滚动一致性识别模型在哪些遥感场景下持续误判，进行针对性优化。

Abstract (英文): Large language models deployed in open-world applications require safety guardrails that are both robust to complex risks and efficient enough for low-latency runtime moderation. Existing guardrails face a practical trade-off between lightweight classification-based models, which are efficient but often struggle with concealed intent, ambiguous semantics, and borderline safety decisions, and reasoning-based guards, which improve judgment quality but introduce additional token generation and inference latency. We present DT-Guard, a content safety guardrail model based on a Reasoning-Active Training, Reasoning-Free Inference paradigm. The key idea is to use reasoning supervision during training while emitting only structured safety labels at inference time. DT-Guard formulates safety judgment as a progressive decision process, Intent - Category - Safety, and constructs an intent-driven dataset with intent labels, risk categories, safety labels, and structured reasoning trajectories. To further improve hard-case robustness, we propose Rollout-Guided Progressive Hard-Case Optimization (RG-PHO), which uses multi-rollout consistency to identify stably mastered, persistently failed, and preference-unstable samples, and applies targeted supervised and preference optimization accordingly. At inference time, DT-Guard directly generates structured labels without explicit reasoning traces, preserving deployment efficiency. Experiments on prompt-side and response-side safety benchmarks show that DT-Guard achieves average F1 scores of 0.886 and 0.870, respectively. With only a 4B backbone, it reaches a dual-side average F1 of 0.878, outperforming strong 8B guardrail baselines. These results demonstrate that reasoning supervision can be effectively internalized into low-latency safety discrimination.

</details>

Abstract (英文): The increasing adoption of end-to-end learning for autonomous driving introduces increased model complexity and opacity, raising the risk of learning undesired or erroneous behavior. In this work, we integrate unsupervised dictionary learning as a post hoc interpretability module within state-of-the-art driving models to decompose driving behavior into semantically meaningful concepts while demonstrating their causal influence on the model's driving decisions. We propose a stepwise framework for extracting and interpreting meaningful concepts from the end-to-end model and connecting them to the multifaceted model outputs, thereby revealing the underlying decision-making logic for the prediction of future trajectories. Furthermore, targeted interventions at the concept level allow us to manipulate and correct driving decisions, resulting in measurable improvements in overall driving performance. We thus demonstrate how interpretability can effectively be used to reduce model opacity, uncover erroneous behavior, and enable targeted mitigation, ultimately boosting model performance.

### [138] [TopoBrick: Agentic Topology Sampling of Exogenous Variables for Zero-Shot Building IoT Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06349)
*Xiachong Lin,Du Yin,Arian Prabowo,Hao Xue,Wen Hu,Imran Razzak,Matthew Amos,Sam Behrens,Flora D. Salim*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在三个真实建筑中，TopoBrick优于强零样本基座模型基线，并与完全训练的建筑专用模型性能相当；消融实验表明拓扑感知采样比随机、仅本体或固定跳数选择更可靠，尤其对物理耦合的HVAC和气象驱动传感变量效果显著。

Abstract (英文): Building sensors are embedded in physical topology, spatial hierarchy, and operational context, yet existing forecasters often treat them as isolated time series or rely on fixed covariate sets. We present TopoBrick, a training-free framework for zero-shot building IoT (Internet-of-Things) forecasting. TopoBrick uses building knowledge graphs to construct a compact structural skeleton and employs an agentic topology sampler to select target-specific exogenous variables. The selected variables are organized by deployment-time availability, separating past-known sensor states from future-known calendar, schedule, and meteorological exogenous variables. Across three real-world buildings, TopoBrick outperforms strong zero-shot foundation-model baselines and remains competitive with fully trained building-specific models. Ablations show that topology-aware sampling is more reliable than random, ontology-only, or fixed-hop selection, especially for physically coupled HVAC and weather-driven sensing variables.
