### [177] [A Stability-Driven Framework for Automated Operational Crop Mapping Using Optical and Radar Satellite Image Time Series](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132149)
*Maryam Choukri,Yacine Bouroubi,Jamal-Eddine Ouzemou,Abdelghani Chehbouni,Ahmed Laamrani*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究系统评估了作物分类中多时相遥感特征的年际稳定性，提出了基于可靠性指数(RI)和自动选择分数(AuSS)的自动化特征选择框架。通过Pareto优化从156个特征中筛选出6个稳定指标(VH, VV, NDVI, NDRE, GCVI, RVI)，在保持87.4%准确率的同时，显著提升了跨年泛化能力，证明特征稳定性是构建 operational 作物分类系统的关键准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有作物分类研究虽广泛使用特征重要性进行模型优化，但鲜有系统探究其年际稳定性，导致在部署可靠监测系统时存在关键空白。研究旨在从识别“最重要”特征转向系统评估和量化特征的年际稳定性，以实现自动化分类。

Method: 利用摩洛哥6个农业年度(2018-2025)的Sentinel-1和Sentinel-2数据，提取12个月度合成影像的156个多传感器特征。通过统计指标、聚类分析和新型复合指数(RI和AuSS)评估特征稳定性，结合Pareto优化自动筛选最小稳定特征集，并采用Voting Ensemble验证性能。

Result: 最具判别力的特征(NDVI、VH、VV)也最不稳定，而稳定特征(NDRE、MSI、NDMI)预测能力有限。层次聚类识别出四种行为类型(主导稳定型、表现波动型、稳定次要型和噪声)。Pareto分析筛选的6个指标(VH, VV, NDVI, NDRE, GCVI, RVI)捕获57.2%的累计预测重要性，Voting Ensemble在时间迁移中保持87.4%准确率和87.2% F1-score，波动极小。

Conclusion: 特征稳定性不仅是诊断指标，更是 operational 设计的基础准则。本研究的度量驱动框架可用于构建对年际气候变异更具鲁棒性的自动化作物分类系统，无需年度重训练或专家干预。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感领域论文，改进方向包括：(1) 将RI和AuSS框架迁移至其他作物类型或区域(如中国复杂种植区)验证泛化能力；(2) 引入SAR极化参数或高光谱特征扩展特征库；(3) 结合深度学习特征自动提取与稳定性筛选融合；(4) 将该稳定性评估框架推广到森林监测、湿地分类等其他遥感领域；(5) 考虑气候异常年份(如极端干旱)进一步验证稳定特征的鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Operational crop mapping requires classifiers capable of robust generalization across years. While feature importance is routinely used for model optimization, its temporal stability has rarely been systematically investigated, creating a critical gap in deploying reliable monitoring systems. This study moves beyond identifying “most important” features to systematically evaluate and quantify their inter-annual stability for enabling automated classification. Using six agricultural years (2018, 2019, 2020, 2023, 2024 and 2025) of Sentinel-1 and Sentinel-2 data over Morocco, we extracted 156 multi-sensor features across 12 monthly composites and analyzed their importance stability through statistical metrics, clustering, and novel composite indices: the Reliability Index (RI) and Automatic Selection Score (AuSS). This framework automates feature selection by ranking features with RI and AuSS and then applying Pareto optimization to identify a minimal stable feature set—without requiring annual retraining or expert intervention. Our analysis confirms a fundamental tension: the most discriminative features (e.g., NDVI, VH, VV) are also the most volatile, while stable features (e.g., NDRE, MSI, NDMI) offer modest predictive power. Hierarchical clustering revealed four behavioral typologies (Dominant Stable, Performant Volatile, Stable Minor, and Noise), guiding strategic feature management. Crucially, a Pareto analysis demonstrated that a refined portfolio of 6 indices (VH, VV, NDVI, NDRE, GCVI, RVI) captures 57.2% of cumulative predictive importance, filtering out inter-annual noise while preserving discriminative signal. The Voting Ensemble leveraging this Stable Portfolio maintained consistent high accuracy (87.4% accuracy, 87.2% F1-score) with minimal performance degradation during temporal transfer, while models based on volatile top features exhibited significant drops. Entropy analysis confirmed that all features in the Stable Portfolio provide consistent informational certainty, indicating that stability-driven selection does not increase model uncertainty. We conclude that feature stability is not merely a diagnostic metric but a foundational criterion for operational design. We propose a practical, metrics-driven framework for constructing automated crop classification systems that are more resilient to inter-annual climate variability.

</details>


### [178] [Bloom or Bluff? Benchmarking Vision–Language Models Against Classical Machine Learning for Harmful Algal Bloom Detection from Satellite Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132147)
*Harsh Deep Singh Narula*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文评估了三种商用视觉语言模型（GPT-4o、GPT-5.5、Claude Sonnet 4.6）与经典机器学习分类器（RF、SVM、XGBoost）在从Sentinel-2卫星影像检测和分类伊利湖西部有害藻华（HAB）严重程度上的表现。结果表明，VLM在二分类和严重度分类上均不如经典分类器，主要受限于RGB通道的光谱信息不足以及模型训练分布偏向陆地场景。多光谱SVM表现最佳（F1=0.833），而VLM存在高假阳性率（73-93%）和预测分布偏向"中等"类别的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索视觉语言模型在定量遥感中的应用潜力，评估其能否替代传统机器学习方法进行有害藻华监测，为实际水文遥感任务提供方法选择依据。

Method: 收集2019-2025年七个藻华季节中NOAA HAB-OFS识别的40个藻华事件的Sentinel-2影像，分别以三波段RGB合成和十波段多光谱反射率表示。使用三种商业VLM进行零样本预测，同时训练RF、SVM、XGBoost作为对照。评估任务包括二分类藻华检测和四分类严重程度分类。

Result: VLM的F1 score（0.69-0.75）低于最佳RGB分类器RF（0.76）和始终预测基线（0.77），假阳性率高达73-93%（RGB分类器为27-40%）。VLM将60-70%预测归为"中等"类别，严重分类精确匹配准确率仅0.20-0.225，远低于经典分类器的0.44-0.59。多光谱SVM在所有指标上最优（F1=0.833，假阳性率27%，准确率0.795）。多光谱相比RGB特征使SVM准确率提升12个百分点。多光谱分类器将NDCI和FAI等叶绿素指数列为重要特征，而RGB分类器只能依赖红波段变异性和绿像素比例。

Conclusion: 现成的视觉语言模型在定量水色遥感中面临两个根本限制：标准RGB通道的光谱信息不足，以及模型训练数据以陆地场景为主与水体光学条件不匹配。基于多光谱数据的领域专用分类器仍然是藻华监测和水质反演更合适的工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。本文是针对遥感的具体应用研究，可从以下方面改进：(1) 使用多光谱预训练的视觉编码器（如SatMAE、SpectralGPT）替代VLM的RGB基础编码器，扩展模型的光谱感知能力；(2) 针对水体场景对VLM进行指令微调或少样本学习，缓解陆地分布漂移问题；(3) 引入物理信息约束（如叶绿素a反演公式）作为VLM推理的先验知识；(4) 结合多光谱分类器的特征重要性分析结果，设计可解释的VLM提示策略，引导模型关注NDCI、FAI等有效光谱指数。

Abstract (英文): In recent years, there has been growing interest in applying vision–language models (VLMs) to quantitative remote sensing. This study evaluates whether three commercial VLMs (GPT-4o, GPT-5.5, and Claude Sonnet 4.6) can detect and classify the severity of harmful algal blooms (HABs) from Sentinel-2 satellite imagery of western Lake Erie and compares them against classical machine learning classifiers (Random Forest (RF), Support Vector Machine (SVM), and eXtreme Gradient Boosting (XGBoost)) trained on both a three-band red, green, blue (RGB) composite representation of the imagery and a 10-band multi-spectral reflectance representation. Forty bloom events identified from the National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration (NOAA) Harmful Algal Bloom Operational Forecast System (HAB-OFS) severity assessments were assembled into the evaluation dataset, spanning seven bloom seasons (2019–2025). For binary bloom detection, the VLMs did not match the classical RGB classifiers; their F1 scores (0.69–0.75) fell below the best RGB classifier (Random Forest, 0.76) and below a trivial always-present baseline (F1 = 0.77), and they carried false positive rates of 73–93% on bloom-absent images, against 27–40% for the RGB classifiers. The VLMs reached high recall by labeling most scenes as bloom-positive, which makes them operationally unreliable in this configuration. For severity classification, the VLMs assigned 60–70% of their predictions to the “moderate” category regardless of actual conditions and identified at most one of the two severe blooms, whereas the classical classifiers tracked the ground-truth distribution and delivered two to nearly three times the exact-match accuracy (0.44–0.59 vs. 0.20–0.225). The strongest method across all metrics was the multi-spectral SVM (F1 = 0.833, false positive rate 27%, accuracy 0.795). Switching the same SVM from RGB to multi-spectral features raised accuracy from 0.675 to 0.795, a 12-percentage-point gain that measures the spectral information carried by red-edge and shortwave infrared bands that are accessible through multi-spectral sensors but unavailable to standard VLM vision encoders. Feature-importance analysis showed that the multi-spectral classifiers ranked chlorophyll-specific indices, the Normalized Difference Chlorophyll Index (NDCI) and the Floating Algae Index (FAI), among their top predictors, the same signatures used in established operational algorithms, while the RGB classifiers relied on red-channel variability and green-dominant pixel fractions because RGB inputs cannot compute those indices. Two compounded limitations therefore constrain off-the-shelf VLMs for aquatic remote sensing: the limited spectral information available through standard RGB channels and a mismatch between the land-dominated training distributions of these models and aquatic optical conditions. Domain-specific classifiers operating on multi-spectral data remain the more suitable tools for continued development of HAB monitoring and water-quality retrieval.

### [179] [Spatiotemporal Dynamics of Dongting Lake During the Flood Season Using Long Time Series SAR Imagery on Google Earth Engine](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132150)
*Wenhua Li,Liangyu Chen,Yunfei Zhang,Bing Sui,Dongsheng Du,Yu Han,Leishi Chen*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于极化合成孔径雷达（SAR）数据的水体提取方法，结合最大类间方差算法、遗传算法阈值优化和动态形态学操作，利用2015-2025年Sentinel-1洪季时间序列数据在洞庭湖进行验证。该方法总体精度超过0.93，并分析了洪水期水体面积呈先增后减的波动趋势（2020年峰值2202.26 km²，2025年降至614.04 km²），主要由极端气象事件驱动。水体面积与水位呈强相关（R²=0.931），流量和降水与水体面积正相关，而温度和日照时长影响微弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 洪水期湖泊时空动态对生态安全和社会经济发展至关重要，需要持续的高分辨率监测。然而，降水波动和泥沙浊度显著改变水质，且水体与洪泛区湿地之间的模糊边界给精准监测带来挑战，现有方法难以在复杂环境下实现稳定、准确的水体提取。

Method: 提出了一种基于极化SAR数据的水体提取方法：利用最大类间方差算法（Otsu）进行初始分割，通过遗传算法优化分割阈值，并采用动态形态学操作细化边界细节。方法在Google Earth Engine平台上使用2015-2025年Sentinel-1洪季时间序列数据进行验证。

Result: 该方法在不同年份和季节均实现了稳定准确的水体提取，总体精度超过0.93。洪水期水体面积呈先增后减的波动趋势，2020年达到峰值2202.26 km²，2025年降至614.04 km²。水体面积与水位呈强相关（R²=0.931），流量和降水与水体面积正相关，温度和日照时长影响微弱。空间上呈现北深南浅、中部高地隔开的淹没格局。

Conclusion: 本研究支持洞庭湖流域的洪涝调控，并为利用长时序SAR数据分析湖泊动态提供了一个稳健的框架。该方法对无资料地区的水位估算提供了定量参考。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是一篇遥感水体提取论文，改进方向包括：(1) 可引入更先进的深度学习语义分割模型（如U-Net、DeepLabV3+）替代Otsu初始分割，提升复杂边界处理能力；(2) 可融合多源遥感数据（如光学影像Landsat/Sentinel-2与SAR结合），利用光学数据弥补SAR在水体边缘模糊问题上的不足；(3) 遗传算法阈值优化可进一步替换为粒子群优化或贝叶斯优化以提高收敛效率；(4) 动态形态学操作可引入自适应结构元素大小，根据水域特征自动调整；(5) 可扩展到其他大型湖泊或湿地系统进行跨区域验证，增强方法泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Flood-season lake spatiotemporal dynamics are vital for ecological security and socioeconomic development, requiring consistent high-resolution monitoring. However, precipitation fluctuations and sediment turbidity significantly alter water quality, while blurred boundaries between water and floodplain wetlands challenge precise monitoring. To address these issues, this study proposes a water body extraction method leveraging polarimetric Synthetic Aperture Radar data. utilizes the maximum between-class variance algorithm for initial segmentation, optimizes the threshold via a genetic algorithm, and employs dynamic morphological operations to refine boundary details. The method was validated using 2015–2025 Sentinel-1 flood-season time series of Dongting Lake on Google Earth Engine. The results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves stable and accurate water extraction across various years and seasons, with an overall accuracy surpassing 0.93, confirming its robustness and broad applicability. Furthermore, the spatiotemporal hydrodynamics and driving mechanisms of Dongting Lake were analyzed by integrating the extracted water areas with multi-source data, including water level, precipitation, discharge, temperature, and sunshine duration. Findings indicate that the flood-season water area exhibited a fluctuating trend, initially increasing and subsequently decreasing, peaking at 2202.26 km2 in 2020 and dropping to 614.04 km2 in 2025, a pattern primarily driven by extreme meteorological events such as heavy rainfall and prolonged droughts. Spatially, inundation patterns were characterized by deeper water in the north and shallower depths in the south, separated by a topographically higher central region. Regression analysis revealed a robust correlation between water area and water level with an R2 of 0.931, providing a quantitative reference for water level estimation in ungauged regions. Additionally, discharge and precipitation were positively correlated with water area, whereas temperature and sunshine duration exerted a negligible influence. This study supports flood regulation in the Dongting Lake basin and provides a robust framework for analyzing lake dynamics using long-term SAR data.

### [180] [Robust Space-Object Association and Recursive Estimation for Ground-Based Optical Observation Under Degraded Orbital Priors and Site-Position Uncertainty](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132139)
*Yan Tingkai,X G Liu,Shuaipeng Hou,Jianing Yang,Hui Li,Fei Xing*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在地面光学观测中，面对退化轨道先验、不精确站点位置和多候选目标条件下的单目标关联与递归估计鲁棒框架。通过将图像候选点转换到预测对齐切线平面、构建运动-光度五维NIS选通统计量以及三维解耦卡尔曼更新，在四组真实数据上实现了85.86%~100%的正确关联率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地面光学观测对空间目标监测至关重要，但在轨道先验退化、站点位置信息不精确以及每帧存在多个点源候选时，可靠关联极具挑战性。现有方法在这些条件下关联性能下降，亟需一种鲁棒的关联与估计框架。

Method: 1) 将图像域候选点转换为单位视线方向(LOS)，并在预测对齐的切平面内表示局部偏差；2) 将角度测量噪声和站点位置不确定性传播到局部协方差模型；3) 构建联合评估局部位置、伪速度和光度一致性的五维(5D)归一化新息平方(NIS)选通统计量；4) 关联后采用仅利用单帧位置和光度测量的三维解耦卡尔曼更新进行递归估计。

Result: 在四组真实地面光学卫星观测序列（包括两个静态场景和两个动态场景）上，正确关联率分别达到100.00%、100.00%、100.00%和85.86%。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架在退化轨道先验和不精确站点位置条件下提高了关联可靠性，同时保持了稳定的递归估计性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该框架可直接应用于遥感领域的光学卫星观测与空间目标监视任务。改进方向：1) 可将五维NIS选通扩展到包含光谱信息的高维特征，提升对相似光度目标的分辨能力；2) 引入深度学习目标检测前端替代传统点源提取，提高密集场景下的候选点质量；3) 将动态场景中的85.86%关联率通过加入运动模型自适应切换（如交互多模型IMM）进一步提升；4) 对于遥感图像序列中的多目标跟踪任务，该框架的局部协方差建模思路可迁移至星上实时处理场景。

Abstract (英文): Ground-based optical observation is a key sensing modality for space-object monitoring, but reliable association becomes challenging when orbital priors are degraded, site-position information is imprecise, and each frame contains multiple point-source candidates. This paper proposes a robust framework for single-target association among multiple image candidates and recursive estimation under such conditions. The method first converts image-domain candidates into unit line-of-sight (LOS) directions and represents their local deviations in a prediction-aligned tangent plane. Angular measurement noise and site-position uncertainty are then propagated into the local covariance model. Based on this representation, a kinematic-photometric five-dimensional (5D) normalized innovation squared (NIS) gating statistic is constructed by jointly evaluating local position, pseudo-velocity, and photometric consistency. After association, a three-dimensional decoupled Kalman update is performed using only the single-frame position and photometric measurements. Experiments on four real ground-based optical satellite observation sequences, including two static scenarios and two dynamic scenarios, show correct association rates of 100.00%, 100.00%, 100.00%, and 85.86%, respectively. These results demonstrate that the proposed framework improves association reliability under degraded orbital priors and imprecise site-position information while maintaining stable recursive estimation.

### [181] [High-Resolution Soil Organic Carbon Content Mapping in Typical Lakeside Oases Using Sentinel-2 Images and Machine Learning Models](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132143)
*Hui Li,LI Xin-guo,Xiangyu Ge*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究集成 Sentinel-2 影像与多种环境协变量，构建四种机器学习模型，实现了博斯腾湖 oasis 10米分辨率土壤有机碳（SOC）高精度制图。Cubist 模型表现最优（R²=0.8166），BSI、地表粗糙度和 NDRE1 是 SOC 空间分布的主要驱动因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 干旱湖泊 oasis 是脆弱的 aquatic-terrestrial 过渡生态系统，现有模型对高度破碎化的 oasis 景观适应性差，且缺乏针对典型博斯腾湖 oasis 的高分辨率 SOC 空间产品，难以满足农业管理和碳库评估的精准需求。

Method: 基于153个表层土壤样本（0–20 cm，分层随机采样），集成 Sentinel-2 影像与地形、生物气候、光谱环境协变量，构建 RF、XGBoost、SVR（RBF核）、Cubist 四种机器学习模型，通过5折交叉验证评估性能，以 SHAP 分析识别主导驱动因子，最终生成10米分辨率 SOC 空间分布图。

Result: SOC含量范围2.37–20.63 g·kg⁻¹（均值10.59 g·kg⁻¹），空间变异中等（CV=34.86%）。Cubist 模型精度最高（R²=0.8166, RMSE=1.5812 g·kg⁻¹, MAE=0.9247 g·kg⁻¹）。制图显示东部井灌农田 SOC 高值、oasis 边缘裸地和盐渍化区域低值的空间格局。BSI、地表粗糙度和 NDRE1 为SOC主要驱动因子。

Conclusion: 本研究填补了干旱湖泊 oasis 高精度 SOC 制图的不足，所提框架可推广至全球其他破碎化干旱景观，为精准农业和可持续土地管理提供可靠空间数据与可扩展技术方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为遥感与机器学习结合的 SOC 制图论文，可从以下方面改进：1) 引入时空融合模型（如 ESTARFM）增强多时相 Sentinel-2 光谱特征；2) 增加 GaoFen-6 或 Planet 等高分辨率影像补充纹理与空间结构信息；3) 尝试深度学习模型（如 CNN、ResNet）捕获复杂非线性空间关系；4) 集成 GEDI/SMAP 等主动遥感数据以提升深层 SOC 估算能力；5) 扩展至时序分析以揭示 oasis SOC 时空动态变化规律。

Abstract (英文): Accurate high-resolution mapping of soil organic carbon (SOC) is essential for agricultural management and carbon pool assessment in arid lakeside oases, a fragile aquatic-terrestrial transition ecosystem. However, targeted high-precision SOC mapping for typical lakeside oases remains insufficient: existing models have poor adaptability to the highly fragmented oasis landscapes, and fine-resolution SOC spatial products for the representative Bosten Lake oasis are lacking. To address this inadequacy, we integrated Sentinel-2 imagery with topographic, bioclimatic, and spectral environmental covariates and developed four machine learning models (Random Forest, XGBoost, SVR with RBF kernel, Cubist) for SOC prediction, based on 153 topsoil samples (0–20 cm) collected via stratified random sampling in the study area. Model performance was validated through 5-fold cross-validation, the optimal model was selected for 10 m resolution SOC mapping, and dominant driving factors were identified via SHAP analysis. The results showed that SOC content in the study area ranged from 2.37 to 20.63 g·kg−1 (mean = 10.59 g·kg−1), with moderate spatial variability (CV = 34.86%). The Cubist model achieved the highest mapping accuracy (R2 = 0.8166, RMSE = 1.5812 g·kg−1, MAE = 0.9247 g·kg−1). The generated high-resolution SOC map clearly revealed a spatial pattern of high values in the eastern well-irrigated cropland and low values in bare and salinized areas at the oasis edge. The Bare Soil Index (BSI), surface roughness, and Normalized Difference Red Edge Index 1 (NDRE1) were the dominant factors controlling SOC spatial distribution. This study mitigates the inadequacy of high-precision SOC mapping in typical arid lakeside oases, and the proposed framework is readily applicable to other fragmented arid landscapes worldwide and provides reliable spatial data and a scalable technical framework for precision agriculture and sustainable land management in similar fragile ecosystems.

### [182] [Estimating Forest Volume and Forest Volume Change Using Random Forests and Sentinel-2 Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132134)
*Temitope Olaoluwa Omoniyi,Allan Sims,Ronald  E. McRoberts*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究结合国家森林调查数据和Sentinel-2多时相遥感数据，采用随机森林算法，比较了间接法和直接法两种估算策略下森林蓄积量及其变化的精度。结果表明，模型辅助估计的精度是简单估计的约5倍，10m分辨率数据预测略优于20m，直接法在估算变化时标准误更小，但两种方法的变化估计值相似。遥感辅助数据主要提高了变化估计的精度，而非改变变化量本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可靠、精确的森林蓄积量及其变化估计是森林可持续经营、资源评估和长期监测的基础。多时相遥感数据可提高基于概率抽样样地的估算精度，但间接法和直接法两种变化估计策略在方差估计和不确定性传播上存在差异，需进行系统比较。

Method: 基于设计推断框架，将概率抽样的国家森林调查数据与多时相Sentinel-2辅助变量（10m和20m分辨率）相结合，使用随机森林预测算法，分别构建间接法（逐年独立估计后求差）和直接法（以样地变化为响应变量）的模型辅助回归估计量，并采用残差方差估计器进行不确定性评估。

Result: 随机森林模型解释了森林蓄积量约51-62%的变异，RMSE为79-97 m³/ha；10m分辨率数据预测略优于20m，但增益不大。模型辅助估计的标准误远小于简单扩展估计，相对效率提高约5倍。直接法和间接法得到的变化估计值相似，但直接法的标准误更小。

Conclusion: 遥感辅助数据主要提升了森林蓄积量变化估计的精度，而非改变变化估计量的大小。直接法在变化估计中具有更小的标准误，推荐用于森林蓄积量变化的精确估算。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。1）该方法可直接应用于遥感领域中的森林资源监测，建议进一步引入LiDAR或SAR数据（如GEDI、TanDEM-X）作为辅助变量，提升对高蓄积量区域的估测能力。2）可探索深度学习模型（如3D-CNN或时序Transformer）替代随机森林，捕捉更复杂的时空特征，进一步提高模型解释方差。3）研究中10m与20m分辨率差异较小，建议在更大尺度上评估不同分辨率（如Sentinel-1、Landsat 30m）的性价比，优化数据选择策略。4）可将直接法的框架拓展到其他林业遥感监测任务（如生物量、碳储量变化），验证其普适性。

Abstract (英文): Accurate and precise estimation of forest volume and its changes are fundamental for sustainable forest management, resource assessment, and long-term inventory monitoring. Multi-temporal remotely sensed data provide spatial auxiliary information that can substantially increase the precision of estimates of volume and volume change obtained from probability-based field samples. However, methodological differences between indirect and direct change estimation approaches may lead to differences in variance estimation and uncertainty propagation. This study, therefore, compares forest volume and forest volume change estimation under design-based inference by integrating probability-sampled National Forest Inventory (NFI) data with multi-temporal Sentinel-2 auxiliary variables at 10 m and 20 m spatial resolutions, using the random forest (RF) prediction algorithm and both indirect and direct estimation approaches. Forest volume means are estimated for two inventory years, 2013 and 2023. For the indirect approach, simple expansion and model-assisted regression estimators are formulated separately for each year, and change is estimated as the difference between time-specific estimates. For the direct approach, plot-level change is used as the response variable, and model-assisted regression estimators are constructed using changes in auxiliary variables, with residual-based variance estimators. Random forest models using Sentinel-2 auxiliary data explained approximately 51–62% of the variation in forest volume, with RMSE values ranging from about 79 to 97 m3/ha. The 10 m resolution data produced slightly more precise predictions than the 20 m data, though the gain was small relative to the greater processing effort required. Model-assisted estimators using both 10 m and 20 m Sentinel-2 data produced substantially smaller standard errors than simple expansion estimators, with relative efficiency analysis indicating an approximately fivefold gain in efficiency. The direct and indirect model-assisted approaches produced similar estimates of volume change, although the direct approach resulted in smaller standard errors. Overall, remotely sensed auxiliary data primarily improved the precision of forest volume change estimates but not the magnitude of the estimated change.

</details>


### [183] [From Raw EO Data to AI-Ready Datasets: Lowering the Barrier to Geospatial Foundation Model Fine-Tuning](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132152)
*Mattia Santoro,Enrico Boldrini,Stefano Nativi,P. Mazzetti*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个软件库，旨在自动化地理空间基础模型微调所需的数据准备流程，将地理空间数据集转化为高质量、格式统一的输入，从而降低技术门槛，提升GFM在环境监测、城市发展、气候变化等领域的可及性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地理空间基础模型（GFMs）的微调依赖于精心整理的高质量训练数据集，而数据准备工作（如图像筛选、空间格式对齐、标签生成）通常劳动密集且耗时，这一瓶颈限制了GFMs在科学研究和操作应用中的可访问性与可扩展性。

Method: 设计并实现一个软件库，自动化地理空间数据集到GFM微调输入的转换流程，包括图像选择、空间格式统一、标签生成等步骤，确保数据的一致性和高质量，减少人工干预和技术开销。

Result: 该库能够显著减少数据准备的技术负担，提高数据就绪度，使基础模型能够更快、更可靠地适应本地环境挑战和特定领域需求。

Conclusion: 该软件库有效解决了GFM微调中的数据准备瓶颈，推动了基础模型在地理空间领域更广泛、更包容的应用。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该软件库直接针对遥感领域的基础模型微调数据预处理问题，本身就是遥感与软件工程的交叉成果。改进方向：（1）集成多模态数据（如SAR、光学、LiDAR）的统一处理管线；（2）支持主动学习策略，用最少标注样本生成高效微调数据集；（3）加入数据质量评估模块，自动检测云覆盖、几何畸变等常见问题；（4）扩展至时序遥感数据的自动化预处理，支持动态变化检测任务。

Abstract (英文): Geospatial foundation models are a new frontier in artificial intelligence, designed to understand and analyze spatial data at scale. Trained on huge sets of EO data, these models can support a wide range of applications—from monitoring natural disasters to guiding urban development and tracking climate change. To this aim, researchers and practitioners need to fine-tune the foundation models for specific tasks, utilizing a relatively small amount of additional data. As a result, geospatial foundation models are reshaping how we observe, manage, and protect our planet. Fine-tuning a geospatial foundation model requires carefully curated training datasets that reflect specific regions, time periods, or tasks—such as detecting deforestation or mapping urban growth. Yet preparing these datasets is often labor-intensive, involving steps like selecting relevant imagery, aligning spatial formats, and generating accurate labels. In practice, this means that the effectiveness of GFMs hinges on the availability of AI-ready data. This bottleneck limits the accessibility and scalability of GFMs for scientific and operational applications. In this work, we introduce a software library designed to automate these preparatory steps, streamlining the transformation of geospatial datasets into consistent, high-quality inputs for GFM fine-tuning. By reducing technical overhead and ensuring data readiness, the library enables faster, more reliable, and more inclusive adaptation of foundation models to local environmental challenges and specialized domain needs.

### [184] [Prediction of Soil Salinity Parameters in the Songnen Plain Using FOD Processing and Machine Learning from Measured Hyperspectral Reflectance Under Different Surface Conditions](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132146)
*Panpan Niu,X B Zheng,Weitong Zhao,Jianhua Ren*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究通过采集松嫩平原盐碱土壤的裂隙与非裂隙表面高光谱数据，采用分数阶微分（FOD，0-2阶，步长0.1）处理，构建了14种一维、二维和三维FOD光谱指数，利用XGBoost-SHAP进行特征选择，并比较了PLSR、GPR、SVR和RFR四种建模方法的预测性能。结果表明：FOD变换显著增强与EC和pH的相关性；裂隙表面条件下所有模型预测精度均高于非裂隙表面，说明裂隙正向调控光谱信号以增强盐分信息表达；PLSR表现最优，在裂隙表面下EC和pH预测R²分别达0.88和0.76。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前在土壤表面裂隙影响下，光谱与盐分之间的定量关系认识仍十分有限，缺乏系统探究裂隙对光谱-盐分响应机制的研究。

Method: 采集裂隙与非裂隙两种表面状态下盐碱土壤的高光谱数据（350-2500 nm），进行0-2阶（步长0.1）分数阶微分处理；构建14种涵盖一维、二维、三维结构的FOD光谱指数；通过皮尔逊相关分析筛选最优分数阶及波段组合；利用XGBoost-SHAP可解释分析进行特征选择；采用PLSR、GPR、SVR、RFR四种模型进行预测对比。

Result: FOD变换显著提高了与EC和pH的相关性；裂隙表面的所有模型预测精度均优于非裂隙表面；模型性能排序为PLSR > GPR > SVR > RFR；PLSR在裂隙表面下对EC和pH预测最优，R²分别为0.88和0.76，RMSE分别为0.29 dS/m和0.35。

Conclusion: 裂隙对光谱信号具有正向调控作用，可增强盐分信息的表达；本研究加深了对盐碱土壤分数阶光谱响应机制的理解，为区域土壤盐渍化监测提供了方法支撑。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）将该方法的分数阶微分与光谱指数构建框架直接应用于遥感卫星影像（如Sentinel-2、Landsat-8/9），建立星地协同的盐渍化监测模型；（2）将裂隙表面作为关键环境因子纳入遥感反演模型，提升大尺度盐分反演精度；（3）XGBoost-SHAP可解释分析框架可推广至其他土壤属性（如有机质、含水量）的高光谱遥感特征选择中；（4）三维光谱指数的构建思路可借鉴至植被盐胁迫遥感监测，拓展多维度光谱特征挖掘方法。

Abstract (英文): Soil salinization severely restricts ecosystem stability and the sustainable development of agricultural productivity. However, current understanding of the spectral–salinity quantitative relationships under the influence of surface cracking still remains limited. To address this gap, this study collected hyperspectral reflectance data (350–2500 nm) from salt-affected soil in both cracked and uncracked surface conditions across the Songnen Plain, and applied fractional-order differentiation (FOD) processing with orders ranging from 0 to 2 and a step size of 0.1. Based on this, 14 types of FOD spectral indices were constructed, incorporating one-dimensional (1D), two-dimensional (2D), and three-dimensional (3D) structures. For each spectral index, the optimal fractional order and corresponding band combinations were first selected through Pearson correlation analysis for pH and EC under both surface conditions; subsequently, feature selection was performed using XGBoost-SHAP explainable analysis among the 14 optimal indices across different dimensions. Furthermore, the predictive performance of four modeling methods, including partial least squares regression (PLSR), Gaussian process regression (GPR), support vector regression (SVR), and random forest regression (RFR), was evaluated. The results showed that FOD transformations significantly enhanced correlations with EC and pH compared to raw reflectance. All prediction models demonstrated higher prediction accuracy under cracked surface conditions than uncracked surface conditions, indicating that desiccation cracks positively modulate spectral signals to enhance salinity information expression. Across different surface states, model performance generally followed the ranking: PLSR &gt; GPR &gt; SVR &gt; RFR, with PLSR achieving the best predictions for EC and pH under cracked surfaces (R2 of 0.88 and 0.76, RMSE of 0.29 dS/m and 0.35). This study not only deepens the understanding of fractional-order spectral response mechanisms in saline–alkali soils but also provides methodological support for regional monitoring of soil salinization.

### [185] [Estimation of Glacier Mass Balance in the Three-River Headwaters Region from 2000 to 2025 Based on ZiYuan-3 Satellite Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132142)
*Da Liang,Lin Liu,Yu Liao,Xueyu Zhang,Z L Li,Haihang Jing,Zhicai Luo*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用2000年SRTM-C DEM和2024-2025年资源三号立体影像，通过大地测量法估算了三江源区2000-2025年的冰川物质平衡，发现冰川整体呈负平衡且存在显著空间异质性，其中澜沧江源区物质损失最严重（-0.70±0.07 m w.e. yr⁻¹），黄河源区损失最轻（-0.37±0.09 m w.e. yr⁻¹），且近年冰川物质损失加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在全球气候变暖背景下，三江源区冰川作为"亚洲水塔"关键组成部分，其物质平衡变化对区域水资源安全和生态稳定性具有深远影响，但由于高海拔恶劣环境导致实地观测数据稀缺，亟需基于遥感技术开展长期监测。

Method: 采用大地测量法，以2000年SRTM-C DEM为基准，利用2024-2025年获取的高分辨率资源三号三线阵立体影像生成近期冰川表面DEM，通过精细DEM配准、差分和系统误差校正，系统估算了三江源区2000-2025年冰川物质平衡。

Result: 三江源区冰川在研究期间整体呈负物质平衡，空间异质性显著：澜沧江源区物质损失最严重（-0.70±0.07 m w.e. yr⁻¹），黄河源区损失最轻（-0.37±0.09 m w.e. yr⁻¹），且与早期研究相比，近年冰川物质损失加速，与区域气候特征密切相关。

Conclusion: 本研究为理解三江源区冰川变化及其水文和生态影响提供了科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。本文本身就是典型的遥感冰川学论文。改进方案：（1）可引入ICESat-2/ICESat激光测高数据作为外部验证，进一步评估资源三号DEM的精度；（2）可结合Sentinel-1/2等中分辨率多时相遥感数据，将分析时段扩展至更长时间序列（如2000-2025年分段分析）；（3）可引入GRACE/GRACE-FO重力卫星数据对冰川物质平衡结果进行交叉验证；（4）可结合气象再分析资料（如ERA5-Land）和遥感地表温度数据，建立冰川物质平衡与气候因子的定量关系模型。

Abstract (英文): Under the background of global climate warming, glaciers in the Three-River Headwaters Region, as a crucial component of the “Asian Water Tower,” exert profound influences on regional water resource security and ecological stability through their mass balance variations. Due to the scarcity of in situ observations caused by the harsh high-altitude environment, long-term monitoring based on remote sensing techniques is urgently required. In this study, the geodetic method was employed, using the SRTM-C DEM acquired in 2000 as the reference, and recent glacier surface DEMs were generated from high-resolution ZiYuan-3 tri-stereo imagery obtained during 2024–2025. Through refined DEM co-registration, differencing, and systematic error corrections, the glacier mass balance in the Three-River Headwaters Region from 2000 to 2025 was systematically estimated. The results indicate that the glaciers in the study area exhibited an overall negative mass balance during the study period, with significant spatial heterogeneity. Among the sub-regions, the Lancang River source region experienced the most pronounced mass loss (−0.70 ± 0.07 m w.e. yr−1), whereas the Yellow River source region showed the lowest mass loss (−0.37 ± 0.09 m w.e. yr−1). Compared with earlier studies, glacier mass loss has accelerated in recent years and is closely associated with regional climatic characteristics. This study provides a scientific basis for understanding glacier changes and their hydrological and ecological impacts in the Three-River Headwaters Region.

### [186] [Long-Term Monitoring of Saline–Alkaline Land Converted to Paddy Fields Using a Time-Series Change Detection Algorithm](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132140)
*Jie Qin,Jia Du,Li J,M Wang,L J Wang,Guanglei Hou,Zhengwei Liang,Kaishan Song,Weilin Yu,Kaizeng Zhuo*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Mann-Kendall（MK）趋势和突变检验的框架，用于监测盐碱地转水田的转换过程。利用Landsat时间序列数据（2007–2021年）对吉林省大安市进行研究，发现LSWI、SI4、SI5等遥感指数在检测转换方面具有高敏感性，其中6月SI5指数检测精度最高（总体精度94.15%，Kappa系数0.86），MK突变检验在确定转换时间方面达到80.36%的时序精度。研究揭示了盐碱地转水田的时空异质性：东部以大面积连片水田为主，西部为碎片化转换，中部活动较少；转换面积在2015年前快速增长，随后逐渐下降，截至2021年累计转换面积达276.29 km²。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 盐碱地作为潜在的耕地储备资源，对提高农业生产力和保障粮食安全具有重要意义。然而，由于植被恢复、地表变化、水文改造和农业物候等因素的影响，长期监测盐碱地转换过程仍然具有挑战性。现有方法（如CCDC和LandTrendr）对密集观测、参数调优和年度分类依赖较强，亟需开发更高效的监测框架。

Method: 本研究基于GEE平台，利用Landsat时间序列数据（2007–2021年），采用Mann-Kendall（MK）趋势和突变检验框架监测盐碱地转水田过程。通过点双列相关分析评估15种遥感指数的敏感性，并利用混淆矩阵验证检测精度，MK突变检验用于确定转换时间。

Result: LSWI、SI4、SI5等指数与转换强相关（|r|=0.788–0.885），转换前后光谱差异显著（p<0.01）。6月SI5指数检测精度最高（总体精度94.15%，Kappa系数0.86）；MK突变检验时序精度达80.36%。空间上东部大面积连片转换、西部碎片化、中部稀少；时间上2015年前快速扩张，后逐渐下降，累计转换面积276.29 km²（截至2021年）。

Conclusion: 本研究所提出的MK框架能有效监测盐碱地转水田的转换过程和时序，相比传统方法减少了对密集观测和参数调优的依赖。研究揭示了转换的时空异质性，为可持续土地利用提供了科学指导。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感在地表覆盖变化监测领域的应用研究。改进方向：（1）可引入Sentinel-2影像（10m分辨率）替代Landsat（30m），提高空间细节捕捉能力，尤其适用于西部碎片化转换区域的精准监测；（2）可结合SAR数据（如Sentinel-1）克服光学影像受云雨天气影响的限制，增强时间序列连续性；（3）可引入深度学习时序模型（如LSTM、Transformer）与MK趋势检验耦合，进一步提升转换时序判别的精度；（4）可扩展至其他盐碱地分布区（如松嫩平原、黄淮海平原），验证框架的泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Saline–alkaline land serves as a potential arable land reserve for augmenting agricultural productivity and safeguarding food security. However, long-term monitoring of saline–alkaline land conversion remains challenging because of vegetation recovery, surface changes, hydrological modification, and agricultural phenology. Compared with CCDC and LandTrendr, the proposed MK-based framework detects conversion occurrence and timing while reducing dependence on dense observations, parameter tuning, and annual classification. This study examines the spatiotemporal dynamics of saline–alkaline land converted into paddies in Da’an City, utilizing Landsat time-series data (2007–2021) from the Google Earth Engine (GEE) platform. The analysis employed Mann–Kendall (MK) trend and mutation tests to monitor conversion processes and analyze spatiotemporal dynamics. Point-biserial correlation analysis was applied to evaluate the sensitivity of various remote sensing indices in detecting land conversion. The top fifteen indices, including the Land Surface Water Index (LSWI), Salinity Index 4 (SI4), and Salinity Index 5 (SI5), demonstrated strong correlations (|r| = 0.788–0.885) and significant pre- and post-conversion spectral differences (p &lt; 0.01). Validation via confusion matrix confirmed that the June SI5 index attained the highest detection accuracy (overall accuracy: 94.15%; Kappa coefficient: 0.86), supporting the MK trend test’s efficacy in monitoring conversion processes. The MK mutation test achieved 80.36% temporal accuracy in determining conversion timing. The spatiotemporal analyses identified heterogeneity in saline–alkaline land conversion patterns. Spatially, large contiguous paddy fields dominated the eastern region, whereas fragmented conversion characterized the west, with minimal activity in the central zone. Temporally, the conversion area expanded rapidly before 2015 and then gradually declined, reaching a cumulative converted area of 276.29 km2 by 2021. This study elucidates spatiotemporal conversion dynamics to guide sustainable land use.

</details>


### [187] [Mapping Building Construction Year from Landsat in Data-Scarce, Cloud-Prone Regions: A Parsimonious Spatial Triage Tool for Physical Vulnerability Screening](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132135)
*Ying Liu,Xi Zhang,Zewen Mo,Zhipan Wang,Qingling Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出一种利用年度无云Landsat NDVI合成影像与开源建筑足迹数据，通过时间模板匹配（TTM）算法检测“植被-建筑”转化信号来估算建筑建造年份的计算高效框架。在深圳和河内两个多云城市验证，精度优于月度LandTrendr方法约1.8倍，证明在持久云污染下年度合成影像比细粒度方案更可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市韧性评估需要准确的建筑年龄数据作为结构脆弱性的时间代理，但热带和亚热带地区持续的云覆盖和快速城市发展限制了数据可用性，现有方法难以在云污染严重的区域可靠获取建筑建造年份信息。

Method: 采用年度无云Landsat NDVI合成影像（优先保证年度数据完整性而非月度粒度）结合开源建筑足迹数据，利用时间模板匹配（TTM）算法检测“植被-建筑”转化过程中NDVI的显著下降信号，从而推断建筑建造年份。

Result: 在中国深圳（月度对比分析）和越南河内两个高动态、重度云污染大都市区评估，该方法实现了高生产者精度；在深圳的月度对比分析中，性能比基于月度LandTrendr的噪声敏感基线高出近1.8倍。

Conclusion: 在持续云污染条件下，粗糙但一致的年度合成影像比细粒度方案提供更可靠的信号；该可扩展方法可生成关键的建筑年龄数据集，为地震风险建模和资源受限地区的韧性城市规划提供基础结构智能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该方法的核心创新在于无视月度细节、专注年度数据完整性以对抗云污染，可改进方向：（1）引入SAR数据（如Sentinel-1）作为NDVI的补充，在极端多云期提供辅助检测信号；（2）融合高分辨率影像（如PlanetScope）对检测到的转化年份进行局部精化；（3）扩展TTM算法以处理多阶段建筑开发周期；（4）结合夜间灯光数据（如VIIRS）作为建筑活动的额外验证源。

Abstract (英文): Assessing urban resilience requires accurate data on building age as a temporal proxy associated with structural vulnerability, yet persistent cloud cover and rapid development constrain data availability in tropical and subtropical regions. We propose a computationally efficient framework that prioritizes annual data integrity over monthly granularity to map building construction years. By combining annual cloud-free Landsat NDVI (Normalized Difference Vegetation Index) composites with open-source building footprints, the framework utilizes a Temporal Template Matching (TTM) algorithm to detect the distinct “vegetation-to-built” transition signal. Evaluated across two dynamic and heavily cloud-contaminated metropolitan areas—Shenzhen, China, and Hanoi, Vietnam—this approach achieves a high producer’s accuracy; furthermore, in Shenzhen, where a monthly comparative analysis was conducted, it outperforms a noise-sensitive monthly LandTrendr-based baseline by a factor of nearly 1.8. Our findings demonstrate that under persistent cloud contamination, a coarser but consistent annual composite provides a more reliable signal than finer-grained alternatives. This scalable methodology generates critical building-age datasets, offering foundational structural intelligence for potential inputs into seismic risk modeling and resilient urban planning in rapid-growth and resource-constrained regions.

### [188] [High-Order Nonlinear Correction for Spaceborne Fourier Transform Spectrometers](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132145)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过仿真分析不同阶次非线性误差引入的畸变光谱特征；提出基于带内和带外两种迭代校正方法的高阶非线性校正方案；利用DQ-2卫星红外高光谱大气成分探测器的发射前辐射定标实验数据，比较二阶、三阶、带内和带外等不同校正方案的性能。

Conclusion: 所提出的高阶非线性校正方案适用于非线性探测器，能够有效提高辐射定标精度。

Abstract (英文): Infrared Fourier transform spectrometers using interferometric spectroscopy are widely used in space remote sensing owing to their high spectral resolution and sensitivity. We investigated the distorted spectral characteristics introduced by nonlinear errors of different orders through simulation for infrared detectors with strong nonlinear effects. A high-order nonlinear correction scheme was proposed based on two iterative correction methods for in-band and out-of-band spectra. Further, the effects of second-order, third-order, in-band, and out-of-band correction methods were compared using prelaunch radiometric calibration experimental data from the DQ-2 satellite infrared hyperspectral atmospheric composition sounder. The results showed that the third-order in-band correction scheme performed the best, while various other correction schemes also effectively reduced nonlinear errors. The maximum average deviation was 0.18–0.25 K for the long-wave band and 0.11–0.19 K for the mid-wave band in the temperature range of 230–300 K. According to the correction evaluation and methods comparison, the proposed method is appropriate for nonlinearity detectors to improve radiometric calibration accuracy.

### [189] [A Weighted Image-Point-Measurement Method of Laser Altimetry Points for Improving Laser-Altimetry-Data-Assisted Positioning Accuracy of Small-Satellite Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132154)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小卫星平台姿轨测定精度有限，导致激光测高点反投到影像上存在数十像素甚至更大的偏差；同时，成像传感器多样、影像分辨率差异大以及影像几何构型弱，使得准确获取激光测高点的像方坐标存在困难，亟需一种适用于小卫星影像的激光测高点量测与联合几何定位方法。

Result: 所有测试的影像组合场景中，垂直定位精度均得到显著提升，验证了该方法在类似地形条件下增强多卫星平台、多传感器、多分辨率小卫星立体影像垂直几何定位性能的能力。

Conclusion: 提出的激光测高点量测方法与联合几何定位模型能够有效解决小卫星影像几何定位精度不足的问题，尤其在高程方向提升显著，适用于多源小卫星立体影像的联合几何定位。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感领域的论文，核心贡献在小卫星影像几何定位方面。改进方案：(1) 可将该激光测高点辅助定位框架推广至其他国产小卫星星座（如珠海一号、高景一号），验证跨星座泛化能力；(2) 考虑引入深度学习特征匹配替代传统像点量测策略，进一步减小弱纹理区域的量测误差；(3) 可探索与ICESat-2/ATLAS等光子计数激光雷达数据的融合，实现不同激光测高数据源与光学小卫星影像的联合定位；(4) Partial-EIV模型可扩展为鲁棒总体最小二乘，以抑制粗差对定位结果的扰动。

Abstract (英文): For small-satellite imagery, traditional image points derived from the direct back-projection of laser altimetry points onto the imagery often exhibit deviations of tens of pixels or more, owing to the relatively limited attitude and orbit determination accuracy of small-satellite platforms. Moreover, the diversity of imaging sensors, variations in image resolution, and inherently weak image geometric configurations further complicate the accurate acquisition of image-space coordinates for laser altimetry points. To facilitate the application of laser altimetry data for geometric positioning across multi-satellite, multi-sensor, and multi-resolution small-satellite imagery, this study proposes a measurement method for laser altimetry points tailored to small-satellite images and establishes a combined geometric positioning model that integrates virtual control points, laser altimetry points, and image-matching tie points. The framework comprises four key procedural components: (1) an image-point-measurement strategy for laser altimetry points; (2) the construction of a laser altimetry data-assisted geometric positioning model for small-satellite imagery; (3) the solution of the geometric positioning model using a total least squares approach based on the partial-EIV (errors-in-variables) models; and (4) a comprehensive accuracy assessment conducted under multiple image-combination scenarios, including single-satellite single-stereo, single-satellite multi-stereo, dual-satellite single-stereo, and multi-satellite multi-stereo imagery configurations. Experimental validation is carried out using Jilin-1 small-satellite panchromatic images (KF01A, GF02A, and GF02B) acquired over the Henan region of China. The experimental results demonstrate that, with the laser altimetry point-measurement method and the combined geometric positioning model, the vertical positioning accuracy is substantially improved across all tested image-combination scenarios. These findings further confirm the capability in enhancing the vertical geometric positioning performance of stereoscopic small-satellite imagery characterized by multi-satellite platforms, multi-sensors, and multi-resolutions over terrain conditions similar to those tested.

### [190] [Glacier Boundary Extraction over the Tibetan Plateau Using a Double Random Forest Model with Multi-Temporal Sentinel-1/2 Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132148)
*Huilan Ding,Chengsheng Yang,Zufeng Li,Chen Fu,Ziqian Wang,Zewei Liu,Yi Yu*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 青藏高原地形崎岖、季节性积雪、广泛表碛覆盖及地形阴影等因素导致传统单源或单时相数据冰川边界提取精度有限，亟需一种自动化、高精度的多源多时相融合方法。

Method: 提出Double-RF框架：1）在GEE上构建包含Sentinel-1极化特征、Sentinel-2光谱特征、纹理特征及地形特征的多维特征空间；2）利用重要性指标和OOB误差进行特征优化；3）采用分层分类策略，第一层RF区分清洁冰川和阴影冰川，第二层RF对表碛覆盖冰川进行精细边界提取，以缓解光谱混淆。

Result: Double-RF方法在所有子流域总体精度超过0.84，最佳可达0.95以上。提取的冰川清单显示：青藏高原西部和边缘地区冰川密度高于东部和内部区域，冰川主要分布在阴坡且坡度缓至中等，体现了气候梯度与地形控制的共同影响。

Conclusion: 多源多时相融合策略为青藏高原长期冰川监测提供了稳健的方法论基础。

Abstract (英文): Glacier boundary extraction on the Tibetan Plateau (TP) faces persistent challenges due to rugged terrain, seasonal snow, extensive debris cover, and topographic shadows. Traditional methods utilizing single-source or single-temporal data often yield limited accuracy. Thus, we propose an automated Double Random Forest (Double-RF) framework integrating single- and multi-temporal features from Sentinel-1 (SAR) and Sentinel-2 (Optical) data within the Google Earth Engine. We established a multidimensional feature space comprising spectral, textural, polarimetric, and topographic attributes. Feature optimization was performed using importance metrics and out-of-bag (OOB) error. A hierarchical classification strategy was employed: the first RF identifies clean glaciers and glaciers in shadow, while the second RF executes refined boundary extraction of debris-covered glaciers to mitigate spectral confusion. The results indicate that the Double-RF method significantly achieves an overall accuracy exceeding 0.84 across all sub-basins and reaching above 0.95 at best. The derived glacier inventory reveals a distinct spatial pattern: higher concentrations in the western and peripheral regions compared to the eastern and interior TP. Glaciers are predominantly distributed on shaded aspects with gentle-to-moderate slopes, highlighting the combined influence of climatic gradients and topographic controls. This multi-source, multi-temporal fusion strategy provides a robust methodological foundation for long-term glacier monitoring over the TP.

*Xingwei Yan,Y Zhang,H T Chen,Y Zhang,Kunlin Zou*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种轻量级尺度自适应多尺度特征融合模型LMF-IR，用于红外无人机快速目标检测。该模型包含多扩张残差块(MDRB)、改进的通道注意力特征金字塔(CAM-FPN)和P-WIoU损失函数三个核心组件，在自建数据集上计算量减少1.4G FLOPs，参数量降至基线62%，mAP@0.5:0.95提升2.4%；在公开ANTI-UAV数据集上mAP@0.5:0.95提升4.8%。

Method: 提出了LMF-IR轻量级模型，包含三个关键组件：1) 多扩张残差块(MDRB)增强多尺度特征表示；2) 改进的通道注意力模型-特征融合金字塔(CAM-FPN)通过通道注意力机制动态调整特征权重；3) 改进的P-WIoU损失函数，综合考虑中心距离、重叠率和宽高比，适应快速尺度变化下的边界框回归。

However, under fast UAV movement or dynamic zooming scenarios, the rapid scale variation of targets poses severe challenges to existing detection models, especially on resource-constrained edge devices. To address this, a lightweight scale-adaptive multi-scale feature fusion model, termed LMF-IR, is proposed for efficient and accurate detection under sudden target size changes. The model integrates three key components: a Multi-Dilation Residual Block (MDRB) for enhanced multi-scale feature representation, an improved Channel Attention Model–Feature Fusion Pyramid Network (CAM-FPN) to boost adaptive feature fusion, and a modified P-WIoU loss function designed for precise bounding box regression under varying target sizes. The MDRB module effectively captures fine-grained features across multiple scales and reliably identifies targets of varying sizes. The CAM-FPN incorporates a channel attention mechanism, which can dynamically adjust the weights of features, enabling the model to focus on informative feature channels. The redesigned P-WIoU loss function is designed to account for the shape characteristics of UAV target bounding boxes. It includes centroid distance, overlap ratio, and aspect ratio, thereby improving localization accuracy under rapid scale changes. The experimental results on our self-built UAV–infrared dataset show that LMF-IR reduces 1.4 G in floating-point operations compared to the baseline model, and the parameter count is reduced to 62% of the baseline. At the same time, mAP@0.5:0.95 increases by 2.4%. Moreover, on the public ANTI-UAV dataset, our method increases mAP@0.5:0.95 by 4.8%, indicating that our method has excellent performance in real-time infrared UAV detection under rapid target scale changes.

### [192] [A Physics-Guided Illumination Compensation Framework for Shadow Removal in Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132133)
*Tingting Zhou,Zhixin Yang,Haoyang Fu,Yi Chen,Zhao Chen,Madal Artur,Wei Y*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出了一种物理引导的阴影去除框架，结合轻量级U-Net阴影检测（LSDU）和改进的照度比方法（MIIRM）及动态半影补偿（MDPCM），在高分辨率城市遥感影像上实现96%以上检测精度和最低补偿误差。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 轻量级U-Net（LSDU）高效捕获多尺度阴影特征；(2) 改进的照度强度比方法（MIIRM）显式建模本影与半影的照度差异；(3) 动态半影补偿方法（MDPCM）缓解过渡区域过补偿并提升辐射一致性。

Result: 在AISD数据集上，阴影检测整体精度超过96%，阴影补偿RMSE优于现有SOTA方法，且在多种城市场景中表现出强鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Shadows in high-resolution urban remote sensing imagery significantly degrade radiometric and structural information, thereby limiting the performance of downstream tasks such as classification and object extraction. Therefore, effective shadow removal is essential for improving the reliability of urban remote sensing applications. Existing methods still exhibit limitations in accurately detecting complex shadows, especially small-scale shadows and ambiguous boundaries, and shadow compensation in umbra regions often suffers from under-correction due to inadequate illumination modeling. To address these challenges, a physics-guided shadow removal framework that integrates lightweight shadow detection with illumination-aware compensation is proposed. A lightweight U-Net (LSDU) is designed to efficiently capture multi-scale shadow features, while a modified illumination intensity ratio method (MIIRM) is developed to explicitly model illumination differences between umbra and penumbra. Furthermore, a dynamic penumbra compensation method (MDPCM) is introduced to alleviate over-compensation effects in transition regions and improve radiometric consistency. Experiments on the Aerial Imagery Shadow Dataset (AISD) demonstrate that the proposed method achieves over 96% overall accuracy in shadow detection and the lowest RMSE in shadow compensation among existing state-of-the-art methods, while maintaining strong robustness across diverse urban scenes.

### [193] [Doppler–Kinematic Spatio-Temporal Graph Learning for Low-Slow-Small Target Recognition Using Multi-Dimensional Radar Observations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132151)
*Jia Liu,Xiaolong Chen,Ningyuan Su,Hongyong Wang,Xinghai Wang,Yong Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对低慢小目标识别中多维度雷达特征异构融合困难问题，提出双流时空交叉注意力图卷积网络（DS-STCAGCN），分别编码多普勒谱和运动学特征，通过双向交叉注意力融合、自注意力捕获长时依赖、图卷积聚合帧间关联，在LSS-DAUR-1.0和LSS-PR-1.0数据集上分别达到99.73%和99.86%的平均准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低慢小目标的多维度雷达观测（多普勒谱和运动学）存在维度、分布和物理含义上的异构性，直接融合难以充分利用其互补判别信息，且无法有效建模时序轨迹演化，导致识别困难。

Method: 提出DS-STCAGCN框架：双流编码器分别处理多普勒谱和运动学特征以保留模态特异性；双向交叉注意力机制实现异构特征融合；自注意力捕获长时序依赖；在时间有序观测图上进行图卷积聚合局部帧间关联。

Result: 在LSS-DAUR-1.0数据集上平均准确率99.73%，5dB SNR下保持98.64%；在LSS-PR-1.0被动雷达数据集上平均准确率99.86%，展示强跨模态泛化能力。

Conclusion: 提出的DS-STCAGCN为多维度雷达感知和鲁棒低慢小目标识别提供了有效的时空建模框架。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身即为遥感雷达目标识别领域研究。改进方向：（1）引入多尺度图卷积以更好捕获不同时间粒度的运动模式；（2）将双向交叉注意力扩展为多头跨模态注意力以增强特征对齐；（3）结合知识蒸馏或对比学习进一步提升低信噪比下的鲁棒性；（4）探索将多普勒-运动学双流架构推广至SAR/InSAR多模态特征融合场景。

Abstract (英文): Low-slow-small (LSS) target recognition using multi-dimensional radar remains challenging due to weak signatures, similar kinematics, and overlapping short-term Doppler patterns. Digital-array radar provides continuous, complementary Doppler-spectrum and kinematic measurements; however, their heterogeneity in dimension, distribution, and physical meaning often makes direct fusion under-exploit discriminative complementarity and inadequately model temporal track evolution. To address this, we propose a Doppler-Kinematic Spatio-Temporal Graph Learning framework named Dual-Stream Spatio-Temporal Cross-Attention Graph Convolutional Network (DS-STCAGCN) for LSS target recognition using multi-dimensional radar observations. The method separately encodes Doppler-spectrum and kinematic features to preserve their modality-specific characteristics, fuses them through bidirectional cross-attention, captures long-range temporal dependencies via self-attention, and aggregates local frame-to-frame correlations through graph convolution on a time-ordered observation graph. On the public L-band digital-array dataset LSS-DAUR-1.0, DS-STCAGCN achieves 99.73% mean accuracy and maintains 98.64% at 5 dB signal-to-noise ratio (SNR). On the passive-radar dataset LSS-PR-1.0, it reaches 99.86% mean accuracy, demonstrating strong cross-modal generalization. This work provides an effective spatio-temporal modelling framework for multi-dimensional radar sensing and robust LSS target recognition.

### [194] [Retrieval of the Vertical Profiles of Aerosols, HONO, and Ozone in Kunming’s Winter and Their Interrelationships Based on the MAX-DOAS](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132141)
*Haoyue Wang,Naicong Yan,Ke Yu,Qianyu Liu,Mengyao Cai*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用MAX-DOAS技术和最优估计方法，分析了2024年冬季昆明气溶胶、HONO和O3的垂直廓线及日变化规律，发现HONO对OH自由基生成和O3形成具有关键作用，不考虑HONO会导致最大O3浓度降低约8 ppb。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阐明昆明冬季气溶胶、HONO和O3的垂直分布特征和日变化规律，揭示HONO在OH自由基生成和O3形成中的关键作用，为区域大气污染防控提供科学依据。

Method: 采用MAX-DOAS（多轴差分吸收光谱）技术结合最优估计方法，反演气溶胶、HONO和O3的垂直廓线；通过模型分析评估HONO对OH自由基净收支和O3生成速率的影响。

Result: 气溶胶主要集中于近地面层，消光系数峰值达1.3 km⁻¹；HONO浓度随高度指数递减，日出前后最高、正午最低，最大浓度超3.14×10¹⁰ molec·cm⁻³；O3下午在2.6–4 km高度浓度最高（>1.16×10¹² molec·cm⁻³）。不考虑HONO时，OH自由基在早晨由净生成转为净损耗，O3最大浓度降低约8 ppb。

Conclusion: 三种污染物存在显著的垂直和日变化特征，HONO在OH自由基生成和O3形成中发挥至关重要的作用，该研究为区域大气化学及污染物分布提供了重要科学支撑。

Abstract (英文): This study adopts MAX-DOAS technology and optimal estimation methods to analyze the vertical profiles of aerosols, HONO, and O3 in Kunming during winter 2024, thereby clarifying their vertical distribution characteristics and diurnal variation rules. Aerosols are predominantly concentrated in the near-surface layer, with concentrations decreasing gradually with increasing altitude; their concentrations rise in the morning, reach a peak at 10 a.m., and then decline, with the maximum extinction coefficient reaching 1.3 km−1. HONO concentrations decrease exponentially with height, being the highest around sunrise, the lowest at noon, and then gradually accumulating, with the maximum concentration exceeding 3.14 × 1010 molec·cm−3. O3 achieves its maximum concentration in the 2.6–4 km altitude range in the afternoon (the highest concentration &gt; 1.16 × 1012 molec·cm−3), while near-surface O3 concentrations increase steadily from morning onward. Model analysis demonstrates that without considering HONO, OH radicals shift from net production to net loss in the morning, leading to reduced O3 production rates and a decrease of approximately 8 ppb in the maximum O3 concentration. These findings highlight the significant vertical and diurnal variations in the three pollutants, emphasize HONO’s crucial role in OH radical generation and O3 formation, provide valuable scientific support for air pollution control, and confirm HONO’s important impact on regional atmospheric chemistry and the distribution of key pollutants.

### [195] [Multi-Source Remote Sensing for Dynamic Landslide Susceptibility Assessment: From Static Mapping to Spatiotemporal Inference and Updating](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132153)
*Hui Deng,Shirong Hu,Yanni Bao,Siyuan Zhao,Y ZHAO,Zi Wang,Han Wang,Xiaojun Chen*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文综述了遥感赋能动态滑坡易发性评估的最新进展，围绕降雨/土壤湿度、InSAR形变、光学时序土地系统和多时相DEM四个过程角色的动态因子构建、时空表征学习、易发性图更新及时空独立验证四个关键环节展开分析。指出当前受限于滑坡编目时间粒度粗、多源产品跨尺度不兼容、融合过程感知不足和物理可解释性弱，未来需发展事件级编目、不确定性感知融合、过程一致时空学习及可科学验证的更新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多源遥感观测为滑坡易发性评估从静态地形分区走向动态时空推断和地图更新提供了可能，但不同遥感产品在空间支撑、时间分辨率、物理意义和不确定性结构上存在显著差异，无法简单作为通用预测因子直接集成。因此亟需梳理如何以过程感知的方式整合这些异构观测流，实现真正可更新的动态滑坡易发性评估。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，将遥感驱动的动态滑坡易发性评估分解为四个关键组件：动态因子构建、时空表征与学习、易发性图更新、时空独立验证。并围绕四种过程角色（降雨/土壤湿度强迫、InSAR运动学状态、光学时序地系统调节、多时相DEM地貌记忆）组织文献，分析其信号编码与融合方式（时序模型、图表示、注意力机制、混合框架）。

Result: 发现当前进展受限于：(1) 滑坡编目时间分辨率粗；(2) 遥感产品跨尺度不兼容；(3) 多模态融合过程感知不足且不均匀；(4) 物理可解释性有限。同时指出需在过程角色、数据结构、映射单元、推理目标和验证设计之间保持一致性。

Conclusion: 未来突破方向包括：事件级分辨率滑坡编目、不确定性感知的多模态融合、过程一致的时空学习，以及能明确检验易发性图在获取新遥感数据后是否可科学更新的验证设计。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。本文本身就是遥感领域的核心综述，直接服务于滑坡灾害评估。改进方案：(1) 引入多任务学习框架，同时学习滑坡易发性与形变速率预测，增强过程一致性；(2) 采用物理信息神经网络(PINN)将边坡稳定性力学方程作为损失约束，提升物理可解释性；(3) 利用扩散模型或生成对抗网络进行遥感产品超分辨率对齐，解决跨尺度不兼容问题；(4) 设计主动学习策略，针对高不确定性区域优先获取高分辨率遥感数据，实现自适应观测。

Abstract (英文): Multi-source remote sensing is transforming landslide susceptibility assessment from static terrain-based zonation toward observation-driven spatiotemporal inference and dynamic map updating. Satellite precipitation products, interferometric synthetic aperture radar (InSAR) deformation time series, optical image sequences, land-cover products, and multi-temporal terrain observations provide complementary evidence of hydrometeorological forcing, slope kinematics, land-system regulation, and geomorphic reorganization. However, these observation streams differ substantially in spatial support, temporal resolution, physical meaning, and uncertainty structure and therefore cannot be reliably integrated as generic predictors without process-aware interpretation. This review synthesizes recent progress in remote sensing-enabled dynamic landslide susceptibility assessment by linking four key components: dynamic factor construction from Earth observation data, spatiotemporal representation and learning, susceptibility map updating, and validation under temporal and spatial independence. The reviewed literature is organized around four process roles: rainfall- and soil moisture-related forcing, kinematic state and response captured by InSAR, land-system and ecological regulation derived from optical time series, and geomorphic memory represented by multi-temporal digital elevation models (DEMs). We further examine how these signals are encoded and integrated through temporal models, graph-based representations, attention mechanisms, and hybrid frameworks, with particular emphasis on consistency among process role, data structure, mapping unit, inference target, and validation design. Current progress remains constrained by temporally coarse landslide inventories, cross-scale incompatibility among remote sensing products, uneven and insufficiently process-aware multimodal fusion, and limited physical interpretability. Future advances require event-resolved inventories, uncertainty-aware multimodal fusion, process-consistent spatiotemporal learning, and validation designs that explicitly test whether susceptibility maps can be updated in a scientifically defensible manner as new Earth observation data become available.

### [196] [Differences and Driving Mechanisms of the Vegetation Dual-Track Recovery Process After Forest Fires Based on the Vegetation Index](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132175)
*Sen Wang,Xingpeng Liu,Rima Ga,Bing Ma,Nile Wu,Zhijun Tong,Jiquan Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用EVI（结构恢复）和SIF（功能恢复）两种指标，结合Transformer和随机森林模型，分析了火灾后植被恢复的时空动态与驱动因素。结果表明，SIF恢复速度慢于EVI，三年后约78%区域EVI恢复至火灾前80%以上，而SIF仅达70%；降水与温度促进恢复，地形与燃烧严重度则起抑制作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 火灾后植被的结构恢复与功能恢复之间存在何种具体差异尚不明确，现有研究缺乏对二者进行量化和对比的框架，亟需从双重视角揭示森林生态系统恢复的完整图景。

Method: 采用EVI表征结构恢复、SIF表征功能恢复；使用Transformer模型模拟火灾前后EVI和SIF的时空变化；采用随机森林模型识别恢复的关键驱动因子；进行双变量依赖性分析评估环境因素的影响。

Result: 火灾后EVI和SIF均显著下降，SIF恢复慢于EVI；三年后约78%过火区域的EVI恢复到火灾前水平80%以上，而SIF恢复仅达70%；降水和温度促进恢复，地形和dNBR起抑制作用。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了分阶段的火灾后森林植被恢复分析方法，建立了结构-功能双重视角的恢复评估框架，为森林可持续恢复与管理提供了可操作的见解。

Abstract (英文): Vegetation recovery after forest fires is a vital indicator of ecosystem resilience. However, the specific differences between structural and functional recovery after fire have remained unclear. In this study, we quantified and compared post-fire recovery using two distinct vegetation indicators: the Enhanced Vegetation Index (EVI) for structural recovery and Solar-Induced Chlorophyll Fluorescence (SIF) for functional recovery. We analyzed the spatiotemporal dynamics and drivers of post-fire recovery. A Transformer model was used to simulate pre- and post-fire variations in EVI and SIF, while a Random Forest model was employed to identify the key drivers of recovery. We analyze the spatiotemporal dynamics and drivers of post-fire recovery. A Transformer model simulates pre- and post-fire variations in EVI and SIF, while a Random Forest model identifies key drivers of recovery. Our results show a steep decline in both indicators after fires, with SIF recovering more slowly than EVI. Three years after the fire, about 78% of burned areas regain at least 80% of their pre-fire EVI levels, but SIF recovery reaches only 70%. Bivariate dependency analysis indicates that precipitation and temperature promote recovery, whereas topography and the Differenced Normalized Burn Ratio (dNBR) have the opposite effect. This study advances a phased, analytical approach to post-fire forest vegetation recovery, offering a dual-perspective framework for understanding forest resilience and providing actionable insights for sustainable restoration and management.

### [197] [Trend Pattern (1980–2025) of Total Ozone Column over Antarctica in Winter–Spring Season, Derived from Heatmap Analysis—A New Approach to Detecting Ozone Hole Recovery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132174)
*Agnieszka Czerwińska,Janusz W. Krzyścin*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文通过分析南极昭和站和阿蒙森-斯科特站1980-2025年冬季-春季总臭氧柱（TOC）趋势的蓝-红热力图，发现2000年前以负趋势（蓝色）为主，之后转为正趋势（红色），证实了臭氧层自21世纪初开始恢复的假设，克服了年际变率对传统分析的干扰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 南极臭氧层恢复的迹象由于大气动力学引起的年际变率过大而难以从原始TOC时间序列中得出明确结论，因此需要一种替代分析方法来揭示被噪声掩盖的恢复信号。

Method: 采用蓝-红热力图模式分析1980-2025年冬季-春季TOC趋势，构建三个年度TOC时间序列（冬季平均、9月15日值、春季最小值），综合使用再分析数据、地面测量和卫星观测等多源数据，对昭和站和阿蒙森-斯科特站进行案例研究。

Result: 两站点的蓝-红热力图均显示：2000年前结束的TOC趋势区域以蓝色（负趋势）为主，2000年后出现的趋势区域以红色（正趋势）为主，且该模式在不同数据源中均一致。

Conclusion: 证实了南极臭氧层趋势反转的假设，即臭氧恢复始于21世纪初，这一信号在传统噪声较大的TOC时间序列中被掩盖，而热力图方法有效揭示了该恢复趋势。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：（1）将该蓝-红热力图方法推广到其他卫星臭氧传感器（如OMI、TROPOMI）数据，验证恢复趋势的全球一致性；（2）结合机器学习方法对热力图模式进行自动分类与异常检测，提升分析效率；（3）扩展至其他大气成分（如NO₂、SO₂、CH₄）的长期趋势分析，监测污染物减排政策效果；（4）与遥感植被指数、海冰覆盖等地理变量进行时空关联分析，评估臭氧恢复对南极生态系统的影响。

Abstract (英文): Numerous attempts have been made to detect signs of ozone layer recovery over Antarctica, which has been expected since the beginning of the 21st century as a result of the reduction in concentrations of ozone-depleting substances in the Antarctic stratosphere, in accordance with the provisions of the 1987 Montreal Protocol and subsequent amendments aimed at protecting the ozone layer. Large year-to-year variability in the Antarctic ozone, driven by changes in atmospheric dynamics, has made it difficult to draw definitive conclusions about the rate of Antarctic ozone recovery. In this paper, we present an alternative approach to analyse ozone recovery by examining patterns in blue–red heatmaps of total ozone column (TOC) trends during the winter–spring period from 1980 to 2025. Three annual TOC time series (winter average, 15 September value, and spring minimum) were analysed to monitor the ozone hole development over the Syowa and Amundsen–Scott stations. Various sources of the daily TOC data were examined, including reanalysis data, ground-based measurements, and satellite observations. Regardless of the data source, we found that, for both stations, blue cells (negative trends) dominated in the areas of the heatmap where the TOC trends ended before 2000, while red cells (positive trends) appeared mostly afterwards. These results confirm the hypothesis of a trend reversal, i.e., a recovery beginning in the early 2000s, which was obscured in the original, noisy TOC time series.

### [198] [Landslide Susceptibility Assessment in a Complex Mountain Basin Transition Zone by Integrating Mamba and SBAS-InSAR Deformation Evidence: A Case Study of the Xining Basin, China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132170)
*Heming Yang,Wenhui Liu,Y Y Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种耦合Mamba模型（Mamba-LSM）与SBAS-InSAR形变信息的滑坡易发性制图（LSM）框架，通过在模型预测后利用独立形变证据进行双向重分类，显著提升了高易发区滑坡空间集中度（25.31%面积包含69.84%滑坡）和物理解释性，在西宁盆地实现AUC=0.9011。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 山地–盆地过渡带的滑坡易发性制图面临挑战：传统方法主要依赖历史编目和静态条件因子，很少引入独立形变证据来优化易发性分区。本研究旨在通过耦合Mamba模型与InSAR形变信息，弥补这一缺陷。

Method: 提出Mamba-LSM框架，融合六通道邻域块、CNN局部空间编码和Mamba潜特征变换以增强地形上下文表示；在模型预测后，利用SBAS-InSAR形变证据进行双向重分类，优化易发性分区。

Result: Mamba-LSM取得最高AUC（0.9011）和F1-score（0.7431）。经形变重分类后，高和极高易发区仅占25.31%面积，却包含69.84%的滑坡，且集中在山谷–山地过渡带、河流侵蚀坡和工程扰动区。

Conclusion: 整合独立SBAS-InSAR形变证据可同时提升滑坡在高易发区的空间集中度和易发性分区的物理解释性，验证了形变信息辅助LSM的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感与滑坡易发性制图的交叉研究。改进方案：（1）可引入多时相InSAR（如PS-InSAR、DS-InSAR融合）提取更密集形变场，增强形变证据的时空完整性；（2）将形变速率作为动态条件因子直接输入Mamba模型（而非仅后处理重分类），构建端到端的形变感知LSM框架；（3）结合时序InSAR形变趋势（加速/减速）识别潜在滑坡的演化阶段，实现动态易发性更新；（4）将Mamba-LSM拓展至多源遥感数据（如光学影像、LiDAR DEM），提升地形上下文特征的鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Landslide susceptibility mapping (LSM) in mountain–basin transition zones remains challenging because conventional approaches rely mainly on historical inventories and static conditioning factors, whereas independent deformation evidence is seldom incorporated to refine susceptibility zonation. This study proposes an integrated LSM framework for the Xining Basin by coupling a Mamba-based model (Mamba-LSM) with SBAS-InSAR-based deformation-informed bidirectional reclassification, with the key innovation lying in the use of independent deformation evidence to refine susceptibility zonation after model prediction. Specifically, Mamba-LSM integrates six-channel neighborhood patches, CNN-based local spatial encoding, and Mamba-based latent feature transformation to improve the representation of local terrain context for landslide susceptibility assessment. Results show that Mamba-LSM achieved the highest AUC among the evaluated models, reaching 0.9011 with an F1-score of 0.7431. After deformation-informed bidirectional reclassification, the high- and very-high-susceptibility classes occupied only 25.31% of the study area but contained 69.84% of the mapped landslides, and were concentrated mainly in valley–mountain transition belts, river-incised slopes, and engineering-disturbed sectors where SBAS-InSAR deformation hotspots were also preferentially distributed. These findings demonstrate that integrating independent SBAS-InSAR deformation evidence can improve both the spatial concentration of landslides in high-susceptibility zones and the physical interpretability of susceptibility zonation.

### [199] [Comprehensive Validation of ICESat-2 ATL08 Terrain Height Product Using High-Resolution DSM: A Multi-Site Study in Central-South China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132160)
*J Y Chen,Wei Wang,Jingqi Liu,Mingjun Deng,Guoshi Liu,Yingfei Gao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文以高分辨率数字地表模型为参考，在中国中南部18个典型地貌区（涵盖平原、丘陵、山地和高山峡谷）对ICESat-2 ATL08产品的949个验证点进行了系统精度评估。结果显示，所有站点的平均均方根误差为3.318 m（范围1.044–5.120 m），平均误差为−1.032 m（范围−4.575至+2.548 m）。精度呈现显著的地形依赖性：平原地区最高（RMSE=1.044 m），丘陵次之（1.610–3.871 m），山地和高山峡谷最差（2.374–5.120 m），建议在高山峡谷区结合地形信息进行后处理校正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ICESat-2 ATL08产品在复杂地形区域的精度尚未被系统评估，尤其是在中国中南部多样化的地貌条件下，缺乏针对不同地形类型的全面验证，导致该产品在地形复杂区域的应用存在不确定性。

Method: 选取中国中南部18个典型地貌区的949个有效验证点，以高分辨率数字地表模型为参考数据，将ICESat-2 ATL08产品的测高结果与参考数据进行对比，计算均方根误差（RMSE）和平均误差（ME），按平原、丘陵、山地和高山峡谷四类地形分别统计精度指标。

Result: 所有站点平均RMSE为3.318 m（1.044–5.120 m），平均ME为−1.032 m（−4.575至+2.548 m）。平原站精度最高（RMSE=1.044 m），丘陵区RMSE约1.610–3.871 m，山地和高山峡谷区RMSE约2.374–5.120 m。精度呈现显著的地形依赖性。

Conclusion: ICESat-2 ATL08产品精度与地形复杂度密切相关，用户在使用时应考虑地形因素；对于RMSE超过5 m的高山峡谷区域，建议结合地形信息进行后处理校正以提高精度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方案：（1）可引入地形复杂度指数（如坡度、粗糙度）作为先验信息，构建地形自适应校正模型；（2）融合高分辨率DEM（如SRTM、ALOS World 3D）进行地形偏差补偿；（3）利用机器学习方法（随机森林、XGBoost）建立地形参数与高程误差的回归模型，实现区域性误差预测与校正；（4）在复杂地形区可结合多源遥感数据（如Sentinel-1 InSAR、LiDAR点云）进行交叉验证与融合优化。

Abstract (英文): ICESat-2 ATL08 is an important data source for global land surface elevation monitoring, while its accuracy has not been systematically evaluated in the complex terrain areas of central and southern China. Taking high-resolution digital surface models as reference data, this study carries out systematic verification with a total of 949 valid verification points covering 18 typical geomorphological areas in central and southern China. The verification sites cover various terrain types including plains, hills, mountains and alpine canyons. The results show that the average root mean square error of all sites is 3.318 m, ranging from 1.044 m to 5.120 m. Among them, plain areas have the highest accuracy (HS, RMSE = 1.044 m), followed by hilly areas with RMSE of approximately 1.610–3.871 m, and mountainous and alpine canyon areas show relatively poorer accuracy with RMSE of approximately 2.374–5.120 m. The overall mean error (ME) is −1.032 m, with ME values ranging from −4.575 m to +2.548 m across sites. The accuracy of ICESat-2 ATL08 in central-southern China is highly terrain-dependent: RMSE is 1.044 m in the plain site and ranges from 1.610 to 3.871 m in hilly areas and from 2.374 to 5.120 m in mountainous and alpine canyon areas. Therefore, users should consider terrain complexity when applying this product, and post-processing correction incorporating topographic information is recommended for alpine canyon areas where RMSE exceeds 5 m.

### [200] [A Lightweight Small-Object Detector for UAV Imagery via Multi-Scale Feature Enhancement and Saliency-Guided Cross-Layer Fusion](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132164)
*Hao Zhen,Guijun Chen,Fangli Guan,Liqi Yan,Zhixiang Fang,Jianhui Zhang,Haosheng Huang,Pan Li*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出基于YOLOv8s优化的轻量化无人机目标检测器，通过多尺度特征增强和显著性引导跨层融合，在VisDrone2019上以7.2M参数达到48.3% mAP@0.5，比YOLOv8s提升10.2个点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机航拍图像存在细节丢失（小目标像素少、弱边缘被稀释）、跨尺度融合失效（深浅层语义差异导致尺度错配与小目标抑制）、环境干扰（杂乱、遮挡、密集布局导致定位漂移）三大挑战，现有检测器难以兼顾精度与实时性。

Method: 基于YOLOv8s框架，主干网络集成RFCAConv和RGCSP模块增强局部细节与空间结构建模；设计多尺度自适应融合模块（MSAFM），通过双池化和自适应通道重校准对齐深浅层特征；提出显著性引导上下文注意力模块（CASM）突出目标区域，配合动态检测头实现自适应特征调制。

Result: 在VisDrone2019上，mAP@0.5达48.3%，mAP@[0.5:0.95]达29.0%，分别超过YOLOv8s 10.2和6.3个点；模型参数量7.2M，模型大小14.4 MB。

Conclusion: 提出的多尺度特征增强与显著性引导融合策略能有效解决无人机航拍中小目标检测的细节丢失、尺度错配和背景干扰问题，在保持轻量化的同时显著提升检测精度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是面向无人机航拍这一遥感典型场景的检测方法。改进方向：（1）可引入遥感影像特有的多光谱/高光谱通道信息，将CASM扩展为跨模态显著性引导注意力机制；（2）针对遥感大场景下的旋转目标，可在动态检测头中增加角度参数回归分支；（3）MSAFM可结合遥感中常用的特征金字塔网络（FPN）变体进行多尺度对齐优化；（4）可迁移到遥感舰船、车辆、建筑物等小目标密集检测场景进行验证。

Abstract (英文): As unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) become central to traffic inspection, urban security, and emergency response, UAV-based environmental perception requires both high accuracy and real-time efficiency. However, UAV imagery remains challenging due to three primary factors: detail loss, where small targets occupy minimal pixels and weak edges are diluted by downsampling; ineffective cross-scale fusion, where semantic gaps between shallow and deep features lead to scale misalignment and small-object suppression; and environmental interference, where clutter, occlusion, and dense layouts cause localization drift. To address these challenges, we propose an optimized efficient detector built upon the YOLOv8s framework, incorporating multi-scale feature enhancement and saliency-guided cross-layer fusion. Specifically, we integrate RFCAConv and RGCSP modules into the backbone to strengthen local detail and spatial structure modeling. Furthermore, we design a Multi-Scale Adaptive Fusion Module (MSAFM) to align deep and shallow cues through dual-pooling and adaptive channel recalibration. To handle complex backgrounds, a Saliency-Guided Contextual Attention Module (CASM) is introduced to emphasize target regions, alongside a dynamic detection head for adaptive feature modulation. Evaluated on the VisDrone2019 dataset, our method achieves 48.3% mAP@0.5 and 29.0% mAP@[0.5:0.95], outperforming YOLOv8s by 10.2 and 6.3 points, respectively, while keeping the model compact with 7.2M parameters and a 14.4 MB model size.

### [201] [A Spectrally Enhanced Multi-Scale CNN for Limited-Sample Lithological Mapping Using Band-Integrated ASTER and Sentinel-2A Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132163)
*Qiuming Pei,Jiale Shen,Li Zhang,Yifei Zhang,Sergei Krivonogov,Shiming Wang,Daren Fang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对多光谱遥感岩性制图中光谱信息有限和标记样本稀缺的挑战，本文通过集成ASTER短波红外与Sentinel-2A可见光-近红外及红边波段构建互补多光谱数据集，并设计了一种紧凑型光谱增强多尺度卷积神经网络（包含残差光谱特征增强模块和平行多尺度混合卷积模块），在甘肃肃北县石包城地区实现了八类岩性单元的高精度分类（OA 94.12%），证明了在缺乏高光谱影像和密集野外样本条件下，融合免费多光谱数据与轻量光谱-空间CNN是一种实用且经济的岩性制图方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多光谱遥感岩性制图面临两大困境：一是多光谱传感器光谱维度有限，诊断性光谱信息不足；二是在偏远或难以到达区域，可靠的标记样本极为稀缺。现有卷积神经网络应用于岩性分类时，受限于有限的光谱维度和训练样本，难以学习到具有判别力的光谱-空间特征。因此，亟需探索如何利用免费可获取的多光谱数据（ASTER和Sentinel-2A）并设计轻量化深度学习模型，在少样本条件下实现高精度岩性制图。

Method: (1) 数据层：将ASTER短波红外（SWIR）波段与Sentinel-2A影像进行配准和重采样，与Sentinel-2A的可见光-近红外（VNIR）和红边波段集成，构建互补多光谱数据集；(2) 模型层：设计紧凑型光谱增强多尺度CNN，包含残差光谱特征增强模块（用于波段间表示学习）和平行多尺度混合卷积模块（用于捕获空间-光谱特征）；(3) 实验层：在甘肃肃北县石包城地区，使用8158个训练样本和3497个空间独立验证样本，对八类岩性单元在少标签条件下进行分类，并与SAM、SVM、3D-CNN等方法对比。

Result: (1) 集成ASTER-Sentinel-2A数据集相比单传感器数据提升了分类性能，所提模型OA达94.12%、AA达94.04%、Kappa系数0.932，而仅用ASTER和仅用Sentinel-2A的OA分别为93.14%和92.40%；(2) 波段集成对SAM、SVM和3D-CNN也有正向效果，其OA分别提升至54.33%、86.12%和92.29%；(3) 所提CNN在所有评估方法中OA最高，优于SAM、SVM和传统3D-CNN；(4) t-SNE可视化表明，融入空间纹理特征比仅用光谱特征产生更紧凑、分离更好的岩性聚类；(5) 消融实验证实光谱特征增强模块和多尺度混合卷积模块各自对分类性能有贡献。

Conclusion: 本文证明，在缺乏高光谱影像和密集野外样本的干旱半干旱基岩裸露区，将免费可获取的多光谱数据（ASTER SWIR与Sentinel-2A VNIR/红边）进行波段级集成，并结合轻量级光谱-空间CNN，是一种实用且经济的岩性制图方案。该方法有效缓解了光谱信息有限和训练样本稀缺的双重挑战，为多光谱遥感岩性制图提供了新的技术路径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。本文本身就是一篇遥感岩性制图论文。改进方向：(1) 可引入注意力机制（如通道注意力、空间注意力或Transformer）替代或增强残差光谱特征增强模块，以更好地捕获长距离波段间依赖关系；(2) 可尝试多模态数据融合，如加入合成孔径雷达（SAR）数据以提供结构信息；(3) 可引入对比学习或自监督预训练策略，进一步缓解少量样本场景下的过拟合问题；(4) 可扩展到时序多光谱影像（如多时相Sentinel-2），利用时间维度的变化信息辅助岩性区分；(5) 可探索域自适应或迁移学习，将模型迁移到其他地质条件相似的区域。

Abstract (英文): Lithological mapping with multispectral remote sensing remains challenging when diagnostic spectral information is limited and reliable labeled samples are scarce. This problem is particularly relevant when convolutional neural networks (CNNs) are applied to lithological classification, because limited spectral dimensionality and scarce training samples may hinder the learning of discriminative spatial–spectral features. In this study, we developed a limited-sample lithological mapping framework for the Shibaocheng area of Subei County, Gansu Province, China, using band-integrated ASTER and Sentinel-2A multispectral imagery. ASTER shortwave infrared (SWIR) bands were co-registered and resampled to Sentinel-2A imagery, and then integrated with Sentinel-2A visible and near-infrared (VNIR) and red-edge bands to construct a complementary multispectral dataset. A compact spectrally enhanced multi-scale CNN was designed, incorporating a residual spectral feature enhancement module for inter-band representation learning and a parallel multi-scale hybrid convolution module for capturing spatial–spectral features. Eight lithological units were classified under limited-label conditions using 8158 training samples and 3497 spatially independent validation samples. Experimental results show that the band-integrated ASTER–Sentinel-2A dataset improved classification performance compared with single-sensor inputs. Using the proposed model, the band-integrated dataset achieved an overall accuracy (OA) of 94.12%, average accuracy (AA) of 94.04%, and Kappa coefficient of 0.932, compared with OA values of 93.14% and 92.40% obtained using ASTER and Sentinel-2A alone, respectively. The positive effect of band-level integration was also observed for spectral angle mapper (SAM), support vector machine (SVM), and 3D-CNN, whose OA values increased to 54.33%, 86.12%, and 92.29%, respectively. The proposed CNN achieved the highest OA among the evaluated methods, outperforming SAM, SVM, and the conventional 3D-CNN. In addition, t-SNE visualization indicated that incorporating spatial texture features produced more compact and better-separated lithological clusters than using spectral features alone. Ablation experiments further demonstrated that the proposed spectral feature enhancement and multi-scale hybrid convolution modules each contributed to improving lithological classification performance. These results demonstrate that integrating freely available multispectral data with a lightweight spectral–spatial CNN provides a practical and cost-effective solution for lithological mapping in bedrock-exposed arid to semi-arid regions, especially where hyperspectral imagery and dense field samples are unavailable.

### [202] [Beyond NDVI: A Multi-Index Remote Sensing Analysis of Wetland Marsh Recovery Following the Mississippi River Gulf Outlet Closure](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132159)
*Lloyd Ndlovu,Robert W. Whalin,Rocky Talchabhadel*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用1984-2025年Landsat卫星数据，通过控制中断时间序列(CITS)分析，评估了2009年密西西比河湾口航道(MRGO)关闭对路易斯安那州Shell Beach沿海湿地植被的因果影响。研究发现整体植被持续衰退，但淡水沼泽显著恢复，表明MRGO关闭对淡水沼泽有特异性恢复效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化2009年MRGO关闭对沿海湿地植被的因果效应，区分人为工程干预与自然气候变化对湿地生态系统的影响，为海岸带恢复管理提供科学依据。

Method: 采用CITS分析框架，结合STL季节分解、分段OLS回归与Newey-West HAC标准误，利用NDVI/kNDVI/NDII等多指数，以Barataria湾北部为未处理对照区，通过单组ITS和CITS双重差分(DiD)双重检验，排除飓风Katrina等混杂因素。

Result: 整体水平上NDVI(β3=-0.0034 yr⁻¹)、NDII(β3=-0.0032 yr⁻¹)、kNDVI(β3=-0.0016 yr⁻¹)显著负向斜率变化；分层分析发现淡水沼泽显著恢复(NDVI β3=+0.0190 yr⁻¹)，而盐水、半咸水和中间沼泽持续衰退；DiD证实NDII和kNDVI衰退为MRGO特异性效应。

Conclusion: 多指数、长时序Landsat监测结合季节分解与传感器间谐波校正，对于评估受管理沿海湿地的恢复轨迹至关重要；MRGO关闭对淡水沼泽有特异性恢复作用，但对其他植被群落产生负面效应。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。1)该方法可直接应用于我国黄河口、长江口等受围垦与水利工程影响的滨海湿地恢复评估；2)可引入国产高分(GF)系列数据与Landsat/Sentinel联合时序分析，提升时空分辨率；3)建议增加SAR数据(如Sentinel-1)监测湿地水文变化，与植被指数互补；4)可扩展至潮沟-盐沼耦合系统的工程效应评估。

Abstract (英文): We present a 42-year (1984–2025) Landsat consistent satellite vegetation trajectory for coastal wetlands in the Shell Beach area in the Breton Sound estuary, Louisiana. We applied the Controlled Interrupted Time Series (CITS) analysis to the satellite record to quantify the causal effect of the 2009 Mississippi River Gulf Outlet (MRGO) closure on the coastal wetland vegetation. The analysis used NDVI, kNDVI, and NDII across 88 vegetation transect plots located within five Coastal Reference and Monitoring Systems (CRMS) stations in the Shell Beach wetlands. Vegetation communities identified included Saline, Brackish, Freshwater, and Intermediate marsh. Sentinel-2 data from 2015 to 2025 were retained as an independent parallel record for NDRE analysis only. Quarterly median composites were decomposed using the Seasonal-Trend decomposition using LOESS (STL) to isolate de-seasonalized vegetation anomalies. The CITS design used segmented Ordinary Least Squares (OLS) regression with Newey–West HAC standard errors (lag = 3) at the study area. Northern Barataria Bay was used as an untreated regional control site to remove concurrent climate and sea level rise confounders. Whilst Hurricane Katrina and subsequent years (2005–2008) were excluded from the models, the single group ITS identified significant negative post-closure slope change across three indices. These were NDVI (β3 = −0.0034 yr−1, p = 0.000), NDII (β3 = −0.0032 yr−1), and kNDVI (β3 = −0.0016 yr−1). These values indicated continued site-level decline relative to the pre-closure trend. Community-stratified ITS analysis showed a distinct divergent pattern with Freshwater marshes demonstrating significant recovery, with NDVI β3 = +0.0190 yr−1, p = 0.000, whilst Saline, Brackish, and Intermediate communities continued to decline. CITS Difference-in-Differences (DiD) confirmed that site-level NDII and kNDVI declines were MRGO-specific. The DiD findings were that NDII = −0.00313 yr−1, p &lt; 0.001; kNDVI = −0.00123 yr−1, p = 0.008. These findings isolated that physiological water stress and the non-linear biomass losses were a result of the MRGO-closure. The Freshwater DiD for NDVI (+0.02071 yr−1, p = 0.000) was the strongest evidence of MRGO-specific recovery. Barataria Freshwater declined, whilst the Shell Beach Freshwater recovered. The results demonstrated that multi-index decadal Landsat monitoring with seasonal decomposition and full inter-sensor harmonization is essential for restoration trajectory assessment in managed coastal wetlands.

### [203] [Environmental Controls and Transition of the Baige Landslide Deformation Revealed by Time-Series Remote Sensing Observations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132169)
*Shuolong Huang,Gang Mei,Yingjie Sun*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 青藏高原东部高山峡谷区高海拔岩质滑坡频发，但对其时空演化过程及环境控制机制的定量理解仍不充分，特别是阶段依赖的驱动机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用SBAS-InSAR技术获取地表形变时序，结合STL时序分解分离季节性和趋势分量，利用PCA-ICA进行信号源分离，并通过斜坡单元空间统计方法分析形变场的空间分布特征。

Result: (1) 形变呈现三个明显阶段，以2018年10月为分界；(2) 失稳导致形变场系统重构，有效像元减少79.7%，变形方向反转，全局标准差从21.40 mm增至40.55 mm；(3) 驱动机制从短期的多因素控制转变为失稳后以温度为主导的长期环境控制。

Conclusion: 滑坡失稳后形变场发生显著重构，驱动机制从短期多因素协同控制转变为温度主导的长期环境控制，斜坡碎裂化和结构重组可能是这一转变的关键原因。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该方法可直接应用于其他高山峡谷区大型滑坡的时序监测分析。改进方向：(1) 融合多源SAR数据（如Sentinel-1与ALOS-2）提高时空分辨率；(2) 引入深度学习时序预测模型（如LSTM、Transformer）替代传统STL分解；(3) 结合光学遥感影像（如高分系列）进行滑坡边界提取验证；(4) 将PCA-ICA与地质力学模型耦合，实现驱动机制的物理约束反演。

Abstract (英文): High-altitude rock slides frequently occur in the high-mountain canyon regions of the eastern Tibetan Plateau, posing significant disaster risks. The Baige landslide catastrophically failed in October 2018, blocking the Jinsha River and forming a major landslide-dammed lake. However, quantitative understanding of the spatiotemporal evolution and environmental control mechanisms remains insufficient, particularly regarding stage-dependent driving mechanisms. This study investigates the Baige landslide using mall Baseline Subset Interferometric Synthetic Aperture Radar (SBAS-InSAR), Seasonal-Trend decomposition based on Loess (STL) time-series decomposition, Principal Component Analysis–Independent Component Analysis (PCA-ICA) signal analysis, and slope-unit spatial statistics. Results indicate that: (1) deformation exhibited three stages separated by October 2018: slow pre-slide deformation, post-slide residual creep, and long-term sustained acceleration; (2) instability caused systematic restructuring of the deformation field, with valid pixels decreasing from 2766 to 560, deformation changing from slight positive line-of-sight (LOS) displacement to pronounced negative LOS displacement, and global standard deviation increasing from 21.40 mm to 40.55 mm, with stronger disturbances in the steep front zone; and (3) the driving mechanism shifted from short-term multi-factor control to a temperature-dominated long-term environmental control regime after failure, while gravity-driven creep and post-failure structural adjustment remained important background controls. Slope fragmentation and structural reorganization likely contributed to this transition.
