### [235] [3D Gaussian Splatting for Large-Scale Remote Sensing: A PRISMA-Informed Scoping Review of Scalability, Geometric Reliability, and Benchmarking Across UAV/Aerial and Satellite Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132224)
*Wenbao Fan,Bo Wang,Junqiang Ye,Ruoyu Zha,H T Chen*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文对3D高斯泼溅（3DGS）在遥感领域的应用进行了PRISMA-informed综述，基于55篇核心文献，构建了分面分类法，并提出了一个平台感知的基准框架，以统一评估视觉保真度、计算成本、度量几何、产品效用、失败行为和可重复性元数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在大规模遥感应用中存在碎片化问题，分散于无人机/航空摄影测量、卫星重建、大场景缩放、表面建模和地理空间评估等多个子领域，缺乏统一的综述和评估框架。

Method: 采用PRISMA-informed范围综述方法，从Web of Science、Scopus、IEEE Xplore等数据库筛选55篇核心研究，构建分面分类法（按平台、传感器模型、可扩展性策略和几何监督组织文献），并在此基础上提出平台感知的基准框架。

Result: 分区、层次化、压缩和前馈推理可提升可扩展性，但不保证度量几何精度。可靠部署需要传感器一致的投影、几何或地理参考约束、明确的监督标签和产品级评估。在无控制点场景下，需区分内部一致性与独立验证的精度。

Conclusion: 提出了一个平台感知的基准框架，涵盖无人机/航空、卫星和混合场景，综合记录视觉质量、计算成本、度量几何、产品实用性、失败行为和可重复性元数据，以推动3DGS在遥感中的标准化评估与可靠部署。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。本文本身就是针对遥感的综述，所提出的平台感知基准框架可直接指导3DGS在遥感中的标准化评估。改进方向包括：(1) 将基准框架与现有遥感评测基准（如MVS、卫星立体匹配）结合；(2) 针对不同平台（UAV/卫星）差异化设计几何约束策略；(3) 引入无控制点场景下的内部一致性验证指标；(4) 扩展至多模态遥感数据（如SAR+光学）的3DGS适配。

Abstract (英文): 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) offers efficient explicit rendering, but large-scale remote-sensing use remains fragmented across UAV/aerial photogrammetry, satellite reconstruction, large-scene scaling, surface modeling, and geospatial evaluation. We present a Preferred Reporting Items for Systematic Reviews and Meta-Analyses (PRISMA)-informed scoping review based on 55 core studies identified through Web of Science, Scopus, IEEE Xplore, and supplementary searches completed on 3 June 2026. A faceted taxonomy organizes the literature by platform, sensor model, scalability strategy, and geometric supervision. The synthesis shows that partitioning, hierarchy, compression, and feed-forward inference improve scalability but do not guarantee metric geometry. Reliable deployment additionally requires sensor-consistent projection, geometric or georeferencing constraints, explicit supervision labels, and product-level evaluation. In control-point-free settings, internal consistency should be distinguished from independently validated accuracy. We therefore propose a platform-aware benchmark framework that jointly records visual fidelity, computational cost, metric geometry, product utility, failure behavior, and reproducibility metadata for UAV/aerial, satellite, and hybrid settings.

### [236] [SC-Net: Structural Constrained Contrastive Learning for Landslide Extraction Toward Power Transmission Corridor Safety Monitoring](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132216)
*Wei Song,S. Liu,S S Wu,Cheng Liao,Zongyuan Wu,Shiming Li,X B Zheng,Yanping Duan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结构约束对比学习网络（SC-Net），用于从遥感图像中提取滑坡信息。通过多结构特征提取、注意力自适应融合和掩码约束的物体级对比学习策略，在CAS滑坡数据集上取得了优于现有方法的性能（CAS-UAV IoU 89.89%，CAS-SAT IoU 79.76%），为电力输电走廊等基础设施的滑坡监测提供了有效解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 滑坡是常见且具有破坏性的地质灾害，威胁基础设施长期稳定性。电力输电走廊常穿越山区和林区，植被遮挡导致滑坡边界模糊、与周围地物视觉相似度高，使得从遥感影像中准确高效识别滑坡仍是一大挑战。

Method: 提出SC-Net：（1）多结构特征提取模块捕捉滑坡几何特征；（2）基于注意力的自适应特征融合模块融合预训练骨干网络的多尺度语义表征；（3）掩码约束的物体级对比学习策略，增强滑坡与非滑坡区域的判别性，保持全局结构一致性。

Result: 在CAS滑坡数据集上，SC-Net在CAS-UAV和CAS-SAT上分别达到89.89%和79.76%的IoU，比最优基线分别高出2.09%和0.46%。

Conclusion: 所提方法为大规模滑坡监测提供了有效解决方案，并展示了在电力输电走廊巡检和基础设施安全评估中的应用潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感滑坡提取论文，改进方向包括：（1）引入多时相遥感数据，利用时序对比学习增强对滑坡动态变化的建模能力；（2）结合InSAR形变测量数据作为辅助监督信号，提升对潜在滑坡的早期识别能力；（3）将对比学习扩展到跨域场景（如不同卫星传感器、不同分辨率），增强模型泛化性；（4）引入轻量化骨干网络或知识蒸馏策略，适配星上实时处理或大规模遥感影像的快速解译需求。

Abstract (英文): Landslides are among the most common and destructive geological hazards and pose a significant threat to the long-term stability of infrastructure systems. In particular, long-distance power transmission corridors often traverse mountainous and forested regions, where landslides can endanger tower foundations and transmission line safety. Such landslides predominantly occur in sloped forested areas, where dense vegetation causes severe occlusion that blurs landslide boundaries and creates strong visual similarity with surrounding land covers. Consequently, accurate and efficient landslide identification from remote sensing imagery remains a significant challenge. To address these challenges, we propose a structural constrained contrastive learning network (SC-Net) for reliable landslide extraction from remote sensing images. First, a multi-structural feature extraction module is designed to capture landslide-specific geometric characteristics. These features are further enhanced by fusing multi-scale semantic representations extracted from a pretrained backbone network through an attention-based adaptive feature fusion module. Additionally, a mask-constrained object-level contrastive learning strategy is introduced to enforce global structural consistency at the landslide object-level, thereby improving the discriminability between landslide and non-landslide regions. Extensive experiments conducted on the publicly available CAS landslide dataset demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method. The proposed SC-Net achieves IoU scores of 89.89% and 79.76% on the CAS-UAV and CAS-SAT datasets, respectively, outperforming the best-performing baseline by 2.09% and 0.46%. The proposed method provides an effective solution for large-scale landslide monitoring and demonstrates potential for applications in power transmission corridor inspection and infrastructure safety assessment.

</details>


### [237] [Multi-Level Classification of Urban Green Space Using Multi-Source Remote Sensing and Geospatial Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132192)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有城市绿地监测仅关注物理层植被提取，忽视了功能属性，导致监测结果无法客观反映绿地规划合理性。为弥合物理解译层与功能语义层之间的语义鸿沟，亟需一种能同时考虑植被物理特征和社会功能属性的多层级分类方法。

Conclusion: 融合多源遥感和地理空间大数据、结合先验知识注入和深度学习的方法，能有效弥合城市绿地的物理层与功能层语义鸿沟，为城市绿地规划合理性评估提供更客观的多层级分类结果。

Abstract (英文): Urban Green Spaces (UGSs) monitoring usually focuses on the extraction of vegetation in the physical layer, while neglecting their functional attributes. This renders the monitoring results unable to objectively reflect the rationality of UGS planning. To address these issues, this study proposes a multi-level classification method integrating multi-source remote sensing and geospatial big data to bridge the semantic gap between the physical layer and the functional layer. In this method, a strategy of prior knowledge injection and semantic reconstruction was developed through the fine-tuning of a BERT model with cross-mapping rules. This strategy aims to classify the urban area into 24 functional categories, generating the social-functional basemap in a functional layer, based on Point of Interest (POI), OpenStreetMap (OSM), and Global Urban Boundary (GUB). Meanwhile, a novel deep learning architecture, namely the Multi-Shape and Spectral Aware Network (MSSANet), was designed for precise vegetation classification of UGSs in the physical layer. Finally, a “function-first, vegetation-second” coupling paradigm containing three functional attribute layers, referring to the Code for Classification of UGS in China (CJJ/T 85-2017), was established. This paradigm integrates the social-functional basemap with physical vegetation patches to build a multi-level UGS classification framework, i.e., the 5 major UGS categories, 11 intermediate UGS categories, and 24 fine-grained UGS sub-categories. Experiments conducted in Jinan and Qingdao, China, demonstrate the efficacy of the proposed method for refined multi-level UGS mapping.

### [238] [Impacts of Extreme Climate on NDVI in China—Response Patterns and Threshold Effects](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132180)
*Mengwei Li,Rong Li,Rui Zhu,Jianan Shan,Zh. Zhao,Fulong Chen,Zhenliang Yin*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 基于2001-2024年中国ERA5-Land温度和降水数据及MODIS NDVI数据，采用Pearson相关分析、小波分析和XGBoost-SHAP模型，研究了极端气候指数对NDVI的影响。结果表明NDVI以0.021/10年速率增长，R25和SDII是主要驱动因子（贡献率31.6%和12.5%），超出阈值（R25>1.85天，SDII>4.35 mm/day）时极端气候显著影响植被生长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究极端气候事件对植被动态的影响对于维持生态系统稳定性至关重要，但目前对中国区域极端气候与NDVI响应的定量归因和阈值分析尚不充分。

Method: 采用Pearson相关分析、小波分析以及XGBoost-SHAP可解释机器学习模型，分析极端温度指数（如FD0）和极端降水指数（如R25、SDII、CDD）与NDVI的关系，并进行贡献率量化与阈值探测。

Result: (1) NDVI以0.021/10年的速率稳步增长，极端温度与降水指数在多数区域呈上升趋势；(2) NDVI与多数极端指数正相关，仅与FD0和CDD显著负相关；(3) R25和SDII是全国NDVI变化的主要驱动因子，贡献率分别为31.6%和12.5%，阈值分别为1.85天和4.35 mm/day。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了极端气候对中国植被变化的关键驱动因子及其阈值，为理解和管理植被对气候极端事件增强的响应提供了科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该论文本身就是遥感与气候交叉研究。改进方向：(1) 可引入更高空间分辨率遥感数据（如Landsat、Sentinel-2）进行多尺度验证；(2) 增加植被类型（林地/草地/农田）分类分析，细化不同生态系统的响应差异；(3) 引入更多遥感植被指数（如EVI、LAI、GPP）进行多指标协同分析；(4) 可耦合CMIP6未来气候情景数据，进行未来极端气候对植被影响的预测建模。

Abstract (英文): Studying the impact of extreme climate events on vegetation dynamics is crucial for maintaining ecosystem stability. Based on ERA5-Land temperature and precipitation data, as well as MOD13C2 data, this study employs Pearson correlation analysis, wavelet analysis, and the XGBoost-SHAP model to analyze the response of the Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) in China to extreme climate variations. The findings reveal the following. (1) NDVI increased steadily at a rate of 0.021/10 yr from 2001 to 2024. Extreme temperature and precipitation indices show an increasing trend in most regions. (2) NDVI was positively correlated with most extreme temperature and precipitation indices, and showed a significant negative correlation exclusively with Frost Days FDO (Frost Days) and CDD (Consecutive Dry Days). (3) R25 (Number of Heavy Precipitation Days) and SDII (Simple daily intensity index) are the primary drivers of nationwide NDVI changes, with contribution rates of 31.6% and 12.5%. Extreme climate indices can significantly affect vegetation growth when surpassing certain thresholds. For instance, the thresholds for R25 and SDII are 1.85 days and 4.35 mm/day. This study provides a scientific basis for understanding and managing vegetation responses to increasing climate extremes.

### [239] [RepLite-YOLO: A Parameter-Efficient Residual-Enhanced Detector for Ship Recognition in Remote Sensing Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132238)
*Ruijia Fu,Zuomin Wang,Zijun Lin,Ying Li,Bingxin Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出RepLite-YOLO轻量级遥感船舶检测框架，基于YOLOv11n，通过ADown模块保留空间特征、C3k2_OREPA_RS模块在线重参数化高效重构、ELANFusion_Block集成深度可分离卷积缓解多尺度聚合瓶颈，以及Detect_DWLite轻量化解耦检测头。在Vessel和Ship Detection数据集上，参数量减少57.4%，GFLOPs降低49.2%，mAP@50分别提升1.2和1.3个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥感船舶检测面临复杂海面背景噪声、目标尺度变化大和边缘硬件限制三大挑战，现有方法难以在轻量化与高精度之间取得平衡。

Method: 1) ADown模块：双分支下采样机制，保留船体边缘响应同时抑制海面随机干扰；2) C3k2_OREPA_RS模块：利用在线重参数化(OREPA)在不增加推理开销的前提下高效重构深层网络；3) ELANFusion_Block：将深度可分离卷积(DSC)集成到ELAN范式，缓解多尺度特征聚合瓶颈；4) Detect_DWLite：高度压缩的解耦预测检测头。

Result: 相较于YOLOv11n，参数量减少57.4%，GFLOPs降低49.2%；在Vessel数据集上mAP@50提升1.2个百分点，在Ship Detection数据集上提升1.3个百分点。

Conclusion: RepLite-YOLO在检测精度与计算效率之间取得了良好的平衡，验证了多模块协同设计在轻量化遥感船舶检测中的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) ADown模块可进一步引入注意力机制（如CBAM或SE）以增强对复杂海面背景中弱小目标的特征聚焦能力；2) C3k2_OREPA_RS模块可尝试与其他重参数化方法（如RepVGG、DBB）结合，探索更优的结构重参数化策略；3) ELANFusion_Block可引入可变形卷积(DCN)以适应船舶目标的任意朝向和形变；4) 检测头可扩展为旋转框检测(OBB)以适应遥感图像中船舶的任意角度分布；5) 可引入频域学习或小波变换等模块增强对云雾、光照变化等遥感特有噪声的鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Remote sensing ship detection plays a pivotal role in maritime surveillance, safety assurance, and traffic management. However, current detection methods often face significant challenges due to complex sea-surface background noise, large target-scale variations, and edge-hardware limitations. In this paper, we propose RepLite-YOLO, a lightweight detection framework based on YOLOv11n. Specifically, to alleviate irreversible spatial information loss during downsampling, we adopt the ADown module, originally introduced in YOLOv9, to generate spatially complementary features through its two-branch downsampling mechanism. This design helps preserve salient hull-edge responses while suppressing part of the random sea-surface interference, thereby improving feature robustness for small ship targets. To achieve substantial structural streamlining while maintaining competitive representational capacity under strict hardware constraints, we design the C3k2_OREPA_RS module, utilizing online re-parameterization (OREPA) to efficiently reconstruct deep layers without additional re-parameterization-induced inference operations. Furthermore, we construct the ELANFusion_Block by integrating Depthwise Separable Convolutions (DSC) into the ELAN paradigm to alleviate the multi-scale aggregation bottleneck, and tailor the Detect_DWLite head for highly compressed decoupled prediction. Experimental results show that RepLite-YOLO achieves a favorable balance between detection accuracy and computational efficiency. Compared with YOLOv11n, it reduces the number of parameters by 57.4% and GFLOPs by 49.2%, while maintaining competitive detection accuracy with slight mAP@50 improvements of 1.2 and 1.3 percentage points on the Vessel dataset and Ship Detection dataset, respectively.

### [240] [HCA-YOLO: A Hierarchical Cross-Scale Attention Learning Framework for UAV Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132196)
*Wei Wang,Y Zhang,Y Zhang,Lingjun Zhao,Xingwei Yan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种层级注意力促进的跨尺度学习框架（HACLF），用于解决复杂场景下不同尺寸无人机（UAV）的准确检测问题。该框架通过层级注意力机制生成多尺度特征，采用双分支准残差结构保护目标内容并重建细节信息，并结合动态聚焦损失度量优化边界框回归。实验表明，该方法在恶劣光照和天气条件下对小而弱的无人机检测效果显著，mAP相比YOLOv6提升18.5%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 骨干网络引入层级注意力机制生成多尺度特征；2) 颈部构建双分支特征：目标特定特征算子分支 + 上采样分支，通过准残差结构连接以保护目标内容并重建细节；3) 动态聚焦损失度量用于边界框回归，提升学习有效性。

Result: 在收集的数据集上，所提方法相比YOLOv6的mAP提升18.5%，尤其在小目标和恶劣光照/天气条件下检测准确。

Abstract (英文): The accurate detection of unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) in various sizes played an important role in the practical applications. Yet the preceding works suffered from the missing inference, the false alarms, and the poor accuracy due to the the adverse scene conditions, as well as the mutable scales. To solve the problems, a hierarchical attention promoted cross-scale learning framework was proposed in this paper. First, the hierarchical attention mechanism was introduced in the backbone to generate the multi-scale features of targets, so they can be discerned and located at different scales. The resulting features were further delivered to the neck, in which two branches of features were built, respectively. The former was obtained by the target-specific feature operator, while the latter was generated by the upsampling operation. The dual branches were further connected in the quasi-residual structure. So the content of targets can be protected well, and the detail information can be reconstructed. Finally, the dynamic focusing loss measurement was presented to regress the bounding box of the target, so the learning effectiveness of presented the architecture can be promoted. To verify the proposed method, multiple rounds of experiments were performed. The results demonstrated that small and weak drones can be detected accurately, especially in adverse lighting and weather conditions. The evaluation metric of mean average precision rate (mAP) can be improved by 18.5% (YOLO6) on the collected dataset.

### [241] [Remote Sensing-Based Identification of Spatial Spillovers and Transmission Pathways in the Heat–Energy–Carbon Nexus: Evidence from the Yangtze River Delta](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132222)
*Gaoneng Lai,Lei Jiang,Yingbiao Chen,Shitai Bao,Jinxin Duan,Zuojie Zhu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用长三角城市群2014-2023年多源地理空间数据，构建多尺度分析框架，通过构建人为能源活动强度（AEAI）指标，结合空间杜宾模型和空间中介方法，揭示了城市热岛（UHI）与碳排放之间的空间关联及其行为中介路径，发现AEAI解释了UHI-碳排放关联的44.63%，表明该关联主要嵌入能源密集型人类活动的空间模式中，而非纯粹的直接热效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管UHI效应与碳排放的关联已受到关注，但其中的行为中介路径和跨区域溢出模式尚未被充分理解，缺乏对"热-能源-碳"耦合系统中空间关联和中介机制的深入分析。

Method: 采用多尺度分析框架：1 km城市群探索性分析和5 km空间计量建模；构建人为能源活动强度（AEAI）作为能源相关人类活动的代理指标；运用空间杜宾模型结合空间中介方法，分析"热-能源-碳"关联中的空间关联和统计中介路径。

Result: (1)碳排放呈现显著的正向空间溢出效应，与热扩散过程和社会经济网络交互一致；(2)AEAI在UHI与碳排放关联中起到显著的部分统计中介作用，解释总关联的44.63%，表明该关联部分嵌入能源密集型人类活动的空间模式中。

Conclusion: 区域气候治理需要超越单一城市干预和纯物理降温策略，转向跨区域协调与行为调控相结合的综合方法；推广被动冷却导向的城市规划和需求侧能源转型有助于降低碳锁定风险，支持气候韧性城市群发展。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该框架可直接应用于遥感驱动的城市气候研究：(1)利用热红外遥感反演地表温度（LST）替代气象站点数据，提升UHI空间表征的精细度；(2)结合夜间灯光遥感（NPP-VIIRS等）和人口密度数据完善AEAI指标构建；(3)引入遥感估算的碳排放产品（如OCO-2、GOSAT数据同化产品）验证空间溢出效应；(4)将多尺度空间分析框架扩展到其他遥感数据密集的城市群，结合植被指数（NDVI/NDBI）和地表反照率等遥感参数，构建更完整的中介路径模型。

Abstract (英文): The urban heat island (UHI) effect represents a critical urban climate phenomenon arising from the combined pressures of rapid urbanization and climate warming. Although its association with carbon emissions has received increasing scholarly attention, the underlying behavior-mediated pathways and cross-regional spillover patterns remain insufficiently understood. Using multi-source geospatial data for the Yangtze River Delta urban agglomeration from 2014 to 2023, this study develops a multi-scale analytical framework integrating 1 km urban agglomeration exploratory analysis and 5 km spatial econometric modeling. Anthropogenic Energy Activity Intensity (AEAI) is constructed as a proxy for energy-related human activities, and a spatial Durbin model, combined with a spatial mediation approach, is employed to examine the spatial associations and statistically mediated pathways within the “heat-energy-carbon” nexus. The results indicate that: (1) carbon emissions exhibit significant positive spatial spillover effects, consistent with thermal diffusion processes and socioeconomic network interactions; (2) AEAI represents a substantial partial statistical mediation pathway in the association between UHI and carbon emissions, accounting for 44.63% of the total association. This suggests that the UHI–carbon emission linkage is partly embedded in spatial patterns of energy-intensive human activities rather than reflecting a purely direct thermal effect. These findings suggest that regional climate governance may need to move beyond single-city interventions and purely physical cooling strategies toward integrated approaches that combine cross-regional coordination with behavioral regulation. Promoting passive cooling-oriented urban planning and demand-side energy transitions may help reduce carbon lock-in risks and support the development of climate-resilient urban agglomerations.

### [242] [Integrating Commercial and Public Imagery to Accelerate Deforestation Alerts](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132221)
*Zhiqiang Yang,Eric L. Bullock,Erik Lindquist,Carole Andrianirina,Sean P. Healey*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了DIAS（Disturbance Index Alert System），一个基于扰动指数Z-score的开源框架，通过融合多源遥感影像（如PlanetScope、Landsat、Sentinel-1/2）生成森林砍伐预警。在马达加斯加的实验表明，相比传统单传感器系统，DIAS能够提供更及时的预警，在10米参考像素尺度上，一个月内可检测出三分之二的森林砍伐事件（假警报率约20%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卫星森林砍伐预警需要快速成像频率，这迫使必须联合使用不同传感器。但现有预警系统大多依赖历史数据比对和稳定的传感器定标，难以有效融合多源异构遥感数据，亟需一种轻量级、跨传感器的通用预警框架。

Method: DIAS框架将不同传感器的影像转换为可互操作的扰动指数（DI）流，核心策略不是将像素与历史状态对比，而是通过计算像素在森林敏感轴上的Z-score位置（相对于整幅影像的森林像素总体分布），实现多传感器DI值的统一。该方法减少了历史归档处理需求、降低了对传感器定标稳定性的依赖，并允许动态增减传感器。

Result: 在马达加斯加的研究中，DIAS融合商业PlanetScope日影像与公共Landsat、Sentinel-1/2数据，一个月内可高置信度检测出三分之二的森林砍伐事件（假警报率约20%），而仅使用公共数据时一个月内可检测40%。融合系统的预警及时性优于传统的单传感器系统及简单的加法组合系统。

Conclusion: 随着商业地球观测选择日益增多，需要像DIAS这样灵活、计算轻量的方法，以适应多样化和仅有松散定标的仪器，从而支持及时的森林监测。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感森林扰动检测领域的核心研究。改进方案：（1）引入高光谱传感器（如EnMAP、PRISMA）增强森林敏感轴的光谱特征维度；（2）结合SAR的极化散射机制与光学Z-score，提升云覆盖区的检测能力；（3）将DIAS扩展到热带泥炭地、红树林等特殊生态系统，调整森林敏感轴以适应不同植被类型；（4）集成边缘计算或星上处理能力，进一步降低数据传输和延迟；（5）结合深度学习（如时序Transformer）对Z-score序列进行异常检测，减少误报率。

Abstract (英文): Generating satellite-based deforestation alerts with actionable latency requires frequent imaging, creating an imperative to use different sensors together. We introduce a simple and open-source framework called the Disturbance Index Alert System (DIAS), which is based upon transformation of imagery from different sources into an interoperable stream of Disturbance Index (DI) values. Whereas most alert systems target divergence of forested pixels from historical states, DIAS targets movement of a pixel’s Z-score position relative to the image-wide population of forest pixels along a forest-sensitive axis. This strategy provides the following practical benefits: (1) it reduces the need to process the historical archive; (2) it reduces dependence upon stable sensor calibration; (3) it allows Z-score-based DI values to be combined across sensors; and (4) it accommodates changes to the group of sensors providing measurements. We demonstrated in Madagascar that sensor integration through DIAS can provide more timely alerts than both conventional individual-sensor systems and additive combination of such systems. Across our study sites, using a commercial source of daily imaging (PlanetScope) in conjunction with imagery from public sources (Landsat, Sentinels-1 and -2) allowed high-confidence detection (false alert rate of approximately 20%) of two-thirds of deforestation occurring at 10 m reference pixels within one month; 40% were detected in that timeframe with public data alone. As commercial options for Earth observation proliferate, flexible and computationally lightweight approaches such as DIAS are needed to accommodate diverse and sometimes only loosely calibrated instruments in support of timely forest monitoring.

### [243] [Detection of Bark Beetle Attacks Using Time-Aggregated Satellite Data with Machine Learning](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132234)
*S. Zeinali,Per‐Ola Olsson,Ted Kronvall,Magnus Wiktorsson,Johan Lindström*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用每周聚合的Sentinel-2卫星数据与静态地理/林业数据，结合XGBoost分类器，探讨了早期树皮甲虫攻击检测。结果表明，静态与卫星数据结合能显著提升检测性能，并识别出关键检测周（第19、25、31、33周），其中Red-edge 3和蓝色波段是最重要的卫星特征，土地覆盖和地形是最重要的静态特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 树皮甲虫攻击对森林生态系统和经济造成严重威胁，早期检测对于及时干预和减少损失至关重要。现有方法多依赖单一数据源，未能充分利用多源数据的互补优势。

Method: 使用XGBoost分类器，对比三种数据组合（仅静态数据、仅卫星数据、两者结合）；利用每周累积的Sentinel-2数据训练模型，追踪模型性能和特征重要性随时间变化；系统分析特征重要性排序。

Result: 静态与卫星数据结合时，Red-edge 3和蓝色Sentinel-2波段最重要；添加静态特征降低了红色和Red-edge 2波段的重要性；土地覆盖和地形是最重要的静态特征；关键检测周为第19周（主要群飞周）、第25周（群飞后6周）、第31和33周（攻击后3个月以上）。

Conclusion: 结合静态特征与每周累积的Sentinel-2数据对提高树皮甲虫攻击检测至关重要，该方法可作为早期预警系统的重要组成部分。

Abstract (英文): In this study, we explored how early bark beetle attacks can be detected using weekly aggregated Sentinel-2 data in combination with static data, such as geo- and forestry data. We used an XGBoost classifier, known for its strength and reliability in classification, and compared three sets of data: static data only, satellite data only, and using both together. Having trained the models on cumulative weekly data, we were able to track changes in model performance and feature importance over time, identifying key weeks for the detection of bark beetle attacks. A systematic overview of feature importance identified the Red-edge 3 and blue Sentinel-2 bands as the most important when combined with static data; it also showed changes in feature importance compared to using satellite-only data, e.g., adding static features reduced the importance of red and red-edge 2 bands. Among the static features, land cover and landforms were the most important. Evaluating the temporal features for the combined model highlighted certain weeks as containing key information for detection: week 19, which was the main swarming week; week 25, which is 6 weeks after swarming and just before the second generation is completed; and weeks 31 and 33, more than 3 months after the tree was attacked and well after the new generation has swarmed. The study shows that combining static features with cumulative Sentinel-2, accumulated across weeks, are all important for improving the detection of bark beetle attacks, and that such ideas form an important part of early warning systems.

### [244] [Semantic Consistency and Uncertainty-Driven Small-Object Detection for Class Imbalance](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132208)
*Nuo Chen,Peng Zhao,Shouquan Hou*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对航拍图像小目标检测中的样本不平衡问题（复杂视角、任意朝向、长尾分布），提出SCUD训练框架，包含标签噪声抑制策略（LNSS，基于语义一致性的对比学习）、尺度感知重采样策略（SARS，缓解小目标重复导致的过拟合）和自适应实例选择机制（AISM，联合预测不确定性与全局统计先验），在DOTA-v1.0和DIOR数据集上分别达到70.7%和88.1%的mAP50，显著提升了稀有类别的检测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 航拍图像小目标检测中，复杂成像视角、任意目标朝向和长尾类别分布共同导致样本不平衡问题，严重降低检测稳定性并造成少数类频繁误分类。

Method: 提出SCUD训练框架，包括三个核心模块：(1) LNSS：基于语义一致性的对比学习机制，约束相似样本在特征空间中的聚合，减少噪声样本对优化的负面影响；(2) SARS：尺度感知重采样策略，缓解小目标过度重复导致的噪声放大和过拟合；(3) AISM：自适应实例选择机制，联合建模预测不确定性和全局统计先验，动态强调从信息丰富样本中学习。

Result: 在DOTA-v1.0数据集上达到70.7% mAP50，在DIOR数据集上达到88.1% mAP50，多个稀有类别的检测精度显著提升。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效解决了航拍图像小目标检测中的样本不平衡问题，证明了在应对样本不平衡方面的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感航拍图像领域的核心工作。改进方向：(1) LNSS中的对比学习可引入多尺度特征对齐机制，提升不同分辨率航拍图像下的语义一致性；(2) SARS可扩展为动态尺度感知采样，结合在线难例挖掘进一步提升小目标多样性；(3) AISM可引入类别自适应阈值，更好地处理遥感场景中更为极端的类别不平衡；此外，该框架可迁移至遥感旋转目标检测任务中，与Swin Transformer等骨干网络结合进一步提升性能。

Abstract (英文): In aerial image small-object detection, complex imaging perspectives, arbitrary object orientations, and long-tailed category distributions jointly exacerbate sample imbalance, which significantly degrades detection stability and leads to frequent misclassification of minority categories. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a novel training framework termed SCUD. Specifically, in the label noise suppression strategy (LNSS), a contrastive learning mechanism based on semantic consistency is introduced to constrain the aggregation of similar samples in the feature space, thereby reducing the adverse impact of noisy samples on model optimization. In addition, a scale-aware resampling strategy (SARS) is designed to alleviate noise amplification and overfitting caused by excessive repetition of small objects during training. Furthermore, an adaptive instance selection mechanism (AISM) is developed by jointly modeling prediction uncertainty and global statistical priors, enabling the model to dynamically emphasize learning from informative samples. Extensive experiments are conducted on two publicly available unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) aerial image datasets to validate the effectiveness of the proposed approach. The proposed method achieves an mAP50 of 70.7% on the DOTA-v1.0 dataset and 88.1% on the DIOR dataset. Notably, the detection accuracy of several rare categories is significantly improved, further demonstrating the effectiveness of the proposed method in addressing sample imbalance in aerial image small-object detection.

### [245] [Sequence-Aware Deep Learning for Field-Scale Surface Soil Moisture Estimation from Sentinel-1, HLS, and Ancillary Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132213)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统卫星土壤水分产品空间分辨率过粗，无法满足田块尺度的农业用水管理需求，亟需发展高精度、场尺度的土壤水分估算方法。

Method: 构建多源数据集（2016-2024年5-9月，1469样本/65特征），包括Sentinel-1 SAR特征、HLS光学特征、气象数据、土壤质地与容重、地形、作物标签、灌溉概率标志及不规则时间步长编码。比较LSTM、TCN及其注意力增强变体（FA、TA、FTA），以湿年（2016）和干年（2023）联合数据进行时间泛化验证。

Result: 最优模型FTA-TCN在验证年取得R²=0.851，RMSE=0.024 m³/m³，MAE=0.020 m³/m³，显著优于基线LSTM（R²=0.422）和TCN（R²=0.746）。SHAP分析表明前期降水和短期降雨累积为主导因子，卫星特征贡献约28.5%的聚合SHAP重要性。

Conclusion: 双注意力时间卷积网络（FTA-TCN）能够在卫星信号与本地土壤-气象-管理背景耦合的条件下，捕获干湿季田块尺度土壤水分动态，为精准农业水分管理提供了有效工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：①可引入多极化SAR特征（如极化分解参数）提升对地表粗糙度和植被结构的解耦能力；②可尝试将FTA-TCN与物理模型（如数据同化）结合，增强物理可解释性；③可扩展至更高分辨率（如3-10m）的国产卫星数据（如高分系列、Sentinel-2 10m）验证泛化能力；④可探索轻量化模型结构以适应星上实时处理需求。

Abstract (英文): Accurate field-scale surface soil moisture (SSM) measures are important for agricultural water management. Conventional satellite SSM products remain too coarse for within-field applications. Here, we developed sequence-aware deep learning models for growing-season SSM estimation by fusing data from Sentinel-1 C-band SAR, harmonized Landsat-8/Sentinel-2 (HLS), and local ancillary datasets. We assembled a multi-source dataset on Sentinel-1 overpass time for 2016–2024 (May–September), yielding 1469 samples and 65 features per sample, including SAR and optical features, meteorological data, soil texture and bulk density, topography, crop labels, irrigation-likelihood flag, and irregular-time-step encoding. We compared long short-term memory (LSTM) and temporal convolutional neural network (TCN) architectures together with attention-augmented variants, including feature attention (FA), temporal attention (TA), and the combined feature–temporal attention (FTA). Models were trained and tested on seven years of data and were validated based on a temporal generalization using combined data of a wet year (2016) and a dry year (2023). The best model, FTA-TCN, achieved R2 = 0.851, RMSE = 0.024 m3.m−3, and MAE = 0.020 m3.m−3 on the withheld validation years, outperforming the base LSTM (R2 = 0.422; RMSE = 0.053 m3.m−3; MAE = 0.043 m3.m−3) and the base TCN (R2 = 0.746; RMSE = 0.034 m3.m−3; MAE = 0.022 m3.m−3). Shapley additive explanations (SHAP) analysis indicated that antecedent precipitation and short-term rainfall accumulations were dominant forcings, while soil texture, elevation, incidence angle, and vegetation indices modulated SSM variability. Satellite-derived features accounted for ~28.5% of aggregated SHAP importance. Overall, the results show that dual-attention temporal convolution can capture field-scale SSM dynamics across wet and dry seasons when satellite signals are coupled with local soil-meteorological-management context.

*Yue Wang,Ningxin Yong,Siyu Zhu,Yang Hong*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球变暖和快速城市化背景下，短时夏季暴雨日益强烈和局地化，但其时空特征、垂直结构和环境驱动因素尚不清楚，亟需深入理解以提升城市洪涝韧性。

Method: 结合多源遥感数据集和中国新一代星载双频降水雷达观测，运用可解释贝叶斯优化XGBoost（EBOX）模型分析暴雨的环境驱动因素，并通过三维雷达探测揭示暴雨垂直结构。

Abstract (英文): With global warming and rapid urbanization, short-duration summer rainstorms are becoming more intense and localized, posing growing challenges to urban flood resilience. However, their spatiotemporal characteristics, vertical structures, and environmental drivers remain poorly understood. Here, we combine multi-source remote sensing datasets and China’s new-generation satellite-borne dual-frequency precipitation radar observations to investigate summer rainstorms in Nanjing, China, during 2017–2024. Results reveal pronounced spatiotemporal heterogeneity, with higher rainfall intensities concentrated over urban and adjacent areas. During the study period, rainstorm intensity and duration increased by 7.44% and 38.63%, respectively, while the affected area decreased by 8.18%, indicating a transition toward more localized yet more intense rainfall events. Environmental analyses suggest that large-scale thermodynamic conditions and regional topographic forcing provide a favorable background for convection development, while local urban thermal effects may further modulate rainfall enhancement. Three-dimensional radar detection of an illustrative rainstorm event indicates an inverted-cone vertical structure, suggesting a mixed convective-stratiform precipitation structure involving both warm-rain and ice-phase processes. An Explainable Bayesian-Optimized XGBoost (EBOX) model further identifies near-surface air temperature and specific humidity as the primary environmental factors associated with rainstorm occurrence and development. Overall, this study highlights the value of integrating satellite remote sensing with explainable artificial intelligence to improve understanding of urban extreme rainfall and provide new insights into how climate change, topography, and urbanization jointly shape precipitation extremes in rapidly urbanizing monsoon regions.

### [247] [Multi-Modal Data Fusion for Dynamic Target Depth Retrieval in Aquatic Environments](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132230)
*Xiangyong Liu,Zhiqiang Xu,Tianhong Ding*

Method: 1) 以光学RGB图像和神经形态视觉(NeuroIV)数据作为联合输入，构建三通道特征提取与融合网络；2) 利用超图结构建立动态（时间）节点与静态（空间）节点之间的关联权重，捕获时空相关性；3) 采用逐元素乘法替代传统点积注意力，降低高维多模态数据的计算复杂度；4) 引入轻量级可变形注意力金字塔(DAP)与扩散模型，优化深度图像边缘，抑制估计结果中的不连续性和突变。

Abstract (英文): To address the challenges of severe optical attenuation and dynamic feature extraction for moving target depth retrieval in complex underwater remote sensing environments, this paper proposes a dynamic target depth estimation method based on multi-source data fusion. Taking optical RGB imagery and neuromorphic vision (NeuroIV) data as joint inputs, the proposed method constructs a three-channel feature extraction and fusion network. By leveraging a hypergraph structure, it establishes association weights between dynamic (temporal) and static (spatial) nodes to capture spatiotemporal correlations. To efficiently process the high-dimensional multi-modal data, the traditional dot-product attention is replaced with element-wise multiplication, significantly reducing computational complexity. Furthermore, a lightweight deformable attention pyramid (DAP) and diffusion model is introduced to refine depth image edges, effectively suppressing discontinuities and abruptness in the estimation results. Compared to single-modality optical imagery, the fused multi-modal data yields a superior signal-to-noise ratio and foreground contrast, achieving an improvement of over 20% in the MAE index. These results validate the effectiveness and superiority of the proposed multi-modal fusion strategy for dynamic target observation and depth retrieval in aquatic environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 臭氧作为一种关键二次污染物，时空异质性显著，给区域协同空气污染控制带来挑战。然而，对于干旱城市群地区高分辨率臭氧空间反演及其驱动机制的系统性理解仍然有限，亟需开展研究。

Method: (1) 建立包含XGBoost、RF、ET、GBDT等16种机器学习和深度学习模型的多模型对比框架，评估臭氧反演性能；(2) 基于最优模型实现2023年研究区高精度每日臭氧空间重建；(3) 利用SHAP方法定量解释各驱动因子贡献及非线性响应关系；(4) 采用后向轨迹模型结合WPSCF和WCWT方法识别潜在源区和传输路径。

Result: (1) XGBoost模型表现最优（R²=0.93，RPD>3），2023年高浓度O3主要分布在乌鲁木齐南部、昌吉南部和塔城南部，乌鲁木齐南部为最突出热点；(2) 向下短波辐射和气温是O3空间变异的主要驱动因子，二者对O3形成呈现显著非线性响应和阈值效应；(3) 西风输送是主要外源贡献路径，潜在源区主要位于天山北坡周边及中亚地区（哈萨克斯坦东部和吉尔吉斯斯坦北部）。

Conclusion: 本研究从高精度反演、驱动机制分析和跨区域传输识别三个方面系统阐明了干旱城市群臭氧污染的形成机制，为精准空气污染控制策略提供了科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身虽未直接使用遥感数据，但方法体系与遥感高度兼容：(1) 可将卫星遥感反演的O3柱浓度数据（如TROPOMI、OMI）作为模型输入或验证数据，提升空间覆盖度和反演精度；(2) 驱动因子中的DSR和TEM均可从遥感数据（如MODIS、ERA5再分析）获取，可进一步扩展遥感衍生变量（如NDVI、气溶胶光学厚度、地表温度）以增强模型解释力；(3) SHAP解释框架可推广至遥感驱动的臭氧估算模型，揭示遥感因子与臭氧的非线性响应机制；(4) 反演得到的O3空间分布可与其他遥感污染物产品（如NO2、HCHO）进行协同分析，完善区域臭氧前体物敏感性诊断。

Abstract (英文): Ozone (O3), as a key secondary pollutant, exhibits pronounced spatiotemporal heterogeneity, posing significant challenges to coordinated regional air pollution control. However, systematic understanding of high-resolution O3 spatial inversion and its driving mechanisms in arid urban agglomerations remains limited. In this study, the Tianshan North Slope Urban Agglomeration (TNSUA) was selected as the study area, and a multi-model comparative framework was established to comprehensively evaluate the O3 inversion performance of 16 machine learning and deep learning models, including Extreme Gradient Boosting (XGBoost), Random Forest (RF), Extremely Randomized Trees (ET), and Gradient Boosting Decision Tree (GBDT). Based on the optimal model performance, high-precision daily O3 spatial reconstruction for the year 2023 was achieved across the study region. The contributions of individual driving factors and their nonlinear response relationships were quantitatively interpreted using Shapley Additive Explanations (SHAP). Furthermore, a backward trajectory model combined with the Weighted Potential Source Contribution Function (WPSCF) and Weighted Concentration Weighted Trajectory (WCWT) methods was employed to identify potential source regions and transport pathways of O3. The results indicate that: (1) The XGBoost model exhibited the best performance (R2 = 0.93, RPD &gt; 3). The reconstructed results reveal that high O3 concentrations in 2023 were primarily distributed in southern Urumqi, southern Changji, and southern Tacheng, with southern Urumqi identified as the most prominent hotspot. (2) The spatial variability of O3 was predominantly driven by downward shortwave radiation (DSR) and air temperature (TEM), both of which showed significant nonlinear responses and threshold effects on O3 formation. (3) Source apportionment analysis indicates that westerly transport serves as a major exogenous contribution pathway, with potential source regions mainly located in the surrounding areas of the northern Tianshan slope as well as Central Asia, particularly eastern Kazakhstan and northern Kyrgyzstan. This study systematically elucidates the formation mechanisms of O3 pollution in arid urban agglomerations from three aspects—high-precision inversion, driving mechanism analysis, and cross-regional transport identification—thereby providing a scientific basis for precise air pollution control strategies.

### [249] [A Multi-Frequency SAR Framework for Methane Emission Estimation in Thai Rice Paddies](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132194)
*Nuntikorn Kitratporn,Kanjana Koedkurang,Panu Nueangjamnong,Kittiphop Simachokchai,Chompunut Chayawat,Shinichi Sobue,Thuy Le Toan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个自动化框架，融合多传感器SAR数据（Sentinel-1 C波段和ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 L波段）与IPCC方法，用于估算泰国中部平原灌溉稻田的甲烷（CH₄）排放。物候检测的种植和收获日期MAE分别为6.1±1.4天和8.3±1.7天，水情分类平衡精度为0.59–0.89，完整管线的MAE为18.5±4.5 kgCH₄/ha（占地面参考的21.4%），偏置为3.5±5.8 kgCH₄/ha。水情分类是算法不确定性的主要来源，而IPCC Tier 1排放因子结构范围（−32%到+48%）超过了所有算法误差的总和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水稻种植是农业部门甲烷（CH₄）排放的主要来源，其全球变暖潜能远高于二氧化碳。准确且可扩展的稻田CH₄排放量化对于碳核算至关重要。现有方法在空间显式、自动化、多频SAR融合与IPCC方法兼容方面存在不足。

Method: 框架整合了三个核心模块：(1) 利用Sentinel-1 C波段SAR时间序列进行水稻物候检测（种植和收获日期）；(2) 利用ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 L波段全极化SAR进行水情分类（连续淹水、单次排水、多次排水），采用基于水稻生长阶段的SVM-RBF分类器；(3) 结合IPCC水情缩放因子进行CH₄排放估算。端到端集成采用四轨反事实分解进行误差分析。

Result: 物候检测：种植日期MAE 6.1±1.4天，收获日期MAE 8.3±1.7天，检测率97.0%±2.7%。水情分类各阶段测试平衡精度0.59–0.89。完整管线MAE 18.5±4.5 kgCH₄/ha（地均参考的21.4%），均值偏置3.5±5.8 kgCH₄/ha。IPCC Tier 1排放因子结构范围（−32%至+48%）超过所有算法误差总和。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种空间显式的方法，将多频SAR数据整合到符合IPCC标准的甲烷估算中，支持监测、报告与核查（MRV）应用。水情分类被确认是算法不确定性的主要来源。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感应用于农业温室气体排放估算的典型工作，改进方向包括：(1) 引入更高时间分辨率的数据源（如Sentinel-2光学数据）辅助物候检测，以降低SAR在快速生长期的时间采样限制；(2) 尝试深度学习模型（如时序Transformer或LSTM）替代SVM-RBF进行水情分类，以提升0.59–0.89中低端精度；(3) 扩展到其他水稻产区（如中国、印度、越南），验证框架在不同气候和耕作制度下的泛化能力；(4) 引入数据同化或贝叶斯方法，将IPCC排放因子的结构不确定性纳入端到端概率估算中；(5) 利用多时相InSAR相干性信息辅助水情判别。

Abstract (英文): Rice cultivation is a major source of methane (CH4) emission in the agricultural sector, with a significantly higher global warming potential than carbon dioxide. Accurate and scalable quantification of CH4 from rice paddies is essential for carbon accounting. This study presents an automated framework for estimating rice CH4 emissions from irrigated paddies in the central plain of Thailand, integrating multi-sensor Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) observations with the IPCC methodology. The framework combines Sentinel-1 C-band SAR time series for phenological detection, ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 L-band full-polarimetric SAR for water regime classification, and IPCC water-scaling factors corresponding to Continuous Flooding, Single Drainage, or Multiple Drainage regimes. Evaluated across five stratified holdout sets, the phenology detection algorithm achieved planting and harvesting date Mean Absolute Errors of 6.1 ± 1.4 and 8.3 ± 1.7 days, with a 97.0% ± 2.7% operational detection rate. Water regime classification employed rice growth stage-specific Support Vector Machine classifiers with Radial Basis Function kernels (SVM-RBF), achieving per-stage test Balanced Accuracy ranging from 0.59 to 0.89. End-to-end integration using a four-track counterfactual decomposition yielded a full-pipeline mean absolute error of 18.5 ± 4.5 kgCH4ha−1 (21.4% of the mean ground-based CH4 calculation) and a mean bias of 3.5 ± 5.8 kgCH4ha−1. Water level classification was confirmed as the dominant algorithmic uncertainty source, while the IPCC Tier 1 emission factor structural range (−32% to +48% of the default) exceeded all algorithmic errors combined. The proposed framework provides a spatially explicit approach for integrating multi-frequency SAR data into IPCC-compliant methane estimation, supporting Monitoring, Reporting, and Verification applications.

### [250] [Inundation Monitoring in Rice Fields Using ALOS-2 PALSAR-2: A Case Study of An Giang, the Mekong Delta in Vietnam](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132190)
*Phung Hoang-Phi,Nguyen Lam-Dao,Nghi Dang-Pham-Bao,Thuy Le-Toan,Thi Truong-Nhat-Kieu,Shinichi Sobue*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 该研究通过融合多时相ALOS-2 PALSAR-2（L波段）和Sentinel-1（C波段）SAR数据，在越南安江省2025年冬春稻季实现了水稻冠层下淹水状况的可靠分类，总体精度81%，Kappa系数0.77，为温室气体清单和气候智慧型水管理（如干湿交替灌溉）提供了关键数据支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水稻田淹水状况的精确监测对优化水分利用效率和减少甲烷排放至关重要，但密集水稻冠层下水的探测仍是一个重大挑战，现有方法难以穿透冠层有效识别淹水状态。

Method: 采用多时相ALOS-2 PALSAR-2（L波段）和Sentinel-1（C波段）SAR数据融合，利用Sentinel-1时间序列估算水稻物候（稻龄），分析ALOS-2 PALSAR-2多极化后向散射系数以区分不同生长阶段的淹水与非淹水状态。

Result: L波段信号（特别是VV极化）能有效穿透密集植被，淹水/非淹水分类总体精度达81%，Kappa系数0.77，生成的多时相遇水图与实地调查观测结果一致。

Conclusion: L波段VV极化SAR数据在表征水稻冠层下淹水状况方面具有显著潜力，多频SAR融合为农业监测和气候智慧型管理提供了有效手段，可为温室气体清单和低排放水管理实践（如AWD）验证提供关键数据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方案：(1) 可引入更高分辨率的X波段SAR（如TerraSAR-X）与L/C波段形成三频融合，提升对幼龄期水稻的淹水检测精度；(2) 结合光学遥感数据（如Sentinel-2）的植被指数辅助冠层状态校正，减少SAR信号中冠层散射干扰；(3) 引入深度学习模型（如CNN或Transformer）对多时相、多极化、多频SAR特征进行端到端分类，替代传统阈值或机器学习方法；(4) 结合水稻生长模型（如ORYZA）进行物理约束，提升淹水时序反演的连续性；(5) 扩展至不同水稻种植制度（如双季稻、深水稻）和地形条件（如梯田）以验证方法的普适性。

Abstract (英文): Accurate monitoring of inundation in rice paddies is essential for optimizing water use efficiency and mitigating methane emissions; yet, detecting water beneath dense rice canopies remains a major challenge. This study proposed a reliable classification approach applied to the Winter–Spring 2025 season in An Giang province, Vietnam, by integrating multi-temporal ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 (L-band) and Sentinel-1 (C-band) SAR data with in situ field surveys. Time-series Sentinel-1 observations were used to estimate rice phenology (rice age), while multi-polarization backscatter from ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 was analyzed to discriminate inundated from non-inundated conditions across different growth stages. Results demonstrated that L-band signals, particularly in VV polarization, penetrated dense vegetation effectively, enabling classification of inundated vs. non-inundated fields with an overall accuracy of 81% and a Kappa coefficient of 0.77. The resulting multi-date inundation maps revealed distinct flooding regimes consistent with local field survey observations. These findings demonstrated the potential of L-band VV SAR data for characterizing sub-canopy inundation conditions under rice canopies. Crucially, the approach provides essential data for greenhouse gas inventories and supports the verification of low-emission water management practices, such as Alternate Wetting and Drying (AWD). Overall, the study demonstrated the value of multi-frequency SAR integration for advancing agricultural monitoring and climate-smart management in rice-growing regions.

### [251] [Village-Scale Winter Wheat Yield Prediction in Coastal Saline–Alkali Farmland Using a Three-Stage Fusion XGBoost Framework and SHAP](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132233)
*Wenxi Jia,Jingzhao Lu,杨其展,Yuhang Xie,Xing Cao,Yuqing Pan,Qi Xu,Yapeng Zhou,Jun Zhao,Li Wang,Xiaofei Liu,Fujun Zhao,Y ZHANG*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种物候引导的特征集成方法，结合Sentinel-2影像、气候因子和地形变量，用于预测滨海盐碱农田的村庄级冬小麦产量。三阶段融合XGBoost模型达到R²=0.6439，RMSE=446.24 kg/ha。SHAP分析表明盐度指数、距离因子、高程等是产量变化的主要驱动因素，内陆产量（5145 kg/ha）显著高于沿海（4198 kg/ha）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 滨海盐碱农田区域空间差异大、环境胁迫因素多样，准确估算村庄级冬小麦产量极具挑战性，现有方法难以有效应对该复杂环境下的产量预测问题。

Method: 基于物候引导的特征集构建（融合Sentinel-2影像、气候因子、地形变量如高程、地形湿度指数、距海岸线距离、距水系距离），采用XGBoost回归模型，并设计三阶段分支结构识别不同阶段的主要驱动因子（盐度指数SI、NDVI与产量），结合SHAP进行模型可解释性分析。

Result: 物候引导特征集成XGBoost的R²=0.6382，RMSE=450.15 kg/ha，优于梯度提升（0.6256）、随机森林（0.6098）、SVR（0.4792）等。三阶段融合XGBoost模型R²=0.6439，RMSE=446.24 kg/ha，MAE=363.38 kg/ha。内陆产量（5145 kg/ha）高于沿海（4198 kg/ha）。

Conclusion: 该框架能够有效支持滨海盐碱农田的村庄级冬小麦产量预测，并通过SHAP提升了模型可解释性，揭示了盐度、距离、高程等环境因子是产量空间差异的主要驱动因素。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：（1）引入更高时间分辨率（如Landsat+Sentinel-2融合）或雷达数据（Sentinel-1）以增强对盐碱胁迫的动态监测能力；（2）将物候引导特征集成方法推广至其他盐碱地作物（如水稻、玉米）或不同气候区的作物产量预测；（3）结合深度学习时序模型（如LSTM、Transformer）捕捉物候长期依赖关系，进一步提高预测精度；（4）考虑加入土壤理化参数（如含盐量、pH值、有机质）作为辅助特征，增强模型对盐碱胁迫机理的刻画能力。

Abstract (英文): Accurately estimating village-level winter wheat yield in coastal saline–alkali farmland is challenging because this region has strong spatial differences and multiple environmental stresses. In this study, Huanghua City, Hebei Province, was selected as a typical coastal saline–alkali area. Sentinel-2 images, climate factors, and topographic variables, including elevation, topographic wetness index, distance to the coastline, and distance to water systems, were combined to build a phenology-guided feature set for winter wheat yield prediction in coastal areas. The results showed that Phenology-Guided Feature Integration XGBoost achieved an R2 of 0.6382 and an RMSE of 450.15 kg/ha, which was slightly better than Gradient Boosting (R2 = 0.6256) and Random Forest (R2 = 0.6098), and clearly better than SVR (R2 = 0.4792), Ridge regression (R2 = 0.4582), and a single Decision Tree (R2 = 0.3088). Then, a three-stage branch was designed to identify the main drivers of SI, NDVI, and winter wheat yield at different stages, helping explain how environmental constraints and vegetation responses jointly affect final yield. The Three-Stage Fusion XGBoost Model achieved an R2 of 0.6439, an RMSE of 446.24 kg/ha, and an MAE of 363.38 kg/ha, showing a slight improvement in prediction accuracy. SHAP analysis showed that SI, distance-related factors, elevation, TWI, and NDVI were important drivers of winter wheat yield variation. Spatial prediction results showed higher winter wheat yield in inland areas (5145 kg/ha) and lower yield in coastal areas (4198 kg/ha). This framework supports village-scale winter wheat yield prediction in coastal saline–alkali farmland and improves model interpretability.

### [252] [Scale Effects on Dominant Drivers of Commercial Plantation Productivity: Novel Insights from High-Resolution Multi-Sensor UAV Remote Sensing and Interpretable AI](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132235)
*Zhansheng Mao,Bo Zheng,Y F LIU,D G Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 该研究通过整合10米高密度土壤采样、无人机激光雷达和多光谱遥感数据，利用可解释机器学习框架（XGBoost–SHAP）揭示了亚热带山地经济林（山核桃）叶片叶绿素指数（LCI）在3-50米尺度上的驱动因素变化规律：细尺度（3-10米）由树冠结构主导，中尺度（10-20米）出现树冠-土壤耦合窗口，>30米尺度转向地形和土壤质地主导，并据此提出了与生态尺度对齐的精准林业分级管理框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚热带山地经济人工林受资源可用性空间异质性的强烈制约，但土壤属性、地形和冠层结构调控植被活力的空间尺度尚不明确。

Method: 构建了空间一致的多尺度数据集（10米高密度土壤采样、UAV-LiDAR、多光谱遥感），采用可解释机器学习框架（XGBoost–SHAP）在3-50米范围内分解冠层、土壤和地形对LCI的尺度依赖性贡献。

Result: 细尺度（3-10米）植被活力由树木冠层结构（尤其是树高）主控；中尺度（10-20米）出现冠层结构-土壤养分交互耦合窗口，单因素效应减弱，且在20米处交互模式减弱并恢复为单指标主导；>30米尺度复杂交互重现，主导贡献从养分和冠层结构转向地形和土壤质地。

Conclusion: 土壤-冠层关系随空间尺度重组而非静态不变；基于此提出了精准林业的尺度层级框架，将管理干预措施与主导相关因子运行的生态尺度对齐。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）将XGBoost–SHAP的尺度分解框架直接应用于其他遥感植被指数（如NDVI、EVI、SIF）的尺度依赖性分析；（2）结合高光谱遥感数据，将叶绿素指标扩展为更全面的生化参数（如氮含量、类胡萝卜素），增强对养分-冠层交互机制的解析；（3）将该框架与卫星遥感（如Sentinel-2）结合，探索更大尺度（>100米）上的尺度转换规律；（4）引入时序遥感数据，研究不同物候期下尺度依赖性驱动因素的变化，为动态精准管理提供依据。

Abstract (英文): Subtropical mountain economic tree plantations are constrained by pronounced spatial heterogeneity in resource availability, yet the spatial scales at which soil properties, topography, and canopy structure regulate vegetation vigor remain poorly resolved. To address this gap, a spatially consistent multi-scale dataset combining 10 m high-density soil sampling, UAV-LiDAR, and multispectral remote sensing was used to quantify the scale-dependent drivers of the Leaf Chlorophyll Index (LCI) across 3–50 m within a Chinese hickory (Carya cathayensis Sarg.) plantation. The relative contributions of canopy, soil, and topography to LCI were decomposed across scales using an interpretable machine-learning framework (XGBoost–SHAP). At fine scales (3–10 m), vegetation vigor was primarily controlled by tree-level canopy structure, particularly tree height, reflecting localized resource acquisition. At intermediate scales (10–20 m), a distinct coupling window emerged, characterized by increased interaction complexity: LCI was predominantly driven by interactions between canopy structure and soil nutrient availability, whereas single-factor effects weakened. Notably, at 20 m this interaction pattern largely weakened and reverted to single-metric dominance. At broader scales (&gt;30 m), complex interactions re-emerged, and dominant SHAP contributions shifted from nutrients and canopy structure toward topography and soil texture. These findings reconcile strong fine-scale drivers with weaker predictability at intermediate extents and demonstrate that soil–canopy relationships reorganize across spatial scales rather than remaining static. On the basis of these findings, a scale-hierarchical framework for precision forestry is proposed that aligns management interventions with the ecological scales at which dominant correlates operate across spatial supports.

### [253] [Diffusion-Model-Based Data Augmentation for Target Detection in Side-Scan Sonar Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132193)
*Yuanxu Yang,Tao Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出基于FLUX扩散模型+LoRA微调的数据增强方法，用于侧扫声纳图像目标检测。通过生成高质量声纳图像并筛选后加入训练集，在YOLOv8n检测器上使mAP@0.5从0.740提升至0.858，mAP@0.5:0.95从0.399提升至0.511，优于传统增强方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 侧扫声纳图像目标检测面临数据集规模小、采集成本高、类别不平衡等问题，现有深度学习检测器性能受限，亟需有效的数据增强方法。

Method: 采用FLUX.1扩散模型作为基础生成框架，通过低秩适配（LoRA）微调使其适应侧扫声纳图像域；对生成样本进行筛选过滤，仅加入训练集（验证/测试集保持真实图像不变）；使用固定YOLOv8n检测器在相同超参数和随机种子下进行评估。

Result: FLUX+LoRA增强使mAP@0.5从0.7400±0.0132提升至0.8582±0.0328，mAP@0.5:0.95从0.3994±0.0187提升至0.5115±0.0164；600样本手动标注子集在图像质量和检测性能上优于FLUX-base和SD1.5+LoRA。

Conclusion: FLUX+LoRA生成的声纳图像能够为检测器训练提供有用的结构多样性，在数据有限条件下有效提升目标检测性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。具体方案：(1) 将该方法直接迁移至遥感图像目标检测（如SAR舰船检测、光学遥感小目标检测），解决遥感领域同样存在的标注数据稀缺和类别不平衡问题；(2) 改进方向：引入遥感图像特有的几何变换（如旋转不变性）作为扩散模型的条件约束，提升生成样本的几何多样性；(3) 结合遥感多模态数据（光学+SAR+高光谱）训练条件扩散模型，实现跨模态数据增强；(4) 将LoRA微调替换为更适合遥感大场景的DreamBooth或自定义适配器，进一步提升生成图像的场景一致性。

Abstract (英文): Side-scan sonar images play an important role in underwater target detection, seabed mapping, and marine environment monitoring. However, the performance of deep learning-based detectors is often limited by the small scale of available sonar datasets, the high cost of data acquisition, and class imbalance among target categories. To address these issues, this paper proposes a diffusion-model-based data augmentation method for side-scan sonar target detection. A FLUX.1 diffusion model is adopted as the base generative framework and is fine-tuned using low-rank adaptation (LoRA) to adapt the pretrained model to the side-scan sonar image domain under limited training data conditions. The generated samples are further filtered and added only to the training set, while the validation and test sets are kept unchanged and contain only real sonar images. To ensure a fair evaluation of the augmentation strategy, all detection experiments are conducted using a fixed YOLOv8n (You Only Look Once version 8 nano) detector under the same training hyperparameters and three random seeds. Compared with training on the original dataset, the proposed FLUX+LoRA augmentation improves mean average precision (mAP)@0.5 from 0.7400 ± 0.0132 to 0.8582 ± 0.0328 and mAP@0.5:0.95 from 0.3994 ± 0.0187 to 0.5115 ± 0.0164. It also outperforms conventional augmentation methods under the same real-only validation/test protocol. In addition, Fréchet Inception Distance (FID)/Kernel Inception Distance (KID)-based image quality evaluation, generated-sample amount ablation, screening-strategy ablation, LoRA-rank sensitivity analysis, and a controlled 600-sample diffusion-backbone comparison are conducted. The results show that the 600-sample manually annotated FLUX+LoRA subset selected from generated samples achieves better image quality and detection performance than FLUX-base and SD1.5+LoRA under the same annotation budget. These findings demonstrate that FLUX+LoRA-generated sonar images can provide useful structural diversity for detector training and improve target detection performance under limited-data conditions.

</details>


### [254] [Land-Cover-Stratified Validation and Uncertainty Prioritization for SSP-Based NDVI Projection at 1 km Resolution in Northeast China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132203)
*Eslam Rashad,Yujie Liu,J S Liu,Tao Pan,Ahmed Refaee*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究在1公里分辨率下对东北地区2040年NDVI进行多情景预测，发现LightGBM模型表现最优，但土地覆盖分层验证揭示了严重的类别级别预测弱点——未利用地R²低至-0.886，水体为负值。通过不确定性风险指数识别出建设用地、未利用地和水体为优先验证类别，表明聚合精度指标会掩盖类别特定投影局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NDVI预测文献缺乏对景观异质性区域中类别级别预测局限性的系统性关注，聚合空间连贯性可能掩盖显著的类别级预测弱点。

Method: 采用四组分评估工作流：多阶段模型选择（空间块交叉验证、时间保留验证、长跳外推、气候扰动测试）、土地覆盖分层验证、分位数回归不确定性特征化、验证优先级排序。比较三种基于树的模型后选择LightGBM，并在SSP1-2.6/SSP2-4.5/SSP5-8.5情景下预测2040年NDVI。

Result: LightGBM空间CV R²=0.654±0.123，时间保留R²=0.710，长跳R²=0.671。区域平均NDVI从2020年0.393增至2040年0.414-0.417。类别R²范围从建设用地的0.576到未利用地的-0.886。水体随机误差大且系统偏差高，未利用地以系统偏差为主。URI在建设用地最高、耕地最低。

Conclusion: 土地覆盖分层的误差分解和不确定性优先级排序能揭示聚合精度指标所掩盖的类别特定投影局限，不同类别需要针对性的模型改进策略。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究本身即为遥感NDVI预测论文。改进方案：(1) 引入多源遥感数据（Sentinel-1 SAR、夜间灯光、DEM）增强未利用地和建设用地的特征表征；(2) 采用类别加权损失函数或过采样方法缓解类别不平衡问题；(3) 引入时空融合模型（如ESTARFM）提升1公里分辨率下混合像元分解精度；(4) 结合深度学习方法（如CNN-LSTM）捕捉类别内部的时空依赖模式；(5) 对水体类别引入水文遥感辅助变量（如MODIS水掩膜、湖泊水位数据）以减少系统偏差。

Abstract (英文): At 1 km resolution, NDVI projections for heterogeneous landscapes can appear spatially coherent in aggregate while concealing substantial class-level prediction weaknesses, a limitation that has received limited systematic attention in the NDVI projection literature. This study applies a four-component assessment workflow to Northeast China (NEC) for 2040 under SSP1-2.6, SSP2-4.5, and SSP5-8.5, integrating multi-stage model selection, land-cover-stratified validation, quantile-regression-based uncertainty characterization, and validation-priority ranking. Among three candidate tree-based models evaluated using spatial block cross-validation, temporal holdout validation, long-jump extrapolation, and climatic perturbation tests, LightGBM showed the most balanced and consistent performance, with spatial CV R2 = 0.654 ± 0.123, temporal holdout R2 = 0.710, and long-jump R2 = 0.671, and was therefore selected for the 2040 projection. Projected regional mean NDVI increased modestly from 0.393 in 2020 to 0.414–0.417 across scenarios, with limited divergence among SSP pathways at this near-term horizon. Class-stratified validation of the 2020 holdout prediction revealed that global model performance masked strong class-level heterogeneity, with R2 values ranging from 0.576 for Construction land to −0.886 for Unused land. Water bodies and Unused land exhibited negative R2 values, indicating weak class-level predictive support relative to a simple class-mean benchmark. Residual decomposition showed that Water bodies combined high random error with elevated systematic deviation, whereas Unused land was mainly characterized by systematic bias, suggesting different needs for class-specific model improvement. The Uncertainty Risk Index (URI), derived from 95% prediction intervals, was highest in Construction land and lowest in Cropland across all scenarios. Integrating historical residuals with future URI-identified Water bodies, Unused land, and Construction land as the highest-priority classes for future targeted validation. These priorities arise from both limited class representation and intrinsic NDVI-related complexity, including low vegetation signal, mixed-pixel effects, and heterogeneous land-surface composition. These results demonstrate that land-cover-stratified error decomposition and uncertainty-informed priority ranking reveal class-specific projection limitations that aggregate accuracy metrics can conceal.

### [255] [Future Climate-Driven Changes in Carbon Stocks in the Yellow River Basin of China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132205)
*Xia Fang,Liangzhong Cao,Ziwei Pei,Shihua Zhu,Yuhong He*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用干旱生态系统模型（AEM）模拟了1981–2060年黄河流域四种主要碳库（总碳、植被碳、土壤有机碳、凋落物碳）的时空演变，发现总碳储量呈增加趋势，CO2施肥效应主导了碳汇增长，而凋落物碳对气候变率最为敏感，并指出上黄河流域为强碳汇区，黄土高原等地区对变暖和水资源减少较为脆弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 干旱和半干旱生态系统的碳动态是全球碳循环评估中的主要不确定性来源，尤其是黄河流域这类区域。本文旨在通过模型模拟量化黄河流域碳储量的时空演变，并评估不同气候情景下各碳库的响应，以支撑区域碳中和目标。

Method: 采用干旱生态系统模型（Arid Ecosystem Model, AEM），模拟1981–2020年历史时期和2021–2060年未来时期（SSP5高排放情景及CO2-only、变暖-only、降水-only等因子情景）的总碳（TOTC）、植被碳（VEGC）、土壤有机碳（SOC）和凋落物碳（LTRC）的时空变化。

Result: 1981–2020年，总碳增加0.09 Pg C（+3.54%），其中植被碳增加0.03 Pg C（+21.43%），土壤有机碳增加0.06 Pg C（+2.78%），凋落物碳净变化较小但年际变异性高。2021–2060年SSP5情景下总碳预计增加0.114 Pg C（+4.81%），植被碳贡献最大（+23.87%）。CO2施肥效应主导，变暖和降水单独作用效果较弱且变异大。凋落物碳在不同情景下变幅为−18%至+22%，变异性最高。

Conclusion: 黄河流域碳汇主要受CO2施肥效应驱动，但区域异质性强，上黄河流域为强汇区，黄土高原和中部西部区域对气候变暖和水资源减少脆弱。需关注非线性气候-碳相互作用，并制定结合生态恢复与气候适应的区域特异性策略以增强碳汇，支持碳中和目标。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1）遥感数据可为AEM模型提供高时空分辨率的植被指数（如NDVI/EVI）、叶面积指数（LAI）和地表温度等关键输入参数，提升模型初始化精度；2）利用GEDI、ICESat-2等激光雷达数据估算植被碳密度，结合Sentinel-1/2时序影像验证和校正模型输出的VEGC空间分布；3）采用SMAP或AMSR-E土壤水分遥感产品约束SOC模拟中的土壤水分动态，减少模型不确定性；4）遥感反演的净初级生产力（NPP）产品可作为模型验证的基准，评估AEM模拟的碳通量可靠性；5）针对凋落物碳的高变异性，可结合高分遥感与无人机多光谱数据建立凋落物覆盖度与碳含量的经验关系，实现凋落物碳时空动态的遥感监测与模型校准。

Abstract (英文): Carbon storage dynamics in dryland and semi-arid ecosystems remain a major uncertainty in global carbon cycle assessments, particularly in regions like the Yellow River Basin (YRB). Using the Arid Ecosystem Model (AEM), we simulated the spatiotemporal evolution of four major carbon pools—total carbon (TOTC), vegetation carbon (VEGC), soil organic carbon (SOC), and litter carbon (LTRC)—from 1981 to 2060 under factorial climate scenarios. During 1981–2020, TOTC increased by 0.09 Pg C (+3.54%), driven by gains in VEGC (+0.03 Pg C, +21.43%) and SOC (+0.06 Pg C, +2.78%). LTRC showed minimal net change but was highly sensitive to interannual variability. From 2021 to 2060, under the high-emission SSP5 scenario, TOTC is projected to increase by 0.114 Pg C (+4.81%), with VEGC contributing most of the gain (+23.87%). CO2_only simulations showed similar increases, underscoring the dominant role of CO2 fertilization. In contrast, warming and precipitation alone produced weaker and more variable effects. Spatially, upper YRB regions are expected to maintain strong sink capacity, while the Loess Plateau and central-western subregions remain vulnerable to warming and moisture decline. LTRC exhibited the highest variability across scenarios (−18% to +22%), highlighting its role as a sensitive indicator of sink stability. These findings emphasize the need to account for nonlinear climate–carbon interactions and regional heterogeneity. Region-specific, adaptive strategies that integrate ecological restoration and climate adaptation will be critical to enhancing carbon sinks and supporting China’s carbon neutrality targets in the Yellow River Basin.

### [256] [Less Is More: Online Spatio-Temporal Selective Learning for Multi-Variable Meteorological Forecasting](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132202)
*Pu Zhang,Deping Xiang,Chunlei Huo,Kun Ding,Shiming Xiang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种选择性监督训练框架ST-SL和变感知的时空Transformer（VASTFormer），用于高维气象场精准预测。ST-SL通过比较主模型与冻结参考模型来评估每个预测单元的可学习性，仅对高收益时空单元计算损失。VASTFormer利用交叉变量依赖、物理增强太阳位置编码和高效时间转换器建模大气轨迹。在ERA5数据集上，VASTFormer+ST-SL相比最强基线将MSE降低8.84%，MAE降低6.70%，RMSE降低4.54%，平均ACC达0.9801，RMSESS达0.8104。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维气象场的精确预测具有挑战性，因为大气系统的复杂时空动态以及不同空间位置和预测时长下训练难度的异质性。现有深度学习方法通常对所有预测单元进行统一优化，这可能会过度强调低收益或弱泛化能力的监督信号，导致模型泛化能力受限。

Method: 提出ST-SL（时空选择性学习）在线训练框架，通过主模型与冻结参考模型的预测差异评估每个时空单元的可学习性，仅对高收益单元计算损失。同时提出VASTFormer，包含：(1) 变感知交叉变量依赖建模；(2) 物理增强的太阳位置编码；(3) 高效时间转换器捕捉大气轨迹。两者结合实现选择性监督训练。

Result: 在ERA5再分析数据集上，VASTFormer超越代表性时空基线模型；ST-SL在不增加推理参数和计算成本的前提下进一步提升精度。与最强基线相比，VASTFormer+ST-SL将MSE降低8.84%，MAE降低6.70%，RMSE降低4.54%。气象技能评估显示平均ACC为0.9801，RMSESS为0.8104。百分位数极端条件评估证实了在标准和极端场景下的一致性改进。

Conclusion: 选择性监督方法能够改善密集气象预测的泛化能力。ST-SL框架通过动态选择高收益训练单元有效避免了低收益监督信号的干扰，结合VASTFormer的变感知和物理增强建模，在高维气象场预测任务中取得了显著优于现有方法的效果。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该文提出的ST-SL选择性监督训练框架可直接应用于遥感领域的密集预测任务，如地表温度反演、植被指数时空插值、土壤湿度场预测等。具体方案：(1) 将ST-SL用于遥感影像时间序列预测，针对不同空间位置（如云覆盖区vs.晴空区）动态选择高收益训练单元；(2) VASTFormer的变感知机制可迁移至遥感多波段数据（如Sentinel-2的13个波段）的交叉依赖性建模；(3) 物理增强编码思路可推广至遥感中的太阳天顶角、卫星观测几何等先验知识的嵌入；(4) 可将VASTFormer的时空编码用于遥感影像超分辨率重建中的时空一致性保持。

Abstract (英文): Accurate forecasting of high-dimensional meteorological fields remains challenging due to the complex spatio-temporal dynamics of atmospheric systems and the presence of heterogeneous training difficulty across space and lead time. Existing deep forecasting approaches usually optimize all prediction units uniformly, which may overemphasize low-benefit or weakly generalizable supervision signals. To address this issue, we propose Spatio-Temporal Selective Learning (ST-SL), an online training framework that estimates the learnability of each prediction unit by comparing the main model with a frozen reference model and computes the loss only over selected high-benefit spatio-temporal units. To provide an effective forecasting backbone, we further introduce VASTFormer, a variable-aware spatio-temporal Transformer that models cross-variable dependencies, incorporates physics-enhanced Solar Positional Encoding, and captures atmospheric trajectories with an efficient temporal translator. Experiments on the ERA5 reanalysis dataset show that VASTFormer outperforms representative spatio-temporal baselines, while ST-SL further improves accuracy without adding inference-time parameters or computational cost. Compared with the strongest baseline, VASTFormer+ST-SL reduces MSE, MAE, and RMSE by 8.84%, 6.70%, and 4.54%, respectively. Meteorological skill evaluation further shows an average ACC of 0.9801 and RMSESS of 0.8104, and percentile-based extreme-condition evaluations confirm consistent improvements across standard and high-impact forecasting scenarios. These results indicate that selective supervision can improve generalization in dense meteorological forecasting.

</details>

### [258] [Experiences of the Scan of Existing Bridge Structures with Multiple Real-World Case Studies in Germany](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132185)
*Monika Lederer,Christoph Stahl,Jan‐Iwo Jäkel,Peter Gölzhäuser,Annette Schmitt,Katharina Klemt-Albert,Alexander Reiterer*

Motivation: 桥梁扫描和文档记录对创建可靠的数字3D模型至关重要，但现有扫描工作流程往往依赖从业者的隐式经验，缺乏标准化协议。本文旨在通过多案例研究，系统化地揭示不同扫描技术的性能权衡，并提供可操作的实践指导。

Method: 采用多案例研究方法（MCS），对德国十座异构真实桥梁进行实验，评估三种技术：地面激光扫描（TLS）、移动激光扫描（MLS）和无人机（UAS）摄影测量。基于实验发现，定义了一个符合BPMN标准的通用流程模型，覆盖法律与空间约束下的完整数据采集生命周期。

Result: TLS精度高但存在阴影遮挡问题；UAS操作灵活但存在几何缺陷，包括精细结构上的摄影测量重建噪声和振动跨度上的SLAM轨迹漂移；MLS介于两者之间。三种技术存在明显的性能权衡。

Conclusion: 研究提供了可操作的实践指南，帮助优化结构工程工作流程中的数据质量和效率，并通过BPMN流程模型填补了扫描协议标准化的空白。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感技术在土木工程中的应用研究。改进方向：（1）可将TLS、MLS和UAS数据与多光谱/高光谱遥感数据融合，实现桥梁结构健康监测（如裂缝检测、材料退化评估）；（2）引入InSAR或GB-SAR技术补充形变监测能力；（3）利用深度学习算法自动检测和分类UAS摄影测量中的重建噪声与SLAM漂移区域；（4）将BPMN流程模型扩展至遥感大数据管理框架（如与Earth Observation数据管道集成）；（5）结合LiDAR点云与光学遥感影像进行多模态语义分割，提升桥梁构件识别精度。

Abstract (英文): Efficient bridge scanning and documentation are crucial for creating reliable digital 3D models. However, scanning workflows often rely on implicit practitioner experience rather than standardized protocols. This paper presents practical insights derived from a Multiple Case Study (MCS) of ten heterogeneous, real-world bridges in Germany. The study evaluates Terrestrial Laser Scanning (TLS), Mobile Laser Scanning (MLS) and Unmanned Aerial Systems (UAS) photogrammetry. The findings isolate distinct performance trade-offs. TLS offers high accuracy but suffers from shadowing occlusions. Conversely, UAS provides operational flexibility but introduces geometric vulnerabilities, including photogrammetric reconstruction noise on fine structures and SLAM trajectory drift on vibrating spans. To unify these insights, a generalized, BPMN-compliant process model mapping the complete data acquisition lifecycle under legal and spatial constraints is defined. This research provides an actionable, practical guide to optimize data quality and efficiency in structural engineering workflows.

### [259] [A Comparative Evaluation of UAV-Based Remote Sensing and Geophysical Techniques for Landmine Detection on a Seeded Minefield](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132182)
*Jasper Baur,Sagar Lekhak,Gabriel Steinberg,Alex Nikulin,Timothy de Smet,Anthony Brinkley,Emmett J. Ientilucci,F. O. Nitsche,Heidi Myers,Jacob Elliott,T. Bauch,Nina Raqueno,John Frucci*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文通过34个多模态数据集，在标准化测试场对9种传感模态（RGB、热红外、多光谱、高光谱、LiDAR、SAR等）进行地雷和未爆弹检测评估。RGB对地表目标检测率最高（94.8%），手持EMI和磁力计对地下铁质目标>95%但塑料目标<10%，车载探地雷达是唯一能检测埋地塑料目标（55.6%）的模态。所有数据公开，并附带交互式网络地图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前基于无人机的地雷探测缺乏标准化基准数据集和统一的性能评估框架，不同传感模态在真实作战环境下的检测能力难以直接比较。

Method: 在标准化种子测试场采集34个多模态数据集，涵盖9种传感模态；引入AIU指数（异常、可识别异常、唯一可识别异常）建立统一的检测保真度量化框架；进行检测率、误报率对比分析和成本效益分析。

Conclusion: 没有单一模态能胜任所有场景，需根据不同污染场景（地表/地下、铁质/塑料）选择最成本有效的检测方法；车载GPR是目前检测埋地塑料目标的唯一可行方案，无人机GPR仍需技术突破。

Abstract (英文): Reliable and scalable landmine detection technologies are essential for humanitarian mine action (HMA), yet standardized benchmarks for Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV)-based sensing in operationally relevant environments remain limited. This study presents a comprehensive evaluation of 34 multimodal datasets acquired over a standardized seeded test site for landmine and unexploded ordnance detection. Nine sensing modalities, including RGB, thermal, multispectral, hyperspectral, LiDAR, and Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR), are evaluated using the Anomaly, Identifiable Anomaly, Unique Identifiable Anomaly (AIU) index to establish a unified framework for quantifying detection fidelity. Results indicate that RGB imagery achieves the highest surface detection rate (94.8%), with 45.4% of targets classified as uniquely identifiable, reducing false-positive risk. For sub-surface detection, handheld electromagnetic induction (EMI) and magnetometry exceed 95% detection for ferrous items but fall below 10% for plastic ordnance. Ground-penetrating radar (GPR) is the only modality capable of detecting buried plastic targets (55.6% for cart-based systems), whereas UAV-mounted GPR remains limited (18.2%) at current operational flight heights. Based on the comparative analysis, we discuss the gaps in current detection capabilities, compare false-positive rates across modalities, and perform a cost–benefit analysis fitting contamination scenarios with the most cost-effective detection method. All datasets are publicly released, along with an interactive web-map, to support reproducible benchmarking and cross-modality comparison in UAV-enabled explosive hazard detection.

### [260] [A Two-Stage Reference-Guided Workflow for Improving VIIRS Leaf Area Index Retrieval over Mixed Pixels](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132214)
*Tengqi Yue,Haiyong Ding,Yuanfei Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种参考引导的两阶段工作流，通过修正聚合标签中的结构偏差并结合亚像素组成信息，显著提升了VIIRS LAI产品在异质性景观下的反演精度（R²从0.752提升至0.908）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异质性景观下，中等分辨率LAI反演不仅受粗分辨率预测器中未解决的亚像素组成影响，还受由高分辨率产品聚合而来的监督标签中的结构偏差影响。现有VIIRS LAI产品在混合像元上精度不足，需要一种能同时校正标签偏差并利用亚像素信息的方法。

Method: 两阶段工作流：第一阶段，利用亚像素PFT分数和森林敏感铰接项，将聚合的Sentinel-2 LAI校准为GBOV参考LAI，生成校正后的500 m标签；第二阶段，使用随机森林模型，输入VIIRS光谱反射率、观测几何、植被指数、纹理和亚像素组成变量进行训练。

Result: 标签校准使R²从0.752提升至0.908，RMSE从1.110降至0.676；LOSO验证下R²=0.901，RMSE=0.703；在与官方VNP产品的对比中，最终模型R²=0.905、RMSE=0.609，显著优于VNP（R²=0.755，RMSE=0.978）。

Conclusion: 参考引导的标签校正结合显式亚像素组成信息，能显著改进VIIRS LAI产品在混合像元上的反演精度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。本文方法可推广至其他中分辨率传感器（如MODIS、FY-3 MERSI）的LAI产品改进，核心思路是将高分辨率参考数据通过亚像素组成信息进行标签校准后训练模型。改进方向：（1）引入更精细的PFT分类或动态PFT时间序列；（2）结合深度学习模型替代随机森林以捕捉更复杂的非线性关系；（3）扩展到全球多站点验证以增强泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Moderate-resolution leaf area index (LAI) retrieval over heterogeneous landscapes is affected not only by unresolved subpixel composition in coarse-resolution predictors, but also by structural bias in supervisory labels aggregated from higher-resolution products. To address this issue, we developed a reference-guided two-stage workflow to improve LAI retrieval from the Visible Infrared Imaging Radiometer Suite (VIIRS). In the first stage, aggregated Sentinel-2 LAI was calibrated against Ground-Based Observations for Validation (GBOV) LP3 reference LAI using subpixel plant functional type (PFT) fractions and forest-sensitive hinge terms to generate corrected 500 m labels. In the second stage, a random-forest model was trained using VIIRS spectral reflectance, viewing geometry, vegetation indices, texture, and subpixel compositional variables. Model development was based on 2020–2021 data from 11 U.S. GBOV sites. Performance was evaluated by same-site temporal transfer to 2019 and 2022 and by strict leave-one-site-out (LOSO) validation. Label calibration improved agreement with GBOV from a coefficient of determination (R2) of 0.752 and a root mean square error (RMSE) of 1.110 to an R2 of 0.908 and an RMSE of 0.676. Under LOSO validation, the final model achieved an R2 of 0.901 with an RMSE of 0.703. On the 2019/2022 overlap subset shared by the final VIIRS retrieval, the official VNP product, and the GBOV reference, the final model achieved an R2 of 0.905 and an RMSE of 0.609, compared with 0.755 and 0.978 for the official VNP product. These results show that reference-guided label correction, combined with explicit subpixel compositional information, can substantially improve VIIRS LAI retrieval over mixed pixels within the evaluated study domain.

### [261] [DST-SARNet: A Dual-Stage Texture-Aware SAR Prior Network for Cloud Removal in Optical Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132199)
*Z Wang,Mingzhi Zhang,Yue Wang,Xudong Qiu,Jingqi Yan,Na Niu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出DST-SARNet，一种双阶段SAR结构引导网络，用于光学遥感图像去云。该网络通过早期结构骨架引导和晚期高频调制两个显式SAR引导位置，结合纹理感知非对称检索模块，在保持模型紧凑的同时有效恢复云污染图像。在SMILE-CR和SEN12MS-CR数据集上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 云污染会遮挡地物、干扰地表反射率并破坏空间连续性。现有CNN方法难以建模大范围云覆盖区域的全局结构和颜色一致性；Transformer方法标准自注意力计算成本高，高效注意力会削弱边缘和纹理区分性；SAR注入方法会传播斑点噪声、跨模态未对齐和成像差异。因此需要一种更有效的SAR辅助光学去云方法。

Method: 提出DST-SARNet双阶段框架：1）早期阶段在输入侧进行结构骨架引导；2）晚期阶段在输出附近进行高频调制；3）两阶段之间设置纹理感知非对称检索模块作为瓶颈记忆检索操作，而非密集的SAR注入。SAR提供结构骨架、可读纹理记忆和终端细节补偿，光学分支负责颜色、语义和光谱外观恢复。

Result: 在SMILE-CR和SEN12MS-CR数据集上的实验表明，DST-SARNet能够有效恢复云污染图像，且模型规模紧凑。

Conclusion: DST-SARNet通过双阶段SAR结构引导设计，实现了高效紧凑的SAR辅助光学遥感图像去云，为未来相关研究提供了可行方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。该论文本身就是遥感去云任务。改进方向：1）可引入多尺度特征融合以增强不同大小云区的恢复效果；2）可探索更轻量的注意力机制进一步压缩模型；3）可结合时间序列遥感数据（如连续多时相影像）提供额外先验信息；4）可考虑自监督或半监督训练策略减少对配对数据的需求；5）可扩展至多模态遥感图像融合（如光学-SAR-红外）场景。

Abstract (英文): Cloud contamination obscures ground objects, interferes with surface reflectance, and disrupts spatial continuity. In thick-cloud regions, surface structures and spectral information are often extensively missing. CNN-based cloud removal methods can recover local textures, but they are less effective at modeling global structures and color consistency over large cloud-covered areas. Transformer-based methods capture long-range dependencies; however, standard self-attention introduces high computational and memory costs for high-resolution remote sensing images. Efficient attention reduces this cost but may weaken edge and texture discriminability. SAR imagery can penetrate clouds and provide surface structural information, yet repeated SAR injections may propagate speckle noise, cross-modal misalignment, and imaging discrepancies through deep restoration layers. To address these issues, this paper proposes DST-SARNet, a dual-stage SAR structural guidance network for optical remote sensing image cloud removal. In this framework, dual-stage refers to two explicit SAR-guidance positions: early structural skeleton guidance at the input side and late high-frequency modulation near the output. The Texture-Aware Asymmetric Retrieval module is placed between these two stages as a bottleneck memory retrieval operation rather than as a third dense SAR injection stage. With this design, SAR provides structural skeletons, readable texture memory, and terminal detail compensation, while the optical branch remains responsible for color, semantics, and spectral appearance recovery. Experiments on the SMILE-CR and SEN12MS-CR datasets show that DST-SARNet effectively restores cloud-contaminated imagery with a compact model scale, demonstrating its potential for efficient SAR-assisted optical cloud removal.

### [262] [Physics-Guided Physical-Coordinate Center Detection for Measured Radar Point Targets Under Ground Clutter](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132204)
*Z H Zhang,Xiaoxiong Li,Jiachen Yang,Weiwei Li,Xi Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种波形与物理联合引导的中心检测器（WPG-Center），用于雷达实测地图中的点目标检测。该方法将检测任务重新定义为连续物理坐标中心定位，构建四通道杂波感知距离-多普勒（RD）表征，使用各向异性主干网络进行距离-杂波响应调制，并采用波形分辨率感知的高斯目标对中心热图进行监督。此外，还设计了条件式物理先验解码作为针对低带宽、近零多普勒情况的目标候选重排序步骤。在实测LSS-Ku-1.0数据集上通过严格的5折LFM协议验证，WPG-Center在检测概率（Pd=0.850±0.101）和距离精度（RMSE=18.16±12.19 m）上均优于所比较的学习型和CFAR类基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实测雷达点目标检测面临两大挑战：弱目标回波常被地杂波峰掩盖，且图像空间检测无法直接反映物理距离-多普勒坐标。现有方法在这两方面均存在不足，亟需一种能够同时处理杂波干扰并直接输出物理坐标的检测方法。

Method: (1) 将检测重新表述为连续物理坐标中心定位；(2) 构建四通道杂波感知距离-多普勒（RD）表征；(3) 采用各向异性主干网络进行距离-杂波响应调制；(4) 使用波形分辨率感知的高斯目标监督中心热图；(5) 设计条件物理先验解码作为低带宽、近零多普勒场景的候选重排序步骤。

Result: 在实测LSS-Ku-1.0数据集上，采用严格分块的5折LFM协议，WPG-Center达到Pd=0.850±0.101，距离RMSE=18.16±12.19 m，在解码中心检测概率和距离精度上均优于所有对比的CFAR类和基于学习的基线方法（包括Radar-FPN热图检测器）。固定sigma消融实验性能明显下降，证实了分辨率感知监督的必要性。

Conclusion: WPG-Center通过波形与物理先验的联合引导，有效提升了实测雷达地图中点目标的检测性能与物理坐标定位精度。分辨率感知的高斯监督是关键设计，条件物理先验解码进一步优化了低带宽场景下的检测结果。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该工作本身即为雷达遥感目标检测领域的前沿研究。改进方向：(1) 将波形-物理联合引导策略引入SAR图像目标检测，用于抑制相干斑噪声；(2) 各向异性主干网络可适配遥感图像中长宽比差异显著的目标（如舰船、桥梁）；(3) 条件物理先验解码可迁移至多模态遥感检测任务，如雷达-光学联合检测中的对齐与重排序。

Abstract (英文): Measured radar point-target detection under ground clutter is difficult because weak target echoes often compete with clutter peaks, and image-space detections do not directly represent physical range-Doppler coordinates. This paper proposes a waveform- and physics-guided center detector (WPG-Center) for measured radar maps. The method reformulates detection as continuous physical-coordinate center localization, constructs a four-channel clutter-aware range-Doppler (RD) representation, uses an anisotropic backbone with range-clutter response modulation, and supervises the center heatmap with waveform-resolution-aware Gaussian targets. Conditional physical-prior decoding is used as a targeted candidate reranking step for low-bandwidth, near-zero-Doppler cases. Experiments are conducted on the measured LSS-Ku-1.0 dataset using a strict blocked 5-fold linear frequency-modulated (LFM) protocol with physical localization tolerances and decoded-center detection metrics. WPG-Center achieves a probability of detection (Pd) of 0.850±0.101 and a range root-mean-square error (RMSE) of 18.16±12.19 m, giving the best average decoded-center detection probability and range accuracy among the compared learned and constant false-alarm rate (CFAR)-style baselines, including an independent radar feature pyramid network (Radar-FPN) heatmap detector. The fixed-sigma ablation is substantially weaker, supporting the need for resolution-aware supervision. Fold-wise, qualitative, and stepped-frequency waveform (SFW) analyses are reported as auxiliary evidence to define the scope of the measured LFM conclusion.

</details>


### [263] [Replacing Yield Detrending with Direct Spatiotemporal Inputs Improves LSTM-Based Rice Yield Estimation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132200)
*Nuo Chen,Fumin Wang,Xi Zhang,Zhen Zhao,Wenkai Wan,Junwei Liu,Zhou Shi,Songchao Chen*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究对比了统计去趋势方法与直接将时空变量输入深度学习模型对水稻产量估算的影响，发现直接输入年份变量显著优于传统去趋势方法，且结合时空信息的模型表现最佳（LSTM R²=0.61），该方法更简单、稳健，适用于大规模作物产量估算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有水稻产量估算方法主要采用统计去趋势（如移动平均、线性回归）来分离时间趋势，但这些方法依赖于对时间-产量关系的事前假设，当假设不成立时会产生系统性偏差；同时，时间和空间信息的各自贡献及其交互效应尚未在统一框架下被系统评估。

Method: 选取美国六个州112个水稻种植县（2000–2021年），使用植被指数（NDVI）、气象指标（生长度日、致死度日、累积降水量）及时空变量（年份、经度、纬度），设计六种输入配置，在LSTM、随机森林、XGBoost和Transformer四种模型架构上进行对比实验。

Result: (1) 直接输入年份在所有模型中均显著优于去趋势方法，时空联合配置表现最佳（LSTM R²=0.61 vs 去趋势0.54）；(2) SHAP分析中年份是最重要预测因子，时空变量排名高于多数气象和遥感变量；(3) 空间信息持续提升精度并减轻极端产量区域的系统性偏差；(4) 联合配置在不同州、年份（含极端气候事件）和产量水平下均表现最佳，在灌浆期（收获前1.5–2个月）即可达到近收获期精度。

Conclusion: 将原始时空数据直接输入深度学习模型比统计去趋势方法更有效，为大规模作物产量估算提供了一种更简单、更稳健的方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。(1) 可将该方法直接应用于遥感水稻产量估算，替代传统去趋势预处理步骤；(2) 引入更多遥感植被指数（如EVI、LSWI）及物候特征（如植被指数时间序列曲线参数）作为输入；(3) 空间变量可扩展至更高分辨率的地理坐标或区域聚类标签；(4) 可结合遥感反演的土壤水分、地表温度等产品进一步丰富特征空间；(5) 该方法框架可直接迁移至小麦、玉米等其他作物的遥感产量估算任务。

Abstract (英文): Accurate rice yield estimation is essential for food security. Two key factors affecting estimation accuracy are the long-term upward trend in yield over time and regional heterogeneity across space. Current studies predominantly employ statistical detrending methods (e.g., moving averages, linear regression) to isolate temporal trends. However, such methods rely on prior assumptions about the time–yield relationship and may introduce systematic bias when these assumptions break down. Meanwhile, the individual contributions of temporal and spatial information, and their interactive effects, have not been systematically evaluated within a unified framework. We selected 112 rice-growing counties across six U.S. states (2000–2021), using vegetation index (Normalized Difference Vegetation Index), meteorological indicators (growing degree days, killing degree days, and cumulative precipitation), and spatiotemporal variables (year, longitude, and latitude). We designed six input configurations to compare conventional detrending against direct temporal variable inclusion, testing across four model architectures (Long Short-Term Memory, Random Forest, XGBoost, and Transformer). Results showed that: (1) directly inputting year significantly outperformed detrending across all models, with the combined spatiotemporal configuration achieving the best performance (LSTM R2 = 0.61 vs. 0.54 for detrending); (2) year was the most important predictor in SHAP analysis, with spatiotemporal variables ranking higher than most meteorological and remote sensing variables; (3) spatial information consistently improved accuracy and mitigated systematic bias for extreme yield regions; (4) the combined configuration performed best across different states, years (including extreme climate events), and yield levels, achieving near-end-of-season accuracy at the grain-filling stage (1.5–2 months before harvest). This study demonstrates that integrating raw spatiotemporal data directly into deep learning models is more effective than statistical detrending, offering a simpler and more robust approach for large-scale crop yield estimation.
