### [264] [UAV-Based Soil Salinity Estimation Using Stagewise Feature Optimization and Dual-Backbone Deep Learning Fusion](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132237)
*Chao Zhang,Yujie Hu,Min Tang,Shaoyuan Feng,Zhen Zheng,Ziang Xie,Zhijun Jia,Huailiang Wang,Lei Xie*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文针对小样本农业条件下土壤盐分估算难题，提出了一种集成轻量级卷积神经网络和分阶段特征优化的无人机土壤盐分估算框架。通过RF-RFE、One-SE准则和VIF分析将129个候选变量精简为16通道特征集，构建并评估了三种单骨干和三种双骨干特征级融合网络。结果表明，ResVGGNet在地表盐分估算中表现最佳（R²=0.820，RMSE=0.626 g/kg），SHAP分析揭示了植被和盐分敏感指数的主导作用。该框架有效提升了小样本条件下无人机土壤盐分估算的准确性、鲁棒性和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小样本农业条件下土壤盐分精确估算面临标记数据稀缺、单骨干神经网络表征能力有限以及地下盐分反演复杂性高等三重挑战，亟需开发更有效的估算方法。

Method: 1) 构建RF-RFE、One-SE准则和VIF分析相结合的特征选择框架，将129个候选变量精简为16通道统一特征集；2) 构建三种单骨干网络（VGGNet、ResNet、DenseNet）和三种双骨干特征级融合网络（DenseResNet、DenseVGGNet、ResVGGNet）；3) 采用SHAP分析进行模型可解释性评估。

Result: 单骨干网络中ResNet统计精度最高，DenseNet趋势保持最优；ResVGGNet在地表盐分估算中表现最佳，R²=0.820，RMSE=0.626 g/kg，MAE=0.409 g/kg，RPD=2.31；SHAP分析显示植被和盐分敏感指数及光谱均值特征起主导作用。

Conclusion: 轻量级多骨干特征级融合与精简特征优化策略的集成，有效提升了小样本农业条件下无人机土壤盐分估算的准确性、鲁棒性和可解释性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) 可引入时空融合策略，将多时序遥感影像（如Sentinel-2）与无人机数据结合，增强小样本下的时序特征学习能力；2) 可尝试Transformer或Mamba等新型骨干网络替代CNN骨干，以捕捉更远距离的空间依赖关系；3) 可加入物理信息约束（如土壤传输方程）作为损失函数正则项，提升地下盐分反演的物理一致性；4) 特征选择阶段可引入因果发现方法替代相关性分析，剔除虚假关联特征；5) 可扩展至多尺度特征融合策略，分别在不同空间分辨率下提取浅层和深层盐分特征。

Abstract (英文): Accurate soil salinity estimation under small-sample agricultural conditions continues to pose a formidable challenge, attributed to the scarcity of labeled data, inherent representational limitations of single-backbone neural networks, and the heightened complexity of subsurface salinity inversion. To mitigate these intertwined challenges, this study developed a UAV-enabled soil salinity estimation framework that integrated lightweight convolutional neural networks and staged feature optimization, leveraging both RGB and multispectral imagery. A feature selection framework integrating random forest recursive feature elimination (RF-RFE), the one-standard-error (One-SE) criterion, and variance inflation factor (VIF) analysis was employed to reduce 129 candidate variables to a unified 16-channel feature set, which served as the common input for estimating both surface and subsurface soil salinity. Three lightweight single-backbone (VGGNet, ResNet, and DenseNet) and dual-backbone feature-level fusion networks (DenseResNet, DenseVGGNet, and ResVGGNet) were constructed and systematically evaluated for their performance in estimating both surface and subsurface soil salinity. Among the single-backbone networks, ResNet yielded the highest overall statistical accuracy, while DenseNet exhibited superior performance in preserving estimation trends. For surface soil salinity estimation, ResVGGNet achieved the best performance among all evaluated models, with an R2 of 0.820, RMSE of 0.626 g/kg, MAE of 0.409 g/kg, and RPD of 2.31 on the test dataset. SHAP analysis further highlighted the dominant role of vegetation and salinity-sensitive indices, together with selected spectral mean features, and revealed spatially complementary response patterns among major input channels. Collectively, the integration of lightweight multi-backbone feature-level fusion with streamlined feature optimization strategies effectively enhances the accuracy, robustness, and interpretability of UAV-enabled soil salinity estimation, particularly under the constraint of small agricultural sample sizes.

### [265] [Memory-Guided Adaptive Spectral–Spatial Perception Model for Hyperspectral Image Classification](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132225)
*Xinhui Wang,Bin Yan,Pengyu Guo,Xiaolong Yang,Hongyu Liu,LZ Cao,Yong Liu,Zhi Yang,Yuhang Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对高光谱图像小样本分类难题，提出了记忆引导自适应光谱-空间感知模型（MGAS-SP），通过单样本级、批内级、跨批级三级全局化策略，在仅用0.5%-1%训练样本的情况下，在多个数据集上取得了优于现有方法的分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高光谱图像分类中标注样本稀缺是核心瓶颈，现有方法在小样本条件下分类性能不足，亟需一种能在极度稀疏标注下仍保持高精度的分类模型。

Method: 提出三级全局化策略：(1) 单样本级：自适应感知Transformer，结合可变形/膨胀卷积与Transformer编码器提取单个样本的全局上下文；(2) 批内级：度量学习策略，显式捕捉小批量内样本间的结构依赖与特征关系，实现局部上下文的特征聚合；(3) 跨批级：记忆引导策略，构建动态记忆库存储并检索历史同类别样本特征，桥接过去与当前分布以增强泛化。

Conclusion: 三级全局化策略有效解决了小样本条件下高光谱图像分类的难题，记忆引导机制能够跨批次利用历史信息，显著提升模型在标注稀缺场景下的泛化能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：(1) 当前模型在单样本级使用卷积+Transformer，计算量较大，可引入轻量化注意力机制（如线性注意力、窗口注意力）降低参数量；(2) 批内度量学习可结合对比学习或原型网络进一步强化小样本判别能力；(3) 动态记忆库可扩展为跨任务记忆，适配少样本增量学习场景；(4) 模型可直接迁移至遥感图像语义分割、变化检测等任务，仅需调整输出头即可。

Abstract (英文): Accurate hyperspectral image classification is fundamental to geospatial applications but is often constrained by annotation scarcity. To achieve high classification performance under small-sample conditions, we propose the Memory-Guided Adaptive Spectral–Spatial Perception model, which incorporates a three-level globalization strategy. At the single-sample level, an adaptive perception Transformer combines deformable and dilated convolutions with a Transformer encoder to capture global context from individual samples. At the intra-batch level, we introduce a metric learning strategy that explicitly captures structural dependencies and feature relationships among samples within each mini-batch, enabling comprehensive feature aggregation in a localized context. At the cross-batch level, a memory-guided strategy constructs a dynamic memory bank to store and retrieve features from same-class samples across training iterations, bridging past and present distributions to enhance generalization. Using only 1% of the SaliLMSS, Pavia University and Kennedy Space Center datasets and 0.5% of the WHU-LongKou dataset as training samples, our method achieves outstanding overall accuracy of 96.15%, 97.81%, 89.22% and 99.32%, respectively, outperforming existing methods.

### [266] [UAV Remote Sensing for Drought-Adaptive Sesame Breeding: Flight-Altitude Benchmarking, Predictive Modelling, and Composite Stress Tolerance Indexing](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132181)
*Christos Petsoulas,Alexandros Tsitouras,Eleftherios Evangelou,Anastasia Kargiotidou,Chrysanthi Pankou,Dimitrios Ν. Vlachostergios*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 该研究利用大疆Phantom 4多光谱无人机在40、80、120米高度对588个芝麻基因型进行高通量表型分析，比较了三种机器学习模型，发现40米高度精度最高（R²=0.812），树集成模型在跨物候期预测中优于OLS，并基于复合耐逆指数筛选出38个优异基因型，富集效率为随机预期的4.1倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期芝麻育种需要对大量未重复群体在不同环境下进行高通量表型分析，传统地面测量效率低，亟需开发基于无人机的高效、准确的表型分析方法。

Method: 使用大疆Phantom 4多光谱无人机在40、80、120米三个高度对588个M2基因型（充分灌溉ENV1和终期干旱ENV2两个环境）进行四次飞行（2025年7-9月）。通过运动恢复结构生成冠层高度模型，从40米影像提取NDVI、NDRE、GNDVI、LCI四种光谱指数。采用OLS、随机森林和梯度提升三种模型，在留一基因型、留一环境和留一日期的交叉验证下评估，用组内相关系数量化基因型重复性，用复合耐逆指数排名干旱表现。

Result: 40米高度冠层高度精度最高（ENV1: R²=0.812, ENV2: R²=0.663）。留一基因型验证精度R²≈0.83，但留一日期验证（更符合实际应用场景）下降至R²≈0.55。全结构-光谱OLS模型在跨物候期预测中崩溃（R²=-0.203），而树集成模型保持稳定。光谱指数在干旱胁迫下重复性提升约2倍（ICC(3,4)>0.84）。复合STI筛选出38个优异基因型（占7.6%），其中前30名中有10个出现在育种者从588行中选出的48个最优品种中，富集效率为随机预期的4.1倍（超几何p=4.5×10⁻⁵）。

Conclusion: 无人机多光谱遥感和机器学习方法可以有效支持芝麻早期育种的高通量表型分析，40米飞行高度是最优选择，树集成模型比OLS更适合跨物候期预测，复合耐逆指数能够有效筛选耐旱基因型。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究直接属于遥感与农业育种的交叉应用。改进方向：（1）可引入深度学习（如3D-CNN或Transformer）替代传统树集成模型，进一步提升跨物候期预测精度；（2）可融合多时相时序特征（如动态变化曲线）替代单时相光谱指数；（3）可加入热红外或激光雷达数据以增强干旱胁迫监测能力；（4）可尝试迁移学习框架，将模型迁移至其他作物（如小麦、玉米）的耐逆性筛选。

Abstract (英文): Early-generation sesame (Sesamum indicum L.) breeding requires high-throughput phenotyping of large unreplicated populations across contrasting environments. A DJI Phantom 4 Multispectral UAV was flown at 40, 80, and 120 m above ground level (AGL) over 588 M2 genotypes under full irrigation (ENV1) and terminal drought (ENV2; irrigation withheld from reproductive onset) on four dates (July–September 2025). Structure-from-motion canopy height models were compared with ground measurements, and four spectral reflectance indices—Normalised Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI), Normalised Difference Red Edge (NDRE), Green Normalised Difference Vegetation Index (GNDVI), and Leaf Chlorophyll Index (LCI)—were derived from 40 m imagery. Ordinary least squares (OLS), Random Forest, and Gradient Boosting were evaluated under leave-one-genotype-out (LOGO), leave-one-environment-out (LOEO), and leave-one-date-out (LODO) cross-validation; genotypic repeatability was quantified by intraclass correlation (ICC), and drought performance was ranked by a composite Stress Tolerance Index (STI) validated against an independent breeder assessment. The 40 m altitude gave the highest height accuracy (R2 = 0.812 in ENV1; 0.663 in ENV2). LOGO accuracy (R2 ≈ 0.83) fell to R2 ≈ 0.55 under LODO—the operationally relevant figure for a new phenological stage—and the full structural–spectral OLS model collapsed (R2 = −0.203) where tree ensembles remained stable. Spectral-index repeatability was up to ~2-fold higher under stress (ICC(3,4) &gt; 0.84). The composite STI flagged 38 elite genotypes (7.6% of 498); 10 of its top 30 were confirmed in the breeder’s 48-best selection from all 588 rows—a 4.1-fold enrichment over chance (hypergeometric p = 4.5 × 10−5).

### [267] [Assessing Urban Ventilation Resistance and Surface Warming Using Multi-Source Data: A Case Study of Kaifeng City](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132227)
*Huiqi Sun,Hao Zheng,Lu Yu,Jingyuan Cheng*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究集成XGBoost、SHAP和多尺度地理加权回归(MGWR)，分析了1986-2024年开封市六种形态、生态和人类活动因子对地表温度(LST)的影响。结果表明：LST显著上升且年际波动减小；夜间灯光(NTL)始终是主导因子，建筑密度(BF)和NTL共同反映城市扩张；建筑迎风面密度(FAD)在城乡边缘区空间异质性远强于城市核心区，虽整体贡献较小但提供了密度指标无法捕捉的非线性、方向性和空间异质性的通风阻力诊断信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市形态变化强烈影响地表热环境，但长期以来对两者关系的定量评估（特别是通风阻力因素的作用）仍十分有限。现有研究多关注短期或单一维度的城市形态-LST关系，缺乏将建筑致密化、通风形态阻力、生态条件和人类活动强度纳入长期LST驱动分析的综合框架。

Method: 集成三种方法：(1) XGBoost用于建模六种因子（形态、生态、人类活动）与LST的非线性关系；(2) SHAP用于解释各因子的特征重要性及边际贡献；(3) 多尺度地理加权回归(MGWR)用于捕捉空间异质性，特别是FAD（建筑迎风面密度）在不同空间位置（城市核心vs.边缘区）的差异化影响。

Result: (1) 1986-2024年LST显著上升，年际变率下降，区域热波动逐渐减小；(2) NTL在五个代表年份中始终是主导指标，BF与NTL共同捕捉了城市扩张和人类活动增强的影响；(3) FAD系数在边缘区的空间异质性远强于核心区：2020年边缘区FAD系数离散度是中心区的2.74倍，表明城市扩张期间通风形态约束存在强烈空间分化；FAD整体预测贡献不大，但提供了常规密度指标无法捕获的补充诊断信息。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了整合建筑致密化、通风形态阻力、生态条件和人类活动强度的长期LST驱动框架，弥补了以往研究主要关注短期或单一维度的不足，为城市更新和向外扩张过程中的热风险管理提供了证据支持。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。具体方案：(1) 遥感数据源扩展：本研究LST来自遥感，可将方法框架直接应用于其他城市或区域的长时间序列热红外遥感数据（如Landsat、MODIS、ECOSTRESS）;(2) 引入更高分辨率遥感数据：使用高空间分辨率遥感影像提取更精细的建筑形态参数（如迎风面密度FAD），结合LiDAR或立体像对DSM数据提升三维通风阻力表征精度；(3) 多源遥感融合：将遥感反演的LST、不透水面比例、NDVI/NDBI生态参数、NTL等多源遥感特征统一纳入该框架，形成全遥感驱动的城市热环境分析体系；(4) 气象卫星数据协同：结合风场遥感数据（如ASCAT散射计）或再分析资料，直接验证FAD通风阻力的实际效果；(5) 时空融合算法应用：针对长时间序列分析需求，采用ESTARFM等时空融合模型填补云遮挡导致的数据缺失，提升时间连续性。

Abstract (英文): Changes in urban form strongly affect surface thermal conditions, yet long-term quantitative assessments of this relationship, particularly the role of ventilation resistance, remain limited. To address this gap, this study integrates XGBoost, SHapley Additive explanations (SHAP), and multi-scale geographically weighted regression (MGWR) to examine how six morphological, ecological, and human-activity factors influence land surface temperature (LST) in Kaifeng City. The results indicate three main findings. First, LST increased significantly from 1986 to 2024, while interannual variability declined, indicating a gradual reduction in regional thermal fluctuations. Second, NTL was consistently the dominant indicator across the five representative years, while BF and NTL together captured the effects of urban expansion and intensified human activity. Third, FAD coefficients were more spatially heterogeneous in urban fringe areas than in the urban core. In 2020, the dispersion of FAD coefficients in fringe areas was 2.74 times greater than that in the central area, indicating stronger spatial differentiation in ventilation-related morphological constraints during urban expansion. Although FAD made only a modest contribution to overall predictive accuracy, it provided supplementary diagnostic information not captured by conventional density indicators and showed nonlinear, directional, and spatially heterogeneous responses. Compared with previous studies that mainly examined short-term or single-dimensional relationships between urban morphology and LST, this study integrates building densification, ventilation-related morphological resistance, ecological conditions, and human activity intensity into a long-term LST-driver framework, providing evidence to support heat-risk management during urban regeneration and outward expansion.

### [268] [Lagged Response of Groundwater Storage to Extreme Precipitation Using Machine-Learning-Downscaled GRACE Data at the Watershed Scale](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132217)
*Xiaoling Zheng,Yilei Yu,Jiyi Jiang,Lihu Yang,Shiqin Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用LightGBM模型降尺度GRACE数据，生成了2002-2024年白洋淀流域1km分辨率地下水储量异常(GWSA)数据集，分析了地下水对极端降水的响应，发现地下水储量呈现三个不同阶段的变化，且极端降水事件对地下水补给的响应存在约两个月的滞后。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估地下水储量对极端降水的响应对于理解气候变化下含水层的恢复力至关重要。

Method: 利用Light Gradient Boosting Machine (LightGBM)模型对GRACE观测数据进行降尺度，生成1km分辨率GWSA数据集；基于该产品分析长期地下水变化，并通过复合分析量化GWSA对极端降水事件的响应。

Result: 地下水储量呈现三个阶段：2014年前快速枯竭(−1.35 cm/yr)、2014-2019年缓慢下降(−1.04 cm/yr)、2020年后显著恢复(+3.45 cm/yr)；GWSA呈西南低东北高的空间格局；极端降水事件后约两个月出现最强地下水响应信号；月有效降水量比短时强降水与GWSA恢复关联更紧密，平原区响应强于山区。

Conclusion: 极端降水事件提供间歇性补给脉冲，而持续的地下水恢复依赖于累积气候输入和人类水管理的影响。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该研究已展示遥感与水文交叉的典范，改进方向：(1)可引入多源遥感数据（如SMAP土壤水分、Sentinel-1 InSAR地表形变）作为辅助变量提升降尺度精度；(2)可扩展到其他流域验证模型泛化能力；(3)可结合深度学习（如CNN-LSTM）与物理机理模型进行时空融合；(4)可加入人类活动遥感指标（如灌溉面积、城市扩张）以分离自然与人为因素对地下水的影响。

Abstract (英文): Understanding how groundwater storage responds to extreme precipitation is essential for assessing aquifer resilience under climate variability. In this study, we developed a 1 km groundwater storage anomaly (GWSA) dataset for the Baiyangdian Watershed from 2002 to 2024 by downscaling GRACE observations with a Light Gradient Boosting Machine (LightGBM) model. The downscaled GWSA showed good consistency with independent hydrological datasets, including GLDAS and groundwater-level anomalies. Based on the downscaled product, we characterized long-term groundwater changes and quantified GWSA responses to extreme precipitation events (EPEs). Groundwater storage exhibited three distinct phases: rapid depletion before 2014 (−1.35 cm/yr), a slower decline during 2014–2019 (−1.04 cm/yr), and marked recovery after 2020 (+3.45 cm/yr). Spatially, GWSA generally increased from the southwest to the northeast of the watershed. Composite analysis of 11 EPEs revealed a delayed groundwater response, with the strongest signal occurring approximately two months after precipitation. Monthly effective precipitation was more closely associated with GWSA recovery than short-duration daily precipitation extremes, and the response was stronger in plains than in mountainous areas. These findings indicate that EPEs provide episodic recharge pulses, while sustained groundwater recovery depends on cumulative climatic inputs and human water-management influences.

### [269] [SAGE: Saliency and Geometry Enhanced Transferable Attacks for LiDAR Point Cloud Perception in Remote Sensing](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132209)
*Yuheng Wu,Shiwei Lin,Shibo Ping,Xingchao Zhai,Zhiyuan Fang,Meijuan Chen,Weiquan Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出SAGE框架，通过结合点坐标先验与源模型梯度生成显著性图，利用显著性引导的扰动分配和几何约束，提升LiDAR点云对抗样本的可迁移性，同时保持几何质量，在分类和3D检测任务上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LiDAR点云的迁移攻击方法存在两个主要问题：(1) 扰动区域对替代模型具有判别性，但在不同架构间不够稳定，导致可迁移性有限；(2) 对抗样本存在明显的几何畸变。为解决这些问题，需要一种既能提升攻击可迁移性又能保持点云几何质量的方法。

Method: SAGE框架包含三个关键组件：(1) 统一点坐标先验与源模型梯度信号生成显著性图，作为脆弱局部结构的可迁移指示器；(2) 基于显著性图的扰动分配，将更多扰动分配到对迁移更有效的区域；(3) 显式几何约束，在增强可迁移性的同时保持点云几何质量。

Result: 在点云分类基准和基于KITTI、nuScenes数据集的LiDAR 3D目标检测任务上，SAGE在攻击成功率上持续优于现有迁移攻击方法，同时保持了对抗点云的良好几何质量。

Conclusion: SAGE为评估基于LiDAR的遥感感知系统的迁移鲁棒性提供了一种有效且实用的框架，证明了结合显著性引导和几何约束可以显著提升点云对抗攻击的可迁移性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是针对遥感感知（LiDAR点云）的论文，改进方案包括：(1) 可将显著性图生成机制引入多模态遥感融合感知（如LiDAR+相机），增强跨模态迁移攻击能力；(2) 几何约束可进一步结合遥感点云特有的地物结构先验（如建筑物立面、道路边界），提升针对特定遥感任务（如电力线检测、地形分类）的攻击针对性；(3) 当前方法仅验证了分类和检测，可扩展至遥感点云分割、变化检测等任务。

Abstract (英文): LiDAR point clouds are widely used in remote sensing perception scenarios, such as autonomous driving. However, LiDAR-based perception models remain vulnerable to adversarial perturbations, which may compromise the reliability of safety-critical 3D perception systems. Among different attack paradigms, transfer-based attacks are particularly practical because they generate adversarial examples on accessible surrogate models and apply the generated examples directly to unknown target models. Nevertheless, existing transferable attacks on point clouds often perturb regions that are discriminative for the surrogate model but insufficiently stable across different architectures, leading to limited transferability and noticeable geometric distortion. To address this problem, we propose SAGE, a Saliency And Geometry Enhanced transferable attack framework for LiDAR point cloud perception in remote sensing. Specifically, SAGE unifies point-coordinate priors with source-model gradient signals to generate a saliency map, which serves as a transferable indicator of vulnerable local structures. SAGE further leverages this map through saliency-guided perturbation allocation and explicit geometric constraints to enhance transferability while preserving point-cloud geometry. To demonstrate the effectiveness of SAGE, we evaluate SAGE on point-cloud classification benchmarks and further validate it on LiDAR-based 3D object detection using KITTI and nuScenes. Experimental results show that SAGE consistently outperforms existing transferable attack methods in attack success rate while preserving favorable geometric quality of adversarial point clouds. These findings demonstrate that SAGE offers an effective and practical framework for assessing the transfer robustness of LiDAR-based remote sensing perception systems.

### [270] [Finding the Features with LiDAR and SAR: Automated Detection of Archaeological Earthworks at Cahokia](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132229)
*Justin M. Vilbig,Vasit Sagan,Joseph A. Jilek,Cagri Gul*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种半自动化遥感处理流程，结合LiDAR（UAV与载人飞机）和SAR（PALSAR-3、Sentinel-1）数据，通过局部地貌模型、K-means聚类、轮廓检测和局部入射角偏差映射，实现卡霍基亚土墩遗址（UNESCO世界遗产）考古特征（土墩、取土坑、堤道）的检测与圈定。结果显示LiDAR擅长高程定义特征，SAR可捕捉坡度方向异常，二者互补。方法具有可扩展性和场地不变性，显著加速了考古勘探并减少了主观性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂混合环境下的考古特征检测需要准确高效的方法来识别细微的地貌形态信号，传统人工目视解译耗时且主观性强，亟需自动化、可迁移的遥感处理流程。

Method: 1) 使用三组LiDAR数据（两组UAV、一组载人飞机）生成DEM并转为局部地貌模型(LRM)；2) 对LRM进行K-means聚类分割特征类别；3) 利用OpenCV库进行轮廓包围圈定土墩和取土坑；4) 对PALSAR-3和Sentinel-1 SAR数据提取局部入射角(LIA)栅格，通过角度偏差映射识别与考古特征相关的坡度异常。

Result: LiDAR在解析高程定义特征（如土墩足迹）方面表现优异；LIA可捕捉方向性坡度行为，突出显示土墩边缘、取土坑边缘和线性特征（如堤道）。LiDAR采集频率（脉冲设置）对考古特征恢复影响极小，传感器平台选择比功率密度权衡更为关键。所有五项数据集均验证了LiDAR与SAR的互补优势。

Conclusion: 集成工作流虽仍需人工审查以过滤现代干扰和自然假阳性，但显著加速了勘探并减少了解释主观性。该方法可扩展、场地不变且兼容开放获取数据，适用于全球考古景观。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该工作流可直接迁移至遥感考古领域其他复杂遗址。改进方向：1) 引入深度学习（如U-Net或Transformer）替代K-means聚类以提升分割精度；2) 融合多时相SAR干涉测量（InSAR）监测微形变辅助考古特征识别；3) 加入高光谱数据补充植被胁迫信号；4) 开发自动化后处理模块减少人工审查负担。

Abstract (英文): Archaeological feature detection at complex, mixed-environment sites requires accurate, efficient methods for identifying subtle morphological signatures. This study presents a semi-automated remote sensing pipeline for the detection and delineation of archaeological earthworks at Cahokia Mounds (Illinois, USA), a major Mississippian urban center and UNESCO World Heritage Site. Three LiDAR datasets, two collected via UAV-mounted sensors and one from a piloted aircraft survey, were processed into Digital Terrain Models and transformed into Local Relief Models (LRM). K-means clustering was applied to segment the LRMs into feature classes, followed by contour bounding using the OpenCV library to outline mounds and borrow pits. Additionally, SAR-derived Local Incidence Angle (LIA) rasters from PALSAR-3 and Sentinel-1 were processed through angular deviation mapping to identify slope anomalies associated with archaeological features. Results across all five datasets demonstrate the complementary strengths of LiDAR and SAR: LiDAR excels at resolving elevation-defined features such as mound footprints, while LIA captures directional slope behavior that highlights mound edges, borrow pit rims, and linear features such as causeways. Comparative analysis of LiDAR acquisition frequencies reveals minimal differences in archaeological feature recovery between pulse settings, suggesting that sensor platform choice matters more than power-density tradeoffs for this application. Despite the need for human review to filter modern disturbances and natural false positives, the integrated workflow meaningfully accelerates prospection and reduces interpretive subjectivity. The methods are scalable, site-invariant, and work with open-access data, making them applicable to archaeological landscapes worldwide.

To address these issues, this study proposes an improved YOLOv12-based crop detection and counting model, named YOLO-DC. By introducing an attention mechanism (LGCB-AM) and a multi-scale detection head (MS-DH), the proposed model effectively enhances local texture extraction, global modeling, foreground–background contrast, and boundary perception for dense small objects. Subsequently, a series of comparative experiments, ablation studies, and transfer experiments were conducted on the wheat and rice datasets. The results show that YOLO-DC achieves a favorable balance among detection accuracy, counting error, and model efficiency and overall outperforms the other comparison models. Ablation studies further verify the effectiveness of the proposed design, showing that LGCB-AM is the key contributor to the performance improvement, while the boundary branch and repulsion branch play critical roles in dense-target discrimination. In addition, an appropriate module insertion strategy can effectively balance high-level semantic enhancement and feature fusion stability. Transfer experiments demonstrate that pretraining on the wheat dataset and fine-tuning on the rice dataset significantly outperform training from scratch, indicating strong cross-crop transfer potential. Overall, the proposed YOLO-DC provides an effective solution for high-precision crop detection and counting in agricultural scenarios.

### [273] [A Hybrid VRT-S-BR Method for Composite Electromagnetic Scattering from Targets Above Vegetated Rough Surfaces](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132183)
*Yu-Feng Zou,Shui‐Rong Chai,Xiao-Jie Qu,Jiajun Li,Kun Chao,Lixin Guo,Wei Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合VRT-S-BR方法，用于预测植被覆盖粗糙表面上目标的复合电磁散射。该方法利用VRT-S模型生成植被诱导的复反射系数离线数据库，在BR射线追踪过程中替代传统菲涅尔反射项，并引入面元依赖的相位补偿方案。在天然草地实测数据上验证，HH和VV极化下的RMSE分别为1.82 dB和3.10 dB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合方法在描述植被覆盖粗糙表面上目标复合电磁散射时，通常采用经验性随机相位扰动，缺乏对植被诱导衰减和相干散射效应的精确建模，导致预测精度受限。

Method: 1) 将植被层建模为分层随机介质；2) 利用VRT-S模型在不同入射角下生成植被诱导复反射系数离线数据库；3) 在BR射线追踪中，用该系数替代传统菲涅尔反射项，逐次考虑植被衰减与相干散射；4) 引入面元依赖的相位补偿方案描述射线穿过植被冠层的传播路径变化。

Result: 在天然草地实测后向散射数据上，HH和VV极化的RMSE分别为1.82 dB和3.10 dB；该方法能有效表征不同植被覆盖度、高度、地形背景及双站观测几何下的目标-植被耦合散射特性。

Conclusion: 所提VRT-S-BR混合方法能够精确预测植被覆盖粗糙表面上目标的复合电磁散射，克服了传统经验相位扰动的局限性，具有较高的工程应用价值。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感电磁散射领域的核心研究。改进方向：1) 可扩展至多频段（如L、C、X波段）的植被散射数据库构建，提升宽频适应性；2) 引入机器学习方法加速VRT-S离线数据库的生成与插值；3) 考虑植被层的时间动态变化（如生长周期、含水量变化），实现时变散射特性预测；4) 结合极化干涉SAR（PolInSAR）应用，进一步优化相位补偿模型以提升植被高度反演精度。

Abstract (英文): This paper proposes a hybrid Vector Radiative Transfer Shooting (VRT-S)-Bouncing Ray (BR) method, referred to as the VRT-S-BR method, for predicting composite electromagnetic scattering from targets above vegetation-covered rough surfaces. In this proposed framework, the vegetation layer is modeled as a stratified random medium and incorporated into the BR solver through VRT-S-derived amplitude modulation and deterministic phase compensation. Specifically, an offline database of vegetation-induced complex reflection coefficients is first generated using the VRT-S model over a set of incidence angles. During the BR ray-tracing process, these coefficients are used to replace the conventional Fresnel reflection terms on a per-interaction basis, thereby accounting for vegetation-induced attenuation and coherent scattering effects. In addition, a facet-dependent phase compensation scheme is introduced to describe propagation-path variations of individual rays through the vegetation canopy, avoiding the empirical random phase perturbation used in previous hybrid models. The proposed method is validated against field-measured backscattering data over natural grassland, achieving root mean square height (RMSE) values of 1.82 dB and 3.10 dB for horizontal-horizontal (HH) and vertical-vertical (VV) polarizations, respectively. Numerical results further demonstrate the capability of the method to characterize target–vegetation coupled scattering under different percentages of vegetation cover, vegetation heights, terrain backgrounds, and bistatic observation geometries.

### [274] [Locally Adaptive Mamba and Multi-Scale Feature Enhancement for Optical Remote Sensing Image Change Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132226)
*Mingxuan Ding,Qirong Zhou,Qiaolin Ye,Le Sun*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: LADENet是一种融合CNN、Transformer和Mamba的新型遥感变化检测框架，通过局部自适应标记、多尺度特征增强和跨尺度融合，在四个基准数据集上取得了领先性能（LEVIR-CD上F1达91.06%，IoU达85.28%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遥感变化检测方法面临三大挑战：1）难以协同建模局部细节与全局特征；2）双时相差异表示方式单一；3）跨尺度特征通信不足。这些限制导致模型在复杂环境下的精度和鲁棒性不足。

Method: LADENet包含四个核心模块：1）权重共享的多级Transformer编码器+序列缩减机制，生成多尺度全局特征并降低计算复杂度；2）基于状态空间扫描（SSS）的双时空自适应局部特征标记模块，实现高显著变化区域定位与像素级融合；3）双分支差异增强模块（注意力增强差异分支+多尺度卷积拼接分支），协同捕获全局变化趋势与细粒度局部特征；4）全局跨尺度空间特征融合解码器，通过空间注意力与二维选择性扫描实现多尺度特征融合与空间分辨率恢复。

Result: 在四个基准数据集上：LEVIR-CD（F1 91.06%, IoU 85.28%）、WHU-CD（F1 90.51%, IoU 82.45%）、CLCD-CD（F1 82.15%, IoU 72.83%）、GVLM-CD（F1 89.12%, IoU 77.78%），均优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: LADENet通过CNN、Transformer与Mamba三种范式的协同融合，在复杂双时相观测环境中展现出优异的检测精度、边界描绘能力和泛化性能，验证了多范式融合在遥感变化检测任务中的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感变化检测领域的创新工作。可能的改进方向：1）可引入多模态数据融合（如SAR+光学），利用Mamba的状态空间建模能力处理异质模态特征；2）将自适应局部标记模块扩展到视频遥感变化检测，实现时序连续变化捕捉；3）结合弱监督或半监督学习范式，降低对像素级标注的依赖；4）探索将状态空间扫描与物理先验知识融合，提升在云雾遮挡等不利条件下的鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Within the domain of Earth observation, tracking terrestrial transitions via high-resolution optical data plays a fundamental role. Nevertheless, current methods face critical challenges, including the difficulty in collaborative modeling of local details and global features and the singularity of bi-temporal difference representation, along with insufficient cross-scale feature communication, thereby constraining both the precision and resilience of models when applied to complicated environments. To solve these problems, we propose LADENet (Locally Adaptive Mamba and Multi-scale Feature Enhancement Network), an innovative framework that synergizes CNN, Transformer, and Mamba paradigms. By leveraging customized local contextual refinement alongside sophisticated hierarchical fusion, this integration delivers highly precise and resilient detection performance. LADENet adopts a weight-sharing multi-level Transformer encoder combined with a sequence reduction mechanism to generate multi-scale global features, achieving precise alignment of bi-temporal features and global context modeling while reducing computational complexity. To realize accurate localization and local enhancement of changed regions, we design a dual spatiotemporal adaptive local feature marking module based on State-Space Scanning (SSS). This module screens high-saliency changed regions through an adaptive scanning strategy, realizes pixel-aligned spatiotemporal feature fusion via cross-temporal state-space scanning, and introduces a sliding window boundary calibration mechanism to alleviate boundary information loss caused by window segmentation. To strengthen the feature representation of changed regions, a dual-branch difference enhancement module is constructed, which collaboratively captures global change trends and fine-grained local features through an attention-enhanced difference branch and a multi-scale convolution concatenation branch, effectively suppressing background interference. To address the semantic gap between cross-scale features, a global cross-scale spatial feature fusion decoder is proposed, which balances local detail preservation and global context perception through the synergy of spatial attention and two-dimensional selective scanning, completing refined multi-scale feature fusion and spatial resolution recovery. To rigorously validate the proposed LADENet, comprehensive experiments were conducted across four widely adopted bi-temporal benchmarks: LEVIR-CD, WHU-CD, CLCD-CD, and GVLM-CD. The presented architecture establishes substantial superiority over existing cutting-edge methodologies across primary evaluation criteria. Specifically, it yields an F1-measure of 91.06% alongside an IoU of 85.28% in the LEVIR-CD tests, while registering 90.51% (F1) and 82.45% (IoU) for WHU-CD. Similarly, robust outcomes are delivered on CLCD-CD (82.15% F1, 72.83% IoU) as well as GVLM-CD (89.12% F1, 77.78% IoU). These results demonstrate that LADENet possesses excellent detection accuracy, boundary delineation capability and generalization performance in diverse and intricate bi-temporal observation environments.

### [275] [Efficient Sea Clutter Suppression Algorithm Based on BCD-Accelerated Dictionary Learning and TQWT Denoising](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132201)
*Jin Wang,Yubing Han,Yancun Lyu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合块坐标下降（BCD）加速字典学习与可调Q因子小波变换（TQWT）去噪的级联海杂波抑制方法，用于复杂海况下的弱雷达目标检测。该方法通过BCD替代全局SVD实现字典学习加速，结合自适应软阈值算子和批量自适应OMP实现高效重构与杂波对消，最后利用TQWT滤除残差非平稳杂波和噪声。在实测IPIX雷达数据上的实验表明，该方法平均SCNR提升17.48 dB，总执行时间仅7.99秒，在抑制性能与计算效率间取得了优异平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 海杂波和海洋尖峰的非平稳特性使得弱雷达目标检测极具挑战性，而传统字典学习算法（如K-SVD）存在计算复杂度高的问题，难以满足实际应用对实时性的要求。现有方法在杂波抑制效果与计算效率之间难以取得良好平衡。

Method: 提出级联框架：（1）BCD加速字典学习阶段，用块坐标下降策略替代全局SVD实现字典原子与稀疏系数的联合低复杂度优化，结合自适应软阈值算子；（2）批量自适应OMP重构阶段，引入Gram矩阵预计算与双停止机制，实现杂波分量高效重构与初步对消；（3）TQWT去噪阶段，利用可调Q因子小波变换的窄带特征表示与位移不变性滤除残差非平稳杂波和噪声。

Result: 在IPIX数据库和《雷达学报》公开数据集上的实测数据实验表明，所提方法平均SCNR提升17.48 dB，总执行时间仅7.99秒，显著优于传统K-SVD算法。

Conclusion: 所提的BCD加速字典学习与TQWT去噪级联方法在杂波抑制性能和计算效率之间实现了极佳平衡，为复杂海况下的弱目标检测提供了一种高效实用的解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。具体方案：（1）将BCD加速字典学习直接应用于SAR海面杂波抑制与舰船目标检测，替代计算昂贵的传统K-SVD方法；（2）可调Q因子小波变换（TQWT）可用于遥感图像的多尺度去噪和特征增强，特别是对海洋遥感图像中非平稳噪声的抑制；（3）可进一步将该框架扩展至SAR图像中的地杂波/植被杂波抑制，将Q因子自适应调整与场景散射特性结合；（4）将Gram矩阵预计算与双停止机制的OMP用于遥感高光谱图像稀疏解混与重建，提升计算效率。

Abstract (英文): Detecting weak radar targets in complex sea conditions is inherently challenging due to non-stationary sea clutter and sea spikes. Furthermore, traditional dictionary learning algorithms for clutter suppression suffer from high computational complexity. To address these issues, this paper proposes an efficient sea clutter suppression method cascading Block Coordinate Descent (BCD)-accelerated dictionary learning with Tunable Q-factor Wavelet Transform (TQWT) denoising. During dictionary learning, a BCD strategy replaces global Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) with analytical optimization. Combined with an adaptive soft-thresholding operator, this enables low-complexity joint optimization of dictionary atoms and sparse coefficients, drastically reducing training time. Subsequently, a batch-adaptive Orthogonal Matching Pursuit (OMP) algorithm featuring Gram matrix precomputation and a dual-stop mechanism achieves efficient reconstruction and preliminary cancellation of clutter components. Finally, TQWT is applied to filter out residual non-stationary clutter and noise by leveraging its narrowband feature representation and shift invariance. Experiments on measured radar data from the IPIX database and datasets published by the Journal of Radars demonstrate that the proposed method significantly outperforms traditional K-SVD-based algorithms. Specifically, it improves the average signal-to-clutter-plus-noise ratio (SCNR) by 17.48 dB and requires a total execution time of only 7.99 s, achieving a highly favorable trade-off between suppression performance and computational efficiency.

Abstract (英文): Multimodal fusion unlocks the potential of point cloud semantic segmentation, thereby driving advancements in surface observation and visual perception tasks. Although light detection and ranging (LiDAR) systems capture precise 3D structural geometry and optical images provide rich semantic and textural information, existing fusion methods struggle with limited cross-modal perception and insufficient information complementarity. To address these limitations, we propose a multi-stage LiDAR-image collaborative perception fusion network (MCPFNet) for point cloud semantic segmentation of urban scenes. ### [277] [Total Ozone Column Changes over Northeast China: Trends and Variability Analysis](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132189)
*Yu Shi,O. Evtushevsky,Gennadi Milinevsky*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 基于MSR-2和ERA5数据集，分析了2015-2024年中国东北地区(40–53°N, 115–135°E)月平均总臭氧柱(TOC)的变化，并结合Longfengshan站地面观测数据，研究了TOC的季节性模式及其与臭氧浓度、气温的关系。未发现显著线性趋势，但区域年均TOC高于纬向均值25 DU(7.4%)，2月最大、8月最小，分别比北半球中纬度早1-2个月。TOC从东北(~415 DU)向西南(~330 DU)递减，与地面臭氧浓度呈强正相关(|r|=0.8-0.9)，与温度呈强负相关。讨论了Brewer-Dobson环流、准定常波和东北冷涡的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示中国东北地区TOC的时空变化特征及其季节异常模式，探究TOC与地表臭氧浓度和温度之间的定量关系，验证区域地面观测站数据作为TOC代表的可靠性，并探讨Brewer-Dobson环流等大尺度动力过程对区域TOC的影响机制。

Method: 采用MSR-2多传感器再分析数据和ERA5再分析数据集，结合Longfengshan WMO/GAW站地面观测数据，对2015-2024年中国东北地区月平均TOC进行趋势分析、空间分布特征分析、季节循环分析与相关分析，并与北半球中纬度纬向均值进行对比。

Result: (1) TOC无显著线性趋势；(2) 区域年均TOC高于纬向均值25 DU(7.4%)；(3) 区域TOC年极大值出现在2月(比北半球中纬度早1个月)，极小值在8月(早2个月)；(4) TOC从东北(~415 DU)向西南(~330 DU)递减；(5) TOC与地表臭氧浓度呈强正相关(|r|=0.8-0.9)，与地表温度呈强负相关；(6) Longfengshan站与MSR-2数据月均差异在±15 DU(±4.2%)内。

Conclusion: 中国东北地区TOC具有独特的季节循环和空间分布特征，与地表臭氧浓度和温度存在强相关，该区域地面观测站数据可有效代表区域TOC变化。研究结果可用于东亚地区臭氧观测分析、TOC变化研究及平流层-对流层耦合研究。

Abstract (英文): Based on the Multi-Sensor Reanalysis Version 2 (MSR-2) and ERA5 datasets, variations in monthly mean total ozone column (TOC) over Northeast China (40–53°N, 115–135°E) from 2015 to 2024 are analyzed. Local ground-based observations at the regional WMO/GAW Longfengshan Station are also used. The aim is to investigate regional seasonality in TOC pattern and the relationship between TOC and ozone concentration and air temperature in the stratosphere and at the surface. No statistically significant linear trend was found for TOC; however, the annual mean TOC in the study region exceeds the zonal mean TOC by 25 DU (7.4%), and the annual maximum in February and minimum in August are observed one and two months earlier, respectively, than in the Northern Hemisphere mid-latitudes. A climatological decrease in TOC from the northeastern (~415 DU) to southwestern (~330 DU) parts of Northeast China was found. We also found a strong correlation, approaching |r| = 0.8–0.9, between TOC and ozone concentration (positive) and temperature (negative) at the surface. The time series from Longfengshan Station for 2015–2022 closely match the MSR-2 data averaged over Northeast China: the monthly mean difference varies within ±15 DU (±4.2%), validating the reliability of the station data as a representative proxy for regional TOC variability. The role of the Brewer–Dobson circulation, quasi-stationary waves, and the Northeast China cold vortex in the detected patterns and quantitative associations of TOC is discussed. The findings of this work can be applied to analyze the ozone observations, TOC variability, and stratosphere–troposphere coupling in East Asia.

Method: 采用不透水面扩张指标（扩张速率、扩张强度）揭示不透水面时空动态，并运用区位中心性指数（LCI）研究五个超大城市（城市尺度）的扩张结构与模式，分析邻接扩张等不同类型占比。

Abstract (英文): Analyzing the impervious surface area (ISA) of China’s three major urban agglomerations and expansion pattern of representative cities is of great significance for formulating context-specific urban planning policies and enhancing the resilience of urban development. This research employs impervious surface expansion indicators to reveal the spatiotemporal dynamics of impervious surface area, and further applies the location centrality index (LCI) to investigate the expansion structures and patterns of five megacities. The results indicate that the ISA of China’s three major urban agglomerations expanded from 22,544.10 km2 to 69,348.59 km2 from 1985 to 2024; both the expansion rate and intensity have exhibited a distinct decelerating trend. However, significant regional variation exists in the peak expansion phases: the Guangdong–Hong Kong–Macao Greater Bay Area Urban Agglomeration (GBA) peaked during the Initial Exploratory Phase (1985–1995), whereas the Yangtze River Delta Urban Agglomeration (YRD) and Beijing–Tianjin–Hebei Urban Agglomeration (BTH) reached their peaks during the High-speed Development Phase (2005–2015). At the urban scale, LCI-based analysis of urban expansion across five megacities reveals that adjacency expansion type has become the predominant form of growth, exceeding 50% in most cities. These findings enhance our understanding of evolutionary trajectories of ISA within urban agglomerations and the expansion patterns of five megacities, providing a scientific basis for sustainable urban planning and urban resilience.

### [279] [MSIA-YOLO: A Multi-Scale Semantic Interaction and Alignment Network for Small Object Detection in Low-Altitude UAV Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132210)
*Wen Zhang,Xiaorong Xue,Bingyan Lu,Yishuo Tian,Jingtong Yang,Xin Zhao,W X Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: MSIA-YOLO是一种基于YOLOv11的小目标检测器，通过多尺度语义交互与对齐（RFAConv增强特征、CHSP-P2高分辨率语义补偿、DTIA-Head任务协同对齐），在VisDrone、TinyPerson和RSOD数据集上分别提升mAP50达7.7%、10.3%和1.0%，优于多种先进检测器。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 在主干中集成RFAConv（感受野注意力卷积）增强边缘纹理等局部细节；2) 构建CHSP-P2小目标检测框架，增加P2分支并通过尺度序列融合机制实现跨尺度高分辨率语义补偿；3) 设计DTIA-Head（动态任务交互与对齐头），通过动态任务交互和空间对齐促进分类与定位的联合优化。

Result: 在VisDrone、TinyPerson、RSOD数据集上，相比YOLOv11n基线，mAP50分别提升7.7%、10.3%和1.0%，且优于多种先进检测器。

Conclusion: MSIA-YOLO在小目标、密集目标和复杂场景目标检测中展现出良好的有效性和泛化能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。本文本身就是遥感相关论文（在RSOD遥感数据集上验证），可直接应用于遥感小目标检测。改进方向：1) 可将CHSP-P2框架与遥感多尺度特征（如不同分辨率遥感影像）进一步适配；2) DTIA-Head可针对遥感目标旋转不变性需求扩展为旋转框对齐模块；3) RFAConv可结合遥感影像的多光谱/高光谱通道信息进行通道级感受野注意力增强。

Abstract (英文): Small object detection is fundamentally constrained by the lack of discriminative fine-grained features. Although introducing higher resolution detection scales can improve performance, it also amplifies background noise. In addition, the independently decoupled design of conventional detection heads is insufficient to address the persistent challenges of missed detections and false positives for small objects. To this end, we propose MSIA-YOLO, a YOLOv11-based detector with multi-scale semantic interaction and alignment, optimized from three complementary perspectives: feature modeling, high resolution semantic compensation, and task coordinated alignment. First, Receptive Field Attention Convolution (RFAConv) is integrated into the backbone to enhance critical local details, such as edge and texture cues, via receptive field aware attention. Second, to alleviate fine detail attenuation caused by repeated downsampling, we construct a CHSP-P2 small object detection framework with an additional P2 branch. A scale sequence fusion mechanism is further introduced to perform high resolution semantic compensation through cross scale hybrid inputs. Finally, we design a DTIA-Head (Dynamic Task Interaction and Alignment Head), which promotes joint optimization of classification and localization through dynamic task interaction and spatial alignment. Extensive experiments on the public datasets VisDrone, TinyPerson, and RSOD show that, compared with the YOLOv11n baseline, MSIA-YOLO improves mAP50 by 7.7%, 10.3%, and 1.0%, respectively, while also outperforming several advanced detectors. These results demonstrate the effectiveness and generalization capability of the proposed method in small object, dense object, and complex scene object detection scenarios.

</details>
